nārāyaṇam namaskṛtya naram ca eva narottamam uvāca tatas droṇe hate rājan duryodhana mukhāḥ nṛpāḥ śukla ambara dharam viṣṇum śaśi varṇam catur bhujam te droṇam upaśocantaḥ kaśmala abhihata ojasaḥ paryupāsanta śoka ārtāḥ tatas śāradvatī sutam muhūrtam te samāśvāsya hetubhiḥ śāstra saṃmitaiḥ rātri āgame mahīpālāḥ svāni veśmāni bhejire viśeṣataḥ sūtaputraḥ rājā ca eva suyodhanaḥ cintayantaḥ kṣayam tīvram nidrām na eva upalebhire sahitāḥ te niśāyām tu duryodhana niveśane ati pracaṇḍāt vidveṣāt pāṇḍavānām mahātmanām yat tat dyūta parikliṣṭām kṛṣṇām āninyire sabhām cintayantaḥ ca pārthānām tān kleśān dyūta kāritān kṛcchreṇa kṣaṇadām rājan ninyuḥ abda śata upamām tatas prabhāte vimale sthitāḥ diṣṭasya śāsane cakruḥ āvaśyakam sarve vidhi dṛṣṭena karmaṇā te kṛtvā avaśya kāryāṇi samāśvasya ca bhārata yogam ājñāpayām āsuḥ yuddhāya ca viniryayuḥ karṇam senāpatim kṛtvā kṛta kautukamaṅgalāḥ vācayitvā dvijaśreṣṭhān dadhi pātra ghṛta akṣataiḥ vardhyamānāḥ jaya āśīrbhiḥ sūta māgadha bandibhiḥ tathā eva pāṇḍavāḥ rājan kṛta sarva āhnika kriyāḥ śibirāt niryayuḥ rājan yuddhāya kṛta niścayāḥ kurūṇām pāṇḍavānām ca paraspara vadha eṣiṇām tatas śatru kṣayam kṛtvā su mahantam raṇe vṛṣaḥ paśyatām dhārtarāṣṭrāṇām phalgunena nipātitaḥ tatas tat saṃjayaḥ sarvam gatvā nāgāhvayam puram ācakhyau dhṛtarāṣṭrāya yat vṛttam kurujāṅgale āpageyam hatam śrutvā droṇam ca samare paraiḥ yaḥ jagāma parām ārtim vṛddhaḥ rājā ambikā sutaḥ sa śrutvā nihatam karṇam duryodhana hita eṣiṇam katham dvijavara prāṇān adhārayata duḥkhitaḥ yasmin jaya āśām putrāṇām amanyata sa pārthivaḥ durmaram bata manye aham nṛṇām kṛcchre api vartatām yatra karṇam hatam śrutvā na atyajat jīvitam nṛpaḥ tathā śāṃtanavam vṛddham brahman bāhlikam eva ca tathā eva ca anyān suhṛdaḥ putra pautrān ca pātitān śrutvā yat na ajahāt prāṇān tat manye duṣkaram dvija na hi tṛpyāmi pūrveṣām śṛṇvānaḥ caritam mahat uvāca hate karṇe mahā rāja niśi gāvalgaṇiḥ tadā sa hāstinapuram gatvā bhṛśam udvigna mānasaḥ jagāma dhṛtarāṣṭrasya kṣayam prakṣīṇa bāndhavam sa samudvīkṣya rājānam kaśmala abhihata ojasam vavande prāñjaliḥ bhūtvā mūrdhnā pādau nṛpasya ha saṃpūjya ca yathānyāyam dhṛtarāṣṭram mahīpatim hitāni uktāni vidura droṇa gāṅgeya keśavaiḥ a gṛhītāni anusmṛtya kaccit na kuruṣe vyathām rāma nārada kaṇvaiḥ ca hitam uktam sabhā tale suhṛdaḥ tvad hite yuktān bhīṣma droṇa mukhān paraiḥ tam evaṃvādinam rājā sūtaputram kṛtāñjalim gāṅgeye nihate śūre divya astravati saṃjaya droṇe ca parama iṣvāse bhṛśam mama vyathitam manaḥ yaḥ rathānām sahasrāṇi daṃśitānām daśa eva hi sa hataḥ yajñasenasya putreṇa iha śikhaṇḍinā pāṇḍaveya abhiguptena bhṛśam mama vyathitam manaḥ sākṣāt rāmeṇa yaḥ bālye dhanurvede upākṛtaḥ yasya prasādāt kaunteyāḥ rāja putrāḥ mahā balāḥ mahā ratha tvam saṃprāptāḥ tathā anye vasudhādhipāḥ tam droṇam nihatam śrutvā dhṛṣṭadyumnena saṃyuge satya saṃdham mahā iṣvāsam bhṛśam mama vyathitam manaḥ tau droṇa bhīṣmau śrutvā tu hatau mama vyathitam manaḥ tam droṇam nihatam śrutvā kim akurvata māmakāḥ saṃśaptakānām ca bale pāṇḍavena mahātmanā nārāyaṇa astre nihate droṇaputrasya dhīmataḥ hata śeṣeṣu anīkeṣu kim akurvata māmakāḥ plavamānān hate droṇe sanna naukān iva arṇave mad putra śeṣasya tathā tathā anyeṣām ca saṃjaya etat sarvam yathā vṛttam tattvam gāvalgaṇe raṇe ācakṣva pāṇḍaveyānām māmakānām ca sarvaśas uvāca pāṇḍaveyaiḥ hi yat vṛttam kauraveyeṣu māriṣa tat śrutvā mā vyathām kārṣīt iṣṭe na vyathate manaḥ yasmāt abhāvī bhāvī vā bhavet arthaḥ naram prati uvāca na vyathā śṛṇvataḥ kā cit vidyate mama saṃjaya uvāca hate droṇe mahā iṣvāse tava putrāḥ mahā rathāḥ babhūvuḥ āśvasta mukhāḥ viṣaṇṇāḥ gata cetasaḥ avāṅmukhāḥ śastrabhṛtaḥ sarve eva viśām pate a prekṣamāṇāḥ śoka ārtāḥ na abhyabhāṣan parasparam tān dṛṣṭvā vyathita ākārān sainyāni te bhārata ūrdhvam eva abhyavekṣanta duḥkha trastāni anekaśas śastrāṇi eṣām ca rāja indra śoṇita aktāni aśeṣatas prābhraśyanta kara agrebhyaḥ dṛṣṭvā droṇam nipātitam tāni baddhāni aniṣṭāni lambamānāni bhārata adṛśyanta mahā rāja nakṣatrāṇi yathā divi tathā ārtam stimitam dṛṣṭvā gatasattvam iva sthitam svam balam tat mahā rāja rājā duryodhanaḥ abravīt bhavatām bāhu vīryam hi samāśritya mayā yudhi pāṇḍaveyāḥ samāhūtāḥ yuddham ca idam pravartitam tat idam nihate droṇe viṣaṇṇam iva lakṣyate paśyadhvam ca mahātmānam karṇam vaikartanam yudhi nivartate sadā amarṣāt siṃhāt kṣudra mṛgaḥ yathā yena nāga ayuta prāṇaḥ bhīmasenaḥ mahā balaḥ mānuṣeṇa eva yuddhena tām avasthām praveśitaḥ yena divya astra vid śūraḥ māyāvī sa ghaṭotkacaḥ pāṇḍu pāñcāla sainyeṣu drakṣyatha api mahātmanoḥ paśyantu pāṇḍu putrāḥ te viṣṇu vāsavayoḥ iva sarve eva bhavantaḥ ca śūrāḥ prājñāḥ kula udgatāḥ pāṇḍu putrān raṇe hantum sa sainyān kim u saṃhatāḥ śīlavantaḥ kṛtāstrāḥ ca drakṣyatha adya parasparam cakre senāpatim tadā senāpatyam atha āsādya siṃhanādam vinadya uccais prāyudhyata mahā balaḥ sa sṛñjayānām sarveṣām pāñcālānām ca paśyatām kekayānām videhānām akarot kadanam mahat tasya iṣu dhārāḥ śataśas prādurāsan śarāsanāt sa pīḍayitvā pāñcālān pāṇḍavān ca tarasvinaḥ śibirāt hastinapuram prāpya bhārata saṃjayaḥ praviveśa mahā prājñaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭra niveśanam śokena upahataḥ sūtaḥ vihvalaḥ bhṛśa duḥkhitaḥ cintayan nidhanam ghoram sūtaputrasya pāṇḍavaiḥ aśru kaṇṭhaḥ bhṛśam trastaḥ rājānam upajagmivān upasthāya ca rājānam viniḥśvasya ca sūtajaḥ saṃjayaḥ na ati hṛṣṭa manāḥ rājan idam vacanam abravīt cedi kāśi karūśānām matsyānām somakaiḥ saha kṛtvā asau kadanam śete vāta nunnaḥ iva drumaḥ goṣṭha madhye ṛṣabhaḥ iva go vrajaiḥ parivāritaḥ nirāśān pāṇḍavān kṛtvā jaye rājan sa sātyakān pāñcālānām rathān ca eva vinihatya sahasraśas hatvā śūrān mahā iṣvāsān vidrāvya ca diśaḥ daśa hataḥ vaikartanaḥ karṇaḥ pāṇḍavena kirīṭinā hatvā karṇam mahā rāja viśalyaḥ pāṇḍavaḥ abhavat śoṣaṇam sāgarāṇām vā pātanam śaśi sūryayoḥ pṛthivyāḥ dāraṇam yādṛś tādṛś karṇasya pātanam yodhāḥ ca bahavaḥ rājan hatāḥ tatra jaya eṣiṇaḥ rājānaḥ rāja putrāḥ ca śūrāḥ parigha bāhavaḥ ratha oghāḥ ca nara oghāḥ ca hatāḥ rājan sahasraśas vāraṇāḥ nihatāḥ tatra vājinaḥ ca mahā āhave kṣatriyāḥ ca mahā rāja senayoḥ ubhayayoḥ hatāḥ kiṃcid śeṣān parān kṛtvā tīrtvā pāṇḍava vāhinīm pārtha velām samāsādya hataḥ vaikartanaḥ vṛṣā jaya āśā dhārtarāṣṭrāṇām vairasya ca mukham nṛpa tīrṇam tat pāṇḍavaiḥ rājan yat purā na avabudhyase tat idam samanuprāptam vyasanam tvām mahā bhayam putrāṇām rājya kāmena tvayā rājan hita eṣiṇā caritāni ahitāni eva teṣām te phalam āgatam hataḥ duḥśāsanaḥ rājan yathā uktam pāṇḍavena tu pratijñā bhīmasenena nistīrṇā sā camū mukhe pītam ca kṣatajam tasya dhārtarāṣṭrasya sayuge pāṇḍavena mahā rāja kṛtvā karma su duṣkaram uvāca etat śrutvā mahā rāja dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ ambikāsutaḥ vihvalaḥ patitaḥ bhūmau naṣṭa cetāḥ iva dvipaḥ ārta nādaḥ mahān āsīt strīṇām bharata sattama sa śabdaḥ pṛthivīm sarvām pūrayām āsa sarvaśas śoka arṇave mahā ghore nimagnāḥ bharata striyaḥ ruruduḥ duḥkha śoka ārtāḥ bhṛśam udvigna cetasaḥ netrāṇi vāriṇā āpūrya saritaḥ sāgaram yathā rājānam ca samāsādya gāndhārī bharata ṛṣabha niḥsaṃjñā patitā bhūmau sarvāṇi antaḥpurāṇi ca tatas tāḥ saṃjayaḥ rājan samāśvāsayat āturāḥ muhyamānāḥ su bahuśas muñcatyaḥ vāri netra jam samāśvastāḥ striyaḥ tāḥ tu vepamānāḥ muhur muhur kadalyaḥ iva vātena dhūyamānāḥ samantataḥ rājānam viduraḥ ca api prajñācakṣuṣam īśvaram āśvāsayām āsa tadā siñcan toyena kauravam sa labdhvā śanakais saṃjñām tāḥ ca dṛṣṭvā striyaḥ nṛpa unmattaḥ iva rājā sa sthitaḥ tūṣṇīm viśām pate tatas dhyātvā ciram kālam niḥśvasan ca punar punar svān putrān garhayām āsa bahu mene ca pāṇḍavān dhyātvā ca su ciram kālam vepamānaḥ muhur muhur punar gāvalgaṇim sūtam paryapṛcchata saṃjayam yat tvayā kathitam vākyam śrutam saṃjaya tat mayā jaye nirāśaḥ putraḥ mama satatam jaya kāmukaḥ brūyāḥ nirāśaḥ satatam putrāṇām śiva kāmukaḥ bhrātṛbhiḥ ca mahā iṣvāsaiḥ sūtaputraiḥ tanutyajaiḥ duḥśāsanaḥ ca nihataḥ pāṇḍavena yaśasvinā pītam ca rudhiram kopāt bhīmasenena saṃyuge etat śrutvā mahā rāja dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ ambikāsutaḥ dahyamānaḥ abravīt sūtam muhūrtam tiṣṭha saṃjaya vyākulam mama manaḥ tāta mā tāvat kim cit ucyatām rājā api na abravīt kim cit saṃjayaḥ viduraḥ tathā tūṣṇīm bhūtaḥ tathā saḥ atha babhūva jagatīpatiḥ śrutvā karṇam hatam yuddhe putrān ca eva palāyinaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ nṛpa śreṣṭhaḥ dvijaśreṣṭha kim abravīt kāle yat uktavan tasmin tat mama ācakṣva tattvāt uvāca etat śrutvā mahā rāja dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ ambikāsutaḥ abravīt saṃjayam sūtam śoka vyākula cetanaḥ duṣpraṇītena me tāta manasā abhipluta ātmanaḥ hatam vaikartanam śrutvā śokaḥ marmāṇi kṛntati kṛtāstra paramāḥ śalye duḥkha pāram titīrṣavaḥ kurūṇām sṛñjayānām ca ke nu jīvanti ke mṛtāḥ uvāca hataḥ śāṃtanavaḥ rājan durādharṣaḥ pratāpavān hatvā pāṇḍava yodhānām arbudam daśabhiḥ dinaiḥ tatas droṇaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ pāñcālānām ratha vrajān hata śiṣṭasya bhīṣmeṇa droṇena ca mahātmanā viviṃśatiḥ mahā rāja rāja putraḥ mahā balaḥ ānarta yodhān śataśas nihatya nihataḥ raṇe kṣīṇa vāha āyudhaḥ śūraḥ sthitaḥ abhimukhatas parān ghora rūpān parikleśān duryodhana kṛtān bahūn pratijñām smaratā ca eva bhīmasenena pātitaḥ sindhu rāṣṭra mukhāni iha daśa rāṣṭrāṇi yasya vai vaśe tiṣṭhanti vīrasya yaḥ sthitaḥ te śāsane akṣauhiṇīḥ daśa ekām ca nirjitya niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ vartamānaḥ pituḥ śāstre saubhadreṇa nipātitaḥ tathā dauḥśāsaniḥ vīraḥ bāhuśālī raṇa utkaṭaḥ kirātānām adhipatiḥ sāgara anūpa vāsinām tathā kaurava dāyādaḥ saumadattiḥ mahā yaśāḥ hataḥ bhūriśravāḥ rājñ śūraḥ sātyakinā yudhi śrutāyuḥ api ca ambaṣṭhaḥ kṣatriyāṇām dhanurdharaḥ duḥśāsanaḥ mahā rāja bhīmasenena pātitaḥ sudakṣiṇaḥ sa saṃgrāme nihataḥ savyasācinā kosalānām adhipatiḥ hatvā bahu śatān parān bahuśas yodhayitvā ca bhīmasenam mahā rathaḥ madra rāja ātmajaḥ śūraḥ pareṣām bhaya vardhanaḥ asi carma dharaḥ śrīmān saubhadreṇa nipātitaḥ vṛṣasenaḥ mahā tejāḥ śīghra astraḥ kṛta niścayaḥ abhimanyoḥ vadham smṛtvā pratijñām api ca ātmanaḥ nitya prasakta vairaḥ yaḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ viśrāvya vairam pārthena śrutāyūḥ sa nipātitaḥ rājā bhagīrathaḥ vṛddhaḥ bṛhatkṣatraḥ ca kekayaḥ pitāmahaḥ tava tathā bāhlikaḥ saha bāhlikaiḥ jayatsenaḥ tathā rājñ jārāsaṃdhiḥ mahā balaḥ asi carma dharaḥ śūraḥ pareṣām bhaya vardhanaḥ durmarṣaṇaḥ durviṣahaḥ durjayaḥ ca mahā rathaḥ sacivaḥ vṛṣa varmā te sūtaḥ parama vīryavān nāga ayuta balaḥ rājā nāga ayuta balaḥ mahān sa gaṇaḥ pāṇḍu putreṇa nihataḥ savyasācinā vasātayaḥ mahā rāja dvi sāhasrāḥ prahāriṇaḥ śūrasenāḥ ca vikrāntāḥ sarve yudhi nipātitāḥ abhīṣāhāḥ kavacinaḥ praharantaḥ mada utkaṭāḥ śibayaḥ ca ratha udārāḥ kaliṅga sahitāḥ hatāḥ te apāvṛttaka vīrāḥ ca nihatāḥ savyasācinā śreṇayaḥ bahu sāhasrāḥ saṃśaptaka gaṇāḥ ca ye syālau tava mahā rāja rājñau vṛṣaka acalau ugra karmā mahā iṣvāsaḥ nāmataḥ karmataḥ tathā śālva rājaḥ mahā rāja bhīmasenena pātitaḥ oghavant ca mahā rāja bṛhantaḥ sahitaḥ raṇe tathā eva rathinām śreṣṭhaḥ kṣemadhūrtiḥ viśām pate tathā rājā mahā iṣvāsaḥ jalasaṃdhaḥ mahā balaḥ su mahat kadanam kṛtvā hataḥ sātyakinā raṇe rādheyāḥ sūtaputrāḥ ca bhrātaraḥ ca mahā rathāḥ kekayāḥ sarvaśas ca api nihatāḥ savyasācinā ripūṇām kadanam kṛtvā gatāḥ vaivasvata kṣayam mālavāḥ madrakāḥ ca eva draviḍāḥ ca ugra vikramāḥ yaudheyāḥ ca lalitthāḥ ca kṣudrakāḥ ca api uśīnarāḥ māvellakāḥ tuṇḍikerāḥ sāvitrīputra kāñcalāḥ prācya udīcyāḥ pratīcyāḥ ca dākṣiṇātyāḥ ca māriṣa pattīnām nihatāḥ saṃghāḥ hayānām ayutāni ca ratha vrajāḥ ca nihatāḥ hatāḥ ca vara vāraṇāḥ sa dhvajāḥ sa āyudhāḥ śūrāḥ sa varma ambara bhūṣaṇāḥ kālena mahatā yattāḥ kule ye ca vivardhitāḥ te hatāḥ samare rājan pārthena akliṣṭa karmaṇā anye tathā amita balāḥ paraspara vadha eṣiṇaḥ nihatāḥ samare śūrāḥ paraspara samāgame ete ca anye ca bahavaḥ rājānaḥ sa gaṇāḥ raṇe hatāḥ sahasraśas rājan yat mām tvam paripṛcchasi evam eṣa kṣayaḥ vṛttaḥ karṇa arjuna samāgame mahā indreṇa yathā vṛtraḥ yathā rāmeṇa rāvaṇaḥ yathā kṛṣṇena nihataḥ muraḥ raṇa nipātitaḥ kārtavīryaḥ ca rāmeṇa bhārgaveṇa hataḥ yathā sa jñāti bāndhavaḥ śūraḥ samare yuddha durmadaḥ raṇe kṛtvā mahā yuddham ghoram trailokya viśrutam sa amātya bāndhavaḥ rājñ karṇaḥ praharatām varaḥ jaya āśā dhārtarāṣṭrāṇām vairasya ca mukham yatas tīrṇam tat pāṇḍavaiḥ rājan yat purā na avabudhyase ucyamānaḥ mahā rāja bandhubhiḥ hita kāṅkṣibhiḥ na kṛtam ca tvayā pūrvam daivena vidhinā balāt tat idam samanuprāptam vyasanam tvām mahā atyayam putrāṇām rājya kāmānām tvayā rājan hita eṣiṇā ahitāni iva cīrṇāni teṣām te phalam āgatam uvāca ākhyātāḥ māmakāḥ tāta nihatāḥ yudhi pāṇḍavaiḥ nihatān pāṇḍaveyānām māmakaiḥ brūhi saṃjaya uvāca kuntayaḥ yudhi vikrāntāḥ mahā sattvāḥ mahā balāḥ sa anubandhāḥ saha amātyāḥ bhīṣmeṇa yudhi pātitāḥ naraḥ ca aśvāḥ sa nāgāḥ ca rathāḥ ca śataśas narāḥ nārāyaṇāḥ ballavāḥ ca rāmāḥ ca śataśas apare anuraktāḥ ca vijaye bhīṣmeṇa nihatāḥ raṇe samaḥ kirīṭinā saṃkhye vīryeṇa ca balena ca pāñcālāḥ ca mahā iṣvāsāḥ prāyas rājñ amarṣitāḥ saḥ eṣa kadanam kṛtvā mahat raṇa viśāradaḥ parivārya mahāmātraiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ paramakaiḥ rathaiḥ tam kṛtam viratham vīram kṣatra dharme vyavasthitam dauḥśāsaniḥ mahā rāja saubhadram hatavan raṇe paṭaccara nihantā ca mahatyā senayā vṛtaḥ ambaṣṭha sahitaḥ śrīmān mitra hetoḥ parākramī āsādya lakṣmaṇam vīram duryodhana sutam raṇe bṛhantaḥ tu mahā iṣvāsaḥ kṛtāstraḥ yuddha durmadaḥ maṇimant daṇḍadhāraḥ ca rājñau yuddha durmadau aṃśumant bhoja rājaḥ tu saha sainyaḥ mahā rathaḥ anūpa vāsī nīlaḥ ca vyāghradattaḥ ca vīryavān aśvatthāmnā mahā rāja gamitaḥ yama sādanam janamejayaḥ gadā yodhī pārvatīyaḥ pratāpavān droṇena yugapad rājan divam saṃpreṣitau śaraiḥ nṛpāḥ ca pratiyudhyantaḥ parākrāntāḥ viśām pate saṃgrāma nirjitān lokān gamitaḥ droṇa sāyakaiḥ kāśirājaḥ ca kāśikaiḥ bahubhiḥ vṛtaḥ amita ojāḥ yudhāmanyuḥ uttamaujāḥ ca vīryavān amita ojāḥ jayatsenaḥ jayānīkaḥ ca vīryavān amitaujāḥ bṛhatkṣetraḥ kṣatradevaḥ ca pārthivaḥ lakṣmaṇena hatau rājñ te pautreṇa māriṣa bṛhatkṣatraḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ kṣatradevaḥ ca pārthivaḥ nihatya śataśas śūrān paraiḥ vinihatau raṇe kṣatradharmā ca pāñcālyaḥ kṣatravarmā ca māriṣa śikhaṇḍi tanayaḥ yuddhe kṣatradevaḥ yudhām patiḥ lakṣmaṇena hataḥ rājñ te pautreṇa bhārata vārddhakṣemiḥ mahā rāja kṛtvā kadanam āhave āyudha kṣayam āsādya praśāntim paramām gataḥ senābinduḥ nṛpa śreṣṭhaḥ śātravān pratapan yudhi bāhlikena mahā rāja kauraveṇa nipātitaḥ dhṛṣṭaketuḥ mahā rāja cedīnām pravaraḥ rathaḥ tathā satyadhṛtiḥ tāta kṛtvā kadanam āhave pāṇḍava arthe parākrāntaḥ gamitaḥ yama sādanam senābinduḥ kuru śreṣṭhaḥ kṛtvā kadanam āhave putraḥ tu śiśupālasya suketuḥ pṛthivīpate virāṭa putraḥ śaṅkhaḥ ca uttaraḥ ca mahā rathaḥ tathā satyadhṛtiḥ vīraḥ madirāśvaḥ ca vīryavān matsyāt avarajaḥ śrīmān śatānīkaḥ nipātitaḥ śreṇimant ca mahā rāja yudhyamānaḥ parākramī bhīṣmeṇa nihataḥ rājan yudhyamānaḥ parākramī vasudānaḥ ca kadanam kurvāṇaḥ atīva saṃyuge pāṇḍya rājaḥ ca vikrāntaḥ balavān bāhu śālinā ete ca anye ca bahavaḥ pāṇḍavānām mahā rathāḥ uvāca ahatān śaṃsa me sūta ye atra jīvanti ke cana eteṣu nihateṣu adya ye tvayā parikīrtitāḥ uvāca yasmin mahā astrāṇi samarpitāni citrāṇi śubhrāṇi caturvidhāni mahā rathaḥ kṛtimān kṣipra hastaḥ dṛḍha āyudhaḥ dṛḍha muṣṭiḥ dṛḍha iṣuḥ ānarta vāsī hṛdika ātmajaḥ asau mahā rathaḥ sātvatānām variṣṭhaḥ śāradvataḥ gautamaḥ ca api rājan mahā balaḥ bahu citra astra yodhī mahā balaḥ kekaya rāja putraḥ ārtāyaniḥ samare duṣprakampyaḥ senā agraṇīḥ prathamaḥ tāvakānām svasreyān tān pāṇḍaveyān visṛjya satyām vācam tām cikīrṣuḥ tarasvī tejaḥ vadham sūtaputrasya saṃkhye pratiśrutvā ajātaśatroḥ purastāt durādharṣaḥ śakra samāna vīryaḥ śalyaḥ sthitaḥ yoddhu kāmaḥ tvad arthe ājāneyaiḥ saindhavaiḥ pārvatīyaiḥ nadīja kāmboja vanāyu bāhlikaiḥ gāndhāra rājaḥ sa sutaḥ ca rājan tathā suṣeṇaḥ api asi carma pāṇiḥ tava ātmajaḥ satyasenaḥ ca vīraḥ hrīniṣedhāḥ bharatāḥ rāja putrāḥ citrāyudhaḥ śrutakarmā jayaḥ ca ugrāyudhaḥ kṣaṇabhojī sudarśaḥ jārāsaṃdhiḥ prathamaḥ ca adṛḍhaḥ ca kaitavyānām adhipaḥ śūra mānī raṇe raṇe śatru hā rāja putraḥ vīraḥ śrutāyuḥ ca śrutāyudhaḥ ca citrāṅgadaḥ citravarmā sa vīraḥ vyavasthitāḥ ye tu sainye nara agryāḥ prahāriṇaḥ māninaḥ satya saṃdhāḥ uvāca ākhyātāḥ jīvamānāḥ ye parebhyaḥ anye yathātatham uvāca evam bruvan eva tadā dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ ambikāsutaḥ hata pravīram vidhvastam kiṃcid śeṣam svakam balam muhyamānaḥ abravīt ca api muhūrtam tiṣṭha saṃjaya iti evam uktvā vacanam dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ ambikāsutaḥ naṣṭa cittaḥ tatas saḥ atha babhūva jagatīpatiḥ śrutvā karṇam hatam yuddhe putrān ca eva apalāyinaḥ narendraḥ kim cit āśvastaḥ dvijaśreṣṭha kim abravīt uvāca bhūta saṃmohanam bhīmam meroḥ paryasanam yathā saṃśoṣaṇam iva acintyam samudrasya akṣaya ambhasaḥ mahī viyat digīśānām sarva nāśam iva adbhutam saṃcintya nipuṇam buddhyā dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ janeśvaraḥ prāṇinām etat ātma tvāt syāt api iti vināśanam śoka agninā dahyamānaḥ dhamyamānaḥ iva āśayaḥ vidhvasta ātmā śvasan dīnaḥ hā hā iti uktvā su duḥkhitaḥ vilalāpa mahā rāja dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ ambikāsutaḥ uvāca ca punar vākyam saṃśayam bhṛśa vihvalaḥ uvāca vṛṣam apratima skandhaḥ vṛṣabha akṣa gati svanaḥ yasya jyā tala śabdena śara vṛṣṭi raveṇa ca ratha aśva nara mātaṃgāḥ na avatiṣṭhanti saṃyuge yam āśritya mahā bāhum dviṣat saṃgha ghnam acyutam sa katham rathinām śreṣṭhaḥ karṇaḥ pārthena saṃyuge na vṛṣṇīn api tān anyān sva bāhu balam āśritaḥ śārṅga gāṇḍīvadhanvānau sahitau aparājitau aham divyāt rathāt ekaḥ pātayiṣyāmi saṃyuge duryodhanam apādīnam rājya kāmukam āturam yaḥ ca ajaiṣīt atibalān amitrān api durjayān gāndhārān madrakān matsyān trigartān taṅgaṇān śakān pāñcālān ca videhān ca kuṇindān kāśi kosalān suhmān aṅgān ca puṇḍrān ca niṣādān vaṅga kīcakān vatsān kaliṅgān taralān aśmakān ṛṣikān tathā yaḥ jitvā samare vīraḥ cakre bali bhṛtaḥ purā śabarān parahūṇān ca prāc mukhān saralān api mleccha rāṣṭra andhipān ca eva durga āṭavikān tathā jitvā etān samare vīraḥ su tīkṣṇaiḥ kaṅka pattribhiḥ karam āhārayām āsa jitvā sarvān arīn tathā śara vrātaiḥ su niśitaiḥ su tīkṣṇaiḥ kaṅka pattribhiḥ ghātitaḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ śūraiḥ samarthaiḥ vīrya śālibhiḥ vṛṣaḥ mahā indraḥ deveṣu vṛṣaḥ karṇaḥ nareṣu api tṛtīyam anyam lokeṣu vṛṣam na eva anuśuśrumaḥ divya astra vid mahā tejāḥ karṇaḥ vaikartanaḥ vṛṣaḥ uccaiḥśravāḥ varaḥ aśvānām rājñām vaiśravaṇaḥ varaḥ varaḥ mahā indraḥ devānām karṇaḥ praharatām varaḥ yojitaḥ pārthivaiḥ śūraiḥ samarthaiḥ vīrya śālibhiḥ yam labdhvā māgadhaḥ rājā sāntva māna artha gauravaiḥ arautsīt pārthivam kṣatram ṛte kaurava yādavān tam śrutvā nihatam karṇam dvairathe savyasācinā nṛ vṛṣam nihatam śrutvā dvairathe rathinām varam śoka arṇave nimagnaḥ aham aplavaḥ sāgare yathā īdṛśaiḥ yadi aham duḥkhaiḥ na vinaśyāmi saṃjaya jñāti saṃbandhi mitrāṇām imam śrutvā parājayam kaḥ mat anyaḥ pumān loke na jahyāt sūta jīvitam viṣam agnim prapātam vā parvata agrāt aham vṛṇe mahāprasthāna gamanam jalam prāya upaveśanam na hi śakṣyāmi duḥkhāni soḍhum kaṣṭāni saṃjaya uvāca śriyā kulena yaśasā tapasā ca śrutena ca śrute mahā ṛṣi pratimaḥ kṛtakṛtyaḥ asi pārthiva paryavasthāpaya ātmānam mā viṣāde manaḥ kṛthāḥ uvāca yatra rāma pratīkāśaḥ karṇaḥ ahanyata saṃyuge hatvā yudhiṣṭhira anīkam pāñcālānām ratha vrajān pratāpya śara varṣeṇa diśaḥ sarvāḥ mahā rathaḥ mohayitvā raṇe pārthān vajrahastaḥ iva asurān sa katham nihataḥ śete vāta rugṇaḥ iva drumaḥ śokasya antam na paśyāmi samudrasya iva viplukāḥ cintā me vardhate tīvrā mumūrṣā ca api jāyate vajra sāra mayam nūnam hṛdayam su dṛḍham mama yat śrutvā puruṣa vyāghram hatam karṇam na dīryate āyuḥ nūnam su dīrgham mama vihitam daivataiḥ purā yatra karṇam hatam śrutvā jīvāmi iha su duḥkhitaḥ adya ca aham daśām etām gataḥ saṃjaya garhitām kṛpaṇam vartayiṣyāmi śocyaḥ sarvasya manda dhīḥ paribhūtaḥ katham sūta punar śakṣyāmi jīvitum duḥkhāt su duḥkham vyasanam prāptavan asmi saṃjaya na atra śeṣam prapaśyāmi sūtaputre hate yudhi sa hi pāram mahān āsīt putrāṇām mama saṃjaya yuddhe vinihataḥ śūraḥ visṛjan sāyakān bahūn śayīta pṛthivīm nūnam śobhayan rudhira ukṣitaḥ mātaṅgaḥ iva mattena mātaṅgena nipātitaḥ yat balam dhārtarāṣṭrāṇām pāṇḍavānām yatas bhayam saḥ arjunena hataḥ karṇaḥ pratimānam dhanuṣmatām sa hi vīraḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ putrāṇām abhayaṃkaraḥ śete vinihataḥ vīraḥ śakreṇa iva yathā balaḥ duryodhanasya ca ākūtam tṛṣitasya iva piplukāḥ palāyamānaḥ kṛpaṇam dīna ātmā dīna pauruṣaḥ kaccit na nīca ācaritam kṛtavan tāta saṃyuge kaccit na nihataḥ śūraḥ yathā na kṣatriyāḥ hatāḥ uvāca iti evam dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ atha vilapya bahu duḥkhitaḥ provāca saṃjayam bhūyas śoka vyākula locanaḥ gāndhārān ca videhān ca jitvā kārya artham āhave duryodhanaḥ na abhyagṛhṇāt mūḍhaḥ pathyam iva auṣadham śara talpe śayānena bhīṣmeṇa su mahātmanā pānīyam yācitaḥ pārthaḥ saḥ avidhyat medinī talam jalasya dhārām vihitām dṛṣṭvā tām pāṇḍavena ha abravīt sa mahā bāhuḥ tāta saṃśāmya pāṇḍavaiḥ bhrātṛ bhāvena pṛthivīm bhuṅkṣva pāṇḍu sutaiḥ saha tat idam samanuprāptam vacanam dīrghadarśiṇaḥ dyūtataḥ kṛcchram āpannaḥ lūna pakṣaḥ iva dvijaḥ yathā hi śakunim gṛhya chittvā pakṣau ca saṃjaya visarjayanti saṃhṛṣṭāḥ krīḍamānāḥ kumārakāḥ tathā aham api saṃprāptaḥ lūna pakṣaḥ iva dvijaḥ kṣīṇaḥ sarva artha hīnaḥ ca nirbandhuḥ jñāti varjitaḥ kām diśam pratipatsyāmi dīnaḥ śatru vaśam gataḥ sa jitaḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ śūraiḥ samarthaiḥ vīrya śālibhiḥ tasmin hate mahā iṣvāse karṇe yudhi kirīṭinā uktam tvayā purā vīra yathā vīrāḥ nipātitāḥ bhīṣmam a pratiyudhyantam śikhaṇḍī sāyaka uttamaiḥ pātayām āsa samare sarva śastrabhṛtām varam dharmarāja vacaḥ śrutvā aśvatthāmā hataḥ tu iti yukta yogaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ śaraiḥ bahubhiḥ ācitaḥ yasya vidyut prabhām śaktim divyām kanaka bhūṣaṇām prāyacchat dviṣatām hantrīm kuṇḍalābhyām puraṃdaraḥ yasya sarpa mukhaḥ divyaḥ śaraḥ kanaka bhūṣaṇaḥ aśeta nihataḥ pattrī candaneṣu ari sūdanaḥ bhīṣma droṇa mukhān vīrān yaḥ avamanya mahā rathān jāmadagnyāt mahā ghoram brāhmam astram aśikṣata yaḥ ca droṇa mukhān dṛṣṭvā vimukhān arditān śaraiḥ yaḥ ca nāga ayuta prāṇam vāta raṃhasam acyutam viratham bhrātaram kṛtvā bhīmasenam upāhasat kṛpayā viratham kṛtvā na ahanat dharma vittayā yaḥ ca māyā sahasrāṇi dhvaṃsayitvā raṇa utkaṭam ghaṭotkacam rākṣasa indram śakra śaktyā abhijaghnivān saṃśaptakānām yodhāḥ ye āhvayanta sadā anyatas etān hatvā haniṣyāmi paścāt vaikartanam raṇe na ced astrāṇi nirṇeśuḥ sa katham nihataḥ paraiḥ kaḥ hi śaktaḥ raṇe karṇam vidhunvānam mahat dhanuḥ vimuñcantam śarān ghorān divyāni astrāṇi ca āhave jetum puruṣa śārdūlam śārdūlam iva vegitam astrāṇi vā pranaṣṭāni yathā śaṃsasi me hatam na hi anyat anupaśyāmi kāraṇam tasya nāśane na hanyām arjunam yāvat tāvat pādau na dhāvaye iti yasya mahā ghoram vratam āsīt mahātmanaḥ trayodaśa samāḥ nidrām na lebhe puruṣa ṛṣabhaḥ yasya vīryavataḥ vīryam samāśritya mahātmanaḥ mama putraḥ sabhām bhāryām pāṇḍūnām nītavan balāt tatra ca api sabhā madhye pāṇḍavānām ca paśyatām dāsa bhāryā iti pāñcālīm abravīt kuru saṃsadi na santi patayaḥ kṛṣṇe sarve ṣaṇḍhatilaiḥ samāḥ upatiṣṭhasva bhartāram anyam vā varavarṇini iti evam yaḥ purā vācaḥ rūkṣāḥ saṃśrāvayan ruṣā sabhāyām sūtajaḥ kṛṣṇām sa katham nihataḥ paraiḥ yadi bhīṣmaḥ raṇa ślāghī droṇaḥ vā yudhi durmadaḥ kim kariṣyati gāṇḍīvam akṣayyau ca mahā iṣudhī yaḥ ca gāṇḍīva muktānām sparśam ugram a cintayan yasya na āsīt bhayam pārthaiḥ sa putraiḥ sa janārdanaiḥ pratīpam upadhāvadbhiḥ kim punar tāta pāṇḍavaiḥ na hi jyām spṛśamānasya talatre ca api gṛhṇataḥ api syāt medinī hīnā soma sūrya prabhā aṃśubhiḥ yadi mandaḥ sahāyena bhrātrā duḥśāsanena ca sa nūnam ṛṣabha skandham dṛṣṭvā karṇam nipātitam duḥśāsanam ca nihatam manye śocati putrakaḥ jayataḥ pāṇḍavān dṛṣṭvā kim svid duryodhanaḥ abravīt durmarṣaṇam hatam śrutvā vṛṣasenam ca saṃyuge prabhagnam ca balam dṛṣṭvā vadhyamānam mahā rathaiḥ parāṅmukhān tathā rājñaḥ palāyana parāyaṇān vidrutān rathinaḥ dṛṣṭvā manye śocati putrakaḥ viṣame śoka duḥkhābhyām aneyaḥ ca abhimānena bāla buddhiḥ amarṣaṇaḥ hata utsāham balam dṛṣṭvā kim svid duryodhanaḥ abravīt svayam vairam mahat kṛtvā vāryamāṇaḥ suhṛd gaṇaiḥ bhrātaram nihatam dṛṣṭvā bhīmasenena saṃyuge saha gāndhāra rājena sabhāyām yat abhāṣata dyūtam kṛtvā purā hṛṣṭaḥ vañcayitvā ca pāṇḍavān kṛtavarmā mahā iṣvāsaḥ sātvatānām mahā rathaḥ karṇam vinihatam dṛṣṭvā hārdikyaḥ kim abhāṣata brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vaiśyāḥ yasya śikṣām upāsate yuvā rūpeṇa saṃpannaḥ darśanīyaḥ mahā yaśāḥ aśvatthāmā hate karṇe kim abhāṣata saṃjaya kṛpaḥ śāradvataḥ tāta hate karṇe kim abravīt madra rājaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ śalyaḥ samiti śobhanaḥ diṣṭam tena hi tat sarvam yathā karṇaḥ nipātitaḥ kim abhāṣata sauvīraḥ madrāṇām adhipaḥ balī dṛṣṭvā vinihatam sarve yodhāḥ vāraṇa durjayāḥ ye ca ke cana rājānaḥ pṛthivyām yoddhum āgatāḥ vaikartanam hatam dṛṣṭvā kim abhāṣanta saṃjaya kim vaḥ mukham anīkānām āsīt saṃjaya bhāgaśas madra rājaḥ katham śalyaḥ niyuj rathin varaḥ ke arakṣan dakṣiṇam cakram sūtaputrasya saṃyuge vāmam cakram rarakṣuḥ vā ke vā vīrasya pṛṣṭhatas ke karṇam vā ajahuḥ śūrāḥ ke kṣudrāḥ prādravan bhayāt katham ca vaḥ same hata karṇa mahat rathaḥ pāṇḍavāḥ ca katham śūrāḥ pratyudīyuḥ mahā ratham sṛjantam śara varṣāṇi vāri dhārāḥ iva ambudam avaśeṣam na paśyāmi kakude mṛdite sati na mṛṣyāmi ca rādheyam hatam āhava śobhinam yasya bāhvoḥ balam tulyam kuñjarāṇām śatam śatam droṇe hate ca yat vṛttam kauravāṇām paraiḥ saha saṃgrāme nara vīrāṇām tat mama ācakṣva saṃjaya yathā ca dviṣatām hantā raṇe śāntaḥ tat ucyatām uvāca dravamāṇe mahā rāja kauravāṇām bale tathā vyūhya pārthaḥ svakam sainyam atiṣṭhat bhrātṛbhiḥ saha dravat ca sva balam dṛṣṭvā pauruṣeṇa nyavārayat yuddhvā ca su ciram kālam pāṇḍavaiḥ saha bhārata labdhalakṣaiḥ paraiḥ hṛṣṭaiḥ vyāyacchadbhiḥ ciram tadā saṃdhyā kālam samāsādya pratyāhāram akārayat śrameṇa mahatā yuktam tathā droṇa vadhena ca dīna rūpāḥ raṇe kṛtvā karma ghorām ca śarvarīm niveśam prāpya sā senā viśramya muditā abhavat kṛtvā avahāram sainyānām praviśya śibiram svakam varāsaneṣu upaviṣṭāḥ sukha śayyāsu iva amarāḥ upaviṣṭeṣu teṣu evam rāja putreṣu bhārata tān ābhāṣya mahā iṣvāsān prāpta kālam abhāṣata matim matimatām śreṣṭhāḥ sarve prabrūta māciram evam gate tu yat kāryam bhavet kārya karam nṛpāḥ cakruḥ nānāvidhāḥ ceṣṭāḥ siṃhāsana gatāḥ tadā teṣām niśamya iṅgitāni yuddhe prāṇān juhūṣatām samudvīkṣya mukham rājñaḥ bāla arka sama varcasaḥ ācārya putraḥ medhāvī vākya jñaḥ vākyam ādade rāgaḥ yogaḥ tathā dākṣyam nayaḥ ca iti artha sādhakāḥ upāyāḥ paṇḍitaiḥ proktāḥ sarve daiva samāśritāḥ loka pravīrāḥ ye naḥ deva kalpāḥ mahā rathāḥ nītimantaḥ tathā yuktāḥ dakṣāḥ raktāḥ ca te hatāḥ te vayam pravaram nṝṇām sarvaiḥ guṇa gaṇaiḥ yutam karṇam eva abhiṣekṣyāmaḥ saināpatyena bhārata karṇam senāpatim kṛtvā pramathiṣyāmahe ripūn eṣa hi atibalaḥ śūraḥ kṛtāstraḥ yuddha durmadaḥ vaivasvataḥ iva asahyaḥ śaktaḥ jetum raṇe ripūn etat ācārya tanayāt śrutvā rājñ te ātmajaḥ duryodhanaḥ mahā rāja priyam prīta manāḥ tadā āśām bahu matīm cakre karṇam prati sa vai tadā hate bhīṣme ca droṇe ca karṇaḥ jeṣyati pāṇḍavān tām āśām hṛdaye kṛtvā samāśvasya ca bhārata tatas duryodhanaḥ prītaḥ priyam śrutvā vacaḥ tadā prīti saṃskāra saṃyuktam tathyam ātma hitam śubham svam manaḥ samavasthāpya bāhu vīryam upāśritaḥ karṇa jānāmi te vīryam sauhṛdam ca param mayi tathā api tvām mahā bāho pravakṣyāmi hitam vacaḥ śrutvā yatheṣṭam ca kuru vīra yat tava rocate bhīṣma droṇau atirathau hatau senāpatī mama senāpatiḥ bhavān astu tābhyām draviṇavattaraḥ pitāmaha tvam saṃprekṣya pāṇḍu putrāḥ mahā raṇe rakṣitāḥ tāta bhīṣmeṇa divasāni daśa eva ha śikhaṇḍinam puraskṛtya phalgunena mahā āhave tvayā ukte puruṣa vyāghra droṇaḥ hi āsīt puraḥsaraḥ tena api rakṣitāḥ pārthāḥ śiṣya tvāt iha saṃyuge nihatābhyām pradhānābhyām tābhyām amita vikrama bhavān eva tu naḥ śaktaḥ vijayāya na saṃśayaḥ abhiṣecaya senānye svayam ātmānam ātmanā devatānām yathā skandaḥ senā nīḥ prabhuḥ avyayaḥ tathā bhavān imām senām dhārtarāṣṭrīm bibhartu me jahi śatru gaṇān sarvān mahā indraḥ iva dānavān avasthitam raṇe jñātvā pāṇḍavāḥ tvām mahā ratham draviṣyanti sa pāñcālāḥ viṣṇum dṛṣṭvā iva dānavāḥ tasmāt tvam puruṣa vyāghra prakarṣethāḥ mahā camūm bhaviṣyanti saha amātyāḥ pāñcālaiḥ sṛñjayaiḥ saha uvāca āśā balavatī rājan putrasya tava yā abhavat hate bhīṣme ca droṇe ca karṇaḥ jeṣyati pāṇḍavān tām āśām hṛdaye kṛtvā karṇam evam tadā bravīt uvāca rājñām madhye mahā bāhuḥ prīta ātmā sa mahā balaḥ uvāca jeṣyāmi pāṇḍavān rājñ sa putrān sa janārdanān senāpatiḥ bhaviṣyāmi te aham na atra saṃśayaḥ sthiraḥ bhava mahā rāja jitān viddhi ca pāṇḍavān krama āgatam mṛtyum iva uttama amṛtāt uvāca senāpatyena satkartum karṇam skandam iva amarāḥ tatas abhiṣiṣicuḥ tūrṇam vidhi dṛṣṭena karmaṇā duryodhana mukhāḥ rājan rājānaḥ vijaya eṣiṇaḥ toya pūrṇaiḥ viṣāṇaiḥ ca dvīpi khaḍga mahā ṛṣabhaiḥ maṇi muktā mayaiḥ ca anyaiḥ puṇya gandhaiḥ tathā auṣadhaiḥ audumbare samāsīnam āsane kṣauma saṃvṛtam śāstra dṛṣṭena vidhinā saṃbhāraiḥ ca su saṃbhṛtaiḥ brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vaiśyāḥ tathā śūdrāḥ ca saṃmatāḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ tam mahātmānam abhiṣiktam varāsane vācayām āsa vipra agryān rādheyaḥ para vīra hā stūyamānaḥ yathā bhānuḥ udaye brahma vādibhiḥ tatas puṇya aha ghoṣeṇa vāditra ninadena ca jaya śabdena śūrāṇām tumulaḥ sarvatas abhavat jaya iti ūcuḥ nṛpāḥ sarve rādheyam tatra saṃgatāḥ jaya pārthān sa govindān sa anugān tvam mahā āhave jahi pārthān sa pāñcālān rādheya vijayāya naḥ na hi alam tvat visṛṣṭānām śarāṇām te sa keśavāḥ kṛtaghnāḥ sūrya raśmīnām jvalatām iva darśane na hi pārthāḥ sa pāñcālāḥ sthātum śaktāḥ tava agratas uvāca sa satkṛtaḥ stūyamānaḥ suhṛd gaṇa vṛtaḥ vṛṣā duryodhana adya sa gaṇam pāṇḍūnām pravaraiḥ saha phalgunam sūdayiṣyāmi tvad priya artham sa bāndhavam sa parvata arṇava dvīpām śādhi gām gata pāṇḍavām amanyata tadā ātmānam kṛtārtham kāla coditaḥ karṇaḥ api rājan saṃprāpya senāpatyam ariṃdamaḥ yogam ājñāpayām āsa sūryasya udayanam prati tava putraiḥ vṛtaḥ karṇaḥ śuśubhe tatra bhārata devaiḥ iva yathā skandaḥ saṃgrāme tārakā maye uvāca tathā uktaḥ ca svayam rājñā snigdham bhrātṛ samam vacaḥ yogam ājñāpya senāyāḥ āditye abhyudite tadā akarot kim mahā prājñaḥ tat mama ācakṣva saṃjaya uvāca yogam ājñāpayām āsa nāndī tūrya puraḥsaram yogaḥ yoga iti sahasā prādurāsīt mahā svanaḥ nāgānām kﾱpamānānām rathānām ca varūthinām saṃnahyatām padātīnām vājinām ca viśām pate krośatām ca api yodhānām tvaritānām parasparam babhūva tumulaḥ śabdaḥ diva su mahān tadā tatas śveta patākena bāla arka ākāra vājinā hema pṛṣṭhena dhanuṣā hasti kakṣyeṇa ketunā tūṇena śara pūrṇena sa aṅgadena varūthinā śataghnī kiṅkiṇī śakti śūla tomara dhāriṇā dhamantam vārijam tāta hema jāla vibhūṣitam vidhunvānam mahat cāpam kārtasvara vibhūṣitam dṛṣṭvā karṇam mahā iṣvāsam ratha stham rathinām varam na bhīṣma vyasanam ke cit na api droṇasya māriṣa na anyeṣām puruṣa vyāghra menire tatra kauravāḥ tatas tu tvarayan yodhān śaṅkha śabdena māriṣa karṇaḥ niṣkāsayām āsa kauravāṇām varūthinīm vyūham vyūhya mahā iṣvāsaḥ mākaram śatru tāpanaḥ makara vyūham āsthāya daṃśitaḥ ravinandanaḥ pratyudyayau tadā karṇaḥ pāṇḍavān vijigīṣayā netrābhyām śakuniḥ śūraḥ ulūkaḥ ca mahā rathaḥ droṇaputraḥ tu śirasi grīvāyām sarva sodarāḥ vāme pāde tu rāja indra kṛtavarmā vyavasthitaḥ pāde tu dakṣiṇe rājan gautamaḥ satya vikramaḥ trigartaiḥ ca mahā iṣvāsaiḥ dākṣiṇātyaiḥ ca saṃvṛtaḥ mahatyā senayā sārdham madra deśa samutthayā dakṣiṇe tu mahā rāja suṣeṇaḥ satya saṃgaraḥ pucche āstām mahā vīrau bhrātarau pārthivau tadā paśya pārtha mahā senām dhārtarāṣṭrasya saṃyuge karṇena nirmitām vīra guptām vīraiḥ mahā rathaiḥ hata vīratamā hi eṣā dhārtarāṣṭrī mahā camūḥ phalgu śeṣā mahā bāho tṛṇaiḥ tulyā matā mama uddhṛtaḥ ca bhavet śalyaḥ mama dvādaśa vārṣikaḥ evam jñātvā mahā bāho vyūham vyūha yathā icchasi bhrātuḥ tat vacanam śrutvā pāṇḍavaḥ śvetavāhanaḥ dakṣiṇe ca mahā iṣvāsaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ mahā balaḥ madhye vyūhasya sākṣāt tu pāṇḍavaḥ kṛṣṇasārathiḥ nakulaḥ sahadevaḥ ca dharmarājaḥ ca pṛṣṭhatas na arjunam jahatuḥ yuddhe pālyamānau kirīṭinā śeṣāḥ nṛpatayaḥ vīrāḥ sthitāḥ vyūhasya daṃśitāḥ yathābhāvam yathotsāham yathāsattvam ca bhārata evam etat mahā vyūham vyūhya bhārata pāṇḍavāḥ tāvakāḥ ca mahā iṣvāsāḥ yuddhāya eva manaḥ dṛṣṭvā vyūḍhām te camūm sūtaputreṇa saṃyuge nihatān pāṇḍavān mene tava putraḥ saha anvayaḥ tathā eva pāṇḍava senām vyūh dṛṣṭvā yudhiṣṭhira dhārtarāṣṭrān hatān mene sa karṇān vai janādhipa tatas śaṅkhāḥ ca bheryaḥ ca paṇava ānaka gomukhāḥ senayoḥ ubhayayoḥ rājan prāvādyanta mahā svanāḥ siṃhanādaḥ ca saṃjajñe śūrāṇām jaya gṛddhinām haya heṣita śabdāḥ ca vāraṇānām ca bṛṃhitam ratha nemi svanāḥ ca ugrāḥ saṃbabhūvuḥ janādhipa dṛṣṭvā karṇam mahā iṣvāsam mukhe vyūhasya daṃśitam anīka madhye rāja indra rejatuḥ karṇa pāṇḍavau tatas pravavṛte yuddham nara vāraṇa vājinām rathinām ca mahā rāja anyonyam nighnatām dṛḍham uvāca te sene anyonyam āsādya prahṛṣṭa aśva nara dvipe tatas gajāḥ rathāḥ ca aśvāḥ pattayaḥ ca mahā āhave saṃprahāram param cakruḥ deha pāpma praṇāśanam pūrṇa candra arka padmānām kānti tviṣ gandhāt samaiḥ uttamāṅgaiḥ nṛ siṃhānām nṛ siṃhāḥ tastaruḥ mahīm paraśvadhaiḥ ca api akṛntan uttamāṅgāni yudhyatām vyāyata āyata bāhūnām vyāyata āyata bāhubhiḥ vyāyatāḥ bāhavaḥ petuḥ chinna muṣṭi āyudha aṅgadāḥ haya syandana nāgebhyaḥ petuḥ vīrāḥ dviṣat hatāḥ vimānebhyaḥ yathā kṣīṇe puṇye svargasadaḥ tathā pothitāḥ śataśas petuḥ vīrāḥ vīrataraiḥ raṇe rathāḥ vara rathaiḥ nāgaiḥ aśva ārohāḥ ca pattibhiḥ aśva ārohaiḥ padātāḥ ca nihatāḥ yudhi śerate ratha aśva pattayaḥ nāgaiḥ rathaiḥ nāgāḥ ca pattayaḥ ratha patti dvipāḥ ca aśvaiḥ nṛbhiḥ ca aśva ratha dvipāḥ ratha aśva ibha narāṇām ca nara aśva ibha rathaiḥ kṛtam tathā aśva nara nāgānām anyonyam saṃkulam babhau pāṇi pādaiḥ ca śastraiḥ ca rathaiḥ ca kadanam mahat asmān abhyāgaman pārthāḥ vṛkodara purogamāḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca draupadeyāḥ prabhadrakāḥ sātyakiḥ cekitānaḥ ca draviḍaiḥ sainikaiḥ saha bhṛtāḥ vittena mahatā pāṇḍyāḥ ca oḍrāḥ sa keralāḥ vyūḍha uraskāḥ dīrgha bhujāḥ prāṃśavaḥ priya darśanāḥ āpīḍinaḥ rakta dantāḥ matta mātaṅga vikramāḥ nānā virāga vasanāḥ gandha cūrṇa avacūrṇitāḥ baddha asayaḥ pāśa hastāḥ vāraṇa prativāraṇāḥ samāna mṛtyavaḥ rājan anīka sthāḥ parasparam kalāpinaḥ cāpa hastāḥ dīrgha keśāḥ priya āhavāḥ pattayaḥ sātyakeḥ andhrāḥ ghora rūpa parākramāḥ atha apare punar śūrāḥ cedi pāñcāla kekayāḥ karūṣāḥ kosalāḥ kāśyāḥ māgadhāḥ ca api dudruvuḥ teṣām rathāḥ ca nāgāḥ ca pravarāḥ ca api pattayaḥ nānāvidha ravaiḥ hṛṣṭāḥ nṛtyanti ca hasanti ca madhyam vṛkodaraḥ abhyāgāt tvadīyam nāga dhūrgataḥ sa tomara prāsa karaḥ cāru mauliḥ su alaṃkṛtaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā dviradam dūrāt kṣemadhūrtiḥ dvipa sthitaḥ vyapasṛtya tu nāgābhyām maṇḍalāni viceratuḥ kṣveḍita āsphoṭita ravaiḥ bāṇa śabdaiḥ ca sarvaśas tau janān harṣayitvā ca siṃhanādān pracakratuḥ samudyata karābhyām tau dvipābhyām kṛtinau ubhau vāta uddhūta patākābhyām yuyudhāte mahā balau śakti tomara varṣeṇa prāvṛṣ meghau iva ambuṣu kṣemadhūrtiḥ tadā bhīmam tomareṇa stanāntare sa bhīmasenaḥ śuśubhe tomaraiḥ aṅgam āśritaiḥ tatas kulūta adhipatiḥ cāpam āyamya sāyakaiḥ daśabhiḥ tomaram chittvā śaktyā vivyādha pāṇḍavam ripoḥ abhyardayat nāgam unmadaḥ pāṇḍavaḥ śaraiḥ nigṛhyamāṇaḥ na atiṣṭhat vāta dhvastaḥ iva ambudaḥ tām abhyadhāvat dviradam bhīmasenasya nāga rāj mahā vāta īritam megham vāta uddhūtaḥ iva ambudaḥ saṃnivartya ātmanaḥ nāgam kṣemadhūrtiḥ prayatnāt vivyādha abhidrutam bāṇaiḥ bhīmasenam sa kuñjaram tatas sādhu visṛṣṭena kṣureṇa puruṣa ṛṣabhaḥ chittvā śarāsanam śatroḥ nāgam āmitram ārdayat tatas khajākayā bhīmam kṣemadhūrtiḥ parābhinat uddhṛtya khaḍgam niśitam abhyadhāvat sa pāṇḍavam udyata asim upāyāntam gadayā ahan vṛkodaraḥ nihatam nṛpatim dṛṣṭvā kulūtānām yaśaskaram uvāca tatas karṇaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm jaghāna samare śūraḥ śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ tathā eva pāṇḍavāḥ rājan tava putrasya vāhinīm karṇaḥ rājñ mahā bāhuḥ nyavadhīt pāṇḍavīm camūm nārācaiḥ arka raśmi ābhaiḥ karmāra parimārjitaiḥ tatra bhārata karṇena nārācaiḥ tāḍitāḥ gajāḥ neduḥ seduḥ ca mamluḥ ca babhramuḥ ca diśaḥ daśa nakulaḥ abhyadravat tūrṇam sūtaputram mahā raṇe bhīmasenaḥ tathā drauṇim kurvāṇam karma duṣkaram śrutakarmāṇam āyāntam citrasenaḥ mahīpatiḥ saṃśaptaka gaṇān kruddhaḥ abhyadhāvat dhanaṃjayaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ kṛpam ca atha tasmin vīra vara kṣaye śikhaṇḍī kṛtavarmāṇam samāsādayat acyutam śrutakīrtiḥ tathā śalyam mādrī putraḥ sutam te duḥśāsanam mahā rāja sahadevaḥ pratāpavān kekayau sātyakim yuddhe śara varṣeṇa bhāsvatā sātyakiḥ kekayau ca eva chādayām āsa bhārata tau enam bhrātarau vīram jaghnatuḥ hṛdaye bhṛśam viṣāṇābhyām yathā nāgau pratināgam mahā āhave śara saṃbhinna varmaṇau tau ubhau bhrātarau raṇe sātyakim satya karmāṇam rājan vivyadhatuḥ śaraiḥ chādayan śara varṣeṇa vārayām āsa bhārata vāryamāṇau tatas tau tu śaineya śara vṛṣṭibhiḥ śaineyasya ratham tūrṇam chādayām āsatuḥ śaraiḥ atha tau sāyakaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ chādayām āsa duḥsahaiḥ atha anye mṛṣṭe pragṛhya ca mahā śarān tābhyām muktāḥ mahā bāṇāḥ kaṅka barhiṇa vāsasaḥ dyotayantaḥ diśaḥ sarvāḥ saṃpetuḥ svarṇa bhūṣaṇāḥ bāṇa andhakāram abhavat tayoḥ rājan mahā āhave dhanuḥ anyat samādāya sajyam kṛtvā ca saṃyuge kṣurapreṇa su tīkṣṇena anuvinda śiraḥ aharat śoṣayan kekayān sarvān jagāma āśu vasuṃdharām tam dṛṣṭvā nihatam śūram bhrātā tasya mahā rathaḥ sa śaktyā sātyakim viddhvā svarṇa puṅkhaiḥ śilā śitaiḥ nanāda balavat nādam tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt sa sātyakim punar kruddhaḥ kekayānām mahā rathaḥ sa śaraiḥ kṣata sarva aṅgaḥ sātvataḥ sattva kovidaḥ hatvā ca sārathī tūrṇam hayān ca rathinām varau vyarocetām mahā raṅge nistriṃśa vara dhāriṇaḥ cacāra maṇḍalāni eva gata pratyāgatāni ca tam carantam mahā raṅge nistriṃśa vara dhāriṇam tam nihatya raṇe śūraḥ śaineyaḥ ratha sattamaḥ yudhāmanyoḥ ratham tūrṇam āruroha paraṃtapaḥ kekayānām mahat sainyam vyadhamat sātyakiḥ śaraiḥ sā vadhyamānā samare kekayasya mahā camūḥ tam utsṛjya ratham śatrum pradudrāva diśaḥ daśa uvāca śrutakarmā mahā rāja citrasenam mahīpatim ājaghne samare kruddhaḥ pañcāśadbhiḥ śilīmukhaiḥ abhisāraḥ tu tam rājā navabhiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ śrutakarmāṇam āhatya sūtam vivyādha pañcabhiḥ nārācena su tīkṣṇena marma deśe samardayat saḥ atividdhaḥ mahā rāja nārācena mahātmanā mūrchām abhiyayau vīraḥ kaśmalam ca āviveśa ha etasmin antare ca enam śrutakīrtiḥ mahā yaśāḥ navatyā jagatīpālam chādayām āsa pattribhiḥ pratilabya tatas saṃjñām citrasenaḥ mahā rathaḥ saḥ anyat kārmukam ādāya vega ghnam rukma bhūṣaṇam sa śaraiḥ citritaḥ rājan citra mālya dharaḥ yuvā yuvā iva samaśobhat sa goṣṭhī madhye su alaṃkṛtaḥ śrutakarmāṇam atha vai nārācena stanāntare susrāva rudhiram bhūri gairika ambhaḥ iva acalaḥ tatas sa rudhira akta aṅgaḥ rudhireṇa kṛta chaviḥ rarāja samare rājan sa puṣpaḥ iva kiṃśukaḥ śrutakarmā tatas rājan śatrūṇām samabhidrutaḥ śatru saṃvaraṇam kṛtvā dvidhā ciccheda kārmukam atha enam chinna dhanvānam nārācānām tribhiḥ śataiḥ vivyādha bharata śreṣṭha śrutakarmā mahā yaśāḥ navatyā jagatīpālam chādayan nata parvabhiḥ tatas apareṇa bhallena bhṛśam tīkṣṇena sa tvaraḥ jahāra sa śirastrāṇam śiraḥ tasya mahātmanaḥ yadṛcchayā yathā candraḥ cyutaḥ svargāt mahī tale rājānam nihatam dṛṣṭvā abhisāram ca māriṣa antakāle yathā kruddhaḥ sarva bhūtāni preta rāj vyadravanta diśaḥ tūrṇam dāva dagdhāḥ iva dvipāḥ tān tu vidravataḥ dṛṣṭvā nirutsāhān dviṣat jaye drāvayan iṣubhiḥ tūrṇam śrutakarmā vyarocata sārathim tribhiḥ ānarcchat dhvajam eka iṣuṇā tatas svarṇa puṅkhaiḥ śilā dhautaiḥ kaṅka barhiṇa vājitaiḥ tatas śaktim mahā rāja hema daṇḍām durāsadām prāhiṇot tava putrāya ghorām agni śikhām iva tām āpatantīm sahasā śaktim ulkām iva ambarāt sā papāta tadā chinnā prativindhya śaraiḥ śitaiḥ yuga ante sarva bhūtāni trāsayantī yathā aśaniḥ śaktim tām prahatām dṛṣṭvā citraḥ gṛhya mahā gadām sā jaghāna hayān tasya sārathim ca mahā raṇe śaktim cikṣepa citrāya svarṇa ghaṇṭām alaṃkṛtām tām āpatatīm jagrāha citraḥ rājan mahā manāḥ samāsādya raṇe śūram prativindhyam mahā prabhā nirbhidya dakṣiṇam bāhum nipapāta mahī tale patitā abhāsayat ca eva tam deśam aśaniḥ yathā preṣayām āsa saṃkruddhaḥ citrasya vadha kāmyayā jagāma dharaṇīm tūrṇam mahā uragaḥ iva āśayam sa papāta tadā rājan tomareṇa samāhataḥ citram saṃprekṣya nihatam tāvakāḥ raṇa śobhinaḥ sṛjantaḥ vividhān bāṇān śataghnīḥ ca sa kiṅkiṇīḥ te enam chādayām āsuḥ sūryam abhra gaṇāḥ iva tān apāsya mahā bāhuḥ śara jālena saṃyuge te vadhyamānāḥ samare tāvakāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ nṛpa drauṇiḥ ekaḥ abhyayāt tūrṇam bhīmasenam mahā balam uvāca bhīmasenam tatas drauṇiḥ rājan vivyādha pattriṇā atha enam punar ājaghne navatyā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ bhīmasenaḥ samākīrṇaḥ drauṇinā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ rarāja samare rājan raśmivān iva bhāskaraḥ tatas śara sahasreṇa su prayuktena pāṇḍavaḥ śaraiḥ śarān tatas drauṇiḥ saṃvārya yudhi pāṇḍavam lalāṭa stham tatas bāṇam dhārayām āsa pāṇḍavaḥ yathā śṛṅgam vane dṛptaḥ khaḍgaḥ dhārayate nṛpa tatas drauṇim raṇe bhīmaḥ yatamānam parākramī lalāṭa sthaiḥ tatas bāṇaiḥ brāhmaṇaḥ sa vyarocata prāvṛṣi iva yathā siktaḥ triśṛṅgaḥ parvata uttamaḥ tatas śara śataiḥ drauṇim ardayām āsa pāṇḍavaḥ tathā eva pāṇḍavam yuddha drauṇi śara śata śā na akampayata saṃhṛṣṭaḥ vāri oghaḥ iva parvatam tau anyonyam śaraiḥ ghoraiḥ chādayānau mahā rathau ratha caryā gatau śūrau śuśubhāte raṇa utkaṭau ādityau iva saṃdīptau loka kṣaya karau ubhau kṛta pratikṛte yatnam kurvāṇau ca mahā raṇe kṛta pratikṛte yatnam cakrāte tau a bhīta vat śara daṃṣṭrau durādharṣau cāpa vyāttau bhayānakau abhūtām tau adṛśyau ca śara jālaiḥ samantataḥ na tu tat mamṛṣe bhīmaḥ śatroḥ vijaya lakṣaṇam maṇḍalānām vibhāgeṣu gata pratyāgateṣu ca caritvā vividhān mārgān maṇḍalam sthānam eva ca śaraiḥ pūrṇa āyata utsṛṣṭaiḥ anyonyam abhijaghnatuḥ tatas drauṇiḥ mahā astrāṇi prāduścakre mahā rathaḥ graha yuddham yathā ghoram prajā saṃharaṇe abhūt te bāṇāḥ samasajjanta kṣiptāḥ tābhyām tu bhārata bāṇa saṃgha āvṛtam ghoram ākāśam samapadyata uklā pāta kṛtam yadvat prajānām saṃkṣaye nṛpa bāṇa abhighātāt saṃjajñe tatra bhārata pāvakaḥ sarva yuddhāni ca etasya kalām na arhanti ṣoḍaśīm na etādṛśam punar yuddham na bhūtam na bhaviṣyati aho śauryeṇa saṃpannau ubhau brāhmaṇa pāṇḍavau aho bhīme balam bhīmam etayoḥ ca kṛtāstra tā yamau vā puruṣa vyāghrau ghora rūpau imau raṇe śrūyante sma tadā vācaḥ siddhānām vai muhur muhur siṃhanādaḥ ca saṃjajñe sametānām divaukasām adbhutam ca api acintyam ca dṛṣṭvā karma tayoḥ mṛdhe siddha cāraṇa saṃghānām vismayaḥ samapadyata praśaṃsanti tadā devāḥ siddhāḥ ca parama ṛṣayaḥ sādhu drauṇe mahā bāho sādhu bhīma iti ca bruvan parasparam udaikṣetām krodhāt udvṛtya cakṣuṣī krodhāt saṃdaṣṭa daśanau saṃdaṣṭa daśanacchadau anyonyam chādayantau sma śara vṛṣṭyā mahā rathau tatas kruddhau mahā rāja bāṇau gṛhya mahā āhave tau paraspara vegāt ca śarābhyām ca bhṛśa āhatau apovāha raṇāt rājan sarva kṣatrasya paśyataḥ tathā eva pāṇḍavam rājan vihvalantam muhur muhur apovāha rathena ājau sārathiḥ śatru tāpanam uvāca śrutakīrtim atha āyāntam kirantam niśitān śarān madra rājaḥ mahā rāja vārayām āsa hṛṣṭa vat madra rājam samāsādya śrutakīrtiḥ mahā rathaḥ vivyādha bhallaiḥ triṃśatyā kārtasvara vibhūṣitaiḥ sārathim ca asya bhallena bhṛśam vivyādha bhārata sa śalyam śara varṣeṇa chādayām āsa saṃyuge mumoca niśitān bāṇān madra rāja ratham prati tatas śalyaḥ mahā rāja śruta kīrti bhuja cyutān ciccheda samare bāṇān bāṇaiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ śrutakīrtiḥ tatas śalyam bhittvā navabhiḥ āyasaiḥ sārathim tribhiḥ ānarchat punar śalyam ca pañcabhiḥ tasya śalyaḥ dhanuḥ chittvā hasta āvāpam nikṛtya ca vivyādha samare tūrṇam sapta tam śara uttamaiḥ atha anyat dhanuḥ ādāya śrutakīrtiḥ mahā rathaḥ madra īśvaram catuḥṣaṣṭyā bāhvoḥ urasi ca arpayat prativivyādha tam ca api navatyā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ tasya madra īśvaraḥ cāpam punar ciccheda māriṣa paṭṭaiḥ jāmbūnadaiḥ baddhām rūpya paṭṭaiḥ ca bhārata bhrājamānām yathā nārīm divya vastra vibhūṣitām tām āpatatīm sahasā dīpyamāna aśani prabhām viṣṭabhya ca gadām vīraḥ pātayitvā ca bhū tale śrutakīrtim atha āyattaḥ rājan vivyādha pañcabhiḥ tasya śaktim raṇe bhūyas cikṣepa bhujaga upamām tām dvidhā ca ācchinat śalyaḥ medinyām sā tu aśīryata tasya śalyaḥ kṣurapreṇa yantuḥ kāyāt śiraḥ aharat bāla hastāt yathā śyenaḥ āmiṣam vai narottama palāyamānaiḥ taiḥ aśvaiḥ saḥ apanītaḥ raṇa ajirāt śruta kīrtiḥ mahā rāja paśyatām sarva yodhinām tatas madra īśvaraḥ rājā pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm lolayām āsa sa balam siṃhaḥ paśu gaṇān iva śalyaḥ tatra mahā raṅge pāṇḍavānām mahātmanām nihatya pāṇḍu pāñcālān pṛtanāsu vyavasthitaḥ uvāca yathā saṃśaptakaiḥ sārdham arjunasya bhavat raṇaḥ sūtaputrasya pāñcālaiḥ katham yuddham pravartitam anyeṣām ca madīyānām pāṇḍavaiḥ tat bravīhi me uvāca śṛṇu rājan yathāvṛttam saṃgrāmam bruvataḥ mama vīrāṇām śatrubhiḥ sārdham deha pāpma praṇāśanam pārthaḥ saṃśaptaka gaṇam praviśya arṇava saṃnibham śirāṃsi unmathya vīrāṇām śitaiḥ bhallaiḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ pūrṇa candra ābha vaktrāṇi su akṣi bhrū daśanāni ca saṃtastāra kṣitim kṣipram vinālaiḥ nalinaiḥ iva su vṛttān āyatān puṣṭān candana aguru bhūṣitān sa āyudhān sa tanutrāṇān pañcāsya uraga saṃnibhān bāhūn kṣuraiḥ amitrāṇām vicakarta arjunaḥ raṇe dhuryān dhuryatarān sūtān dhvajān cāpāni sāyakān pāṇīn aratnīn asakṛt bhallaiḥ ciccheda pāṇḍavaḥ dvipān hayān rathān ca eva sa ārohān arjunaḥ raṇe tam pravīram nardamānāḥ iva ṛṣabhāḥ vāśitā artham abhikruddhāḥ huṃkṛtvā ca abhidudruvuḥ nighnantam abhijaghnuḥ te śaraiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ iva ṛṣabhāḥ trailokya vijaye yādṛś daityānām saha vajriṇā astraiḥ astrāṇi saṃvārya dviṣatām sarvatas arjunaḥ iṣubhiḥ bahubhiḥ tūrṇam viddhvā prāṇān rarāsa saḥ chinna triveṇu cakra akṣān hata yodha aśva sārathīn saṃchinna yoktra raśmīkān vitriveṇūn vikūbarān rathān viśakalīkurvan mahā abhrāṇi iva mārutaḥ vismāpayan prekṣaṇīyam dviṣātām bhaya vardhanam siddha deva ṛṣi saṃghāḥ ca cāraṇāḥ ca eva tuṣṭuvuḥ deva dundubhayaḥ neduḥ puṣpa varṣāṇi ca apatan keśava arjunayoḥ mūrdhni prāha vāc ca aśarīriṇī candra arka anila vahnīnām kānti dīpti bala dyutīḥ sarva bhūta varau vīrau nara nārāyaṇau ubhau iti etat mahat āścaryam dṛṣṭvā śrutvā ca bhārata aśvatthāmā su saṃyattaḥ kṛṣṇau abhyadravat raṇe atha pāṇḍavam asyantam yama kāla antakān śarān sa iṣuṇā pāṇinā āhūya hasan drauṇiḥ atha abravīt evam ācārya putreṇa samāhūtaḥ yuyutsayā saṃśaptakāḥ ca mama vadhyāḥ drauṇiḥ āhvayate ca mām yat atra anantaram prāptam praśādhi tvam mahā bhuja evam uktaḥ avahat pārtham kṛṣṇaḥ droṇa ātmaja antikam nirveṣṭum bhartṛ piṇḍam hi kālaḥ ayam upajīvinām sūkṣmaḥ vivādaḥ viprāṇām sthūlau kṣātrau jaya ajayau yām na saṃkṣamase mohāt divyām pārthasya satkriyām vivyādha keśavam ṣaṣṭyā nārācaiḥ arjunam tribhiḥ sajyam kṛtvā nimeṣāt tat vivyādha arjuna keśavau tribhiḥ śaraiḥ vāsudevam sahasreṇa ca pāṇḍavam tatas śara sahasrāṇi prayutāni arbudāni ca iṣudheḥ dhanuṣaḥ jyāyāḥ aṅgulībhyaḥ ca māriṣa bāhvoḥ karābhyām urasaḥ vadana ghrāṇa netrāt śara jālena mahatā viddhvā keśava pāṇḍavau tasya nānadataḥ śrutvā pāṇḍavaḥ acyutam abravīt paśya mādhava daurātmyam droṇaputrasya mām prati eṣaḥ asya hanmi saṃkalpam śikṣayā ca balena ca dhanuḥ citram patākām ca ratham śaktim gadām śubhām aśvatthāmnaḥ śarān astān chittvā ekaikam tridhā tridhā vyadhamat bharata śreṣṭhaḥ nīhāram iva mārutaḥ tatas saṃśaptakān bhūyas sa aśva sūta ratha dvipān dhvaja patti gaṇān ugraiḥ bāṇaiḥ vivyādha pāṇḍavaḥ ye ye dadṛśire tatra yat yat rūpam yathā yathā te gāṇḍīva praṇuditāḥ nānā rūpāḥ patatriṇaḥ krośe sāgre sthitān ghnanti dvipān ca puruṣān raṇe bhallaiḥ chinnāḥ karāḥ petuḥ kariṇām mada karṣiṇām chinnāḥ yathā paraśubhiḥ pravṛddhāḥ śaradi drumāḥ paścāt tu śaila vat petuḥ te gajāḥ saha sādibhiḥ śaraiḥ viśakalīkurvan amitrān abhyavīvṛṣat te śarāḥ sūrya saṃkāśāḥ patantaḥ sarvatodiśam alaṃkṛtān aśva sādīn pattīn ca ahan dhanaṃjayaḥ dhanaṃjaya yuga anta arkaḥ saṃśaptaka mahā arṇavam vyaśoṣayata duḥśoṣam tīvraiḥ śara gabhastibhiḥ punar drauṇi mahā śailam nārācaiḥ sūrya saṃnibhaiḥ tam ācārya sutaḥ kruddhaḥ sa aśva yantāram āśugaiḥ tatas parama saṃkruddhaḥ kāṇḍa kośān avāsṛjat aśvatthāmā abhirūpāya gṛhān atithaye yathā atha saṃśaptakān tyaktvā pāṇḍavaḥ drauṇim abhyayāt a pāṅkteyam iva tyaktvā dātā pāṅkteyam arthinam sthitāḥ saṃśaptakāḥ rājan dṛṣṭvā yuddham mahātmanoḥ saṃtāpayantau anyonyam dīptaiḥ śara gabhastibhiḥ loka trāsa karau āstām vimārga sthau grahau iva atha kṛṣṇau śara śataiḥ aśvatthāmnā arditau bhṛśam sa raśmi jāla nikarau yuga anta arkau iva āsatuḥ drauṇāyanim ca abhyahanat pṛṣatkaiḥ vajra agni vaivasvata daṇḍa kalpaiḥ drauṇeḥ iṣūn arjunaḥ saṃnivārya vyāyacchataḥ tat dviguṇaiḥ su puṅkhaiḥ tam sa aśva sūta dhvajam eka vīram āvṛtya saṃśaptaka sainyam ārchat dhanūṃṣi bāṇān iṣudhīḥ dhanuḥ jyāḥ pāṇīn bhujān pāṇi gatam ca śastram chatrāṇi ketūn turagān atha eṣām carmāṇi varmāṇi manorathān ca priyāṇi sarvāṇi śirāṃsi ca eva ciccheda pārthaḥ dviṣatām pramuktaiḥ bāṇaiḥ sthitānām a parāṅmukhānām su kalpitāḥ syandana vāji nāgāḥ samāsthitāḥ kṛta yatnaiḥ nṛ vīraiḥ pārtha īritaiḥ bāṇa gaṇaiḥ nirastāḥ taiḥ eva sārdham nṛ varaiḥ nipetuḥ padma arka pūrṇa indu sama ānanāni kirīṭa mālā mukuṭa utkaṭāni bhalla ardhacandra kṣura hiṃsitāni prapetuḥ urvyām nṛ śirāṃsi ajasram kaliṅga vaṅga aṅga niṣāda vīrāḥ jighāṃsavaḥ pāṇḍavam abhyadhāvan teṣām dvipānām vicakarta pārthaḥ varmāṇi marmāṇi karāt niyantṝn dhvajāḥ patākāḥ ca tatas prapetuḥ vajra āhatāni iva gireḥ śirāṃsi teṣu prarugṇeṣu guroḥ tanūjam bāṇaiḥ kirīṭī nava sūrya varṇaiḥ pracchādayām āsa mahā abhra jālaiḥ vāyuḥ samudyuktam iva aṃśumantam bāṇa andhakāram sahasā eva kṛtvā vivyādha sarvān iṣubhiḥ su puṅkhaiḥ na api ādadat saṃdadhat na eva muñcan bāṇān raṇe adṛśyata savyasācī hatān ca nāgān turagān padātīn saṃsyūta dehān dadṛśuḥ rathān ca saṃdhāya nārāca varān daśa āśu drauṇiḥ tvaran ekam iva utsasarja teṣām ca pañca arjunam abhyavidhyan pañca acyutam nirbibhiduḥ su muktāḥ atha arjunam prāha daśārha nāthaḥ pramādyase kim jahi yodham etam kuryāt dhi doṣam samupekṣitaḥ asau kaṣṭaḥ bhavet vyādhiḥ iva a kriyāvān vakṣaḥ śiraḥ atha apratimau tathā ūrū gāṇḍīva muktaiḥ kupitaḥ vikarṇaiḥ drauṇim śaraiḥ saṃyatyām nirbibheda chittvā aśva raśmīn turagān avidhyat te tam raṇāt ūhuḥ atīva dūram drauṇiḥ dṛḍham pārtha śara abhibhūtaḥ āvṛtya na iyeṣa punar tu yuddham pārthena sārdham matimān vimṛśya jānan jayam niyatam vṛṣṇi vīre dhanaṃjaye ca aṅgirasām variṣṭhaḥ bhagna utsāhaḥ kṣīṇa bāṇa astra yogaḥ niyamya tu hayān drauṇiḥ samāśvasya ca māriṣa ratha aśva nara saṃbādham karṇasya prāviśat balam pratīpa kāye tu raṇāt aśvatthāmni hṛte hayaiḥ mantra oṣadhi kriyā dānaiḥ vyādhau dehāt iva āhṛte uvāca atha uttareṇa pāṇḍūnām senāyām dhvaniḥ utthitaḥ ratha nāga aśva pattīnām daṇḍadhāreṇa vadhyatām vāhayan eva turagān garuḍa anila raṃhasaḥ enam hatvā nihantāsi punar saṃśaptakān iti vākya ante prāpayat pārtham daṇḍadhāra antikam prati sa māgadhānām pravaraḥ aṅkuśa grahaḥ graheṣu asahyaḥ vikacaḥ yathā grahaḥ sapatna senām pramamātha dāruṇaḥ mahīm samagrām vikacaḥ yathā grahaḥ ratha aśva mātaṃga gaṇān sahasraśas samāsthitaḥ hanti śaraiḥ dvipān api rathān adhiṣṭhāya sa vāji sārathīn rathān ca padbhiḥ tvaritaḥ vyapothayat dvipān ca padbhyām caraṇaiḥ kareṇa ca dvipa āsthitaḥ hanti sa kālacakra vat sapatti saṃghān turagān sa sādinaḥ dvipān ca bāṇaiḥ nijaghāna vīryavān narān ca kārṣṇāyasa varma bhūṣaṇān nipātya sa aśvān api pattibhiḥ saha vyapothayat danti vareṇa śuṣmiṇā sa śabda vat sthūla naḍān yathā tathā tatas arjunam dvādaśabhiḥ śara uttamaiḥ janārdanam ṣoḍaśabhiḥ samārdayat atīva cukṣobhayiṣuḥ janārdanam dhanaṃjayam ca abhijaghāna tomaraiḥ atha asya bāhū dvipa hasta saṃnibhau śiraḥ ca pūrṇa indu nibha ānanam tribhiḥ kṣuraiḥ praciccheda saha eva pāṇḍavaḥ tatas dvipam bāṇa śataiḥ samārdayat sa pārtha bāṇaiḥ tapanīya bhūṣaṇaiḥ samārucat kāñcana varma bhṛt dvipaḥ tathā cakāśe niśi parvataḥ yathā dava agninā prajvalita oṣadhi drumaḥ papāta rugṇaḥ sa niyantṛkaḥ tathā yathā giriḥ vajra nipāta cūrṇitaḥ hima avadātena suvarṇa mālinā himādri kūṭa pratimena dantinā hate raṇe bhrātari daṇḍaḥ āvrajat jighāṃsuḥ indrāvarajam dhanaṃjayam samarpayitvā vinanāda ca ardayan tatas asya bāhū vicakarta pāṇḍavaḥ atha ardhacandreṇa hṛtam kirīṭinā papāta daṇḍasya śiraḥ kṣitim dvipāt tat śoṇita ābham nipatat vireje divākaraḥ astāt iva paścimām diśam atha dvipam śveta naga agra saṃnibham divākara aṃśu pratimaiḥ śara uttamaiḥ bibheda pārthaḥ sa papāta nānadan himādri kūṭaḥ kuliśa āhataḥ yathā gajāḥ ratha aśvāḥ puruṣāḥ ca saṃghaśas paraspara ghnāḥ paripetuḥ āhave paraspara praskhalitāḥ samāhatāḥ bhṛśam ca tat tat kula bhāṣiṇaḥ hatāḥ atha arjunam sve parivārya sainikāḥ puraṃdaram deva gaṇāḥ iva bruvan abhaiṣma yasmāt maraṇāt iva prajāḥ sa vīra diṣṭyā nihataḥ tvayā ripuḥ na ced paritrāsye imān janān bhayāt dviṣadbhiḥ evam balibhiḥ prapīḍitān tathā abhaviṣyat dviṣatām pramodanam yathā hateṣu eṣu iha naḥ ariṣu tvayā iti iva bhūyas ca suhṛdbhiḥ īritāḥ niśamya vācaḥ su manāḥ tatas arjunaḥ yathānurūpam pratipūjya tam janam jagāma saṃśaptaka saṃgha hā punar uvāca pratyāgatya punar jiṣṇuḥ ahan saṃśaptakān bahūn pārtha bāṇa hatāḥ rājan nara aśva ratha kuñjarāḥ dhuryam dhuryatarān sūtān rathān ca parisaṃkṣipan pāṇīn pāṇi gatam śastram bāhūn api śirāṃsi ca ciccheda amitra vīrāṇām samare pratiyudhyatām tam pravīrāḥ tvadīyānām nardamānāḥ abhidudruvuḥ vāśitā arthe yuyutsantaḥ vṛṣabhāḥ vṛṣabham yathā āpatanti arjunam śūrāḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas trailokya vijaye yādṛś daityānām saha vajriṇā ugrāyudhaḥ tatas tasya śiraḥ kāyāt apāharat te arjunam sarvatas kruddhāḥ nānā śastraiḥ avīvṛṣan marudbhiḥ preṣitāḥ meghāḥ himavantam iva uṣṇage astraiḥ astrāṇi saṃvārya dviṣatām sarvatas arjunaḥ chinna triveṇu jaṅghā īṣān nihata pārṣṇisārathīn saṃchinna raśmi yoktra akṣān vyanukarṣa yugān rathān te rathāḥ tatra vidhvastāḥ parārdhyāḥ bhānti anekaśas dvipāḥ saṃbhinna marmāṇaḥ vajra aśani samaiḥ śaraiḥ sa ārohāḥ turagāḥ petuḥ bahavaḥ arjuna tāḍitāḥ nirjihva antrāḥ kṣitau kṣīṇāḥ rudhira ārdrāḥ su durdṛśaḥ nara aśva nāgāḥ nārācaiḥ saṃsyūtāḥ savyasācinā aṇakaiḥ ca śilā dhautaiḥ vajra aśani viṣa upamaiḥ mahārha varma ābharaṇāḥ nānā rūpa ambara āyudhāḥ sa rathāḥ sa dhvajāḥ vīrāḥ hatāḥ pārthena śerate vijitāḥ puṇya karmāṇaḥ viśiṣṭa abhijana śrutāḥ gatāḥ śarīraiḥ vasudhām ūrjitaiḥ karmabhiḥ divam atha arjuna ratham vīrāḥ tvadīyāḥ samupādravan nānā janapada adhyakṣāḥ sa gaṇāḥ jāta manyavaḥ uhyamānāḥ ratha aśvaiḥ te pattayaḥ ca jighāṃsavaḥ tad āyudha mahā varṣam kṣiptam yodha mahā ambudaiḥ vyadhamat niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ kṣipram arjuna mārutaḥ sahasā saṃtitīrṣantam pārtham śastra astra setunā atha abravīt vāsudevaḥ pārtham kim krīḍase anagha ete bala adhikāḥ prāptāḥ pārtha kim krīḍase anagha saṃśaptakān pramathya etān tatas karṇa vadhe tvara tathā iti uktvā arjunaḥ kṣipram śiṣṭān saṃśaptakān tadā ākṣipya śastreṇa balāt daityān indraḥ iva avadhīt ādadhat saṃdadhat na iṣūn dṛṣṭaḥ kaiḥ cit raṇe arjunaḥ vimuñcan vā śarān śīghram dṛśyate sma hi kaiḥ api haṃsa aṃsa gaurāḥ te senām haṃsāḥ saraḥ iva āviśan tatas te haṃsa sadṛśāḥ turagāḥ vāta raṃhasaḥ tām senām viviśuḥ hṛṣṭāḥ haṃsāḥ iva mahat saraḥ tatas saṃgrāma bhūmim tām vartamāne jana kṣaye avekṣamāṇaḥ govindaḥ savyasācinam abravīt pṛthivyām pārthivānām vai duryodhana kṛte mahān paśya bhārata cāpāni rukma pṛṣṭhāni dhanvinām mahatām apaviddhāni kalāpān tathā jātarūpa mayaiḥ puṅkhaiḥ śarān ca nata parvṇaḥ taila dhautān ca nārācān nirmuktān iva pannagān hasti danta tsarūn khaḍgān jātarūpa pariṣkṛtān ākīrṇān tomarān cāpān citrān hema vibhūṣitān daṇḍān kanaka citrān ca saṃvṛttāḥ raṇa bhūmayaḥ varmāṇi ca apaviddhāni rukma pṛṣṭhāni bhārata suvarṇa vikṛtān prāsān śaktīḥ kanaka bhūṣitāḥ jāmbūnada mayaiḥ paṭṭaiḥ baddhāḥ ca vipulāḥ gadāḥ jātarūpa mayīḥ ca ṛṣṭīḥ paṭṭiśān hema bhūṣitān daṇḍaiḥ kanaka citraiḥ ca vipraviddhān paraśvadhān parighān bhindipālān ca bhuśuṇḍīḥ kuṇapān api ayaskuśa antān patitān musalāni gurūṇi ca śataghnīḥ paśya citrāḥ ca vipulān parighān tathā cakrāṇi ca apaviddhāni mudgarān ca bahūn raṇe nānāvidhāni śastrāṇi pragṛhya jaya gṛddhinaḥ gaja vāji ratha kṣuṇṇān paśya yodhān sahasraśas manuṣya gaja vājīnām śara śakti ṛṣṭi tomaraiḥ nistriṃśaiḥ paṭṭiśaiḥ prāsaiḥ nakharaiḥ laguḍaiḥ api śarīraiḥ bahudhā bhinnaiḥ śoṇita ogha pariplutaiḥ gatāsubhiḥ amitra ghna saṃvṛtāḥ raṇa bhūmayaḥ bāhubhiḥ candana ādigdhaiḥ sa aṅgadaiḥ śubha bhūṣaṇaiḥ baddha cūḍāmaṇi varaiḥ śirobhiḥ ca sa kuṇḍalaiḥ nikṛttaiḥ vṛṣabha akṣāṇām virājati vasuṃdharā kabandhaiḥ śoṇita ādigdhaiḥ chinna gātra śirodharaiḥ bhūḥ bhāti bharata śreṣṭha śānta arcirbhiḥ iva agnibhiḥ rathān bahuvidhān bhagnān hema kiṅkiṇinaḥ śubhān aśvān ca bahudhā paśya śoṇitena pariplutān anukarṣān upāsaṅgān patākāḥ vividhān dhvajān yodhānām ca mahā śaṅkhān pāṇḍurān ca prakīrṇakān nirasta jihvān mātaṃgān śayānān parvata upamān vaijayantī vicitrān ca hatān ca gaja yodhinaḥ vāraṇānām paristomān su yukta ambara kambalān vipāṭitāḥ vicitrāḥ ca rūpa citrāḥ kuthāḥ tathā bhinnāḥ ca bahudhā ghaṇṭāḥ patadbhiḥ cūrṇitāḥ gajaiḥ vaiḍūrya maṇi daṇḍān ca patitān aṅkuśān bhuvi aśvānām ca yuga āpīḍān ratna citrān uraśchadān baddhāḥ sādi dhvaja agreṣu suvarṇa vikṛtāḥ kaśāḥ vicitrān maṇi citrān ca jātarūpa pariṣkṛtān aśva āstara paristomān rāṅkavān patitān bhuvi cūḍāmaṇīn narendrāṇām vicitrāḥ kāñcana srajaḥ chatrāṇi ca apaviddhāni cāmara vyajanāni ca candra nakṣatra bhāsaiḥ ca vadanaiḥ cāru kuṇḍalaiḥ kḷpta śmaśruṣu atyartham vīrāṇām samalaṃkṛtaiḥ vadanaiḥ paśya saṃchannām mahīm śoṇita kardamām kumuda utpala pattrāṇām ṣaṇḍaiḥ phullaiḥ yathā saraḥ tathā mahībhṛtām vaktraiḥ kumuda utpala saṃnibhaiḥ paśya gām nabhasaḥ tulyām graha nakṣatra mālinaḥ sa jīvān ca narān paśya kūjamānān samantataḥ upāsyamānān bahuṣu nyasta śastraiḥ viśām pate vyutkrāntān aparān yodhān chādayitvā tarasvinaḥ jñātibhiḥ patitaiḥ śūraiḥ yācyamānāḥ tathā udakam jala artham ca gatāḥ ke cit niṣprāṇāḥ bahavaḥ arjuna saṃnivṛttāḥ ca te śūrāḥ tān dṛṣṭvā eva vicetasaḥ jalam dṛṣṭvā pradhāvanti krośamānāḥ parasparam jalam pītvā mṛtān paśya pibataḥ anyān ca bhārata vyutkrāntāḥ samadṛśyanta tatra tatra mahā raṇe paśya aparān nara śreṣṭha saṃdaṣṭa oṣṭha puṭān punar bhrukuṭi kuṭilaiḥ vaktraiḥ prekṣamāṇān samantataḥ evam bruvan tadā kṛṣṇaḥ yayau yena yudhiṣṭhiraḥ arjunaḥ ca api nṛpateḥ darśana artham mahā raṇe tām yuddha bhūmim pārthasya darśayitvā ca mādhavaḥ evam tām darśayan kṛṣṇaḥ yuddha bhūmim kirīṭine śaṅkha dundubhi nirghoṣān bherī paṇava miśritān ratha aśva gaja nādān ca śastra śabdān ca dāruṇān praviśya tat balam kṛṣṇaḥ turagaiḥ vāta vegibhiḥ pāṇḍyena abhyarditām senām tvadīyām vīkṣya dhiṣṭhitaḥ sa hi nānāvidhaiḥ bāṇaiḥ iṣvāsa pravaraḥ yudhi nyahanat dviṣatām vrātān gatāsūn antakaḥ yathā gaja vāji manuṣyāṇām śarīrāṇi śitaiḥ śaraiḥ bhittvā praharatām śreṣṭhaḥ videha asūn cakāra saḥ śatru pravīraiḥ astāni nānā śastrāṇi sāyakaiḥ bhittvā tān ahanat pāṇḍyaḥ śatrūn śakraḥ iva asurān uvāca śikṣām prabhāvam vīryam ca pramāṇam darpam eva ca uvāca droṇa bhīṣma kṛpa drauṇi karṇa arjuna janārdanān samāpta vidyān dhanuṣi śreṣṭhān yān manyase yudhi yaḥ hi ākṣipati vīryeṇa sarvān etān mahā rathān tulya tā karṇa bhīṣmābhyām ātmanaḥ yena dṛśyate vāsudeva arjunābhyām ca nyūna tām na ātmani icchati sa pāṇḍyaḥ nṛpati śreṣṭhaḥ sarva śastrabhṛtām varaḥ karṇasya anīkam avadhīt paribhūtaḥ iva antakaḥ kulāla cakra vat bhrāntam pāṇḍyena adhiṣṭhitam balam samyak astaiḥ śaraiḥ pāṇḍyaḥ vāyuḥ meghān iva ākṣipat sa pādarakṣān avadhīt vajreṇa arīn iva ari hā sa śakti prāsa tūṇīrān aśva ārohān hayān api pulinda khasa vāhlīkān niṣādān dākṣiṇātyān ca bhojān ca krūrān saṃgrāma karkaśān viśastra kavacān bāṇaiḥ kṛtvā pāṇḍyaḥ akarot vyasūn catur aṅgam balam bāṇaiḥ nighnantam pāṇḍyam āhave dṛṣṭvā drauṇiḥ asambhrāntam asaṃbhrāntataraḥ abhyayāt prāha praharatām śreṣṭhaḥ smita pūrvam samāhvayan rājan kamala pattra akṣa pradhāna āyudha vāhana muṣṭi śliṣṭa āyudhābhyām ca vyāyatābhyām mahat dhanuḥ dorbhyām visphārayan bhāsi mahā jalada vat bhṛśam mat anyam na anupaśyāmi prativīram te āhave mṛga saṃghān iva araṇye vibhīḥ bhīma balaḥ hariḥ mahatā ratha ghoṣeṇa divam bhūmim ca nādayan varṣā ante sasya hā pīthaḥ bhābhiḥ āpūrayan iva saṃspṛśānaḥ śarān tīkṣṇān tūṇāt āśīviṣa upamān smayan abhyahanat drauṇiḥ pāṇḍyam ācārya sattamaḥ tatas nava aparān tīkṣṇān nārācān kaṅka vāsasaḥ gatyā daśamyā saṃyuktān aśvatthāmā vyavāsṛjat teṣām pañca ācchinat pāṇḍyaḥ pañcabhiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ catvāraḥ abhyāhanan vāhān āśu te vyasavaḥ abhavan atha droṇa sutasya iṣūn tān chittvā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ dhanuḥ jyām vitatām pāṇḍyaḥ ciccheda āditya varcasaḥ vijyam dhanuḥ atha adhijyam kṛtvā drauṇiḥ amitra hā tatas śara sahasrāṇi preṣayām āsa pāṇḍyataḥ iṣu saṃbādham ākāśam akarot diśaḥ eva ca tatas tān asyataḥ sarvān drauṇeḥ bāṇān mahātmanaḥ jānānaḥ api akṣayān pāṇḍyaḥ aśātayat puruṣa ṛṣabhaḥ prahitān tān prayatnena chittvā drauṇeḥ iṣūn ariḥ cakrarakṣau tatas tasya prāṇudat niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ atha areḥ lāghavam dṛṣṭvā maṇḍalīkṛta kārmukaḥ prāsyat droṇa sutaḥ bāṇān vṛṣṭim pūṣānujaḥ yathā aṣṭau aṣṭagavāni ūhuḥ śakaṭāni yat āyudham ahnaḥ tat aṣṭa bhāgena drauṇiḥ cikṣepa māriṣa ye ye dadṛśire tatra visaṃjñāḥ prāyaśas abhavan parjanyaḥ iva gharma ante vṛṣṭyā sa adri drumām mahīm ācārya putraḥ tām senām bāṇa vṛṣṭyā abhyavīvṛṣat drauṇi parjanya muktām tām bāṇa vṛṣṭim su duḥsahām vāyavya astreṇa sa kṣipram ruddhvā pāṇḍya anilaḥ anadat tasya nānadataḥ ketum candana aguru bhūṣitam malaya pratimam drauṇiḥ chittvā aśvān caturaḥ ahanat sūtam eka iṣuṇā hatvā mahā jalada nisvanam astraiḥ astrāṇi saṃvārya chittvā sarva āyudhāni ca drāvayām āsa sa tadā pāṇḍavānām mahat balam virathān rathinaḥ cakre gajān aśvān ca bhārata atha drauṇiḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ pāṇḍyam śatru nibarhaṇam viratham rathinām śreṣṭham na ahanat yuddha kāṅkṣayā hata īśvaraḥ danti varaḥ su kalpitaḥ tvarā abhisṛṣṭaḥ prati śarma gaḥ balī tam ādravat drauṇi śara āhataḥ tvaran tam vāraṇam vāraṇa yuddha kovidaḥ tam adhyatiṣṭhat malaya īśvaraḥ mahān yathā adri śṛṅgam hariḥ unnadan tathā sasarja śīghram pratipīḍayan gajam guroḥ sutāya adripati īśvaraḥ nadan maṇi pratāna uttama vajra hāṭakaiḥ alaṃkṛtam ca aṃśuka mālya mauktikaiḥ hataḥ asi asau iti asakṛt mudā nadan parābhinat drauṇi varāṅga bhūṣaṇam tat arka candra graha pāvaka tviṣam bhṛśa abhighātāt patitam vicūrṇitam mahā indra vajra abhihatam mahā vanam yathā adri śṛṅgam dharaṇī tale tathā samādadhe ca antaka daṇḍa saṃnibhān iṣūn amitra anta karān caturdaśa jaghāna ṣaḍbhiḥ ṣaṭ ṛtu uttama tviṣaḥ sa pāṇḍya rāja anucarān mahā rathān śiraḥ ca tat pūrṇa śaśi prabhā ānanam sa roṣa tāmra āyata netram unnasam kṣitau vibabhrāja patat sa kuṇḍalam viśākhayoḥ madhya gataḥ śaśī yathā kṛtaḥ ṣaṣ aṃśaḥ caturaḥ nṛpaḥ tribhiḥ kṛtaḥ daśa aṃśaḥ kuśalena yudhyatā sa pādaśas rākṣasa bhojanān bahūn pradāya pāṇḍyaḥ aśva manuṣya kuñjarān tatas praśāntaḥ salila pravāhataḥ samāpta vidyam tu guroḥ sutam nṛpaḥ samāpta karmāṇam upetya te sutaḥ suhṛd vṛtaḥ atyartham apūjayat mudā jite balau viṣṇum iva amara īśvaraḥ uvāca eka vīreṇa karṇena drāviteṣu pareṣu ca samāpta vidyaḥ balavān yuktaḥ vīraḥ ca pāṇḍavaḥ sarva bhūteṣu anujñātaḥ śaṃkareṇa mahātmanā uvāca hate pāṇḍye arjunam kṛṣṇaḥ tvaran āha vacaḥ hitam paśya ati mānyam rājānam apayātān ca pāṇḍavān aśvatthāmnaḥ ca saṃkalpāt hatāḥ karṇena sṛñjayāḥ tathā aśva nara nāgānām kṛtam ca kadanam mahat iti ācaṣṭa su durdharṣaḥ vāsudevaḥ kirīṭine etat śrutvā ca dṛṣṭvā ca bhrātuḥ ghoram mahat bhayam vāhaya aśvān hṛṣīkeśa kṣipram iti āha pāṇḍavaḥ tatas prāyāt hṛṣīkeśaḥ rathena apratiyodhinā dāruṇaḥ ca punar tatra prādurāsīt samāgamaḥ tatas punar samājagmuḥ abhītāḥ kuru pāṇḍavāḥ bhīmasena mukhāḥ pārthāḥ sūtaputra mukhāḥ vayam tatas pravavṛte bhūyas saṃgrāmaḥ rāja sattama karṇasya pāṇḍavānām ca yama rāṣṭra vivardhanaḥ dhanūṃṣi bāṇān parighān asi tomara paṭṭiśān musalāni bhuśuṇḍīḥ ca śakti ṛṣṭi paraśvadhān gadāḥ prāsān asīn kuntān bhindipālān mahā aṅkuśān pragṛhya kṣipram āpetuḥ paraspara jigīṣayā bāṇa jyā tala śabdena dyām diśaḥ pradiśaḥ viyat pṛthivīm nemi ghoṣeṇa nādayantaḥ abhyayus parān tena śabdena mahatā saṃhṛṣṭāḥ cakruḥ āhavam vīrāḥ vīraiḥ mahā ghoram kalaha antam titīrṣavaḥ jyā talatra dhanuḥ śabdāḥ kuñjarāṇām ca bṛṃhitam tāḍitānām ca patatām ninādaḥ su mahān abhūt bāṇa śabdān ca vividhān śūrāṇām abhigarjatām śrutvā śabdam bhṛśam tresuḥ jaghnuḥ mamluḥ ca bhārata teṣām nānadyatām ca eva śastra vṛṣṭim ca muñcatām bahūn ādhirathiḥ karṇaḥ pramamātha raṇa iṣubhiḥ pañca pāñcāla vīrāṇām rathān daśa ca pañca ca sa aśva sūta dhvajān karṇaḥ śaraiḥ ninye yama kṣayam yodha mukhyāḥ mahā vīryāḥ pāṇḍūnām karṇam āhave śīghra astrāḥ divam āvṛtya parivavruḥ samantataḥ tatas karṇaḥ dviṣat senām śara varṣaiḥ viloḍayan vijagāhe aṇḍaja āpūrṇām padminīm iva yūthapaḥ vidhunvānaḥ śitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ śirāṃsi unmathya pātayat hastinaḥ su mahāmātrān sa aśva ārohān hayān api viṣehuḥ na asya saṃparkam dvitīyasya patatriṇaḥ pāṇḍu sṛñjaya pāñcālān śara gocaram ānayat mamarda karṇaḥ tarasā siṃhaḥ mṛga gaṇān iva tatas pāñcāla putrāḥ ca draupadeyāḥ ca māriṣa vyāyacchamānāḥ su bhṛśam kuru pāṇḍava sṛñjayāḥ su saṃnaddhāḥ kavacinaḥ sa śirastrāṇa bhūṣaṇāḥ gadābhiḥ musalaiḥ ca anye parighaiḥ ca mahā rathāḥ samabhyadhāvanta bhṛśam devāḥ daṇḍaiḥ iva udyataiḥ tatas nijaghnuḥ anyonyam petuḥ ca āhava tāḍitāḥ jīvantaḥ iva ca api ete tasthuḥ śastra upabṛṃhitāḥ śaktibhiḥ bhindipālaiḥ ca nakhara prāsa tomaraiḥ tatakṣuḥ cicchiduḥ ca anye bibhiduḥ cikṣipuḥ tathā kṣarantaḥ sva rasam raktam prakṛtāḥ candanāḥ iva narāḥ nara varaiḥ petuḥ aśvāḥ ca aśvaiḥ sahasraśas dhvajāḥ śirāṃsi chatrāṇi dvipa hastāḥ nṛṇām bhujāḥ kṣuraiḥ bhalla ardhacandraiḥ ca chinnāḥ śastrāṇi tatyajuḥ vadhyatām dāruṇaḥ śabdaḥ patatām stanatām api nara aśva ibha rathānām hi nara aśva ibha rathaiḥ tadā narān ca nāgān ca rathān hayān mamṛduḥ āhave tathā hatāḥ rathāḥ petuḥ aśva ārohaiḥ sahasraśas aśva ārohaiḥ hatāḥ śūrāḥ chinna hastāḥ ca dantinaḥ sa patākāḥ dhvajāḥ petuḥ viśīrṇāḥ iva parvatāḥ prahatāḥ hanyamānāḥ ca patitāḥ ca eva sarvaśas aśva ārohāḥ samāsādya tvaritāḥ pattibhiḥ hatāḥ sādibhiḥ patti saṃghāḥ ca nihatāḥ yudhi śerate mṛditāni iva padmāni pramlānāḥ iva ca srajaḥ hatānām vadanāni āsan gātrāṇi ca mahāmate rūpāṇi atyartha kāmyāni dvirada aśva nṛṇām nṛpa samunnāni iva vastrāṇi prāpuḥ durdarśa tām param tathā eva mukha varṇaḥ ca keṣām cit tatra dṛśyate madāt iva prasuptānām vikṣipta ābharaṇa srajām uvāca hastibhiḥ tu mahāmātrāḥ tava putreṇa coditāḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnam jighāṃsantaḥ kruddhāḥ pārṣatam abhyayus prācyāḥ ca dākṣiṇātyāḥ ca pravīrāḥ gaja yodhinaḥ aṅgāḥ vaṅgāḥ ca puṇḍrāḥ ca māgadhāḥ tāmraliptakāḥ mekalāḥ kośalāḥ madrāḥ daśārṇāḥ niṣadhāḥ tathā gaja yuddheṣu kuśalāḥ kaliṅgaiḥ saha bhārata śara tomara nārācaiḥ vṛṣṭimantaḥ iva ambudāḥ siṣicuḥ te tatas sarve pāñcāla acalam āhave tān nāgān pārṣṇi aṅguṣṭha aṅkuśaiḥ bhṛśam pothitān pārṣataḥ bāṇaiḥ nārācaiḥ ca abhyavīvṛṣat ekaikam daśabhiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ aṣṭābhiḥ api bhārata dviradān abhivivyādha kṣiptaiḥ giri nibhān śaraiḥ pāṇḍu pāñcālāḥ nadantaḥ niśita āyudhāḥ tān nāgān abhivarṣantaḥ jyā tantrī śara nāditaiḥ vīra nṛtyam pranṛtyantaḥ śūra tāla pracoditaiḥ sātyakiḥ ca śikhaṇḍī ca cekitānaḥ ca vīryavān samantāt siṣicuḥ vīrāḥ meghāḥ toyaiḥ iva acalān te mlecchaiḥ preṣitāḥ nāgāḥ narān aśvān rathān api hastaiḥ ākṣipya mamṛduḥ paḍbhiḥ ca api ati manyavaḥ bibhiduḥ ca viṣāṇa agraiḥ samākṣipya ca cikṣipuḥ viṣāṇa lagnaiḥ ca api anye paripetuḥ vibhīṣaṇāḥ nārācena abhinat vakṣaḥ saḥ apatat bhuvi sātyakeḥ tam kṛtvā dviradam bhūyas sahadevaḥ aṅgam abhyagāt nārācaiḥ yama daṇḍa ābhaiḥ tribhiḥ nāgam śatena ca divākara kara prakhyān aṅgaḥ cikṣepa tomarān tathā ardhacandreṇa śiraḥ tasya ciccheda pāṇḍavaḥ ācārya putre nihate hasti śikṣā viśārade aṅgāḥ kruddhāḥ mahāmātrāḥ nāgaiḥ nakulam abhyayus mekala utkala kāliṅgāḥ niṣādāḥ tāmraliptakāḥ śara tomara varṣāṇi vimuñcantaḥ jighāṃsavaḥ taiḥ chādyamānam nakulam divākaram iva ambudaiḥ pari petuḥ su saṃrabdhāḥ pāṇḍu pāñcāla somakāḥ sṛjatām śara varṣāṇi tomarān ca sahasraśas nāgānām prasphuṭuḥ kumbhāḥ marmāṇi vividhāni ca dantāḥ ca eva atividdhānām nārācaiḥ bhūṣaṇāni ca teṣām aṣṭau mahā nāgān catuḥṣaṣṭyā su tejanaiḥ sahadevaḥ jaghāna āśu te petuḥ saha sādibhiḥ tatas śaineya pāñcālyau draupadeyāḥ prabhadrakāḥ śikhaṇḍī ca mahā nāgān siṣicuḥ śara vṛṣṭibhiḥ te pāṇḍu yodha ambudharaiḥ śatru dvirada parvatāḥ bāṇa varṣaiḥ hatāḥ petuḥ vajra varṣaiḥ iva acalāḥ evam hatvā tava gajān te pāṇḍu nara kuñjarāḥ drutam senām avaikṣanta bhinna kūlām iva āpagām te tām senām ava ālokya pāṇḍu putrasya sainikāḥ duḥśāsanaḥ mahā rāja bhrātā bhrātaram abhyayāt tau same mahat yuddha dṛṣṭvā tatra narādhipāḥ siṃhanāda ravān cakruḥ vāsāṃsi ādudhuvuḥ ca ha pāṇḍu putraḥ tribhiḥ bāṇaiḥ vakṣasi abhihataḥ balī duḥśāsanaḥ tadā rājñ chittvā cāpam mahā āhave vyāvidhyata yudhām śreṣṭhaḥ śrīmān tava sutam prati sa mārgaṇa gaṇam cāpam chittvā tasya mahān asiḥ atha anyat dhanuḥ ādāya sahadevaḥ pratāpavān duḥśāsanāya cikṣepa bāṇam anta karam tatas tam āpatantam viśikham yama daṇḍa upama tviṣam dhanuḥ ca anyat samādāya śaram jagrāha vīryavān tam āpatantam sahasā nistriṃśam niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ tatas bāṇān catuḥṣaṣṭim te putraḥ mahā raṇe sahadeva rathe tūrṇam pātayām āsa bhārata tān śarān samare rājan vegena āpatataḥ bahūn sa nivārya mahā bāṇān tava putreṇa preṣitān atha asmai su bahūn bāṇān mādrī putraḥ samācinot preṣayām āsa saṃyuge tān bāṇān te putraḥ api chittvā ekaikam tribhiḥ śaraiḥ nanāda su mahā nādam dārayāṇaḥ vasuṃdharām tatas duḥśāsanaḥ rājan viddhvā pāṇḍu sutam raṇe sārathim navabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ tatas kruddhaḥ mahā rāja sahadevaḥ pratāpavān samādhatta śaram ghoram mṛtyu kāla antaka upamam vikṛṣya balavat cāpam tava putrāya saḥ asṛjat prāviśat dharaṇīm rājan valmīkam iva pannagaḥ mūḍham ca enam samālakṣya sārathiḥ tvaritaḥ ratham apovāha bhṛśam trastaḥ vadhyamānam śitaiḥ śaraiḥ nādaḥ tu su mahān āsīt nādayan vai vasuṃdharām parājitya raṇe tam tu pāṇḍavaḥ pāṇḍu pūrvaja duryodhana balam hṛṣṭaḥ prāmathat vai samantataḥ pipīlikā puṭam rājan yathā amṛdnāt naraḥ ruṣā tathā sā kauravī senā mṛditā tena bhārata karṇaḥ vaikartanaḥ rājñ vārayām āsa vai tadā cirasya bata dṛṣṭaḥ aham daivataiḥ saumya cakṣuṣā yasya me tvam raṇe pāpa cakṣuḥ viṣayam āgataḥ tvad doṣāt kuravaḥ kṣīṇāḥ samāsādya parasparam sadṛśam rāja putrasya dhanvinaḥ ca viśeṣataḥ karma kṛtvā raṇe śūra tatas katthitum arhasi an uktvā samare tāta śūrāḥ yudhyanti śaktitas iti uktvā prāharat tūrṇam pāṇḍu putrāya sūtajaḥ aśīti āśīviṣa prakhyaiḥ sūtaputram avidhyata tasya karṇaḥ dhanuḥ chittvā svarṇa puṅkhaiḥ śilā śitaiḥ triṃśatā parama iṣvāsaḥ śaraiḥ pāṇḍavam ārdayat te tasya kavacam bhittvā papuḥ śoṇitam āhave āśīviṣāḥ yathā nāgāḥ bhittvā gām salilam papuḥ atha anyat dhanuḥ ādāya hema pṛṣṭham durāsadam karṇam vivyādha viṃśatyā sārathim ca tribhiḥ śaraiḥ tatas kruddhaḥ mahā rāja nakulaḥ para vīra hā atha enam chinna dhanvānam sāyakānām śataiḥ tribhiḥ karṇam abhyarditam dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍu putreṇa māriṣa atha asya dhanuṣaḥ koṭim punar ciccheda māriṣa nakulasya tatas bāṇaiḥ sarvatas avārayat diśaḥ saṃchādyamānaḥ sahasā karṇa cāpa cyutaiḥ śaraiḥ ciccheda sa śarān tūrṇam śaraiḥ eva mahā rathaḥ tatas bāṇa mayam jālam vitatam vyomni adṛśyata khadyotānām gaṇaiḥ eva saṃpatadbhiḥ yathā nabhaḥ taiḥ vimuktaiḥ śara śataiḥ chāditam gaganam tadā śalabhānām yathā vrātaiḥ tadvat āsīt samākulam te śarāḥ hema vikṛtāḥ saṃpatantaḥ muhur muhur śreṇīkṛtāḥ abhāsanta haṃsāḥ śreṇi gatāḥ iva bāṇa jāla āvṛte vyomni chādite ca divākare samasarpat tatas bhūtam kim cit eva viśām pate vyarocatām mahābhāgau bāla sūryau iva uditau karṇa cāpa cyutaiḥ bāṇaiḥ vadhyamānāḥ tu somakāḥ avālīyanta rāja indra vedanā ārtāḥ śara arditāḥ nakulasya tathā bāṇaiḥ vadhyamānā camūḥ te vyaśīryata diśaḥ rājan vāta nunnāḥ iva ambudāḥ te sene vadhyamāne tu tābhyām divyaiḥ mahā śaraiḥ protsārite jane tasmin karṇa pāṇḍavayoḥ śaraiḥ mahātmanau anyonyam śara vṛṣṭibhiḥ nakulena śarāḥ muktāḥ kaṅka barhiṇa vāsasaḥ tathā eva sūtaputreṇa preṣitāḥ parama āhave pāṇḍu putram avacchādya vyatiṣṭhanta ambare śarāḥ śara veśma praviṣṭau tau dadṛśāte na kaiḥ cana candra sūryau yathā rājan chādyamānau jalāgame tatas kruddhaḥ raṇe karṇaḥ kṛtvā ghorataram vapuḥ pāṇḍavam chādayām āsa samantāt śara vṛṣṭibhiḥ sa chādyamānaḥ samare sūtaputreṇa pāṇḍavaḥ tatas prahasya ādhirathiḥ śara jālāni māriṣa preṣayām āsa samare śataśas atha sahasraśas ekacchāyam abhūt sarvam tasya bāṇaiḥ mahātmanaḥ abhra chāyā iva saṃjajñe saṃpatadbhiḥ śara uttamaiḥ tatas karṇaḥ mahā rāja dhanuḥ chittvā mahātmanaḥ sārathim pātayām āsa rathanīḍāt hasan iva tathā aśvān caturaḥ ca asya caturbhiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ yamasya sadanam tūrṇam preṣayām āsa bhārata atha asya tam ratham tūrṇam tilaśas vyadhamat śaraiḥ patākām cakrarakṣau ca dhvajam khaḍgam ca māriṣa suvarṇa vikṛtam tat ca dhanuḥ sa śaram āhave hata aśvaḥ virathaḥ ca eva vivarmā ca viśām pate avatīrya rathāt tūrṇam parigham gṛhya viṣṭhitaḥ vyahanat sāyakaiḥ rājan śataśas atha sahasraśas vyāyudham ca enam ālakṣya śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ ārdayat bahuśas karṇaḥ na ca enam samapīḍayat sa vadhyamānaḥ samare kṛtāstreṇa balīyasā sajyam asya dhanuḥ kaṇṭhe saḥ avāsṛjata bhārata tatas sa śuśubhe rājan kaṇṭha āsakta mahā dhanūḥ aśobhata mahā rāja pāṇḍu putraḥ tathā raṇe tam abravīt tadā karṇaḥ vyartham vyāhṛtavan asi vada idānīm punar hṛṣṭaḥ vadhyam mām tvam punar punar mā yotsīḥ gurubhiḥ sārdham balavadbhiḥ ca pāṇḍava sadṛśaiḥ tāta yudhyasva vrīḍām mā kuru pāṇḍava gṛham vā gaccha mādreya yatra vā kṛṣṇa phalgunau vadha prāptam tu tam rājan na avadhīt sūtanandanaḥ visṛṣṭaḥ pāṇḍavaḥ rājan sūtaputreṇa dhanvinā vrīḍan iva jagāma atha yudhiṣṭhira ratham prati āruroha ratham ca api sūtaputra pratāpitaḥ niḥśvasan duḥkha saṃtaptaḥ kumbhe kṣiptaḥ iva uragaḥ tam visṛjya raṇe karṇaḥ pāñcālān tvaritaḥ yayau tatra ākrandaḥ mahān āsīt pāṇḍavānām viśām pate dṛṣṭvā senāpatim yāntam pāñcālānām ratha vrajān tatra akarot mahā rāja kadanam sūtanandanaḥ sa sūtaiḥ hata sūtaiḥ ca bhagna akṣaiḥ ca eva māriṣa hṛ apaśyāma pāñcālānām ratha vraja dava agninā parīta aṅgāḥ yathā eva syuḥ mahā vane bhinna kumbhāḥ virudhirāḥ chinna hastāḥ ca vāraṇāḥ bhinna gātra varāḥ ca eva chinna vālāḥ ca māriṣa chinna abhrāṇi iva saṃpetuḥ vadhyamānāḥ mahātmanā apare trāsitāḥ nāgāḥ nārāca śata tomaraiḥ tam eva abhimukhāḥ yānti śalabhāḥ iva pāvakam apare niṣṭanantaḥ sma vyadṛśyanta mahā dvipāḥ kṣarantaḥ śoṇitam gātraiḥ nagāḥ iva jala plavam uraśchadaiḥ vimuktāḥ ca vālabandhaiḥ ca vājinaḥ rājataiḥ ca tathā kāṃsyaiḥ sauvarṇaiḥ ca eva bhūṣaṇaiḥ hīnāḥ āstaraṇaiḥ ca eva khalīnaiḥ ca vivarjitāḥ cāmaraiḥ ca kuthābhiḥ ca tūṇīraiḥ patitaiḥ api nihataiḥ sādibhiḥ ca eva śūraiḥ āhava śobhibhiḥ vātāyamānān sahasā prapaśyāma haya uttamān apaśyāma raṇe tatra bhrāmyamāṇān haya uttamān prāsaiḥ khaḍgaiḥ ca saṃsyūtān ṛṣṭibhiḥ ca narādhipa haya yodhān apaśyāma kañcuka uṣṇīṣa dhāriṇaḥ nihatān vadhyamānān ca vepamānān ca bhārata nānā aṅga avayavaiḥ hīnān tatra tatra eva bhārata vihayān sa hayān ca api veṣṭamānān tatas tatas rathān hema pariṣkārān su yuktān javanaiḥ hayaiḥ bhramamāṇān apaśyāma hateṣu rathiṣu drutam bhagna akṣa kūbarān kān cit chinna cakrān ca māriṣa vipatākā dhvajān ca anyān chinna īṣā yuga bandhurān rathān tu tatra vicchinnān tilaśas karṇa vikramaiḥ sūryaputra śaraiḥ trastān apaśyāma viśām pate viśastrān ca tathā eva anyān sa śastrān ca bahūn hatān tāvakān jāla saṃchannān uras ghaṇṭā vibhūṣitān nānā varṇa vicitrābhiḥ patākābhiḥ alaṃkṛtān padātīn anvapaśyāma dhāvamānān samantataḥ śirāṃsi bāhūn ūrūn ca chinnān anyān tathā yudhi chinnān śaraiḥ tathā bāhūn ūrūḥ cāpān janādhipa karṇa cāpa cyutaiḥ bāṇaiḥ apaśyāma vinākṛtān karṇa sāyaka nunnānām hatānām niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ te vadhyamānāḥ samare sūtaputreṇa sṛñjayāḥ tam eva abhimukhāḥ yānti pataṃgāḥ iva pāvakam kṣatriyāḥ varjayām āsuḥ yugānta agnim iva ulbaṇam hata śeṣāḥ tu ye vīrāḥ pāñcālānām mahā rathāḥ tān prabhagnān drutān karṇaḥ pṛṣṭhatas vikiran śaraiḥ abhyadhāvata tejasvī viśīrṇa kavaca dhvajān tāpayām āsa tān bāṇaiḥ sūtaputraḥ mahā rathaḥ madhyaṃdinam anuprāptaḥ bhūtāni iva tamonudaḥ uvāca ulūkaḥ abhyapatat tūrṇam tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt yuyutsuḥ tu tatas rājan śita dhāreṇa pattriṇā ulūkam tāḍayām āsa vajreṇa indraḥ iva acalam kṣurapreṇa dhanuḥ chittvā tāḍayām āsa karṇinā śākunim ca tatas ṣaṣṭyā vivyādha bharata ṛṣabha ulūkaḥ tam tu viṃśatyā viddhvā hema vibhūṣitaiḥ sa chinna yaṣṭiḥ su mahān śīryamāṇaḥ mahā dhvajaḥ dhvajam unmathitam dṛṣṭvā yuyutsuḥ krodha mūrchitaḥ ulūkam pañcabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ ājaghāna stanāntare tārā rūpam yathā citram nipapāta mahī tale jaghāna caturaḥ aśvān ca tam ca vivyādha pañcabhiḥ pāñcālān sṛñjayān ca eva vinighnan niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ śatānīkam mahā rāja śrutakarmā sutaḥ tava vyaśva sūta ratham cakre nimeṣa ardhāt asaṃbhramam hata aśve tu rathe tiṣṭhan śatānīkaḥ mahā balaḥ sā kṛtvā syandanam bhasma hayān ca eva sa sārathīn papāta dharaṇīm tūrṇam dārayantī iva bhārata tau ubhau virathau vīrau kurūṇām kīrti vardhanau apākrametām yuddha ārtau prekṣamāṇau parasparam sutasomaḥ tu śakunim vivyādha niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ śaraiḥ aneka sāhasraiḥ chādayām āsa bhārata tān śarān śakuniḥ tūrṇam ciccheda anyaiḥ patatribhiḥ nivārya samare ca api śarān tān niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ ājaghāna su saṃkruddhaḥ sutasomam tribhiḥ śaraiḥ tasya aśvān ketanam sūtam tilaśas vyadhamat śaraiḥ dhanvī dhanuḥ varam gṛhya rathāt bhūmau atiṣṭhata vyasṛjat sāyakān ca eva svarṇa puṅkhān śilā śitān pataṃgānām iva vrātāḥ śara vrātāḥ mahā ratham pramṛdnan ca śarān tān tān śara vrātaiḥ mahā yaśāḥ tatra atuṣyanta yodhāḥ ca siddhāḥ ca api divi sthitāḥ vyahanat kārmukam rājā tūṇīram ca eva sarvaśas saḥ acarat sahasā khaḍgī maṇḍalāni sahasraśas caturviṃśatī mahā rāja śikṣā bala samanvitaḥ saṃpātam samudīryam ca darśayām āsa saṃyuge saubalaḥ tu tatas tasya śarān cikṣepa vīryavān tān āpatataḥ eva āśu ciccheda parama asinā tatas kruddhaḥ mahā rāja saubalaḥ para vīra hā prāhiṇot sutasomasya śarān āśīviṣa upamān ciccheda tān ca khaḍgena śikṣayā ca balena ca darśayan lāghavam yuddhe tārkṣya vīrya sama dyutiḥ tasya saṃcarataḥ rājan maṇḍala āvartane tadā kṣurapreṇa su tīkṣṇena khaḍgam ciccheda su prabham sa chinnaḥ sahasā bhūmau nipapāta mahān asiḥ avaśasya sthitam haste tam khaḍgam sa tsarum tadā chinnam ājñāya nistriṃśam avaplutya padāni ṣaḍ saḥ anyat kārmukam ādāya su dṛḍham vegavattaram prāvidhyata tatas śeṣam sutasomaḥ mahā rathaḥ sa chittvā sa guṇam cāpam raṇe tasya mahātmanaḥ papāta dharaṇīm tūrṇam svarṇa vajra vibhūṣitaḥ abhyayāt pāṇḍava anīkam nighnan śatru gaṇān bahūn tatra nādaḥ mahān āsīt pāṇḍavānām viśām pate saubalam samare dṛṣṭvā vicarantam abhīta vat tāni anīkāni dṛptāni śastravanti mahānti ca drāvyamāṇāni adṛśyanta saubalena mahātmanā tathā eva pāṇḍavīm senām saubaleyaḥ vyanāśayat dhṛṣṭadyumnam kṛpaḥ rājan vārayām āsa saṃyuge yathā dṛptam vane nāgam śarabhaḥ vārayet yudhi padāt padam vicalitum na aśaknot tatra bhārata gautamasya vapuḥ dṛṣṭvā dhṛṣṭadyumna ratham prati vitresuḥ sarva bhūtāni kṣayam prāptam ca menire droṇasya nidhane nūnam saṃkruddhaḥ dvipadām varaḥ śāradvataḥ mahā tejāḥ divya astra vid udāra dhīḥ api iyam vāhinī kṛtsnā mucyeta mahataḥ bhayāt api ayam brāhmaṇaḥ sarvān na naḥ hanyāt samāgatān yādṛśam dṛśyate rūpam antaka pratimam bhṛśam ācāryaḥ kṣipra hastaḥ ca vijayī ca sadā yudhi pārṣataḥ ca bhṛśam yuddhe vimukhaḥ adya api lakṣyate iti evam vividhāḥ vācaḥ tāvakānām paraiḥ saha viniḥśvasya tatas kruddhaḥ kṛpaḥ śāradvataḥ nṛpa pārṣatam chādayām āsa niśceṣṭam sarva marmasu īdṛśam vyasanam yuddhe na te dṛṣṭam kadā cana daiva yogāt tu te bāṇāḥ na ataran marma bhedinaḥ preṣitāḥ dvijamukhyena marmāṇi uddiśya sarvaśas vyāvartaye tatra ratham nadī vegam iva arṇavāt dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ tatas rājñ śanakais abravīt vacaḥ vepathum ca śarīre me romaharṣam ca paśya vai arjunam bhīmasenam vā samare prāpya sārathe tatas prāyāt mahā rāja sārathiḥ tvarayan hayān pradrutam tu ratham dṛṣṭvā dhṛṣṭadyumnasya māriṣa śaṅkham ca pūrayām āsa muhur muhur ariṃdamaḥ śikhaṇḍinam tu samare bhīṣma mṛtyum durāsadam śikhaṇḍī ca samāsādya hṛdikānām mahā ratham kṛtavarmā tu saṃkruddhaḥ bhittvā ṣaṣṭibhiḥ āśugaiḥ tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti saṃkruddhaḥ hārdikyam pratyabhāṣata tatas asya navatim bāṇān rukma puṅkhān su tejanān preṣayām āsa rāja indra te asya abhraśyanta varmaṇaḥ vitathān tān samālakṣya patitān ca mahī tale kṣurapreṇa su tīkṣṇena kārmukam cicchide balī atha enam chinna dhanvānam bhagna śṛṅgam iva ṛṣabham aśītyā mārgaṇaiḥ kruddhaḥ bāhuvoḥ urasi ca ārdayat kṛtavarmā tu saṃkruddhaḥ mārgaṇaiḥ kṛta vikṣataḥ dhanuḥ anyat samādāya sa mārgaṇa gaṇam prabho śikhaṇḍinam bāṇa varaiḥ skandha deśe abhyatāḍayat skandha deśe sthitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ śikhaṇḍī ca rarāja ha śākhā pratānaiḥ vimalaiḥ su mahān sa yathā drumaḥ tau anyonyam bhṛśam viddhvā rudhireṇa samukṣitau poplūyamānau hi yathā mahantau śoṇita hrade anyonya śṛṅga abhihatau rejatuḥ vṛṣabhau iva rathābhyām ceratuḥ tatra maṇḍalāni sahasraśas kṛtavarmā mahā rāja pārṣatam niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ raṇe vivyādha saptatyā svarṇa puṅkhaiḥ śilā śitaiḥ tatas asya samare bāṇam bhojaḥ praharatām vara jīvitānta karam ghoram vyasṛjat tvarayā anvitaḥ sa tena abhihataḥ rājan mūrchām āśu samāviśat dhvaja yaṣṭim ca sahasā śiśriye kaśmala āvṛtaḥ apovāha raṇāt tam tu sārathiḥ rathinām varam hārdikya śara saṃtaptam niḥśvasantam punar punar prādravat pāṇḍavā senā vadhyamānā samantataḥ uvāca śvetāśvaḥ api mahā rāja vyadhamat tāvakam balam yathā vāyuḥ samāsādya tūla rāśim samantataḥ śālvāḥ saṃśaptakāḥ ca eva nārāyaṇa balam ca yat trigarta rājaḥ samare bhrātṛbhiḥ parivāritaḥ te sṛjantaḥ śara vrātān kirantaḥ arjunam āhave te tu arjunam samāsādya yodhāḥ śata sahasraśas agacchan vilayam sarve tārkṣyam dṛṣṭvā iva pannagāḥ te vadhyamānāḥ samare na ajahuḥ pāṇḍavam tadā dahyamānāḥ yathā rājan śalabhāḥ iva pāvakam mitravarmā trisaptatyā sauśrutiḥ ca api pañcabhiḥ śatruṃjayaḥ ca viṃśatyā suśarmā navabhiḥ śaraiḥ sauśrutim pañcaviṃśatyā candradevam tathā aṣṭabhiḥ śatruṃjayam ca viṃśatyā candradevam tathā aṣṭabhiḥ mitradevam śatena eva śrutasenam tribhiḥ śaraiḥ navabhiḥ
