rakṣyamāṇaḥ su saṃrabdhaiḥ putraiḥ śastrabhṛtām varaḥ vāhinī pramukham vīraḥ saṃprakarṣan aśobhata ayaḥ ratniḥ mahā bāhuḥ sūrya vaiśvānara dyutiḥ duḥśāsanaḥ vṛtaḥ sainyaiḥ sthitaḥ vyūhasya pṛṣṭhatas tam anvayāt mahā rāja svayam duryodhanaḥ nṛpaḥ citra aśvaiḥ citra saṃnāhaiḥ sodaryaiḥ abhirakṣitaḥ rakṣyamāṇaḥ mahā vīryaiḥ sahitaiḥ madra kekayaiḥ aśvatthāmā kurūṇām ca ye pravīrāḥ mahā rathāḥ nitya mattāḥ ca mātaṃgāḥ śūraiḥ mlecchaiḥ adhiṣṭhitāḥ ārohaṇaiḥ mahāmātraiḥ tomara aṅkuśa pāṇibhiḥ anvayuḥ tat ratha anīkam kṣarantaḥ iva toyadāḥ sādibhiḥ ca āsthitāḥ rejuḥ drumavantaḥ iva acalāḥ teṣām padāti nāgānām pādarakṣāḥ sahasraśas paṭṭiśa asi dharāḥ śūrāḥ babhūvuḥ anivartinaḥ bhindipāla dharāḥ ca eva śūla hastāḥ su cakriṇaḥ teṣām samāgamaḥ ghoraḥ deva asura raṇa upamaḥ sādibhiḥ syandanaiḥ nāgaiḥ adhikam samalaṃkṛtaiḥ nṛtyati iva mahā vyūhaḥ pareṣām ādadhat bhayam patti aśva ratha mātaṃgāḥ prāvṛṣi iva balāhakāḥ tatas senā mukhe karṇam dṛṣṭvā rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ paśya arjuna mahā vyūham karṇena vihitam raṇe yuktam pakṣaiḥ prapakṣaiḥ ca senā anīkam prakāśate yathā na abhibhavati asmān tathā nītiḥ vidhīyatām evam uktaḥ arjunaḥ rājñā prāñjaliḥ nṛpam abravīt uvāca duḥśāsanam śatānīkaḥ hārdikyam śini puṃgavaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ tathā drauṇim svayam yāsyāmi aham kṛpam draupadeyāḥ dhārtarāṣṭrān śiṣṭān saha śikhaṇḍinā te te ca tān tān ahitān mamakam ghnantu māmakāḥ uvāca vyādideśa sva sainyāni svayam ca agāt camū mukham agniḥ vaiśvānaraḥ pūrvaḥ brahmā induḥ sapti tām gataḥ tasmāt yaḥ prathamam jātaḥ tam devāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ viduḥ tam ādyam prathamam sṛṣṭam brahmaṇā loka kartṛṇā brahma īśāna indra varuṇān kramaśas yaḥ avahat purā tam ādyam ratham āsthāya prayātau keśava arjunau dhanaṃjayaḥ mahā rāja dakṣiṇam pakṣam āsthitaḥ bhīmasenaḥ mahā bāhuḥ vāmam pakṣam upāśritaḥ sātyakiḥ draupadeyāḥ ca svayam rājā ca pāṇḍavaḥ vyūhasya pramukhe tasthuḥ svena anīkena saṃvṛtāḥ sva balena ari sainyam tat pratyavasthāpya pāṇḍavaḥ pratyavyūhat puraskṛtya dhṛṣṭadyumna śikhaṇḍinau dhṛṣṭadyumna mukham vyūham aśobhata mahā balam atha tam ratham āyāntam dṛṣṭvā ati adbhuta darśanam ayam sa rathaḥ āyāti śveta aśvaḥ kṛṣṇa sārathiḥ durvāraḥ sarva sainyānām vipākaḥ karmaṇām iva eṣa reṇuḥ samudbhūtaḥ divam āvṛtya tiṣṭhati camūm tava imām vipulām samṛddhām asaṃkhyeyām aśru kula ākulām ca katham dahan dīptaḥ iva āśraya āśaḥ amī hayāḥ candra marīci varṇāḥ kṛṣṇa pratodena pratudyamānāḥ sita prabhāḥ su abhram iva abhra saṃghāḥ pravāti eṣa mahā vāyuḥ abhitas tava vāhinīm paśya karṇa mahā ghoram bhaya dam loma harṣaṇam kabandham megha saṃkāśam bhānum āvṛtya saṃsthitam paśya yūthaiḥ bahuvidhaiḥ mṛgāṇām sarvatodiśam balibhiḥ dṛpta śārdūlaiḥ ādityaḥ abhinirīkṣyate rarāsa dīpta lāṅgūlam ādityam abhitas sthitam paśya kaṅkān ca gṛdhrān ca samavetān sahasraśas ādityam abhivīkṣante hi aśivāḥ karṇa sa tvarāḥ sitāḥ ca aśvāḥ samāyuktāḥ te karṇa mahā rathe udīryataḥ hayān paśya mahā kāyān mahā javān plavamānān darśanīyān ākāśe garuḍān iva dhruvam eṣu nimitteṣu bhūmim āvṛtya pārthivāḥ svapsyanti nihatāḥ karṇa śataśas atha sahasraśas śaṅkhānām tumulaḥ śabdaḥ śrūyate loman harṣaṇaḥ ānakānām ca rādheya mṛdaṅgānām ca sarvaśas bāṇa śabdān bahuvidhān nara aśva ratha nisvanān jyā talatra iṣu śabdān ca śṛṇu karṇa mahātmanām hema rūpya pramṛṣṭānām vāsasām śilpi nirmitāḥ nānā varṇāḥ rathe bhānti śvasanena prakampitāḥ sa hema candra tārā arkāḥ patākāḥ kiṅkiṇī yutāḥ paśya karṇa arjunasya etāḥ saudāminyaḥ iva ambude dhvajāḥ kaṇakaṇāyante vātena abhisamīritāḥ vibhrājanti raṇe karṇa vimāne devatā yathā sa patākāḥ rathāḥ ca api pāñcālānām mahātmanām paśya kuntī sutam vīram bībhatsum aparājitam eṣa dhvaja agre pārthasya prekṣamāṇaḥ samantataḥ dṛśyate vānaraḥ bhīmaḥ dviṣatām agha vardhanaḥ etat cakram gadā śārṅgam śaṅkhaḥ kṛṣṇasya dhīmataḥ atyartham bhrājate kṛṣṇe kaustubhaḥ tu maṇiḥ tatas eṣa śārṅga gadā pāṇiḥ vāsudevaḥ ati vīryavān vāhayan eti turagān pāṇḍurān vāta raṃhasaḥ etat kūjati gāṇḍīvam vikṛṣṭam savyasācinā ete hastavatā muktāḥ ghnanti amitrān śitāḥ śarāḥ viśāla āyata tāmra akṣaiḥ pūrṇa candra nibha ānanaiḥ eṣā bhūḥ kīryate rājñām śirobhiḥ apalāyinām ete su parigha ākārāḥ puṇya gandha anulepanāḥ udyata āyudha śauṇḍānām pātyante sa āyudhāḥ bhujāḥ nirasta netra jihvā antāḥ vājinaḥ saha sādibhiḥ patitāḥ pātyamānāḥ ca kṣitau kṣīṇāḥ ca śerate ete parvata śṛṅgāṇām tulya rūpāḥ hatāḥ dvipāḥ gandharvanagara ākārāḥ rathāḥ hata nareśvarāḥ vimānāni iva puṇyāni svargiṇām nipatanti amī vyākulīkṛtam atyartham paśya sainyam kirīṭinā nānā mṛga sahasrāṇām yūtham kesariṇā yathā ghnanti ete pārthivān vīrāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ samabhidrutāḥ nāga aśva ratha pattyā oghān tāvakān samabhighnataḥ dhvaja agram dṛśyate tu asya jyā śabdaḥ ca api śrūyate adya draṣṭāsi tam vīram śvetāśvam kṛṣṇasārathim nighnantam śātravān saṃkhye yam karṇa paripṛcchasi yatra kṛṣṇaḥ jagannāthaḥ yatra rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ yatra gāṇḍīvadhṛk pārtho katham tvam haṃsi tat balam sārathiḥ yasya vārṣṇeyaḥ gāṇḍīvam yasya kārmukam tam ced hantāsi rādheya tvam naḥ rājā bhaviṣyasi śrūyate vai yathā vyaktam etau kṛṣṇa dhanaṃjayau eṣa saṃśaptaka āhūtaḥ tān eva abhimukhaḥ gataḥ karoti kadanam ca eṣām saṃgrāme dviṣatām balī iti bruvāṇam madra īśam karṇaḥ prāha ati manyumān eṣa sūryaḥ iva ambhodaiḥ channaḥ pārthaḥ na dṛśyate uvāca kaḥ vā anilam nigṛhṇīyāt pibet vā kaḥ mahā arṇavam bāhubhyām uddharet bhūmim dahet kruddhaḥ imāḥ prajāḥ paśya kuntī sutam vīram bhīmam akliṣṭa kāriṇam prabhāsantam mahā bāhum sthitam merum iva acalam eṣa dharma bhṛtām śreṣṭhaḥ dharmarājaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ tiṣṭhati asukaraḥ saṃkhye paraiḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ dṛśyante ete kārṣṇeyāḥ pañca pañca acalāḥ iva ete drupada putrāḥ ca dhṛṣṭadyumna purogamāḥ hīnāḥ satyajitā vīrāḥ tiṣṭhanti parama ojasaḥ asau indraḥ iva asahyaḥ sātyakiḥ sātvantām varaḥ yatra kṛṣṇa arjunau vīrau yatra rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ te sene samasajjetām gaṅgā yamunā vat bhṛśam uvāca tathā vyūḍheṣu anīkeṣu saṃsakteṣu ca saṃjaya saṃśaptakān katham pārthaḥ gataḥ karṇaḥ ca pāṇḍavān na hi tṛpyāmi vīrāṇām śṛṇvānaḥ vikramān raṇe uvāca candra āditya sama dyutiḥ divya varma āyudha bhṛtaḥ śārdūla sama vikramāḥ sa anugāḥ bhīma vapuṣaḥ candram tārā gaṇāḥ iva atha vyūḍheṣu anīkeṣu prekṣya saṃśaptakān raṇe kruddhaḥ arjunaḥ abhidudrāva vyākṣipan gāṇḍivam dhanuḥ atha saṃśaptakāḥ pārtham abhyadhāvan vadha eṣiṇaḥ vijaye kṛta saṃkalpāḥ mṛtyum kṛtvā nivartanam udīryamāṇam saṃrabdham dhanaṃjayam abhidravat pārtha velām samāsādya viṣṭhitam samadṛśyata sa saṃprahāraḥ tumulaḥ teṣām āsīt kirīṭinā tasya eva naḥ śrutaḥ yādṛś nivāta kavacaiḥ saha rathān aśvān dhvajān nāgān pattīn rathapatīn api iṣūn dhanūṃṣi khaḍgān ca cakrāṇi ca paraśvadhān sa āyudhān udyatān bāhūn udyatāni āyudhāni ca ciccheda dviṣatām pārthaḥ śirāṃsi ca sahasraśas nimagnam tam ratham matvā neduḥ saṃśaptakāḥ mudā sa purastāt arīn hatvā paśca ardhena uttareṇa ca dakṣiṇena ca bībhatsuḥ kruddhaḥ rudraḥ paśūn iva atha pāñcāla cedīnām sṛñjayānām ca māriṣa tvadīyaiḥ saha saṃgrāmaḥ āsīt parama dāruṇaḥ kṛpaḥ ca kṛtavarmā ca śakuniḥ ca api saubalaḥ hṛṣṭa senāḥ su saṃrabdhāḥ ratha anīkaiḥ prahāriṇaḥ kosalaiḥ kāśi matsyaiḥ ca kārūṣaiḥ kekayaiḥ api śūrasenaiḥ śūravīraiḥ yuyudhuḥ yuddha durmadāḥ teṣām anta karam yuddham deha pāpma praṇāśanam śūdra viś kṣatra vīrāṇām dharmyam svargyam yaśaskaram guptaḥ kuru pravīraiḥ ca madrāṇām ca mahā rathaiḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha pāñcālaiḥ cedibhiḥ sātyakena ca yudhyamānam raṇe karṇam kuru vīraḥ abhyapālayat karṇaḥ api niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ vinihatya mahā camūm pramṛdya ca ratha śreṣṭhān yudhiṣṭhiram apīḍayat vipatra āyudha deha asūn kṛtvā śatrūn sahasraśas evam māriṣa saṃgrāmaḥ nara vāji gaja kṣayaḥ kurūṇām sṛñjayānām ca deva asura samaḥ abhavat tat vigāhya ratha anīkam sūtaputraḥ mahā rathaḥ nadīm pravartayām āsa śoṇita ogha taraṃgiṇīm śoṇita udām kṣudra matsyām nāga nakrām duratyayām māṃsa majjā kardaminīm cakra kūrmām ratha uḍupām aśanībhiḥ iva dhvastā mahī rājan virājate tām śara ūrmi mahā vartām chattra haṃsa samākulām tanutra uṣṇīṣa saṃghāṭām hasti pāṣāṇa saṃkulām apārām anapārām tām śaṅkha dundubhi ghoṣiṇīm raudrām nadīm mahā rāja rajasā sarvatas vṛtām ati tīkṣṇām nada ākīrṇām nadīm antaka gāminīm samam ca viṣamam ca eva samāyāntam mahā bhayām ā gulphāt ca atra sīdatīm narān śoṇita kardame naraiḥ abhiparikṣiptāḥ yathā rājan mahā drumāḥ viceruḥ sarvatas yodhāḥ nauvāraṇa mahā āsanaiḥ śoṇitena samam rājan kṛtam āsīt samantataḥ nadī vegaiḥ yathā bhūmiḥ tadvat āsīt viśām pate uvāca yat tat praviśya pārthānām senām kurvan jana kṣayam ke ca pravīrāḥ pārthānām yudhi karṇam avārayan kān ca pramathya ādhirathiḥ yudhiṣṭhiram apīḍayat uvāca dhṛṣṭadyumna mukhān pārthān dṛṣṭvā karṇaḥ vyavasthitān samabhyadhāvat tvaritaḥ pāñcālān śatru karśanaḥ tam tūrṇam abhidhāvantam pāñcālāḥ jita kāśinaḥ pratyudyayuḥ mahā rāja haṃsāḥ iva mahā arṇavam tatas śaṅkha sahasrāṇām nisvanaḥ hṛdayaṃgamaḥ prādurāsīt ubhayatas bherī śabdaḥ ca dāruṇaḥ nānā vāditra nādaḥ ca dvipa aśva ratha nisvanaḥ siṃhanādaḥ ca vīrāṇām abhavat dāruṇaḥ tadā sa adri druma arṇavā bhūmiḥ sa vāta ambudam ambaram ati bhūtāni tam śabdam menire ati ca vivyathuḥ yāni ca aplava sattvāni prāyas tāni mṛtāni ca atha karṇaḥ bhṛśam kruddhaḥ śīghram astram udīrayan jaghāna pāṇḍavīm senām āsurīm maghavā iva sa pāṇḍava rathān tūrṇam praviśya visṛjan śarān tatas su puṅkhaiḥ niśitaiḥ ratha śreṣṭhaḥ ratheṣubhiḥ avadhīt pañcaviṃśatyā pāñcālān pañcaviṃśatim suvarṇa puṅkhaiḥ nārācaiḥ para kāya vidāraṇaiḥ cedikān avadhīt vīraḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas tam tathā samare karma kurvāṇam ati mānuṣam parivavruḥ mahā rāja pāñcālānām ratha vrajāḥ tatas saṃdhāya viśikhān pañca bhārata duḥsahān pāñcālān avadhīt pañca karṇaḥ vaikartanaḥ vṛṣaḥ bhānudevam citrasenam senābindum ca bhārata tapanam śūrasenam ca pāñcālān avadhīt raṇe pāñcāleṣu ca śūreṣu vadhyamāneṣu sāyakaiḥ hāhākāraḥ mahān āsīt pāñcālānām mahā āhave parivavruḥ mahā rāja pāñcālānām rathāḥ daśa teṣām saṃkīryamāṇānām hāhākāra kṛtāḥ diśaḥ punar eva ca tān karṇaḥ jaghāna āśu patatribhiḥ suṣeṇaḥ satyasenaḥ ca tyaktvā prāṇān ayudhyatām pṛṣṭhagopaḥ tu karṇasya jyeṣṭhaḥ putraḥ mahā rathaḥ vṛṣasenaḥ svayam karṇam pṛṣṭhatas paryapālayat dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ sātyakiḥ ca draupadeyāḥ vṛkodaraḥ nakulaḥ sahadevaḥ ca sātyakiḥ ca mahā rathaḥ janamejayaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca pravīrāḥ ca prabhadrakāḥ cedi kekaya pāñcālāḥ yamau matsyāḥ ca daṃśitāḥ samabhyadhāvan rādheyam jighāṃsantaḥ prahāriṇaḥ te enam vividhaiḥ śastraiḥ śara dhārābhiḥ eva ca abhyavarṣan vimṛdnantaḥ prāvṛṣi iva ambudāḥ girim pitaram tu parīpsantaḥ karṇa putrāḥ prahāriṇaḥ tvadīyāḥ ca apare rājan vīrāḥ vīrān avārayan nārācaiḥ sapta viddhvā hṛdi bhīmam nanāda ha atha anyat dhanuḥ ādāya su dṛḍham bhīma vikramaḥ sajyam vṛkodaraḥ kṛtvā suṣeṇasya ācchinat dhanuḥ karṇam ca tūrṇam vivyādha trisaptatyā śitaiḥ śaraiḥ satyasenam ca daśabhiḥ sa aśva sūta dhvaja āyudham paśyatām suhṛdām madhye karṇa putram apātayat śubha darśanam eva āsīt nāla bhraṣṭam iva ambujam hatvā karṇa sutam bhīmaḥ tāvakān punar ārdayat kṛpa hārdikyayoḥ chittvā cāpe tau api atha ārdayat duḥśāsanam tribhiḥ viddhvā śakunim ṣaḍbhiḥ āyasaiḥ suṣeṇāya asṛjat bhīmaḥ tam api asya ācchinat vṛṣaḥ punar karṇaḥ trisaptatyā bhīmasenam ratheṣubhiḥ putram parīpsan vivyādha krūram krūraiḥ jighāṃsayā nakulaḥ tam tu viṃśatyā viddhvā bhāra sahaiḥ dṛḍhaiḥ tam suṣeṇaḥ mahā rāja viddhvā daśabhiḥ āśugaiḥ ciccheda ca dhanuḥ śīghram kṣurapreṇa mahā rathaḥ suṣeṇam bahubhiḥ bāṇaiḥ vārayām āsa saṃyuge sa tu bāṇaiḥ diśaḥ rājñ ācchādya para vīra hā ājaghne sārathim ca asya suṣeṇam ca tatas tribhiḥ atha anyat dhanuḥ ādāya suṣeṇaḥ krodha mūrchitaḥ avidhyat nakulam ṣaṣṭyā sahadevam ca sapta sātyakiḥ vṛṣasenam tu viddhvā sapta āśugaiḥ punar vivyādha saptatyā sārathim ca tribhiḥ śaraiḥ vṛṣasenaḥ tu śaineyam śareṇa nata parvaṇā ājaghāna mahā rāja śaṅkha deśe mahā ratham śaineyaḥ vṛṣasenena pattriṇā paripīḍitaḥ jagrāha iṣu varān vīraḥ śīghram sa daśa pañca ca sātyakiḥ vṛṣasenasya hatvā sūtam tribhiḥ śaraiḥ dhanuḥ ciccheda bhallena jaghāna aśvān ca sapta sa raṇe yuyudhānena visūta aśva ratha dhvajaḥ atho jighāṃsuḥ śaineyam khaḍga carma bhṛt abhyayāt tasya ca āplavataḥ śīghram vṛṣasenasya sātyakiḥ duḥśāsanaḥ tu tam dṛṣṭvā viratham vyāyudham kṛtam atha anyam ratham āsthāya vṛṣasenaḥ mahā rathaḥ draupadeyān trisaptatyā yuyudhānam ca pañcabhiḥ bhīmasenam catuḥṣaṣṭyā sahadevam ca pañcabhiḥ nakulam triṃśatā bāṇaiḥ śatānīkam ca sapta śikhaṇḍinam ca daśabhiḥ dharmarājam śatena ca etān ca anyān ca rāja indra pravīrān jaya gṛddhinaḥ abhyardayat mahā iṣvāsaḥ karṇa putraḥ viśām pate karṇasya yudhi durdharṣaḥ punar pṛṣṭham apālayat duḥśāsanam tu śaineyaḥ navaiḥ navabhiḥ āśugaiḥ visūta aśva ratham kṛtvā lalāṭe tribhiḥ ārpayat yuyudhe pāṇḍubhiḥ sārdham karṇasya āpyāyayan balam dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ tatas karṇam avidhyat daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ bhīmasenaḥ catuḥṣaṣṭyā sahadevaḥ ca pañcabhiḥ nakulaḥ triṃśatā bāṇaiḥ śatānīkaḥ ca sapta śikhaṇḍī daśabhiḥ vīraḥ dharmarājaḥ śatena tu ete ca anye ca rāja indra pravīrāḥ jaya gṛddhinaḥ abhyardayat mahā iṣvāsam sūtaputram mahā mṛdhe tān sūtaputraḥ viśikhaiḥ daśabhiḥ daśabhiḥ śitaiḥ sātyakim bhīmasenam ca dhṛṣṭadyumnam śikhaṇḍinam draupadeyān ca saṃrabdhān yatamānān mahā rathān paśyatām sarva sainyānām atha etān sūtanandanaḥ virathān rathinaḥ śreṣṭhān nimeṣa ardhāt cakāra ha amogha tvāt ca bāṇānām bhūta saṃghāḥ visiṣmiyuḥ tatra astra vīryam karṇasya lāghavam ca mahātmanaḥ na hi ādadānam dadṛśuḥ saṃdadhānam ca sāyakān vimuñcantam ca saṃrambhāt dadṛśuḥ te mahā ratham pratyañci diśi tam dṛṣṭvā prācyām paśyāma lāghavāt iṣūn eva sma paśyāmaḥ vikirantam samantataḥ chādayantaḥ diśaḥ rājan śalabhānām iva vrajān tasya taiḥ iṣubhiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ saṃpatadbhiḥ sahasraśas marīcibhiḥ iva uṣṇāṃśoḥ śitaiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ vyāptāḥ sarvāḥ diśaḥ rājñ yodhāḥ ca dadṛśuḥ tadā śaraiḥ saṃvṛtam ākāśam tatra abhram iva ca abhavat dyauḥ viyant bhūḥ diśaḥ ca āśu praṇunnāḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ aruṇa abhra āvṛta ākāram tasmin deśe babhau viyat tatas punar ameya ātmā karṇaḥ rājan mahā rathaḥ nṛtyan iva hi rādheyaḥ cāpa hastaḥ pratāpavān te hanyamānāḥ karṇena palāyante diśaḥ daśa nādayantaḥ diśaḥ sarvāḥ karṇa trastāḥ vicetasaḥ tān pramṛdnan mahā iṣvāsān rādheyaḥ śara vṛṣṭibhiḥ rāja anīkam asaṃbādham prāviśat śatru karśanaḥ sa rathān tri śatān hatvā cedīnām anivartinām tatas te virathāḥ śūrāḥ rathān anyān samāsthitāḥ tatas te pāṇḍavāḥ rājan śikhaṇḍī ca sa sātyakiḥ rādheyāt parirakṣantaḥ rājānam paryavārayan muñcantaḥ vividhān bāṇān svarṇa puṅkhān śilā śitān tathā eva tāvakāḥ sarve karṇam durvāraṇam raṇe yattāḥ senā mahā iṣvāsāḥ paryarakṣanta sarvaśas nānā vāditra ghoṣāḥ ca prādurāsan viśām pate siṃhanādaḥ ca saṃjajñe śūrāṇām anivartinām tatas punar samājagmuḥ abhīta kuru pāṇḍavāḥ yudhiṣṭhira mukhāḥ pārthāḥ sūtaputra mukhāḥ vayam uvāca vidārya karṇaḥ tām senām dharmarājam upādravat ratha hasti aśva pattīnām sahasraiḥ parivāritaḥ nānā āyudha sahasrāṇi preṣitāni aribhiḥ vṛṣaḥ chittvā bāṇa śataiḥ ugraiḥ tān avidhyat asaṃbhramaḥ nicakarta śirāṃsi eṣām bāhūn ūrūn ca sarvaśas prahartu kāmān aparān saṃdhita iṣūn tathā aparān pragṛhīta āyudhān bāhūn anyeṣām ca pradhāvatām nijaghāna raṇe karṇaḥ nānā śastra niṣevitān te hatāḥ vasudhām petuḥ bhagnāḥ ca anye vidudruvuḥ draviḍa andhra niṣādāḥ tu punar sātyaki coditāḥ abhyardayan jighāṃsantaḥ pattayaḥ karṇam āhave te vibāhu śirastrāṇāḥ prahatāḥ karṇa sāyakaiḥ petuḥ pṛthivyām yugapad chinnam śāla vanam yathā evam yodha śatāni ājau sahasrāṇi ayutāni ca hatāni iyuḥ mahīm dehaiḥ yaśasā apūrayan diśaḥ rurudhuḥ pāṇḍu pāñcālāḥ vyādhim mantra auṣadhaiḥ iva sa rāja gṛddhibhiḥ ruddhaḥ pāṇḍu pāñcāla kekayaiḥ na aśakat tān atikrāntum mṛtyuḥ brahma vidaḥ yathā tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ karṇam adūra stham nivāritam taiḥ yodhaiḥ pramukhe vīram dṛṣṭvā vivyādha sāyakaiḥ pramathya sahitān vīrān yudhiṣṭhiram apīḍayat tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ karṇam āsādya jayatām varam karṇa karṇa vṛthak dṛṣṭe sūtaputra vacaḥ śṛṇu tathā asmān bādhase nityam dhārtarāṣṭra mate sthitaḥ yat balam yat ca te vīryam pradveṣaḥ yaḥ ca pāṇḍuṣu tat sarvam darśayasva adya pauruṣam mahat āsthitaḥ yuddha śraddhām sa te adya aham vineṣyāmi mahā āhave evam uktvā mahā rāja karṇam pāṇḍu sutaḥ tadā suvarṇa puṅkhaiḥ daśabhiḥ vivyādha ayasmayaiḥ śitaiḥ saḥ avajñāya tu nirviddhaḥ sūtaputreṇa māriṣa prajajvāla tatas krodhāt haviṣā iva hutāśanaḥ samādhatta śitam bāṇam girīṇām api dāraṇam tatas pūrṇa āyatam tīkṣṇam yama daṇḍa nibham śaram mumoca tvaritaḥ rājā sūtaputra jighāṃsayā sa tu vegavatā muktaḥ bāṇaḥ vajra aśani svanaḥ viveśa sahasā karṇam savye pārśve mahā ratham tatas hāhākṛtam sarvam dhārtarāṣṭra balam mahat vivarṇa mukha bhūyiṣṭham karṇam dṛṣṭvā tathāgatam siṃhanādaḥ ca saṃjajñe kṣveḍāḥ kilakilāḥ tathā pāṇḍavānām mahā rāja dṛṣṭvā rājñaḥ parākramam pratilabhya tu rādheyaḥ saṃjñām na ati cirāt iva dadhre rāja vināśāya manaḥ krūra parākramaḥ sa hema vikṛtam cāpam visphārya vijayam mahat avākirat ameya ātmā pāṇḍavam niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ tatas kṣurābhyām pāñcālyau cakrarakṣau mahātmanaḥ jaghāna samare śūraḥ śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ ratha abhyāśe cakāśete candrasya iva punarvasū yudhiṣṭhiraḥ punar karṇam avidhyat triṃśatā śaraiḥ bhittvā bhallena rājānam viddhvā ṣaṣṭyā anadat mudā tatas pravīrāḥ pāṇḍūnām abhyadhāvan yudhiṣṭhiram sūtaputrāt parīpsantaḥ karṇam abhyardayan śaraiḥ sātyakiḥ cekitānaḥ ca yuyutsuḥ pāṇḍyaḥ eva ca karṇaḥ vivyādha saṃkruddhaḥ dākṣiṇātyān samantataḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca draupadeyāḥ prabhadrakāḥ yamau ca bhīmasenaḥ ca śiśupālasya ca ātmajaḥ kārūṣāḥ matsya śeṣāḥ ca kekayāḥ kāśi kosalāḥ ete ca tvaritāḥ vīrāḥ vasuṣeṇam avārayan janamejayaḥ ca pāñcālyaḥ karṇam vivyādha sāyakaiḥ varāhakarṇaiḥ nārācaiḥ nālīkaiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ vatsadantaiḥ vipāṭhaiḥ ca kṣurapraiḥ caṭakāmukhaiḥ nānā praharaṇaiḥ ca ugraiḥ ratha hasti aśva sādinaḥ sarvatas abhyādravan karṇam parivārya jighāṃsayā sa pāṇḍavānām pravaraiḥ sarvatas samabhidrutaḥ chādyamānaiḥ śitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ sva sva nāma aṅkitaiḥ tadā udairayat brāhmam astram śaraiḥ saṃpūrayan diśaḥ saṃjayaḥ nijaghāna mahā iṣvāsān pāñcālān ekaviṃśatim tatas punar ameya ātmā cedīnām pravarān daśa tasya bāṇa sahasrāṇi saṃprapannāni māriṣa dṛśyante dikṣu sarvāsu śalabhānām iva vrajāḥ karṇa nāma aṅkitāḥ bāṇāḥ svarṇa puṅkhāḥ su tejanāḥ nara aśva kāyān nirbhidya petuḥ urvyām samantataḥ karṇena ekena samare cedīnām pravarāḥ rathāḥ sṛñjayānām ca sarveṣām śataśas nihatāḥ raṇe karṇasya śara saṃchannam babhūva vipulam tamaḥ na ajñāyata tatas kim cit pareṣām ātmanaḥ api vā tasmin tamasi bhūte ca kṣatriyāṇām bhayaṃkare vicacāra mahā bāhuḥ nirdahan kṣatriyān bahūn tatas śara mahā jvālaḥ vīrya ūṣmā karṇa pāvakaḥ nirdahan pāṇḍava vanam cāru paryacarat raṇe tatas teṣām mahā rāja pāṇḍavānām mahā rathāḥ sṛñjayānām ca sarveṣām śataśas atha sahasraśas astraiḥ karṇam mahā iṣvāṃsa samantāt paryavāraya sa saṃvārya mahā astrāṇi mahā iṣvāsaḥ mahātmanām tatas saṃdhāya navatim nimeṣān nata parvaṇām bibheda kavacam rājñaḥ raṇe karṇaḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ sa vidyut abhram savituḥ śiṣṭam vāta hatam yathā sa vivarmā śaraiḥ pārthaḥ rudhireṇa samukṣitaḥ babhāse puruṣa śreṣṭhaḥ udyan iva divākaraḥ sa śara arpita sarva aṅgaḥ chinna varmā atha saṃyuge kṣatra dharmam samāsthāya siṃhanādam atha akarot naditvā ca ciram kālam pāṇḍavaḥ rabhasaḥ raṇe kruddhaḥ sarva āyasīm śaktim cikṣepa ādhirathim prati tām jvalatīm iva ākāśe śaraiḥ ciccheda sapta sā chinnā bhūmim apatat mahā iṣvāsasya sāyakaiḥ tatas bāhvoḥ lalāṭe ca hṛdi ca eva yudhiṣṭhiraḥ caturbhiḥ tomaraiḥ karṇam tāḍayitvā mudā anadat jaghāna sūtam pārthasya pārṣṇim ca navabhiḥ śaraiḥ hatvā sūtam ca pārthasya pṛṣṭhagopam ca sāyakaiḥ kāla vālāḥ tu ye pārtham danta varṇāḥ avahan hayāḥ taiḥ yuktam ratham āsthāya prāyāt rājā parāṅmukhaḥ etasmin antare śūrāḥ pāṇḍavānām mahā rathāḥ vavarṣuḥ śara varṣāṇi rādheyam prati bhārata sātyakiḥ pañcaviṃśatyā śikhaṇḍī navabhiḥ śaraiḥ avarṣatām mahā rāja rādheyam śatru karśanam śaineyam tu tatas kruddhaḥ karṇaḥ pañcabhiḥ āyasaiḥ vivyādha samare rājan tribhiḥ ca anyaiḥ śilīmukhaiḥ savyam ṣoḍaśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ yantāram ca asya saptabhiḥ atha asya caturaḥ vāhān caturbhiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ sāratheḥ sa śirastrāṇam śiraḥ kāyāt apāharat hata aśva sūte tu rathe sthitaḥ sa śini puṃgavaḥ śaktim cikṣepa karṇāya vaiḍūrya maṇi bhūṣitām tām āpatatīm sahasā dvidhā ciccheda bhārata karṇaḥ vai dhanvinām śreṣṭhaḥ tān ca sarvān avārayat tatas tān niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ pāṇḍavānām mahā rathān nyavārayat ameya ātmā śikṣayā ca balena ca ardayitvā śaraiḥ tān tu siṃhaḥ kṣudra mṛgān iva pīḍayan dharmarājānam śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ evam pārthaḥ vyapāyāt sa aśaknuvan pramukhatas sthātum karṇasya durmanāḥ tam abhidrutya rādheyaḥ skandham saṃspṛśya pāṇinā lakṣaṇaiḥ upapannena pāṇinā pāṇḍu nandanam tam śalyaḥ prāha mā karṇa gṛhṇīthāḥ pārthiva uttamam gṛhīta mātraḥ hatvā tvām mā kariṣyati bhasmasāt prajahyāt samare śatrūn prāṇān rakṣan mahā āhave na bhavān kṣatra dharmeṣu kuśalaḥ asi iti me matiḥ brāhme bale bhavān yuktaḥ svādhyāye yajña karmaṇi mā ca enān apriyam brūhi mā ca vraja mahā raṇam vaktavyāḥ māriṣa anye tu na vaktavyāḥ tu mādṛśāḥ na hi tvām samare rājan hanyāt karṇaḥ katham cana saṃjayaḥ vara pradānam kuntyāḥ tu karṇaḥ smṛtvā mahā rathaḥ evam uktvā tatas pārtham visṛjya ca mahā balaḥ nyahanat pāṇḍavīm senām vajrahastaḥ iva āsurīm tatas prāyāt drutam rājan vrīḍan iva janeśvaraḥ cedi pāṇḍava pāñcālāḥ sātyakiḥ ca mahā rathaḥ draupadeyāḥ tathā śūrāḥ mādrī putrau ca pāṇḍavau tatas yudhiṣṭhira anīkam dṛṣṭvā karṇaḥ parāṅmukham kurubhiḥ sahitaḥ vīraiḥ pṛṣṭha gaiḥ pṛṣṭham anvayāt śaṅkha bherī ninādaiḥ ca kārmukāṇām ca nisvanaiḥ babhūva dhārtarāṣṭrāṇām siṃhanāda ravaḥ tadā śruta kīrteḥ mahā rāja dṛṣṭavan karṇa vikramam kālyamānam balam dṛṣṭvā dharmarājaḥ yudhiṣṭhira tatas rājñā abhyanujñātāḥ pāṇḍavānām mahā rathāḥ abhavat tumulaḥ śabdaḥ yodhānām tatra bhārata hasti aśva ratha pattīnām śastrāṇām ca tatas tatas udgataḥ pratisṛṣṭānām śastrāṇām ca tatas tatas iti bruvāṇāḥ anyonyam jaghnuḥ yodhāḥ raṇa ajire vipatākā dhvaja chatrāḥ vyaśva sūta āyudhāḥ raṇe vyaṅga aṅga avayavāḥ petuḥ kṣitau kṣīṇāḥ hata īśvarāḥ pravarāṇi iva śailānām śikharāṇi dvipa uttamāḥ pralutvā vīra śailānām śikharāṇi dvipa upamāḥ sa ārohāḥ nihatāḥ petuḥ vajra bhinnāḥ iva adrayaḥ sa ārohāḥ turagāḥ petuḥ hata vīrāḥ sahasraśas vipraviddha āyudha aṅgāḥ ca dvirada aśva rathaiḥ hatāḥ prativīraiḥ ca saṃmarde patti saṃghāḥ sahasraśas viśāla āyata tāmra akṣaiḥ padma indu sadṛśa ānanaiḥ śirobhiḥ yuddha śauṇḍānām sarvatas saṃstṛtā mahī hatān kṛttān abhimukhān vīrān vīraiḥ sahasraśas āropya āropya gacchanti vimāneṣu apsaraḥ gaṇāḥ tava ayam na tava eva ayam mama ayam iti vallabhaḥ pariṣvaktaḥ vijānāti nārībhiḥ upari sthitaḥ iti bāhu latā pāśa pāśinaḥ divya rūpiṇaḥ samādhāya apsaraḥ saṃghāḥ nānā yānaiḥ divam yayuḥ tat dṛṣṭvā mahat āścaryam pratyakṣam svarga lipsayā prahṛṣṭa manasaḥ śūrāḥ kṣipram jagmuḥ parasparam pattayaḥ pattibhiḥ nāgāḥ nāgaiḥ saha hayaiḥ hayāḥ evam pravṛtte saṃgrāme gaja vāji jana kṣaye muṣṭi yuddham niyuddham ca deha pāpma vināśanam nara aśva gaja dehebhyaḥ prasṛtā lohita āpagā nara aśva gaja dehān sā vyuvāha patitān bahūn nara aśva gaja sambādhe nara aśva gaja sādinām nara aśva gaja dehān sā vahatī bhīru bhīṣaṇā tasyāḥ parama pāram ca vrajanti vijaya eṣiṇaḥ te tu lohita digdha aṅgāḥ rakta varma āyudha ambarāḥ sasnuḥ tasyām papuḥ ca asṛj mamluḥ ca bharata ṛṣabha rathān aśvān narān nāgān āyudha ābharaṇāni ca vasanāni atha varmāṇi hanyamānān hatān api bhūmim kham dyām diśaḥ ca eva prāyas paśyāma lohitam viṣādaḥ su mahān āsīt prāyas sainyasya bhārata bhūyas samādravan vīrāḥ sātyaki pramukhāḥ rathāḥ teṣām āpatatām vegam a viṣahya mahātmanām putrāṇām te mahat sainyam āsīt rājan parāṅmukham tat prakīrṇa ratha aśva ibham nara vāji samākulam vyadravat tāvakam sainyam loḍyamānam samantataḥ siṃha arditam mahā araṇye yathā gaja kulam tathā uvāca tān abhidravataḥ dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavān tāvakam balam duryodhanaḥ mahā rāja vārayām āsa sarvaśas tatas pakṣāt prapakṣāt ca prapakṣaiḥ ca api dakṣiṇāt karṇaḥ api dṛṣṭvā dravataḥ dhārtarāṣṭrān parāṅmukhān madra rājam uvāca idam yāhi bhīma ratham prati haṃsa varṇān haya agryān tān praiṣīt yatra vṛkodaram te preṣitāḥ mahā rāja śalyena āhava śobhinā dṛṣṭvā karṇam samāyāntam bhīmaḥ krodha samanvitaḥ saḥ abravīt sātyakim vīram dhṛṣṭadyumnam ca pārṣatam enam rakṣata rājānam dharma ātmānam yudhiṣṭhiram hantā vā asmi raṇe karṇam sa vā mām nihaniṣyati saṃgrāmeṇa su ghoreṇa satyam etat bravīmi vaḥ rājānam adya bhavatām nyāsa bhūtam dadāmi vai evam uktvā mahā bāhuḥ prāyāt ādhirathim prati siṃhanādena mahatā sarvāḥ saṃnādayan diśaḥ dṛṣṭvā tvaritam āyāntam bhīmam yuddha abhinandinam sūtaputram atha uvāca madrāṇām īśvaraḥ vibhuḥ paśya karṇa mahā bāhum kruddham pāṇḍava nandanam dīrgha kāla arjitam krodham moktu kāmam tvayi dhruvam īdṛśam na asya rūpam me dṛṣṭa pūrvam kadā cana bibharti yādṛśam rūpam kālāgni sadṛśam śubham iti bruvati rādheyam madrāṇām īśvare nṛpa tathāgatam tu saṃprekṣya bhīmam yuddha abhinandinam bhīmasenam prati vibho tat satyam na atra saṃśayaḥ eṣa śūraḥ ca vīraḥ ca krodhanaḥ ca vṛkodaraḥ nirapekṣaḥ śarīre ca prāṇāt ca bala adhikaḥ ajñāta vāsam vasatā virāṭa nagare tadā draupadyāḥ priya kāmena kevalam bāhu saṃśrayāt gūḍha bhāvam samāśritya kīcakaḥ sa gaṇaḥ hataḥ saḥ adya saṃgrāma śirasi saṃnaddhaḥ krodha mūrcchitaḥ kiṃkara udyata daṇḍena mṛtyunā api vrajet raṇam cira kāla abhilaṣitaḥ mama ayam tu manorathaḥ arjunam samare hanyām mām vā hanyāt dhanaṃjayaḥ saṃśayaḥ su mahān śalya prāpya bhīmam ariṃdamam bhīmasenam samāsādya mayā śakyam nivartitum mūrtimantam aham manye mārutim marutām patim yudhiṣṭhiram bhīmam iha atha śaknuyām uvāca vacanam śalyaḥ sūtaputram tathāgatam abhiyāsi mahā bāho bhīmasenam mahā balam nirapekṣaḥ ca yudhyasva śaktim svām saṃpradarśayan yaḥ te kāmaḥ abhilaṣitaḥ cirāt prabhṛti hṛd gataḥ evam ukte tatas karṇaḥ śalyam punar abhāṣata hantā aham arjunam saṃkhye mām vā hantā dhanaṃjayaḥ evam uktvā tatas rājñ rādheyaḥ rathinām varaḥ yuddhe manaḥ samādhāya yāhi yāhi iti acodayat tatas prāyāt rathena āśu śalyaḥ tatra viśām pate yatra bhīmaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ vyadrāvayata vāhinīm tatas tūrya ninādaḥ ca bherīṇām ca mahā svanaḥ udatiṣṭhata rāja indra karṇa bhīma samāgame nārācaiḥ vimalaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ diśaḥ prādrāvayat balī sa saṃnipātaḥ tumulaḥ bhīma rūpaḥ viśām pate āsīt raudraḥ mahā rāja karṇa pāṇḍavayoḥ mṛdhe tatas muhūrtāt rāja indra pāṇḍavaḥ karṇam ādravat bhīmasenaḥ mahā bāhuḥ tam āpatantam saṃprekṣya karṇaḥ vaikartanaḥ vṛṣaḥ punar ca enam ameya ātmā śara varṣaiḥ avākirat sa viddhaḥ sūtaputreṇa chādayām āsa pattribhiḥ nārācena su tīkṣṇena sarva āvaraṇa bhedinā saḥ anyat kārmukam ādāya sūtaputram vṛkodaraḥ rājñ marmasu marma jñaḥ viddhvā su niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ tam karṇaḥ pañcaviṃśatyā nārācānām samārdayat tatas sāyaka bhinna aṅgaḥ pāṇḍavaḥ krodha mūrchitaḥ saṃrambha amarṣa tāmra akṣaḥ sūtaputra vadha icchayā girīṇām api bhettāram sāyakam samayojayat vikṛṣya balavat cāpam ā karṇāt ati mārutiḥ tam mumoca mahā iṣvāsaḥ kruddhaḥ karṇa jighāṃsayā sa visṛṣṭaḥ balavatā bāṇaḥ vajra aśani svanaḥ niṣasāda rathopasthe visaṃjñaḥ pṛtanāpatiḥ rudhireṇa avasikta aṅgaḥ gatāsu vat ariṃdamaḥ etasmin antare dṛṣṭvā madra rājaḥ vṛkodaram jihvām chettum samāyāntam sāntvayan idam abravīt bhīmasena mahā bāho yat tvā vakṣyāmi tat śṛṇu arjunena pratijñātaḥ vadhaḥ karṇasya śuṣmiṇaḥ uvāca tām tathā kuru bhadram te pratijñām savyasācinaḥ dṛḍha vrata tvam pārthasya jānāmi nṛpa sattama rājñaḥ tu dharṣaṇam pāpaḥ kṛtavan mama saṃnidhau tatas krodha abhibhūtena śeṣam na gaṇitam mayā patite ca api rādheye na me manyuḥ śamam gataḥ anena tu nṛśaṃsena samaveteṣu rājsu mākam śṛṇvatām kṛṣṇāḥ yāni vākyāni mātula asahyāni ca nīcena bahūni śrāvitāni bhoḥ nūnam te tat parijñātam dūra sthasya api pārthiva chedanam ca asya jihvāyāḥ tat eva ākāṅkṣitam mayā rājñaḥ tu priya kāmena kālaḥ ayam paripālitaḥ tat gṛhītam mahā rāja kaṭuka stham iva auṣadham asmin vinaṣṭe naṣṭāḥ smaḥ sarve eva sa keśavāḥ adya ca eva nṛśaṃsa ātmā pāpaḥ pāpa kṛtām varaḥ gamiṣyati parābhāvam dṛṣṭa mātraḥ kirīṭinā yudhiṣṭhirasya kopena pūrvam dagdhaḥ nṛśaṃsa kṛt tvayā saṃrakṣitaḥ tu adya mad samīpāt upāyatas tatas madra adhipaḥ dṛṣṭvā visaṃjñam sūtanandanam tatas parāji karṇe dhārtarāṣṭrīm mahā camūm uvāca su duṣkaram idam karma kṛtam bhīmena saṃjaya yena karṇaḥ mahā bāhuḥ rathopasthe nipātitaḥ karṇaḥ hi ekaḥ raṇe hantā sṛñjayān pāṇḍavaiḥ saha iti duryodhanaḥ sūta prābravīt mām muhur muhur parājitam tu rādheyam dṛṣṭvā bhīmena saṃyuge uvāca vibhrāntam prekṣya rādheyam sūtaputram mahā āhave mahatyā senayā rājan sodaryān samabhāṣata śīghram gacchata bhadram vaḥ rādheyam parirakṣata te tu rājñā samādiṣṭāḥ bhīmasena jighāṃsavaḥ śrutāyuḥ durdharaḥ krāthaḥ vivitsuḥ vikaṭaḥ samaḥ niṣaṅgī kavacī pāśī tathā nanda upanandakau ete rathaiḥ parivṛtāḥ vīryavantaḥ mahā balāḥ bhīmasenam samāsādya samantāt paryavārayan te vyamuñcan śara vrātān nānā liṅgān samantataḥ teṣām āpatatām kṣipram sutānām te narādhipa rathaiḥ pañcāśatā sārdham pañcāśat nyahanat rathān sa kuṇḍala śirastrāṇam pūrṇa candra upamam tadā aśobhata mahā rāja pūrṇa candraḥ iva ambare tam dṛṣṭvā nihatam śūram bhrātaraḥ sarvatas prabho tatas aparābhyām bhallābhyām putrayoḥ te mahā āhave jahāra samare prāṇān bhīmaḥ bhīma parākramaḥ hāhākāraḥ tatas tīvraḥ saṃbabhūva janeśvara vadhyamāneṣu te rājñ tadā putreṣu dhanviṣu teṣām saṃlulite sainye bhīmasenaḥ mahā balaḥ tatas te prādravan bhītāḥ putrāḥ te vihvalīkṛtāḥ bhīmasenam raṇe dṛṣṭvā kāla antaka yama upamam putrān te nihatān dṛṣṭvā sūtaputraḥ mahā manāḥ haṃsa varṇān hayān bhūyas prāhiṇot yatra pāṇḍavaḥ te preṣitāḥ mahā rāja madra rājena vājinaḥ sa saṃnipātaḥ tumulaḥ ghora rūpaḥ viśām pate āsīt raudraḥ mahā rāja karṇa pāṇḍavayoḥ mṛdhe dṛṣṭvā mama mahā rāja tau sametau mahā rathau sārathim ca asya bhallena preṣayām āsa mṛtyave chittvā ca kārmukam tūrṇam pāṇḍavasya āśu pattriṇā tatas bhīmaḥ raṇa ślāghī chādayām āsa pattribhiḥ karṇam raṇe mahā rāja putrāṇām te paśyatām tatas karṇaḥ bhṛśam kruddhaḥ bhīmam navabhiḥ āyasaiḥ āhataḥ sa mahā bāhuḥ bhīmaḥ bhīma parākramaḥ ākarṇapūrṇaiḥ viśikhaiḥ karṇam vivyādha sapta tatas karṇaḥ mahā rājaḥ āśīviṣaḥ iva śvasan śara varṣeṇa mahatā chādayām āsa pāṇḍavam bhīmaḥ api tam śara vrātaiḥ chādayitvā mahā ratham paśyatām kauraveyāṇām vinanarda mahā balaḥ tatas karṇaḥ bhṛśam kruddhaḥ dṛḍham ādāya kārmukam bhīmam vivyādha daśabhiḥ kaṅka pattraiḥ śilā śitaiḥ tatas bhīmaḥ mahā bāhuḥ hema paṭṭa vibhūṣitam parigham ghoram ādāya mṛtyu daṇḍam iva aparam karṇasya nidhana ākāṅkṣī cikṣepa atibalaḥ nadan ciccheda bahudhā karṇaḥ śaraiḥ āśīviṣa upamaiḥ tatas kārmukam ādāya bhīmaḥ dṛḍhataram tadā chādayām āsa viśikhaiḥ karṇam para bala ardanam tatas yuddham abhūt ghoram karṇa pāṇḍavayoḥ mṛdhe tatas karṇaḥ mahā rāja bhīmasenam tribhiḥ śaraiḥ ākarṇa mūlam vivyādha dṛḍham āyamya kārmukam saḥ atividdhaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ karṇena balinām varaḥ ghoram ādatta viśikham karṇa kāya avadāraṇam tasya bhittvā tanutrāṇam bhittvā kāyam ca sāyakaḥ prāviśat dharaṇīm rājan valmīkam iva pannagaḥ saṃcacāla rathe karṇaḥ kṣiti kampe yathā acalaḥ tatas karṇaḥ mahā rāja roṣa amarṣa samanvitaḥ pāṇḍavam pañcaviṃśatyā nārācānām samārpayat viratham bhīma karmāṇam bhīmam karṇaḥ cakāra ha tatas amarṣī mahā tejāḥ virathaḥ rathinām varaḥ vyadhamat gadayā bhīmaḥ śarad meghān iva anilaḥ pothayām āsa saṃkruddhaḥ samare śatru tāpanaḥ sa krodha vaśam āpannaḥ pāṇḍu putraḥ pratāpavān nāgān saptaśatān rājan īṣā dantān prahāriṇaḥ vyadhamat sahasā bhīmaḥ kruddha rūpaḥ paraṃtapaḥ dantaveṣṭeṣu netreṣu kambheṣu sa kaṭeṣu ca te abhyarditāḥ mārutinā vinadantaḥ bhṛśa āturāḥ tatas te prādravan bhītāḥ pratīpam prahitāḥ punar tān sa saptaśatān nāgān sa āroha āyudha ketanān bhūmiṣṭhaḥ gadayā jaghne śarad meghān iva anilaḥ pothayām āsa kaunteyaḥ dvāpañcāśatam āhave tathā ratha śatam sāgram pattīn ca śataśas aparān nyahanat pāṇḍavaḥ yuddhe tāpayan tava vāhinīm pratāpyamānam sūryeṇa bhīmena ca mahātmanā rathāḥ pañcaśatāḥ ca anye hrādinaḥ carma varmiṇaḥ bhīmam abhyadravan tūrṇam śara pūgaiḥ samantataḥ tān sa sūta rathān sarvān sa patākā dhvaja āyudhān pothayām āsa gadayā bhīmaḥ viṣṇuḥ iva asurān tatas śakuni nirdiṣṭāḥ sādinaḥ śūra saṃmatāḥ tri sāhasrāḥ yayuḥ bhīmam śakti ṛṣṭi prāsa pāṇayaḥ tān pratyudgamya yavanān aśva ārohān vara ari hā teṣām āsīt mahān śabdaḥ tāḍitānām ca sārvaśaḥ asibhiḥ chidyamānānām naḍānām iva bhārata śaraiḥ pracchādayām āsa sārathim ca api apātayat tatas saṃpradrutam saṃkhye ratham dṛṣṭvā mahā rathaḥ rājānam abhi dhāvantam śaraiḥ āvṛtya rodasī kruddhaḥ pracchādayām āsa śara jālena mārutiḥ saṃnivṛt tatas tūrṇam rādheyaḥ śatru karśana bhīmam pracchādayām āsa samantāt niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ bhīmasena ratha vyagram karṇam bhārata sātyakiḥ abhyardayat ameya ātmā pārṣṇigrahaṇa kāraṇāt tau anyonyam samāsādya vṛṣabhau sarva dhanvinām visṛjantau śarān citrān vibhrājetām manasvinaḥ tābhyām viyati rāja indra vitatam bhīma darśanam krauñca pṛṣṭha aruṇam raudram bāṇa jālam vyadṛśyata na eva sūrya prabhām kham vā na diśaḥ pradiśaḥ kutas vayam tābhyām śaraiḥ muktaiḥ sahasraśas hṛtāḥ sarvāḥ śara oghaiḥ taiḥ karṇa mādhavayoḥ tadā saubalam kṛtavarmāṇam drauṇim ādhirathim kṛpam saṃsaktān pāṇḍavaiḥ dṛṣṭvā nivṛttāḥ kuravaḥ punar teṣām āpatatām śabdaḥ tīvraḥ āsīt viśām pate uddhūtānām yathā vṛṣṭyā sāgarāṇām bhaya āvahaḥ te sene bhṛśa saṃvigne dṛṣṭvā anyonyam mahā raṇe yādṛśam na kadā cit hi dṛṣṭa pūrvam na ca śrutam āsīt ninādaḥ su mahān bala oghānām parasparam garjatām sāgara oghānām yathā syāt nisvanaḥ mahān tatas pravavṛte yuddham ghora rūpam viśām pate harṣeṇa mahatā yuktaiḥ kuru pāṇḍava sainikaiḥ kurūṇām pāṇḍavānām ca lipsatām su mahat yaśaḥ kurūṇām garjatām tatra aviccheda kṛtāḥ giraḥ śrūyante vividhāḥ rājan nāmāni uddiśya bhārata yasya yat hi raṇe nyaṅgam pitṛtaḥ mātṛtaḥ api vā tān dṛṣṭvā samare śūrān tarjayānān parasparam abhavat me matiḥ rājan na eṣām asti iti jīvitam teṣām dṛṣṭvā tu kruddhānām vapūṃṣi amita tejasām tatas te pāṇḍavāḥ rājan kauravāḥ ca mahā rathāḥ uvāca kṣatriyāḥ te mahā rāja paraspara vadha eṣiṇaḥ ratha oghāḥ ca haya oghāḥ ca nara oghāḥ ca samantataḥ gaja oghāḥ ca mahā rāja saṃsaktāḥ sma parasparam gadānām parighāṇām ca kaṇapānām ca sarpatām prāsānām bhindipālānām bhuśuṇḍīnām ca sarvaśas saṃpātam ca anvapaśyāma saṃgrāme bhṛśa dāruṇe śalabhāḥ iva saṃpetuḥ samantāt śara vṛṣṭayaḥ nāgāḥ nāgān samāsādya vyadhamanta parasparam hastinaḥ aśvān rathān ca eva nāgāḥ ca samare tri aṅgam mamṛduḥ śīghra gāḥ nṛpa hayāḥ tri aṅgam ca māriṣa narāḥ ca mamṛduḥ tri aṅgam rathāḥ tri aṅgam ca māriṣa śara tomara nārācaiḥ gadā śakti paraśvadhaiḥ patatām tatra śūrāṇām krośatām ca parasparam ghoram āyodhanam jajñe paśūnām vaiśasam yathā rudhireṇa samāstīrṇā bhāti bhārata medinī śakragopa gaṇa ākīrṇā prāvṛṣi iva yathā dharā yathā vā vāsasī śukle mahārajana rañjite bibhṛyāt yuvatiḥ śyāmā tadvat āsīt vasuṃdharā baddha cūḍāmaṇi varaiḥ śirobhiḥ cāru kuṇḍalaiḥ ujjhitaiḥ vṛṣabha akṣāṇām bhrājate sma vasuṃdharā māṃsa śoṇita citrā iva śātakaumbha mayā iva ca bhūḥ babhau bharata śreṣṭha śānta arcirbhiḥ iva agnibhiḥ chinnānām ca uttamāṅgānām bāhūnām ca ūrubhiḥ saha kuṇḍalānām praviddhānām bhūṣaṇānām ca bhārata niṣkāṇām adhi sūtrāṇām śarīrāṇām ca dhanvinām varmaṇām sa patākānām saṃghāḥ tatra apatan bhuvi agamya kalpā pṛthivī sarvatas bhṛśa durgamā gajān gajāḥ samāsādya viṣāṇa agraiḥ adārayan viṣāṇa abhihatāḥ te ca bhrājante dviradāḥ yathā rudhireṇa avasikta aṅgāḥ gairika prasravāḥ iva yathā bhrājanti syandantaḥ parvatāḥ dhātu maṇḍitāḥ tathā rejuḥ raṇe nāgāḥ rudhireṇa samāplutāḥ tomarān gajibhiḥ muktān pratīpān āsthitān bahūn nārācaiḥ chinna varmāṇaḥ bhrājante sma gaja uttamāḥ hima āgame mahā rāja vyabhrāḥ iva mahīdharāḥ ulkābhiḥ saṃpradīpta agrāḥ parvatāḥ iva māriṣa ke cit abhyāhatāḥ nāgāḥ nāgaiḥ naga nibhāḥ bhuvi apare prādravan nāgāḥ śalya ārtāḥ vraṇa pīḍitāḥ mamluḥ ca bahavaḥ rājan cukūjuḥ ca apare tathā hayāḥ ca nihatāḥ bāṇaiḥ svarṇa bhāṇḍa paricchadāḥ niṣeduḥ ca eva mamluḥ ca babhramuḥ ca diśaḥ daśa apare kṛṣyamāṇāḥ ca viveṣṭantaḥ mahī tale bhāvān bahuvidhān cakruḥ tāḍitāḥ śara tomaraiḥ narāḥ tu nihatāḥ bhūmau kūjantaḥ tatra māriṣa dṛṣṭvā ca bāndhavān anye pitṝn anye pitāmahān dhāvamānān parān ca eva dṛṣṭvā anye tatra bhārata gotra nāmāni khyātāni śaśaṃsuḥ itaretaram teṣām chinnāḥ mahā rāja bhujāḥ kanaka bhūṣaṇāḥ vegān ca anye raṇe cakruḥ sphurantaḥ iva pannagāḥ te bhujāḥ bhogi bhoga ābhāḥ candana aktāḥ viśām pate lohita ārdrāḥ bhṛśam rejuḥ tapanīya dhvajāḥ iva bhaumena rajasā kīrṇe śastra saṃpāta saṃkule śoṇita udāḥ mahā nadyaḥ prasasruḥ tatra ca asakṛt śīrṣa pāṣāṇa saṃchannāḥ keśa śaivala śādvalāḥ asthi saṃghāta saṃkīrṇāḥ dhanuḥ śara vara uttamāḥ māṃsa kardama paṅkāḥ ca śoṇita oghāḥ su dāruṇāḥ nadīḥ pravartayām āsuḥ yama rāṣṭra vivardhanīḥ bhīru vitrāsa kārinyaḥ śūrāṇām harṣa vardhanāḥ kravyādānām nara vyāghra nardatām tatra tatra ha nṛtyanti vai bhūta gaṇāḥ saṃtṛptāḥ māṃsa śoṇitaiḥ pītvā ca śoṇitam tatra vasām pītvā ca bhārata medaḥ majjā vasā tṛptāḥ tṛptāḥ māṃsasya ca eva hi dhāvamānāḥ ca dṛśyante kāka gṛdhra balāḥ tathā yodha vrata samākhyātāḥ cakruḥ karmāṇi abhīta vat śara śakti samākīrṇe kravyāda gaṇa saṃkule vyacaranta gaṇaiḥ śūrāḥ khyāpayantaḥ sva pauruṣam anyonyam śrāvayanti sma nāma gotrāṇi bhārata pitṛ nāmāni ca raṇe gotra nāmāni ca abhitas śrāvayantaḥ hi bahavaḥ tatra yodhāḥ viśām pate anyonyam avamṛdnantaḥ śakti tomara paṭṭiśaiḥ vyaṣīdat kauravā senā bhinnā nauḥ iva sāgare uvāca vartamāne tadā yuddhe kṣatriyāṇām nimajjane gāṇḍīvasya mahān ghoṣaḥ śuśruve yudhi māriṣa saṃśaptakānām kadanam akarot yatra pāṇḍavaḥ kosalānām tathā rājan nārāyaṇa balasya ca saṃśaptakāḥ tu samare śara vṛṣṭim samantataḥ apātayan pārtha mūrdhni jaya gṛddhāḥ pramanyavaḥ tām vṛṣṭim sahasā rājan tarasā dhārayan prabhuḥ nigṛhya tu ratha anīkam kaṅka patraiḥ śilā śitaiḥ āsasāda raṇe pārthaḥ suśarmāṇam mahā ratham sa tasya śara varṣāṇi vavarṣa rathinām varaḥ tathā saṃśaptakāḥ ca eva pārthasya samare sthitāḥ suśarmā tu tatas pārtham viddhvā navabhiḥ āśugaiḥ kapeḥ tu ninadam śrutvā saṃtrastā te vāhinī bhayam vipulam ādāya niśceṣṭā samapadyata tatas sā śuśubhe senā niśceṣṭā avasthitā nṛpa nānā puṣpa samākīrṇam yathā caitraratham vanam arjunam siṣicuḥ bāṇaiḥ parvatam jaladāḥ iva nigṛhya tam pracukruśuḥ vadhyamānāḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ nigrahītum upākrāman krodha āviṣṭāḥ samantataḥ ratham āruruhuḥ ke cit pārtha kṛṣṇau jighṛkṣavaḥ saṃśaptakānām yodhāḥ te siṃhanādān ca nedire sa rathaḥ taiḥ gṛhītaḥ tu pāṇḍavasya mahātmanaḥ tatas pārthaḥ mahā bāhuḥ saṃvṛtaḥ taiḥ mahā rathaiḥ nigṛhītam ratham dṛṣṭvā tān ca abhidravataḥ bahūn te hayān ratha cakre ca ratha īṣāḥ ca api bhārata nigṛhya balavat tūrṇam siṃhanādam atha anadan keśavaḥ tu tadā bāhū vidhunvan raṇa mūrdhani pātayām āsa tān sarvān duṣṭa hastī iva hastinaḥ tatas kruddhaḥ raṇe pārthaḥ saṃvṛtaḥ taiḥ mahā rathaiḥ nigṛhītam ratham dṛṣṭvā keśavam ca api abhidrutam ratha ārūḍhān ca su bahūn padātīn ca api apātayat āsannān ca tatas yodhān śaraiḥ āsanna yodhibhiḥ tān tāpayitvā samare pārthaḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ cyāvayām āsa samare keśavam ca idam abravīt paśya kṛṣṇa mahā bāho saṃśaptaka gaṇān mayā kurvāṇān dāruṇam karma vadhyamānān sahasraśas ratha bandham imam ghoram pṛthivyām na asti kaḥ cana patyamānān raṇe kṛṣṇa śaraiḥ āśīviṣa upamaiḥ vyanādayat ameya ātmā devadattam mahā mṛdhe devadatta svanam śrutvā keśavaḥ api mahā yaśāḥ pāñcajanyam ca kṛṣṇaḥ api pūrayan iva rodasī tam tu śaṅkha svanam śrutvā saṃśaptaka varūthinī saṃcacāla mahā rāja vitrastā ca abhavat bhṛśam pada bandham tatas cakre pāṇḍavaḥ para vīra hā nāgam astram mahā rāja saṃprodīrya muhur muhur nāgam astram tatas pārthaḥ prāduś cakre hasan iva yān uddiśya raṇe pārthaḥ pada bandham cakāra ha te baddhāḥ pada bandhena pāṇḍavena mahātmanā niśceṣṭāḥ abhavan rājan aśmasāra mayāḥ iva niśceṣṭān tu tatas yodhān avadhīt pāṇḍu nandanaḥ āyudhāni ca sarvāṇi visraṣṭum upacakramuḥ te baddhāḥ pāda bandhena na śekuḥ ceṣṭitum nṛpa tatas tān avadhīt pārthaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ tatas suśarmā rāja indra gṛhītām vīkṣya vāhinīm sauparṇam astram tvaritaḥ prāduścakre mahā rathaḥ tatas suparṇāḥ saṃpetuḥ bhakṣayantaḥ bhujaṃgamān te vai vidudruvuḥ nāgāḥ dṛṣṭvā tān kha carān nṛpa megha vṛndāt yathā muktaḥ bhāskaraḥ tāpayan prajāḥ sasṛjuḥ bāṇa saṃghān ca śastra saṃghān ca māriṣa tām mahā astra mayīm vṛṣṭim saṃchidya śara vṛṣṭibhiḥ vyavātiṣṭhat tatas yodhān vāsaviḥ para vīra hā suśarmā tu tatas rājan bāṇena ānata parvaṇā arjunam hṛdaye viddhvā vivyādha anyaiḥ tribhiḥ śaraiḥ saḥ atividdhaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ śaraiḥ āśīviṣa upamaiḥ suśarmāṇam mahā rāja krodha āviṣṭaḥ mahā rathaḥ tatas śara śataiḥ pārthaḥ saṃchādya enam kṣaṇāt raṇe diśaḥ āvārayām āsa bāṇaiḥ tatra mahā astra vid vimukhīkṛtya samare suśarmāṇam dhanaṃjayaḥ tatas śaṅkha ninādāḥ ca bherī śabdāḥ ca puṣkalāḥ nānā vāditra ninadāḥ siṃhanādāḥ ca jajñire pratilabhya tatas saṃjñām śvetāśvaḥ kṛṣṇa sārathiḥ tatas bāṇa sahasrāṇi samutpannāni māriṣa hayān rathān ca samare śastraiḥ śata sahasraśas rarāja samare rājñ śakraḥ nighnan iva asurān vadhyamāne tatas sainye vipulā bhī samāviśat saṃśaptaka gaṇānām ca gopālānām ca bhārata paśyatām tatra vīrāṇām ahanyata mahat balam hanyamānam apaśyan ca niśceṣṭāḥ sma parākrame ayutam tatra yodhānām hatvā pāṇḍu sutaḥ raṇe caturdaśa sahasrāṇi yāni śiṣṭāni bhārata rathānām ayutam ca eva tri sāhasrāḥ ca dantinaḥ tatas saṃśaptakāḥ bhūyas parivavruḥ dhanaṃjayam tatra yuddham mahat hi āsīt tāvakānām viśām pate śūreṇa balinā sārdham pāṇḍavena kirīṭinā jitvā tān nyahanat pārthaḥ śatrūn śakraḥ iva asurān uvāca kṛtavarmā kṛpaḥ drauṇiḥ sūtaputraḥ ca māriṣa ulūkaḥ saubalaḥ ca eva rājā ca saha sodaraiḥ sīdamānām camūm dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍu putra bhaya arditām samujjihīrṣuḥ vegena bhinnām nāvam iva arṇave bhīrūṇām trāsa jananam śūrāṇām harṣa vardhanam bhīmasenam sa pāñcālam cedi kaikeya saṃvṛtam vaikartanaḥ svayam yuddhvā vārayām āsa kārmukaiḥ tatas cedi karūṣān ca sṛñjayān ca mahā rathān kṛpeṇa śara varṣāṇi vipramuktāni saṃyuge sṛñjayāḥ śātayām āsuḥ śalabhānām vrajāḥ iva vavarṣa śara varṣāṇi samantāt eva brāhmaṇe mahat āsīt tadā yuddham muhūrtāt iva dāruṇam śikhaṇḍinam raṇe kruddhaḥ vivyādha daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ tatas śikhaṇḍī śaraiḥ sapta āhave kṛpam vivyādha su bhṛśam kaṅka pattraiḥ ajihmagaiḥ tatas kṛpaḥ śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ saḥ atividdhaḥ mahā rathaḥ tatas tu niśitaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ kṣurapraiḥ hema bhūṣaṇaiḥ vyaśva sūta ratham cakre pārṣatam tu dvijottamaḥ hata aśvāt tu tatas yānāt avaplutya mahā rathaḥ carma khaḍge ca saṃgṛhya sa tvaram brāhmaṇam yayau tam āpatantam sahasā śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ tatra adbhutam apaśyāma śilānām plavanam yathā niśceṣṭaḥ yat raṇe rājñ śikhaṇḍī samatiṣṭhata kṛpeṇa chāditam dṛṣṭvā nṛpa uttama śikhaṇḍinam pratyudyayau kṛpam tūrṇam dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ mahā rathaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnam tatas yāntam śāradvata ratham prati yudhiṣṭhiram atha āyāntam śāradvata ratham prati pratijagrāha te putraḥ śara varṣeṇa vārayan bhīmasenam karūṣān ca kekayān saha sṛñjayān śikhaṇḍinaḥ tatas bāṇān kṛpaḥ śāradvataḥ yudhi prāhiṇot tvarayā yuktaḥ didhakṣuḥ iva māriṣa tān śarān preṣitān tena samantāt hema bhūṣaṇān ciccheda khaḍgam āvidhya bhrāmayan ca punar punar vyadhamat sāyakaiḥ tūrṇam tatas uccukruśuḥ janāḥ sa vicarmā mahā rāja khaḍga pāṇiḥ upādravat kṛpasya vaśam āpannaḥ mṛtyoḥ āsyam iva āturaḥ śāradvata śaraiḥ grastam kliśyamānam mahā balam vikiran brāhmaṇam yuddhe bahubhiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ dṛṣṭvā aviṣahyam tam yuddhe brāhmaṇam carita vratam apayātaḥ tatas tūrṇam śikhaṇḍī rāja sattama viddhvā vivyādha saptatyā punar ca enam tribhiḥ śaraiḥ atha asya sa śaram cāpam punar ciccheda māriṣa sārathim ca śareṇa asya bhṛśam marmaṇi atāḍayat suketum triṃśatā bāṇaiḥ sarva marmasu atāḍayat bhūmicāle yathā vṛkṣaḥ calati ākampitaḥ bhṛśam sa uṣṇīṣam sa śirastrāṇam kṣurapreṇa anvapātayat tat śiraḥ prāpatat bhūmau śyena āhṛtam iva āmiṣam tatas asya kāyaḥ vasudhām paścāt prāpa tadā cyutaḥ tasmin hate mahā rāja trastāḥ tasya padānugāḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnam tu samare saṃnivārya mahā balaḥ kṛtavarmā abravīt dhṛṣṭaḥ tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti pārṣatam tat abhūt tumulam yuddham vṛṣṇi pārṣatayoḥ raṇe āmiṣa arthe yathā yuddham śyenayoḥ gṛddhayoḥ nṛpa dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ tu samare hārdikyam navabhiḥ śaraiḥ ājaghāna urasi kruddhaḥ pīḍayan hṛdika ātmajam kṛtavarmā tu samare pārṣatena dṛḍha āhataḥ pārṣatam sa ratham sa aśvam chādayām āsa sāyakaiḥ sa rathaḥ chāditaḥ rājan dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ na dṛśyate vidhūya tam bāṇa gaṇam śaraiḥ kanaka bhūṣaṇaiḥ vyarocata raṇe rājan dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ kṛta vraṇaḥ tatas tu pārṣataḥ kruddhaḥ śastra vṛṣṭim su dāruṇām kṛtavarmāṇam āsādya vyasṛjat pṛtanāpatiḥ tām āpatantīm sahasā śastra vṛṣṭim nirantarām gṛhītvā carma khaḍgam ca ratham tasya avapupluve miśriteṣu atha vāheṣu pratyāsanne ca pārṣate dṛṣṭvā apadānam tasya āśu gadām jagrāha sātvataḥ gadā pāṇiḥ tatas rājan rathāt tūrṇam avaplutaḥ tam a dṛṣṭvā rathopasthe sārathim samatāḍayat khaḍgena śita dhāreṇa sa hataḥ prāpatat rathāt kṛtavarmā tatas hṛṣṭaḥ tala śabdam cakāra ha pārṣatam ca abravīt rājan ehi ehi iti punar punar sa tam na mamṛṣe yuddhe tala śabdam samīritam yathā nāgaḥ sadā mattaḥ tala śabdam samīritam abhyayāt sa tu tam tūrṇam tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt dhṛṣṭadyumna mukhān sarvān pāṇḍavān paryavārayat tatas rājan mahā iṣvāsaḥ kṛtavarmāṇam āśu vai gadām gṛhya punar vegāt kṛtavarmāṇam āhanat tatas rājñ mahā iṣvāsam kṛtavarmāṇam āśu vai śrutavān ratham āropya apovāha raṇa ajirāt dṛṣṭvā tu dāritām yuddhe śastra vṛṣṭim duruttarām kṛtavarmāṇam abhyetya vārayām āsa pārṣataḥ hārdikyam chādayām āsa pārṣataḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ sārathim ca asya tarasā prāhiṇot yama sādanam dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ tu balavān jitvā śatrum mahā ratham kauravān samare tūrṇam vārayām āsa sāyakaiḥ tatas te tāvakāḥ yodhāḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnam upādravan uvāca drauṇiḥ yudhiṣṭhiram dṛṣṭvā śaineyena abhirakṣitam kiran iṣu gaṇān ghorān svarṇa puṅkhān śilā śitān darśayan vividhān mārgān śikṣā artham laghu hasta vat tatas kham pūrayām āsa śaraiḥ divya astra mantritaiḥ drauṇāyani śara channam na prājñāyata kim cana bāṇa bhūtam abhūt sarvam āyodhana śiraḥ hi tat bāṇa jālam diviṣṭham tat svarṇa jāla vibhūṣitam śuśubhe bharata śreṣṭha vitānam iva viṣṭhitam tena channe raṇe rājan bāṇa jālena bhāsvatā tatra āścaryam apaśyāma bāṇa bhūte tathāvidhe na sma saṃpatate bhūmau dṛṣṭvā drauṇeḥ parākramam lāghavam droṇaputrasya dṛṣṭvā tatra mahā rathāḥ sātyakiḥ yatamānaḥ tu dharmarājaḥ ca pāṇḍavaḥ sātyakiḥ dharmarājaḥ ca pāñcālāḥ ca api saṃgatāḥ tyaktvā mṛtyu bhayam ghoram drauṇāyanim upādravan sātyakiḥ pañcaviṃśatyā drauṇim viddhvā śilā mukhaiḥ punar vivyādha nārācaiḥ sapta svarṇa bhūṣitaiḥ śrutakarmā tribhiḥ bāṇaiḥ śrutakīrtiḥ tu sapta sutasomaḥ ca navabhiḥ śatānīkaḥ ca saptabhiḥ anye ca bahavaḥ śūrāḥ vivyadhuḥ tam samantataḥ saḥ ati kruddhaḥ tatas rājan āśīviṣaḥ iva śvasan sātyakim pañcaviṃśatyā prāvidhyata śilā śitaiḥ śrutakīrtim ca navabhiḥ sutasomam ca pañcabhiḥ aṣṭabhiḥ śrutakarmāṇam prativindhyam tribhiḥ śaraiḥ atha itarān tatas śūrān dvābhyām dvābhyām atāḍayat śrutakīrteḥ tathā cāpam ciccheda niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ atha anyat dhanuḥ ādāya śrutakīrtiḥ mahā rathaḥ drauṇāyanim tribhiḥ viddhvā vivyādha anyaiḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ tatas drauṇiḥ mahā rāja śara varṣeṇa bhārata chādayām āsa tat sainyam samantāt ca śaraiḥ nṛpān ardhacandreṇa tīkṣṇena dhanuḥ chittvā anadat bhṛśam chinna dhanvā tatas drauṇiḥ śaktyā śaktimatām varaḥ sārathim pātayām āsa śaineyasya rathāt drutam atha anyat dhanuḥ ādāya droṇaputraḥ pratāpavān śaineyam śara varṣeṇa chādayām āsa bhārata tasya aśvāḥ pradrutāḥ saṃkhye patite ratha sārathau yudhiṣṭhira purogāḥ te drauṇim śastrabhṛtām varam abhyavarṣanta vegena visṛjantaḥ śitān śarān āgacchamānān tān dṛṣṭvā raudra rūpān paraṃtapaḥ tatas śara śata jvālaḥ senā kakṣam mahā rathaḥ tat balam pāṇḍaveyasya droṇaputra śara arciṣā tāpayan bharata śreṣṭha gabhastibhiḥ iva aṃśumant tat tāpyamānam tīkṣṇa agraiḥ brāhmaṇasya ca sāyakaiḥ kṣubhyate pāṇḍavam sainyam tat bhajyamānam marṣeṇa brāhmaṇasya śara āhatam dṛṣṭvā te ca mahā rāja droṇaputra parākramam nihatān menire sarvān pāṇḍūn droṇa sutena vai yudhiṣṭhiraḥ tu tvaritaḥ drauṇim śliṣya mahā ratham abravīt droṇaputram tu roṣa amarṣa samanvitaḥ jānāmi tvām yudhi śreṣṭham vīryavantam bala anvitam kṛtāstram kṛtinam ca eva tathā laghu parākramam sa hi vai pārṣatam dṛṣṭvā samare śatru sūdanam na eva nāma tava prītiḥ na eva nāma kṛtajña tā yatas tvam puruṣa vyāghra mām eva adya jighāṃsasi brāhmaṇena tapaḥ kāryam dānam adhyayanam tathā kṣatriyeṇa dhanuḥ nāmyam sa bhavān brāhmaṇabruvaḥ miṣataḥ te mahā bāho jeṣyāmi yudhi kauravān an uktvā ca tatas kim cit śara varṣeṇa pāṇḍavam saṃchādyamānaḥ tu tadā droṇaputreṇa māriṣa pārthaḥ apayātaḥ śīghram vai vihāya mahatīm camūm droṇaputraḥ sthitaḥ rājñ pratyādeśāt mahātmanaḥ tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ rājā tyaktvā drauṇim mahā āhave prayayau tāvakam sainyam yuktaḥ krūrāya karmaṇe uvāca bhīmasenam sa pāñcālyam cedi kekaya saṃvṛtam vaikartanaḥ svayam ruddhvā vārayām āsa sāyakaiḥ tatas tu cedi kārūṣān sṛñjayān ca mahā rathān sūtaputraḥ api samare pāñcālān kekayān tathā sṛñjayān ca mahā iṣvāsān nijaghāna sahasraśas saṃśaptakeṣu pārthaḥ ca kauraveṣu vṛkodaraḥ pāñcāleṣu tathā karṇaḥ kṣayam cakruḥ mahā rathāḥ te kṣatriyāḥ dahyamānāḥ tribhiḥ taiḥ pāvaka upamaiḥ vivyādha bharata śreṣṭha caturaḥ ca asya vājinaḥ tau ubhau bharata śreṣṭhau śreṣṭhau sarva dhanuṣmatām vivyādha urasi saṃkruddhaḥ pañcabhiḥ pañcabhiḥ śaraiḥ tatas aparābhyām bhallābhyām dhanuṣī samakṛntata tau anye dhanuṣī śreṣṭhe śakra cāpa nibhe śubhe pāṇḍu putrau mahā iṣvāsau vārayām āsa pattribhiḥ dhanuḥ maṇḍalam eva asya dṛśyate yudhi bhārata sāyakāḥ ca eva dṛśyante niścarantaḥ samantataḥ tasya sāyaka saṃchannau cakāśetām ca pāṇḍavau te tu bāṇāḥ mahā rāja hema puṅkhāḥ śilā śitāḥ ācchādayan diśaḥ sarvāḥ sūryasya iva aṃśavaḥ tadā tām bāṇa vṛṣṭim rājñaḥ tu śaraiḥ śata sahasrabhiḥ tatas tayoḥ mahā rāja sṛjatoḥ aniśam śarān yamābhyām dadṛśe rūpam kāla antaka yama upamam parākramam tu tam dṛṣṭvā tava sūnoḥ mahā rathāḥ krodham āsthāya paramam niḥśvasan ca yathā uragaḥ bāṇa andhakāram sasṛje te putraḥ tayoḥ tadā tatas senāpatiḥ rājan pāṇḍavasya mahātmanaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ te sutam tāḍayām āsa sāyakaiḥ pāñcālyam pañcaviṃśatyā prahasya puruṣa ṛṣabha viddhvā nanāda pāñcālyam ṣaṣṭyā pañcabhiḥ eva ca atha asya sa śaram cāpam hasta āvāpam ca māriṣa kṣurapreṇa su tīkṣṇena rājā ciccheda saṃyuge tat apāsya dhanuḥ chinnam pāñcālyaḥ śatru karśanaḥ aśobhata mahā iṣvāsaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ kṛta vraṇaḥ sa pañcadaśa nārācān śvasataḥ pannagān iva jighāṃsuḥ bharata śreṣṭham dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ vyavāsṛjat te varma hema vikṛtam bhittvā rājñaḥ śilā śitāḥ viviśuḥ vasudhām vegāt kaṅka barhiṇa vāsasaḥ vasante puṣpa śabalaḥ sa puṣpaḥ iva kiṃśukaḥ atha enam chinna dhanvānam tvaramāṇaḥ mahīpatiḥ vivyādha vividhaiḥ bāṇaiḥ kāla antaka yama upamaiḥ tat apāsya dhanuḥ chinnam dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ mahā manāḥ anyat ādatta vegena dhanuḥ bhallān ca ṣoḍaśa tatas duryodhanasya aśvān hatvā sūtam ca pañcabhiḥ ratham sa upaskaram chatram śaktim khaḍgam gadām dhvajam tapanīya aṅgadam citram nāgam maṇi mayam śubham dhvajam kuru pateḥ chinnam dadṛśuḥ sarva pārthivāḥ tam āropya rathe rājan daṇḍadhāraḥ janādhipam apovāha ca saṃbhrāntaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnasya paśyataḥ karṇaḥ tu sātyakim jitvā rāja gṛddhī mahā balaḥ droṇa hantāram ugra iṣum sasāra abhimukham raṇe tam pṛṣṭhatas abhyayāt tūrṇam śaineyaḥ vitudan śaraiḥ vāraṇam jaghana upānte viṣāṇābhyām iva dvipaḥ sa bhārata mahān āsīt yodhānām su mahātmanām karṇa pārṣatayoḥ madhye tvadīyānām mahā raṇaḥ na pāṇḍavānām na asmākam yodhaḥ kaḥ cit parāṅmukhaḥ pratyadṛśyata yat karṇaḥ pāñcālān tvaritaḥ yayau tasmin kṣaṇe nara śreṣṭha gaja vāji nara kṣayaḥ pāñcālāḥ tu mahā rāja tvaritāḥ vijigīṣavaḥ teṣām ādhirathiḥ kruddhaḥ yatamānān manasvinaḥ vicinvan eva bāṇa agraiḥ samāsādayat agratas vyāghraketum suśarmāṇam śaṅkum ca ugram dhanaṃjayam śuklam ca rocamānam ca siṃhasenam ca durjayam sṛjantam sāyakān kruddham karṇam āhava śobhinam yudhyamānān tu tān śūrān manuja indraḥ pratāpavān aṣṭābhiḥ aṣṭau rādheyaḥ nyahanat niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ atha aparān mahā rāja sūtaputraḥ pratāpavān jaghāna bahu sāhasrān yodhān yuddha viśāradaḥ viṣṇum ca viṣṇukarmāṇam devāpim bhadram eva ca daṇḍam ca samare rājñ citram citrāyudham harim siṃhaketum rocamānam śalabham ca mahā ratham nijaghāna su saṃkruddhaḥ cedīnām ca mahā rathān teṣām ādadataḥ prāṇān āsīt ādhiratheḥ vapuḥ śoṇita abhyukṣita aṅgasya rudrasya iva ūrjitam mahat tatra bhārata karṇena mātaṃgāḥ tāḍitāḥ śaraiḥ nipetuḥ urvyām samare karṇa sāyaka pīḍitāḥ kurvantaḥ vividhān nādān vajra nunnāḥ iva acalāḥ na eva bhīṣmaḥ na ca droṇaḥ na api anye yudhi tāvakāḥ cakruḥ sma tādṛśam karma yādṛśam vai kṛtam raṇe sūtaputreṇa nāgeṣu ratheṣu ca hayeṣu ca pāñcālānām tathā madhye karṇaḥ acarat abhīta vat yathā mṛga gaṇān trastān siṃhaḥ drāvayate diśaḥ pāñcālānām ratha vrātān karṇaḥ drāvayate tathā siṃha āsyam ca yathā prāpya na jīvanti mṛgāḥ kva cit tathā karṇam anuprāpya na jīvanti mahā rathāḥ vaiśvānaram yathā dīptam dahyante prāpya vai janāḥ karṇa agninā raṇe tadvat dagdhāḥ bhārata sṛñjayāḥ karṇena cediṣu ekena pāñcāleṣu ca bhārata viśrāvya nāma nihatāḥ bahavaḥ śūra saṃmatāḥ mama ca āsīt manuṣya indra dṛṣṭvā karṇasya vikramam pāñcālān vidhaman saṃkhye sūtaputraḥ pratāpavān pāñcālān atha nighnantam karṇam dṛṣṭvā mahā raṇe dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ ca rājānam draupadeyāḥ ca māriṣa parivavruḥ amitra ghnam śataśas ca apare janāḥ śikhaṇḍī sahadevaḥ ca nakulaḥ nākuliḥ tathā ete purogamāḥ bhūtvā dhṛṣṭadyumnasya saṃyuge tān tatra ādhirathiḥ saṃkhye cedi pāñcāla pāṇḍavān sātyakim ca mahā rāja na atyavartata saṃyuge taiḥ karṇasya bhavat yuddham ghora rūpam viśām pate tādṛś yādṛś purā vṛttam devānām dānavaiḥ saha tān sametān mahā iṣvāsān śara varṣa ogha varṣiṇaḥ vāhlīkān kekayān matsyān vāsātyān madra saindhavān tatra marmasu bhīmena nārācaiḥ tāḍitāḥ gajāḥ vājinaḥ ca hata ārohāḥ pattayaḥ ca gatāsavaḥ tāḍitāḥ sahasā nāgāḥ bhīmasenena māriṣaiḥ śuśubhe vasudhā rājan vikīrṇaiḥ iva parvataiḥ sahasraśas ca rathinaḥ patitāḥ patita āyudhāḥ akṣatāḥ samadṛśyanta bhīmāt bhītāḥ gatāsavaḥ rathibhiḥ vājibhiḥ sūtaiḥ pattibhiḥ ca tathā gajaiḥ bhīmasena śara chinnaiḥ āstīrṇā vasudhā bhavat niśceṣṭam tumule dīnam babhau tasmin mahā raṇe prasanna salilaḥ kāle yathā syāt sāgaraḥ nṛpa sūtaputraḥ raṇe kruddhaḥ pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm bhīmasenaḥ kurūn ca api drāvayan bahu aśobhata nihatya pṛtanā madhye saṃśaptaka gaṇān bahūn arjunaḥ jayatām śreṣṭhaḥ vāsudevam atha abravīt ete dhāvanti sa gaṇāḥ saṃśaptaka mahā rathāḥ a pārayantaḥ mad bāṇān siṃha śabdāt mṛgāḥ iva kuravaḥ ca api dhāvanti bhīmasena bhaya arditāḥ dīryate ca mahat sainyam sṛñjayānām mahā raṇe hasti kakṣyaḥ hi asau kṛṣṇa ketuḥ karṇasya dhīmataḥ na ca karṇam raṇe śaktāḥ jetum anye mahā rathāḥ durjayāḥ hi eṣa samare deva dānava rākṣasaiḥ jānīte hi bhavān karṇam vīryavantam parākrame varjayitvā raṇe yāhi sūtaputram mahā ratham śramaḥ mā bādhate kṛṣṇa yathā vā tava rocate abravīt arjunam tūrṇam kauravān jahi pāṇḍava haṃsa varṇāḥ praviviśuḥ vahantaḥ kṛṣṇa pāṇḍavau keśava prahitaiḥ aśvaiḥ śvetaiḥ kāñcana bhūṣaṇaiḥ calat patākaḥ tām senām vimānam divam iva āviśata tau vidārya mahā senām praviṣṭau keśava arjunau kruddhau saṃrambha rakta akṣau vyabhrājetām mahā dyutī yuddha śauṇḍau samāhūtau aribhiḥ tau raṇa adhvaram krodha tāmra īkṣaṇau śūrau śuśubhāte mahā balau mada utkaṭau yathā nāgau dṛṣṭi saṃcāra cāriṇaḥ vigāhan sa ratha anīkam aśva saṃghān ca phalgunaḥ vyacarat pṛtanā madhye pāśa hastaḥ iva antakaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā yudhi vikrāntam senāyām te bhārata tatas ratha sahasreṇa dviradānām tribhiḥ śataiḥ caturdaśa sahasraiḥ ca turagāṇām mahā āhave dvābhyām śata sahasrābhyām padātīnām ca dhanvinām śūrāṇām nāma labdhānām viditānām samantataḥ śara varṣaiḥ mahā rāja sarvatas pāṇḍu nandanam sa chādyamānaḥ samare śaraiḥ para bala ardanaḥ darśayan raudram ātmānam pāśa hastaḥ iva antakaḥ nighnan saṃśaptakān pārthaḥ prekṣaṇīyataraḥ abhavat tatas vidyut prabhaiḥ bāṇaiḥ kārtasvara vibhūṣitaiḥ nirantaram iva ākāśam āsīt nunnaiḥ kirīṭinā kirīṭi bhuja nirmuktaiḥ saṃpatadbhiḥ mahā śaraiḥ rukma puṅkhān prasanna agrān śarān saṃnata parvṇaḥ adarśayat ameya ātmā dikṣu sarvāsu pāṇḍavaḥ mahī viyant diśaḥ sarvāḥ samudrāḥ girayaḥ api vā sphuṭanti iti janāḥ jajñuḥ pārthasya tala nisvanāt hatvā daśa sahasrāṇi pārthivānām mahā rathaḥ saṃśaptakānām kaunteyaḥ prapakṣam tvaritaḥ abhyayāt prapakṣam sa samāsādya pārthaḥ kāmboja rakṣitam pramamātha balāt bāṇaiḥ dānavān iva vāsavaḥ praciccheda āśu bhallaiḥ ca dviṣatām ātatāyinām śastra pāṇīn tathā bāhūn tathā api ca śirāṃsi uta aṅga aṅga avayavaiḥ chinnaiḥ vyāyudhāḥ te apatan kṣitau viṣvak vāta abhisaṃbhagnāḥ bahu śākhāḥ iva drumāḥ kāmbojaḥ tu tatas kruddhaḥ dṛṣṭvā pārtham mahā ratham tatas tam rathinām śreṣṭham bahu dakṣiṇam āhave arjunasya ratham kṣipram prāpayām āsa sārathiḥ keśavam navabhiḥ rājan bāhvoḥ urasi cāparyat tatas kruddhaḥ mahā rāja pāṇḍavaḥ para vīra hā sudakṣiṇāt avarajaḥ śara vṛṣṭyā abhyavīvṛṣat pūrṇa candra ābha vaktram ca kṣureṇa abhyahanat śiraḥ manaḥśilā gireḥ śṛṅgam vajreṇa iva avadāritam sudakṣiṇāt avarajam kāmbojam dadṛśuḥ hatam prāṃśum kamala pattra akṣam atyartham priya darśanam kāñcana stambha saṃkāśam bhinnam hemagirim yathā nānā avasthāḥ ca yodhānām babhūvuḥ tatra yudhyatām eteṣu āvarjitaiḥ aśvaiḥ kāmbojaiḥ yavanaiḥ śakaiḥ śoṇita aktaiḥ tadā raktam sarvam āsīt viśām pate rathaiḥ ratha aśva sūtaiḥ ca hata ārohaiḥ ca vājibhiḥ arjunam jayatām śreṣṭham tvaritaḥ drauṇiḥ āyayau ādadānaḥ śarān ghorān sva raśmīn iva bhāskaraḥ krodha amarṣa vivṛtta āsyaḥ lohita akṣaḥ babhau balī antakāle yathā kruddhaḥ mṛtyuḥ kiṃkara daṇḍa bhṛt tatas prāsṛjat ugrāṇi śara varṣāṇi saṃghaśas taiḥ visṛṣṭaiḥ mahā rāja vyadravat pāṇḍavā camūḥ sa dṛṣṭvā eva tu dāśārham syandana stham viśām pate punar prāsṛjat ugrāṇi śara varṣāṇi māriṣa visiṣmāpayiṣoḥ lokam yaśaḥ ca uttamam icchatoḥ saṃśaptakān tu kaunteyaḥ kurūn ca api vṛkodaraḥ sūtaputraḥ tu pāñcālān bhūyas aghnan tvaritāḥ śaraiḥ evam eṣa mahā rāja vināśaḥ pṛthivīkṣitām āsīt kruddhe arjune karṇe bhīmasene ca dāruṇe yuddham ghoram tathā tu āsīt tridhā bhūte camū mukhe saṃchāditau ratha sthau tau ubhau kṛṣṇa dhanaṃjayau tatas śara śataiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavān niśceṣṭau tau ubhau cakre yuddhe mādhava pāṇḍavau hāhākṛtam abhūt sarvam jaṅgamam sthāvaram tathā carācarasya goptārau dṛṣṭvā saṃchāditau śaraiḥ siddha cāraṇa saṃghāḥ ca saṃpetuḥ vai samantataḥ na mayā tādṛśa rājan dṛś pūrvaḥ parākramaḥ saṃjajñe yādṛśaḥ drauṇeḥ kṛṣṇau saṃchādayiṣyataḥ drauṇeḥ tu dhanuṣaḥ śabdam ahita trāsanam raṇe aśrauṣam bahuśas rājan siṃhasya nadataḥ yathā sa tathā kṣiprakārī ca dṛḍha hastaḥ ca pāṇḍavaḥ saṃmoham paramam gatvā praikṣata droṇa jam tatas sa vikramam hṛtam mene ātmanaḥ su mahātmanā tathā asya samare rājan vapuḥ āsīt su durdṛśam drauṇi pāṇḍavayoḥ evam vartamāne mahā raṇe hī ca kaunteye kṛṣṇam roṣaḥ samabhyayāt sa roṣāt niḥśvasan rājan nirdahan iva cakṣuṣā drauṇim hi apaśyat saṃgrāme phalgunam ca muhur muhur tatas krudh abravīt kṛṣṇa pārtham sa praṇaya tadā kaccit vīryam yathāpūrvam bhujayoḥ vā balam tava kaccit te gāṇḍivam haste rathe tiṣṭhasi ca arjuna udīryamāṇam hi raṇe paśyāmi drauṇim āhave upekṣām kuru mā pārtha na ayam kālaḥ upekṣitum evam uktaḥ tu kṛṣṇena kṣiptvā bhallān caturdaśa dhvajam chatram patākām ca ratham śaktim gadām tathā jatru deśe ca su bhṛśam vatsadantaiḥ atāḍayat sa mūrcchām paramām gatvā dhvaja yaṣṭim samāśritaḥ tam visaṃjñam mahā rāja kirīṭi bhaya pīḍitam apovāha raṇāt sūtaḥ rakṣamāṇaḥ dhanaṃjayāt nyavadhīt tāvakam sainyam śataśas atha sahasraśas evam eṣa kṣayaḥ vṛttaḥ tāvakānām paraiḥ saha saṃśaptakān ca kaunteyaḥ kurūn ca api vṛkodaraḥ vasuṣeṇam ca pāñcālaḥ kṛtsnena vyadhamat raṇe yudhiṣṭhiraḥ api saṃgrāme prahāraiḥ gāḍha vedanaḥ saṃjayaḥ abravīt madra rājam ca tathā eva anyān mahā rathān yadṛcchayā upasaṃprāptam svarga dvāram apāvṛtam sukhinaḥ kṣatriyāḥ karṇa labhante yuddham īdṛśam sadṛśaiḥ kṣatriyaiḥ śūraiḥ śūrāṇām yudhyatām yudhi hatvā vā pāṇḍavān yuddhe sphītām urvīm avāpsyatha hṛṣṭāḥ nādān udakrośan vāditrāṇi ca sarvaśas harṣayan tāvakān yodhān drauṇiḥ vacanam abravīt pratyakṣam sarva sainyānām bhavatām ca api paśyatām nyasta śastraḥ mama pitā dhṛṣṭadyumnena pātitaḥ sa tena aham amarṣeṇa mitra arthe ca api pārthivāḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnam a hatvā aham na vimokṣyāmi daṃśanam anṛtāyām pratijñāyām na aham svargam avāpnuyām arjunaḥ bhīmasenaḥ ca yaḥ ca mām pratyudeṣyati sarvān tān pramathiṣye aham iti me na asti saṃśayaḥ evam ukte tatas sarvā sahitā bhāratī camūḥ abhyadravata kaunteyān tathā te ca api pāṇḍavāḥ sa saṃnipātaḥ ratha yūthapānām mahātmanām bhārata mohanīyaḥ jana kṣayaḥ kāla yuga anta kalpaḥ prāvartata agre kuru sṛñjayānām bhūtāni sarvāṇi sa daivatāni didṛkṣamāṇāni nara pravīrān avākiran apsarasaḥ prahṛṣṭāḥ samīraṇaḥ tān ca niṣevya gandhān niṣevyamāṇāḥ tu anilena yodhāḥ paraspara ghnāḥ dharaṇīm nipetuḥ sā divya puṣpaiḥ avakīryamāṇā suvarṇa puṅkhaiḥ ca śaraiḥ vicitraiḥ vāditra ghoṣaiḥ samudīryamāṇaḥ samākulaḥ saḥ abhavat saṃprahāraḥ duryodhanaḥ krodham amṛṣyamāṇaḥ abhyetya bhīmam balinam baliṣṭhaḥ samarpayat kṣudrakāṇām śatena duḥśāsanaḥ citrasenaḥ ca vīras gaja anīkaiḥ sarvatas bhīmasenam tam āpatantam saṃprekṣya gaja anīkam vṛkodaraḥ duryodhanam mahā bāhuḥ śara varṣaiḥ avākirat duryodhanam tathā bhīmaḥ sāyakaiḥ śataśas śitaiḥ pāṇḍavaḥ vimukhīkṛtya gajān abhyadravat balī tatas pāvaka saṃkāśaiḥ bhīmaḥ bāṇaiḥ avakra gaiḥ śalabhaiḥ iva nāgān tān ardayām āsa pāṇḍavaḥ tatas kuñjara yūthāni bhīmasenaḥ mahā balaḥ vyadhamat niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ mahā abhrāṇi iva mārutaḥ anvayuḥ tat ratha anīkam maṇi jālaiḥ ca kuñjarāḥ rūpya jāmbūnada ābhāsāḥ kṣura mālya abhyalaṃkṛtāḥ vadhyamānāḥ śaraiḥ rājan bhīmasenena te gajāḥ nipatadbhiḥ mahā vegaiḥ hema bhāṇḍa vibhūṣitaiḥ aśobhata mahā rāja dhātu citraiḥ iva acalaiḥ dīpta ābharaṇavadbhiḥ ca gaja pṛṣṭhāt nipātitaiḥ sa raṇaḥ śuśubhe rājan kṣīṇa puṇyaiḥ iva amaraiḥ mahā parigha saṃkāśau candana agaru rūṣitau śrutvā hi abhyadravan nāgāḥ bhīmasenam bhaya arditāḥ uvāca evam eṣa mahān āsīt saṃgrāmaḥ pṛthivīkṣitām droṇaputram parājitya jitvā ca anyān mahā rathān paśya kṛṣṇa mahā bāho dravantīm pāṇḍavīm camūm karṇam paśya ca saṃgrāme kālayantam mahā rathān na ca paśyāmi dāśārha dharmarājam yudhiṣṭhiram na api ketuḥ yudhām śreṣṭha dharmarājasya dṛśyate tri bhāgaḥ ca avaśiṣṭaḥ ayam divasasya janārdana na ca mām dhārtarāṣṭreṣu kaḥ cit yudhyati saṃyuge dṛṣṭvā kuśalinam yuddhe dharmaputram sahānujam punar yoddhāsmi vārṣṇeya śatrubhiḥ saha saṃyuge tatas prāyāt rathena āśu bībhatsoḥ vacanāt hariḥ yatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ rājā sṛñjayāḥ ca mahā rathāḥ ayudhyan tāvakaiḥ sārdham mṛtyum kṛtvā nivartanam uvāca tvaramāṇaḥ punar kṛṣṇaḥ pārtham abhyavadat śanais paśya kauravya rājānam apayātān ca pāṇḍavān karṇam paśya mahā raṅge jvalantam iva pāvakam asau bhīmaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ saṃnivṛttaḥ raṇam prati pāñcālānām sṛñjayānām pāṇḍavānām ca yat mukham tam eṣa pradrutaḥ saṃkhye dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ mahā rathaḥ anuprayāti saṃgrāme hatān paśya ca sṛñjayān sarvam vyācaṣṭa durdharṣaḥ vāsudevaḥ kirīṭine tatas rājan prādurāsīt mahā ghoraḥ mahā raṇaḥ siṃhanāda ravāḥ ca atra prādurāsan samāgame ubhayoḥ senayoḥ rājan mṛtyum kṛtvā nivartanam evam eṣa kṣayaḥ vṛttaḥ pṛthivyām pṛthivīpate tāvakānām pareṣām ca rājan durmantrite te uvāca tatas punar samājagmuḥ abhītāḥ kuru sṛñjayāḥ yudhiṣṭhira mukhāḥ pārthāḥ vaikartana mukhāḥ vayam tatas pravavṛte bhīmaḥ saṃgrāmaḥ loma harṣaṇaḥ karṇasya pāṇḍavānām ca yama rāṣṭra vivardhanaḥ saṃśaptakeṣu śūreṣu kiṃcid śiṣṭeṣu bhārata dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ mahā rāja sahitaḥ sarva rājbhiḥ karṇam eva abhidudrāva pāṇḍavāḥ ca mahā rathāḥ āgacchamānān tān saṃkhye prahṛṣṭān vijaya eṣiṇaḥ tam āsādya tu te karṇam vyaśīryanta mahā rathāḥ yathā acalam samāsādya jala oghāḥ sarvatodiśam tayoḥ āsīt mahā rāja saṃgrāmaḥ loma harṣaṇaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ tu rādheyam śareṇa nata parvaṇā tāḍayām āsa saṃkruddhaḥ tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt vijayam tu dhanuḥ śreṣṭham vidhunvānaḥ mahā rathaḥ vavarṣa śara varṣāṇi toya varṣān iva ambudaḥ pārṣatasya dhanuḥ chittvā śarān āśīviṣa upamān tāḍayām āsa saṃkruddhaḥ pārṣatam navabhiḥ śaraiḥ śoṇita aktāḥ vyarājanta śakragopāḥ iva anagha tat apāsya dhanuḥ chinnam dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ mahā rathaḥ anyat dhanuḥ upādāya śarān ca āśīviṣa upamān karṇam vivyādha saptatyā śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ tathā eva rājan karṇaḥ api pārṣatam śatru tāpanam chādayām āsa samare śaraiḥ āśīviṣa upamaiḥ droṇa śatrum mahā iṣvāsaḥ vivyādha niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ tasya karṇaḥ mahā rāja śaram kanaka bhūṣaṇam preṣayām āsa saṃkruddhaḥ mṛtyu daṇḍam iva aparam tam āpatantam sahasā ghora rūpam viśām pate dṛṣṭvā vinihitam bāṇam śaraiḥ karṇaḥ viśām pate sātyakim śara varṣeṇa samantāt paryavārayat tatas yuddham atīva āsīt cakṣuḥ śrotra bhaya āvaham rājan ghoram ca citram ca prekṣaṇīyam samantataḥ sarveṣām tatra bhūtānām lomaharṣaḥ vyajāyata tat dṛṣṭvā samare karma karṇa śaineyayoḥ nṛpa pārṣatam śatru damanam śatru vīrya asu nāśanam sa dṛṣṭvā samare karṇam pārṣatam ca mahā ratham ratham rathena saṃpīḍya śatru vīrya praṇāśanaḥ tiṣṭha tiṣṭha adya brahma ghna na me jīvan vimokṣyase iti uktvā su bhṛśam vīraḥ śīghra kṛt niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ pārṣatam chādayām āsa ghora rūpaiḥ su tejanaiḥ yatamānam param śaktyā yatamānaḥ mahā rathaḥ chādayām āsa samare yatamānaḥ mahā rathaḥ yatnatas parayā śaktyā dhṛṣṭadyumnam mahā raṇe yodhayām āsa samare kruddha rūpaḥ viśām pate yathā hi samare drauṇiḥ pārṣatam vīkṣ māriṣa tathā drauṇim raṇe dṛṣṭvā pārṣataḥ para vīra hā na ati hṛṣṭa manāḥ bhūtvā manyate mṛtyum ātmanaḥ sa jñātvā samare ātmānam śastreṇa avadhyam eva tu javena abhiyayau drauṇim kālaḥ kālam iva kṣaye drauṇiḥ tu dṛṣṭvā rāja indra dhṛṣṭadyumnam raṇe sthitam krodhena niḥśvasan vīraḥ pārṣatam samupādravat tau anyonyam tu dṛṣṭvā eva saṃrambham jagmatuḥ param tatas roṣa parīta ātmā dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ api amarṣaṇaḥ provāca ca enam saṃrabdhaḥ droṇaputram paraṃtapaḥ pragṛhya mahatī cāpe śarāsana virājite atha abravīt mahā rāja droṇaputraḥ pratāpavān dhṛṣṭadyumnam samīpa stham tvaramāṇaḥ viśām pate pāñcāla apasada adya tvām preṣayiṣyāmi mṛtyave pāpam hi yat tvayā karma ghnatā droṇam purā kṛtam śaśi smaraṇa tanmātrān vaṃśān kṛtam apohyate mayā mārayitavyaḥ tvam paśumāreṇa pārṣata arakṣyamāṇaḥ pārthena yadi tiṣṭhasi saṃyuge evam uktaḥ pratyuvāca dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ pratāpavān eṣa te prativākyam vai asiḥ dāsyati māmakaḥ yadi tāvat mayā droṇaḥ nihataḥ brāhmaṇabruvaḥ tvām idānīm katham yuddhe na haniṣyāmi vikramāt evam uktvā mahā rāja senāpatiḥ amarṣaṇaḥ niśitena atha bāṇena drauṇim vivyādha pārṣataḥ tatas drauṇiḥ su saṃkruddhaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ prācchādayat diśaḥ rājan dhṛṣṭadyumnasya saṃyuge na eva antarikṣam na diśaḥ na eva yodhāḥ samantataḥ dṛśyante vai mahā rāja śaraiḥ channāḥ sahasraśas śaraiḥ saṃchādayām āsa sūtaputrasya paśyataḥ rādheyaḥ api mahā rāja pāñcālān saha pāṇḍavaiḥ ekaḥ sa vārayām āsa prekṣaṇīyaḥ samantataḥ sātyakim ca mahā rāja yodhān ca anyān sahasraśas kṣurapreṇa su tīkṣṇena paśyatām sarva yodhinām vegavat samare ghoram śarān ca āśīviṣa upamān sa pārṣatasya rāja indra dhanuḥ śaktim gadām dhvajam sa śaktim prāhiṇot tasmai tām drauṇiḥ vyadhamat śaraiḥ tām nikṛttām raṇe dṛṣṭvā drauṇinā pārṣataḥ balī parigham ghoram ādāya kārtasvara vibhūṣitam cikṣepa bhuja vīryeṇa pārṣataḥ vai purā nadan hayān sūtam ratham ca eva nimeṣāt vyadhamat śaraiḥ pārṣatasya tatas kruddhaḥ droṇaputraḥ paraṃtapaḥ ciccheda samare vīraḥ kṣipra hastaḥ dṛḍha āyudhaḥ dhanvinaḥ bāhu śālinaḥ paśyatām sarva sainyānām dhṛṣṭadyumnam tu viratham hata aśvam chinna kārmukam śaraiḥ ca bahudhā viddham astraiḥ ca śakalīkṛtam na atarat bharata śreṣṭha yatamānaḥ mahā rathaḥ tasya antam iṣubhiḥ rājan yadā drauṇiḥ na jagmivān atha tyaktvā dhanuḥ vīraḥ pārṣatam tvaritaḥ anvagāt pragṛhya vipulam khaḍgam jātarūpa pariṣkṛtam āsīt ādravataḥ rājan vegaḥ tasya mahātmanaḥ paśya pārtha yathā drauṇiḥ pārṣatasya vadham prati abravīt bharata śreṣṭham arjunam jayatām varam paśya drauṇim pārṣatasya yatamānam vadham prati tam mocaya mahā bāho pārṣatam śatru tāpanam drauṇeḥ āsyam anuprāptam mṛtyoḥ āsya gatam yathā evam uktvā mahā rāja vāsudevaḥ pratāpavān te hayāḥ candra saṃkāśāḥ keśavena pracoditāḥ dṛṣṭvā āyāntau mahā vīryau ubhau kṛṣṇa dhanaṃjayau dhṛṣṭadyumna vadhe rājñ cakre yatnam mahā balaḥ vikṛṣyamāṇam dṛṣṭvā eva dhṛṣṭadyumnam janeśvara śarān cikṣepa vai pārthaḥ drauṇim prati mahā balaḥ te śarāḥ hema vikṛtāḥ gāṇḍīva preṣitāḥ bhṛśam drauṇim āsādya viviśuḥ valmīkam iva pannagāḥ ratham āruruhe vīraḥ dhanaṃjaya śara arditaḥ pragṛhya ca dhanuḥ śreṣṭham pārtham vivyādha sāyakaiḥ apovāha rathena ājau pārṣatam śatru tāpanam krodhitaḥ tu raṇe pārthaḥ nārācam kāla saṃmitam droṇaputrāya cikṣepa kāla daṇḍam iva aparam sa brāhmaṇasya aṃsa deśe nipapāta mahā dyutiḥ tatas karṇaḥ mahā rāja vyākṣipat vijayam dhanuḥ dvairatham ca api pārthena kāmayānaḥ mahā raṇe tam tu hitvā hatam vīram sārathiḥ śatru karśanam apovāha rathena ājau tvaramāṇaḥ raṇa ajirāt atha utkruṣṭam mahā rāja pāñcālaiḥ jita kāśibhiḥ mokṣitam pārṣatam dṛṣṭvā droṇaputram ca pīḍitam vāditrāṇi ca divyāni prāvādyanta sahasraśas siṃhanādaḥ ca saṃjajñe dṛṣṭvā ghoram mahā adbhutam evam kṛtvā bravīt pārthaḥ vāsudevam dhanaṃjayaḥ yāhi saṃśaptakān kṛṣṇa kāryam etat param mama tatas prayātaḥ dāśārhaḥ śrutvā pāṇḍava bhāṣitam uvāca teṣām pravṛtte saṃgrāme vipule śoṇita udake rarāja lohitena urvī saṃraktā bahudhā bhṛśam tadā vilokya pārtham ca kṛṣṇaḥ vacanam abravīt etasmin antare kṛṣṇaḥ pārtham vacanam abravīt eṣa pāṇḍava te bhrātā dhārtarāṣṭraiḥ mahā balaiḥ jighāṃsubhiḥ mahā iṣvāsaiḥ drutam pārtha anusaryate tathā anuyānti saṃrabdhāḥ pāñcālāḥ yuddha durmadāḥ yudhiṣṭhiram mahātmānam parīpsantaḥ mahā javāḥ eṣa duryodhanaḥ pārtha ratha anīkena daṃśitaḥ jighāṃsuḥ puruṣa vyāghram bhrātṛbhiḥ sahitaḥ balī āśīviṣa sama sparśaiḥ sarva yuddha viśāradaiḥ ete jighṛkṣavaḥ yānti dvipa aśva ratha pattayaḥ yudhiṣṭhiram dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ ratna uttamam iva arthinaḥ paśya sātvata bhīmābhyām niruddha adhiṣṭhitaḥ prabhuḥ jihīrṣavaḥ amṛtam daityāḥ śakra agnibhyām iva avaśāḥ samudram iva vāri oghāḥ prāvṛṣ kāle mahā rathāḥ nadantaḥ siṃhanādān ca dhamantaḥ ca api vārijān balavantaḥ mahā iṣvāsāḥ vidhunvantaḥ dhanūṃṣi ca yathā yuktam anīkam hi dhārtarāṣṭrasya pāṇḍava na asya śakraḥ api mucyeta saṃprāptaḥ bāṇa gocaram duryodhanasya śūrasya śara oghān śīghram asyataḥ karṇena ca kṛtaḥ rājā vimukhaḥ śatru tāpanaḥ balavān laghu hastaḥ ca kṛtī yuddha viśāradaḥ rādheyaḥ pāṇḍava śreṣṭham śaktaḥ pīḍayitum raṇe sahitaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭrasya putraiḥ śūraḥ mahātmabhiḥ tasya evam yudhyamānasya saṃgrāme saṃyata ātmanaḥ upavāsa kṛśaḥ rājā bhṛśam bharata sattama sute kṛtam rāṣṭram jīvitam śatru tāpanaḥ nitya anaśana saṃgrāme samāpta vrata niścayaḥ yaḥ vatsa udayikam śrāddhe viśeṣeṇa mahībhujā karṇena ca abhiyuktaḥ ayam bhūpatiḥ śatru tāpanaḥ saṃśayam samanuprāptaḥ pāṇḍavaḥ vai yudhiṣṭhiraḥ na jīvati mahā rājaḥ manye pārtha yudhiṣṭhiraḥ yat bhīmasenaḥ sahate siṃhanādam amarṣaṇaḥ nardatām dhārtarāṣṭrāṇām punar punar ariṃdama dhamatām ca mahā śaṅkhān saṃgrāme jita kāśinām yudhiṣṭhiram pāṇḍaveyam hata iti bharata ṛṣabha saṃcodayati asau karṇaḥ dhārtarāṣṭrān mahā balān astraiḥ nānāvidhaiḥ citraiḥ kauravāḥ pārtha saṃyuge sthūṇākarṇa indrajālena pārtha pāśupatena ca pracchādayantaḥ rājānam anuyānti mahā rathāḥ āturaḥ mama mataḥ rājā saṃniṣevyaḥ ca bhārata yathā enam anuvartante pāñcālāḥ saha pāṇḍavaiḥ tvaramāṇāḥ tvarā kāle sarva śastrabhṛtām varāḥ na ketuḥ dṛśyate rājñaḥ karṇena nihataḥ śaraiḥ paśyatoḥ yamayoḥ pārtha sātyakeḥ ca śikhaṇḍinaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnasya bhīmasya śatānīkasya vā vibho pāñcālānām ca sarveṣām cedīnām ca eva bhārata eṣa karṇaḥ raṇe pārtha pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm ete dravanti rathinaḥ tvadīyāḥ pāṇḍu nandana drāvyamāṇāḥ raṇe pārtha karṇena amita tejasā paśya paśya yathā pārtha gacchanti ete mahā rathāḥ ete bhārata mātaṅgāḥ karṇena abhihatāḥ raṇe ārta nādān vikurvāṇāḥ vidravanti diśaḥ daśa rathānām dravatām vṛndam paśya pārtha samantataḥ drāvyamāṇam raṇe ca eva karṇena amitra karśiṇā hasti kakṣyām raṇe paśya caratīm tatra tatra ha kiran śara śatāni iva vinighnan te vāhinīm etān paśya ca pāñcālān drāvyamāṇān mahātmanā śakreṇa iva yathā daityān hanyamānān mahā āhave eṣa karṇaḥ raṇe jitvā pāñcālān pāṇḍu sṛñjayān paśya pārtha dhanuḥ śreṣṭham vikarṣan sādhu śobhate śatrūn jitvā yathā śakraḥ deva saṃghaiḥ samāvṛtaḥ trāsayantaḥ raṇe pārthān sṛñjayān ca sahasraśas eṣa sarva ātmanā pāṇḍūn trāsayitvā mahā raṇe trāsayitvā raṇe pārthaiḥ rādheyaḥ rathinām varaḥ abhibhāṣati rādheyaḥ sarva sainyāni mānadaḥ yathā jīvan na vaḥ kaḥ cit mucyate yudhi sṛñjayaḥ tathā kuruta saṃyattāḥ vayam yāsyāma pṛṣṭhatas evam uktvā yayau eṣa pṛṣṭhatas vikiran śaraiḥ rādheyaḥ kauravām senām rakṣamāṇaḥ samantataḥ paśya karṇam raṇe pārtha śveta chavi virājitam pūrṇa candra nikāśena mūrdhani chatreṇa bhārata dhriyamāṇena samare tathā śata śalākinā eṣa tvām prekṣate karṇaḥ sa kaṭākṣaḥ viśām pate paśya hi enam mahā bāho vidhunvānam mahat dhanuḥ śarān ca āśīviṣa ākārān visṛjantam mahā balam eṣa hi amarṣī śūraḥ ca dhārtarāṣṭra hite rataḥ ekākinam ca dṛṣṭvā enam dhārtarāṣṭraḥ raṇa ajire tvām ca pārtha abhisaṃrabdham karṇam prati mahā ratham karṇam ekākinam dṛṣṭvā ratha anīkena bhārata rirakṣiṣuḥ su saṃyattaḥ dhārtarāṣṭraḥ abhivartate sārvaiḥ saha ebhiḥ duṣṭa ātmā vadhyaḥ eṣa prayatnāt tvām ca dṛṣṭvā ati saṃrabdham karṇam ca bharata ṛṣabha tvayā yaśaḥ ca rājyam ca sukham ca uttamam icchatā ātmānam ca kṛtātmānam samīkṣya bharata ṛṣabha kṛta āgasam ca rādheyam dharma ātmani yudhiṣṭhire sahitaḥ sa tu duṣṭa ātmā dhārtarāṣṭraḥ abhyavartate mūle chinne yathā nāśaḥ śākhānām jāyate dhruvam dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ mahā bāho sa bhṛtya amātya bāndhavāḥ bhīmaḥ api śeṣa tāmra akṣaḥ hanti śatrūn aśeṣatas eṣa dharmasutaḥ rājā yamābhyām paripālitaḥ kṛtavarmā kṛpaḥ drauṇiḥ rakṣantaḥ anyonyam uttamāḥ kulūkaḥ śakuniḥ ca eva kṛtvā rakṣām sthitau ubhau āryām yuddhe matim kṛtvā pratyehi ratha yūthapam pañca hi etāni mukhyānām rathānām ratha sattama śatāni āyānti vegena balinām bhīma tejasām pañca nāga sahasrāṇi dviguṇāḥ vājinaḥ tathā droṇaputram puraskṛtya tatas śīghram ca sūdaya sūtaputre mahā iṣvāse darśaya ātmānam ātmanā bhūtāni ca eva sarvāṇi kuru pāñcāla sṛñjayāḥ asau karṇaḥ su saṃrabdhaḥ pāñcālān abhidhāvati asau bhimaḥ mahā bāhuḥ saṃnivṛttaḥ camū mukhe vṛtaḥ sṛñjaya sainyena sātyakena ca bhārata bhīmasenena kaunteya pāñcālaiḥ ca mahātmabhiḥ senā hi dhārtarāṣṭrasya vimukhā ca bhavat raṇāt bhāratī bharata śreṣṭha senā kṛpaṇa darśanā nivṛttam paśya kaunteya bhīmasenam yudhām patim āśīviṣam iva kruddham tasmāt dravati vāhinī pīta rakta asita sitāḥ tārā candra arka maṇḍitāḥ patākāḥ viprakīryante chatrāṇi etāni ca arjuna sauvarṇāḥ rājatāḥ ca eva taijasāḥ ca pṛthagvidhāḥ nānā varṇaiḥ hatāḥ bāṇaiḥ pāñcālaiḥ apalāyibhiḥ nirmanuṣyān gajān aśvān rathān ca eva dhanaṃjaya samādravanti pāñcālāḥ dhārtarāṣṭrān tarasvinaḥ mṛdnanti ca nara vyāghrāḥ bhīmasena vyapāśrayāt balam pareṣām durdharṣam tyaktvā prāṇān ariṃdama ete nadanti pāñcālāḥ dhamanti api ca vārijān paśya svargasya māhātmyam pāñcālāḥ hi paraṃtapa dhārtarāṣṭrān vinighnanti kruddhāḥ siṃhāḥ iva dvipān śastram ācchidya śatrūṇām sa āyudhānām nirāyudhāḥ śirāṃsi etāni pātyante śatrūṇām bāhavaḥ api ca ratha nāga hayāḥ vīrāḥ yaśasyāḥ sarve eva ca sarvatas ca abhipannā eṣā dhārtarāṣṭrī mahā camūḥ pāñcālaiḥ māgadhaiḥ ca eva yodhāḥ nītāḥ yama kṣayam tyaktvā prāṇān mahā iṣvāsaiḥ pāñcālaiḥ paripātyate pāñcālaiḥ mānasāt etya haṃsaiḥ gaṅgā iva vegitaiḥ su bhṛśam ca parākrāntāḥ pāñcālānām nivāraṇe kṛpa karṇa ādayaḥ vīrāḥ ṛṣabhāṇām iva ṛṣabhāḥ suhṛdaḥ ca parākrāntāḥ kṛpa karṇa ādayaḥ vibho nivāraṇe mahā iṣvāsāḥ pāñcālānām paraṃtapa su nimagnān ca bhīma astraiḥ dhārtarāṣṭrān mahā rathān dhṛṣṭadyumna mukhāḥ vīrāḥ ghnanti śatrūn sahasraśas pāñcāleṣu abhibhūteṣu dviṣadbhiḥ apabhīḥ nadan śatru pakṣam avaskandya śarān asyati mārutiḥ viṣaṇṇa bhūyiṣṭha rathā dhārtarāṣṭrī mahā camūḥ rathāḥ ca ete su vitrastāḥ bhīmasena bhaya arditāḥ paśya bhīmena nārācaiḥ chinnāḥ nāgāḥ patanti amī nānā nāgāḥ hatāḥ bāṇaiḥ bhīmena prapatanti amī vajri vajra āhatāni iva śikharāṇi mahībhṛtām bhīmasenena mātaṃgāḥ prāpitāḥ yama sādanam girīṇām śikharāṇi iva nipatanti nara ṛṣabha bhīmasenasya nirviddhāḥ bāṇaiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ svāni anīkāni mṛdnantaḥ dravanti ete mahā gajāḥ tyaktvā rathān gajān ca eva hayān ca eva sahasraśas dravatām nisvanam śṛṇu bhīmasenasya ninadam drāvayāṇasya kauravān na abhijānāsi bhīmasya siṃhanādam durutsaham nadataḥ arjuna saṃgrāme vīrasya jita kāśinaḥ eṣa naiṣādaḥ abhyeti dvipa mukhyena pāṇḍavam jighāṃsuḥ tomaraiḥ kruddhaḥ daṇḍa pāṇiḥ iva antakaḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ agni śikhā prakhyaiḥ nārācaiḥ daśabhiḥ hataḥ hatvā enam punar āyāti nāgān anyān prahāriṇaḥ paśya nīla ambuda nibhān mahāmātraiḥ adhiṣṭhitān sapta sapta ca nāgān tān vaijayantīḥ ca sa dhvajāḥ nihatya niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ chinnāḥ pārtha agrajena te na ca asau dhārtarāṣṭrāṇām śrūyate ninadaḥ tathā akṣauhiṇyaḥ tathā tisraḥ dhārtarāṣṭrasya saṃhatāḥ na śaknuvanti vai pārtham pārthivāḥ samudīkṣitum madhyaṃdina gatam sūryam yathā durbala cakṣuṣaḥ ete bhīmasya saṃtrastāḥ siṃhasya iva itare mṛgāḥ śaraiḥ saṃtrāsitāḥ saṃkhye na labhante sukham kva cit rājānam ca mahā bāhum pīḍayanti ātta manyavaḥ varjayitvā tu bhīrum tam pārśvatas hi ānayat dhanuḥ tam pālayan mahā rājam dhārtarāṣṭraḥ bala anvitaḥ uvāca etat śrutvā mahā bāhuḥ vāsudevāt dhanaṃjayaḥ bhīmasenena tat karma kṛtam dṛṣṭvā su duṣkaram arjunaḥ vyadhamat śiṣṭān ahitān niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ te vadhyamānāḥ samare saṃśaptaka gaṇāḥ prabho prabhagnāḥ samare bhītāḥ diśaḥ daśa mahā balāḥ śakrasya atithi tām gatvā viśokāḥ hi abhavan mudā śakrasya atithi tām prāptāḥ samapadyanta vijvarāḥ viśokāḥ samapadyanta śakrasya antika tām gatāḥ nārāyaṇān tu gopālān vyadhamat pāṇḍu nandanaḥ uttamam vegam āsthāya caṇḍa vāyuḥ ghanān iva lulitān ca tatas śūrān ahanat puruṣottamaḥ pārthaḥ ca puruṣa vyāghraḥ śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ jaghāna dhārtarāṣṭrasya caturvidha balām camūm uvāca nivṛtte bhīmasene ca pāṇḍave ca yudhiṣṭhire vadhyamāne bale ca api māmake pāṇḍu sṛñjayaiḥ avaśeṣam na paśyāmi mama sainyeṣu saṃjaya aho bata daśām prāptaḥ na hi śakṣyāmi jīvitum jaya kāṅkṣī katham sūta putrāṇām anivartinām katham jīvāmi nihatān śrutvā ca mama sainikān bahunā adya kim uktena daivam teṣām parāyaṇam uvāca kṣayaḥ teṣām mahān jātaḥ rājan durmantrite tava dṛṣṭvā bhīmam mahā bāhum sūtaputraḥ pratāpavān tiṣṭha tiṣṭha pṛthā putra paśya mama adya parākramam adya tvām preṣayiṣyāmi yamasya sadanam prati tāvakam ca balam dṛṣṭvā bhīmasenāt parāṅmukham pratyudyayau tadā karṇaḥ pāṇḍavān yuddha durmadān pratyudyayuḥ tu rādheyam pāṇḍavānām mahā rathāḥ dhunvānāḥ kārmukāṇi ājau vikṣipantaḥ ca sāyakān bhīmasenaḥ śineḥ naptā śikhaṇḍī janamejayaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ ca balavān sarve ca api prabhadrakāḥ pāñcālāḥ ca nara vyāghrāḥ samantāt te vāhinīm tathā eva tāvakāḥ rājan pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm śikhaṇḍī ca yayau karṇam dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ sutam te duḥśāsanam mahā rāja mahatyā senayā vṛtam nakulaḥ vṛṣasenam ca citrasenam yudhiṣṭhiraḥ sātyakiḥ śakunim ca api bhīmasenaḥ ca kauravān arjunam ca raṇe yattam droṇaputraḥ mahā rathaḥ kṛtavarmā mahā iṣvāsaḥ paryavārayat āhave bhīmasenaḥ kurūn sarvān putrān ca te māriṣa saha anīkān mahā bāhuḥ ekaḥ eva abhyavārayat śikhaṇḍī ca tatas karṇam vicarantam abhīta vat bhīṣma hantā mahā rāja vārayām āsa pattribhiḥ śikhaṇḍinam tribhiḥ bāṇaiḥ bhruvoḥ madhye vyatāḍayat dhārayan tu sa tān bāṇān śikhaṇḍī bahu aśobhata rājataḥ parvataḥ yadvat tribhiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ samanvitaḥ saḥ atividdhaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ sūtaputreṇa saṃyuge karṇam vivyādha samare navatyā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ tasya karṇaḥ hayān hatvā sārathim ca tribhiḥ śaraiḥ unmamātha dhvajam ca asya kṣurapreṇa mahā rathaḥ hata aśvāt tu tatas yānāt avaplutya mahā rathaḥ saṃchinna kārmukaḥ rājan sūtaputreṇa saṃyuge śaktim cikṣepa karṇāya saṃkruddhaḥ śatru tāpanaḥ tām chittvā samare karṇaḥ tribhiḥ bhārata sāyakaiḥ śikhaṇḍinam atha avidhyat navabhiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ karṇa cāpa cyutān bāṇān varjayan tu nara uttamaḥ apayātaḥ tatas tūrṇam śikhaṇḍī jayatām varaḥ tatas karṇaḥ mahā rāja pāṇḍu sainyāni aśātayat tūla rāśim samāsādya yathā vāyuḥ mahā javaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ mahā rāja te putreṇa pīḍitaḥ duḥśāsanam tribhiḥ bāṇaiḥ abhyavidhyat stanāntare tasya duḥśāsanaḥ bāhum savyam vivyādha māriṣa dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ tu nirviddhaḥ śaram ghoram amarṣaṇaḥ duḥśāsanāya saṃkruddhaḥ preṣayām āsa bhārata āśīviṣa samam bāṇam āśu māruta raṃhasam āpatantam mahā vegam dhṛṣṭadyumna samīritam atha aparaiḥ saptadaśaiḥ bhallaiḥ kanaka bhūṣaṇaiḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnam samāsādya bāhuvoḥ urasi ca ārdayat tatas sa pārṣataḥ kruddhaḥ dhanuḥ ciccheda māriṣa kṣurapreṇa su tīkṣṇena tatas uccukruśuḥ janāḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnam śara vrātaiḥ samantāt paryavārayat tava putrasya te dṛṣṭvā vikramam tam mahātmanaḥ vyahasanta raṇe yodhāḥ siddhāḥ ca apsarasām gaṇāḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnam na paśyāma ghaṭamānam mahā balam duḥśāsanena saṃruddham siṃhena iva mahā gajam tatas sa ratha nāga aśvāḥ pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍu pūrvaja tatas pravavṛte yuddham tāvakānām paraiḥ saha ghoram prāṇabhṛtām kāle ghora rūpam paraṃtapa nakulam vṛṣasenaḥ tu viddhvā pañcabhiḥ āyasaiḥ nārācena su tīkṣṇena vivyādha hṛdaye dṛḍham saḥ atividdhaḥ balavatā śatruṇā śatru karśanaḥ śatrum vivyādha viṃśatyā sa ca tam pañcabhiḥ śaraiḥ tatas śara sahasreṇa tau ubhau puruṣa ṛṣabhau anyonyam ācchādayatām atha abhajyata vāhinī dṛṣṭvā tu pradrutām senām dhārtarāṣṭrasya sūtajaḥ nivārayām āsa balāt anupatya viśām pate etasmin antare kaṣṭam yuddham āsīt viśām pate vṛṣasenaḥ tu pāñcālān pitrā sārdham viśām pate nivāritaḥ śara śataiḥ kruddhena raṇa mūrdhani tasya aśvān caturaḥ hatvā sahadevaḥ pratāpavān sārathim preṣayām āsa yamasya sadanam prati ulūkaḥ tu tatas yānāt avaplutya viśām pate apayātaḥ tatas tūrṇam ulūkaḥ raṇa mūrdhani trigartānām balam pūrṇam jagāma pitṛ nandanaḥ sātyakiḥ śakunim viddhvā viṃśatyā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ sārathim preṣayām āsa yamasya
