prājñāyata kim cana rādheya cāpa nirmuktaiḥ śaraiḥ kāñcana bhūṣitaiḥ saṃchāditāḥ mahā rāja yatamānāḥ mahā rathāḥ te pāṇḍaveyāḥ samare karṇena sma punar punar abhajyanta mahā rāja yatamānāḥ mahā rathāḥ mṛga saṃghān yathā kruddhaḥ siṃhaḥ drāvayate vane pāñcālānām ratha śreṣṭhān drāvayan śātravān tathā karṇaḥ tu samare yodhān tatra tatra mahā yaśāḥ kālayām āsa tat sainyam yathā paśu gaṇān vṛkaḥ dṛṣṭvā tu pāṇḍavīm senām dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ parāṅmukhīm vādayām āsa saṃhṛṣṭaḥ nānā vādyāni sarvaśas pāñcāla api mahā iṣvāsāḥ bhagnāḥ bhagnāḥ nara uttamāḥ nyavartanta yathā śūrāḥ mṛtyum kṛtvā nivartanam tān nivṛttān raṇe śūrān rādheyaḥ śatru tāpanaḥ anekaśas mahā rāja babhañja puruṣa ṛṣabhaḥ tatra bhārata karṇena pāñcālāḥ viṃśatiḥ rathāḥ nihatāḥ sādayaḥ krodhāt cedayaḥ ca paraḥśatāḥ kṛtvā śūnyān rathopasthān vāji pṛṣṭhān ca bhārata nirmanuṣyān gaja skandhān pādātān ca eva vidrutān ādityaḥ iva madhyāhne durnirīkṣyaḥ paraṃtapaḥ kāla antaka vapūḥ krūraḥ sūtaputraḥ cacāra ha hatvā tasthau mahā iṣvāsaḥ karṇaḥ ari gaṇa sūdanaḥ yathā bhūta gaṇān hatvā kālaḥ tiṣṭhet mahā balaḥ tathā sa somakān hatvā tasthau ekaḥ mahā rathaḥ tatra adbhutam apaśyāma pāñcālānām parākramam vadhyamānā api karṇena na ajahuḥ raṇa mūrdhani rājā duḥśāsanaḥ ca eva kṛpaḥ śāradvataḥ tathā aśvatthāmā kṛtavarmā śakuniḥ ca api saubalaḥ nyahanan pāṇḍavām senām śataśas atha sahasraśas anāśayetām balinaḥ pāñcālān vai tatas tatas tatra yuddham tadā hi āsīt krūram viśasanam mahat tathā eva pāṇḍavāḥ śūrāḥ dhṛṣṭadyumna śikhaṇḍinau evam eṣa kṣayaḥ vṛttaḥ pāṇḍavānām tatas tatas tāvakānām api raṇe bhīmam prāpya mahā balam uvāca sūtaputram su saṃrabdham dṛṣṭvā ca eva mahā raṇe hatvā tu phalgunaḥ sainyam kauravāṇām pṛthak pṛthak sūtaputrasya saṃrambham dṛṣṭvā ca api mahā āhave śoṇita udām mahīm kṛtvā māṃsa majja asthi vāhinīm manuṣya śīrṣa pāṣāṇām hasti aśva kṛta rodhasam śūra asthi caya saṃkīrṇām kāka gṛdhra anunāditām chatra haṃsa plava upetām vīra vṛkṣa apahāriṇīm hāra padma ākaravatīm uṣṇīṣa vara phenilām dhanuḥ śara dhvaja upetām nara kṣudra kapālinīm jaya eṣiṇām ca sutarām bhīrūṇām ca su dustarām tām nadīm prāpayitvā tu bībhatsuḥ para vīra hā vāsudevam idam vākyam abravīt puruṣa ṛṣabha eṣa ketuḥ raṇe kṛṣṇa sūtaputrasya dṛśyate ete dravanti pāñcālāḥ karṇāt trastāḥ janārdana eṣa duryodhanaḥ rājā śveta chatreṇa bhāsvatā karṇena bhagnān pāñcālān drāvayan bahu śobhate kṛpaḥ ca kṛtavarmā ca drauṇiḥ ca eva mahā balaḥ ete rakṣanti rājānam sūtaputreṇa rakṣitāḥ eṣa śalyaḥ rathopasthe raśmi saṃcāra kovidaḥ sūtaputra ratham kṛṣṇa vāhayan bahu śobhate na a hatvā samare karṇam nivartiṣye katham cana rādheyaḥ api anyathā pārthān sṛñjayān ca mahā rathān niḥśeṣān samare kuryāt paśyatoḥ āvayoḥ janārdana evam uktaḥ tu pārthena kṛṣṇaḥ rājñ tvarā anvitaḥ tatas prāyāt rathena āśu keśavaḥ te vāhinīm karṇam prati mahā iṣvāsam dvairathe savyasācinā prayātaḥ ca mahā bāhuḥ pāṇḍava anujñayā hariḥ sa prayātaḥ rathena āśu kṛṣṇaḥ rājñ mahā āhave āśvāsayan rathena eva pāṇḍu sainyāni sarvaśas ratha ghoṣaḥ sa saṃgrāme pāṇḍaveyasya saṃbabhau vāsava astra nipātena parvateṣu iva māriṣa mahatā ratha ghoṣeṇa pāṇḍavaḥ satya vikramaḥ tam āyāntam samīkṣya eva śvetāśvam kṛṣṇasārathim madra rājaḥ abravīt karṇam ketum dṛṣṭvā mahātmanaḥ ayam sa rathaḥ āyāti śveta aśvaḥ kṛṣṇa sārathiḥ eṣa tiṣṭhati kaunteyaḥ saṃspṛśan gāṇḍivam dhanuḥ ghṛṇām tyaktvā prasādam ca bhṛgoḥ astram ca saṃsmaran dṛṣṭim muṣṭim ca saṃdhānam smṛtvā rāma upadeśa jam na mām vijeṣyate karṇa gadā yuddhe viśeṣataḥ dhanuḥ jyā candra tārā arka patākā kiṅkiṇī yutā paśya karṇa arjunasya eṣā saudāminī ambare yathā eṣa dhvaja agre pārthasya prekṣamāṇaḥ samantataḥ dṛśyate vānaraḥ bhīmaḥ vīkṣatām bhaya vardhanaḥ etat cakram gadā śaṅkhaḥ śārṅgam kṛṣṇasya ca prabho dṛśyate pāṇḍava rathe vāha yānasya vājinaḥ etat kūjati gāṇḍīvam vikṛṣṭam savyasācinā ete hastavatā muktāḥ ghnanti amitrān śitāḥ śarāḥ viśāla āyata tāmra akṣaiḥ pūrṇa candra nibha ānanaiḥ eṣā bhūḥ kīryate rājñām śirobhiḥ apalāyinām ete parigha saṃkāśāḥ puṇya gandha anulepanāḥ udyatāḥ raṇa śauṇḍānām pātyante sa āyudhāḥ bhujāḥ nirasta jihvā netra antāḥ vājinaḥ sahasā ādibhiḥ patitāḥ pātyamānāḥ ca kṣitau kṣīṇāḥ viśerate ete parvata śṛṅgāṇām tulyāḥ haimavatāḥ gajāḥ gandharvanagara ākārāḥ rathāḥ hata nareśvarāḥ vimānāni iva puṇya ante svargiṇām nipatanti amī vyākulīkṛtam atyartham paśya sainyam kirīṭinā nānā mṛga sahasrāṇām yūtham kesariṇā yathā eṣā vidīryate senā dhārtarāṣṭrā samantataḥ arjunasya bhayāt tūrṇam nighnataḥ śātravān bahūn tvām ṛte krodha dīptaḥ hi pīḍyamāne vṛkodare viratham dharmarājam ca dṛṣṭvā su dṛḍha vikṣatam śikhaṇḍinam sātyakim ca dhṛṣṭadyumnam ca pārṣatam na ca asya rakṣām paśyāmi pṛṣṭhatas na ca pārśvatas ekaḥ eva abhiyāti tvām paśya sāphalyam ātmanaḥ tvam hi kṛṣṇau raṇe śaktaḥ saṃsādhayitum āhave tvam kṛtaḥ hi eva bhīṣmeṇa droṇa drauṇi kṛpaiḥ api savyasācinam āyāntam nivāraya mahā raṇe lelihānam yathā sarpam garjantam ṛṣabham yathā ete dravanti samare dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ mahā rathāḥ arjunasya bhayāt tūrṇam nirapekṣāḥ janādhipāḥ dravatām atha teṣām tu yudhi na anyaḥ asti mānavaḥ ete tvām kuravaḥ sarve dvīpam āsādya saṃyuge viṣṭhitāḥ puruṣa vyāghra tvattaḥ śaraṇa kāṅkṣiṇaḥ vaideha ambaṣṭha kāmbojāḥ tathā nagnajitaḥ tvayā gāndhārāḥ ca yayā dhṛtyā jitāḥ saṃkhye su durjayāḥ tām dhṛtim kuru rādheya tatas pratyehi pāṇḍavam vāsudevam ca vārṣṇeyam prīyamāṇam kirīṭinā kaliṅga adhipatim jitvā te ānītā tad antare uvāca prakṛti sthaḥ hi me śalyaḥ idānīm saṃmataḥ tathā pratibhāsi mahā bāho vibhīḥ ca eva dhanaṃjayāt ekaḥ adya nihaniṣyāmi pāṇḍavānām mahā camūm kṛṣṇau ca puruṣa vyāghrau tat ca satyam bravīmi te na a hatvā yudhi tau vīrau apayāsye katham cana kṛtārthaḥ vā bhaviṣyāmi hatvā tau atha vā hataḥ nihataḥ vā gamiṣyāmi na ekāntaḥ asti raṇe jayaḥ kṛtārthaḥ vā gamiṣyāmi hataḥ vā svagam āpnuyām uvāca mahā rathāḥ karṇa ratha pravīram ekākinam kim kṛṣṇa abhiguptam na etādṛśaḥ jātu babhūva loke adya aham tam nihaniṣyāmi saṃkhye tam īdṛśam pratiyotsyāmi pārtham mahā āhave paśya ca pauruṣam mama sa vā adya mām neṣyati kṛcchram etat karṇasya antāt etat antāḥ stha sarve śīghraiḥ hayaiḥ kaurava rāja putraḥ sa ca adya mām neṣyati kṣipram antam dṛḍha āyudhaḥ kṛtimān kṣipra hastaḥ na pāṇḍaveyena samaḥ asti yodhaḥ gṛhṇāti anekān api kaṅka patrān ekam yathā tān kṣitipān pramathya gṛhṇan vimuñcan sa nimeṣa mātrāt na pāṇḍavasya sadṛśaḥ asti kaḥ cit atīva anyān dhanuṣā rāja putraḥ tu atīva anyān keśavaḥ cakra yuddhe atoṣayat pāṇḍaveyaḥ hutāśam kṛṣṇa dvitīyaḥ atirathaḥ tarasvī lebhe cakram yatra kṛṣṇaḥ mahātmā dhanuḥ gāṇḍīvam pāṇḍavaḥ savyasācī śveta aśva yuktam ca su ghoṣam agryam ratham mahā bāhuḥ adīna sattvaḥ mahā iṣudhī ca akṣayau divya rūpau śastrāṇi divyāni ca havyavāhāt tathā indra loke nijaghāna daityān asaṃkhyeyān kālakeyān ca sarvān lebhe śaṅkham devadattam sma tatra kaḥ nāma tena abhyadhikaḥ pṛthivyām mahādevam toṣayām āsa ca eva lebhe tatas pāśupatam su ghoram trailokya saṃhāra karam mahā astram pṛthak pṛthak lokapālāḥ sametāḥ daduḥ hi astrāṇi aprameyāṇi yasya yaiḥ tān jaghāna āśu raṇe nṛ siṃhān sa kāla khañjān asurān sametān tam īdṛśam vīrya guṇa upapannam kṛṣṇa dvitīyam varaye raṇāya mahātmanaḥ śaṅkha cakra asi pāṇeḥ viṣṇoḥ jiṣṇoḥ vasudeva ātmajasya bhayam me vai jāyate sādhvasam ca nārāyaṇaḥ ca aprati cakra yuddhe evaṃvidhau pāṇḍava vāsudevau calet sva deśāt hi bhavān na kṛṣṇau karṇaḥ mām bhīṣayasi adya raṇe apramattam na aham tvayā bhīṣayitum hi śakyaḥ bandī iva tasya eva guṇān ca stauṣi tūṣṇīm sthitaḥ codaya tāvat aśvān dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇau eka rathe sametau etādṛśau nara vīrau sametau yama antakau vā śaśi pūṣaṇau vā bhaga aṃśa mitrāvaruṇa aśvinau vā marut gaṇāḥ vā vasavaḥ saha indrāḥ vyastāḥ samastāḥ ca yudhā na śaktā etādṛśau phalguna vāsudevau kaḥ anyaḥ pratīyāt mat ṛte nu śalya madra īśa yuddham prati pāṇḍavasya na idam cirāt āśu bhaviṣyati idam sarveṣām vṛṣṇi vīrāṇām kṛṣṇe lakṣmīḥ pratiṣṭhitā sarveṣām pāṇḍu putrāṇām jayaḥ pārthe pratiṣṭhitaḥ asmin muhūrte nihatau paśya kṛṣṇau tābhyām hatam vā yudhi mām ripubhyām etau aham yudhi vā pātayiṣye mām vā kṛṣṇau nihaniṣyataḥ adya asmin muhūrte nihatau paśya kṛṣṇau mayā hatam vā yudhi mām aribhyām evam bruvāṇaḥ sahasā mahā rathaḥ tu abhyadravat pāṇḍavam sūtaputraḥ kṛpam ca bhojam ca mahā bhujau ubhau tathā eva gāndhāra nṛpam saha anujam guroḥ sutam ca avara jam tathā ātmanaḥ padātinaḥ atha dvipa sādinaḥ anyān padāti sādi dviradāḥ rathāḥ tathā nirundhata abhidravata acyuta arjunau śrameṇa saṃyojayata āśu sarvatas tathā iti ca uktvā tvaritāḥ sma te arjunam jighāṃsavaḥ vīratamāḥ samabhyayus śaraiḥ ca jaghnuḥ yudhi tam mahā rathāḥ dhanaṃjayam karṇa nideśa kāriṇaḥ na saṃdadhānaḥ na tathā śara uttamān pramuñcamānaḥ ripubhiḥ pradṛśyate na ca abhimuñcan aribhiḥ sa dṛśyate dhanaṃjayaḥ tasya śaraiḥ ca dāritā hatāḥ ca petuḥ nara vāji kuñjarāḥ śara arciṣam gāṇḍiva cāru maṇḍalam yugānta sūrya pratimāna tejasam na kauravāḥ śekuḥ udīkṣitum jayam yathā ravim vyādhita cakṣuṣaḥ janāḥ śara uttamān sa prahitān mahā rathaiḥ bhūyas ca tān ahanat bāṇa saṃghān gāṇḍīvadhanvā āyata pūrṇa maṇḍalam yathā ugraraśmiḥ śuci śukra madhya gaḥ tathā arjunaḥ bāṇa gaṇān nirasya jighāṃsavaḥ pātham asahya vikramam yathā eva vahnim śalabhāḥ mahā arciṣam jighāṃsubhiḥ tān kuśalaiḥ śara uttamān mahā āhave saṃjavitān prayatnāt sa gāṇḍiva abhyāyata pūrṇa maṇḍalaḥ tapan ripūn arjuna bhāskaraḥ babhau atha agrya bāṇaiḥ daśabhiḥ dhanaṃjayam parābhinat droṇa sutaḥ acyutam tribhiḥ caturbhiḥ aśvān caturaḥ kapim tathā śaraiḥ sa nārāca varaiḥ avākirat tathā tu tat tat sphurat ātta kārmukam tribhiḥ śaraiḥ yantṛ śiraḥ kṣureṇa sa droṇaputrasya śarāsanam balī sa roṣa pūrṇaḥ aśani vajra hāṭakaiḥ alaṃkṛtam takṣaka bhoga varcasam svam āyudham ca upavikīrya bhū tale dhanuḥ ca kṛtvā sa guṇam guṇa adhikaḥ kṛpaḥ ca bhojaḥ ca tathā ātmajaḥ ca te tamonudam vāridharāḥ iva apatan śaraiḥ anekaiḥ yudhi pāṇḍava ṛṣabham mahā rathāḥ saṃyuga mūrdhani sthitāḥ mahā balāḥ vīta bhayāḥ raṇa ajire kṛpasya pārthaḥ sa śaram śarāsanam hayān dhvajam sārathim eva pattribhiḥ tathā yathā vajradharaḥ purā baleḥ sa pārtha bāṇaiḥ vinipātita āyudhaḥ kṛtaḥ kṛpaḥ bāṇa sahasra yantritaḥ yathā āpageyaḥ prathamam kirīṭinā jaghāna ca aśvān kṛtavarmaṇaḥ śubhān dhvajam ca ciccheda tatas pratāpavān sa vāji sūteṣu asanān sa ketanān jaghāna nāga aśva rathān tvaran ca saḥ tatas prakīrṇam su mahat balam te pradāritam setuḥ iva ambhasā yathā tatas arjunasya āśu rathena keśavaḥ cakāra śatrūn apasavyam āturān tatas prayāntam tvaritam dhanaṃjayam śatakratum vṛtra nijaghniṣam yathā atha abhisṛtya prativārya tān arīn dhanaṃjayasya abhi ratham mahā rathāḥ śikhaṇḍi śaineya yamāḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ vidārayantaḥ vyanadan su bhairavam kuru pravīrāḥ saha sṛñjayaiḥ yathā surāḥ purā deva varaiḥ ayodhayan jaya īpsavaḥ svar gamanāya ca utsukāḥ patanti nāga aśva rathāḥ paraṃtapa śara andhakāre tu mahātmabhiḥ kṛte mahā mṛdhe yodha varaiḥ parasparam babhuḥ daśa āśāḥ na divam ca pārthiva prabhā ca sūryasya tamaḥ vṛtā abhavat śara andhakāram ca kṛtam mahātmabhiḥ tadā diśaḥ na prababhuḥ śara arditāḥ uvāca vimṛdya sūtaputrasya senām bhārata sāyakaiḥ prāhiṇot mṛtyu lokāya para vīrān dhanaṃjayaḥ tatas asya ambaram āvṛtya śara jālāni bhāgaśas sa pakṣi saṃgha ācaritam ākāśam pūrayan śaraiḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ mahā rāja kurūṇām antakaḥ abhavat gātrāṇi prākṣiṇot pārthaḥ śirāṃsi ca cakarta ha dhanaṃjaya śara abhyastaiḥ syandana aśva nara dvipaiḥ saṃchinna bhinna vidhvastaiḥ vyaṅga aṅga avayavaiḥ stṛtā su durgamā su viṣamā ghorā atyartham su durdṛśā raṇa bhūmiḥ abhūt rājan mahā vaitaraṇī yathā gatasattvaiḥ sa sattvaiḥ ca saṃvṛtā āsīt vasuṃdharā īṣā cakra akṣa bhaṅgaiḥ ca vyaśvaiḥ sa aśvaiḥ ca yudhyatām sa sūtaiḥ hata sūtaiḥ ca rathaiḥ stīrṇā abhavat mahī sa sūtaiḥ hata sūtaiḥ ca sādi hīnaiḥ ca vājibhiḥ īṣā cakra akṣa bhagnaiḥ ca rathaiḥ stīrṇā vasuṃdharā suvarṇa varma saṃnāhaiḥ yodhaiḥ kanaka bhūṣaṇaiḥ āsthitāḥ kṛta varmāṇaḥ bhadrāḥ nitya madāḥ dvipāḥ kruddhāḥ kruddhaiḥ mahāmātraiḥ preṣitāḥ arjunam abhyayus catur śatāḥ śara varṣaiḥ hatāḥ petuḥ kirīṭinā paryastāni iva śṛṅgāṇi sa sattvāni mahā gireḥ dhanaṃjaya śara abhyastaiḥ stīrṇā bhūḥ vara vāraṇaiḥ samantāt jalada prakhyān vāraṇān mada varṣiṇaḥ tatas prādīryata camūḥ dhanaṃjaya śara āhatā mahā vāta samāviddhā mahā nauḥ iva sāgare nānā rūpāḥ praharaṇāḥ śarāḥ gāṇḍīva coditāḥ mahā girau veṇu vanam niśi prajvalitam yathā saṃpiṣṭa dagdha vidhvastam te sainyam kirīṭinā hatam pravihatam bāṇaiḥ sarvatas pradrutam diśaḥ mahā vane mṛga gaṇāḥ dāva agni grasitāḥ yathā utsṛjya hi mahā bāhum bhīmasenam tadā raṇe balam kurūṇām udvignam sarvam āsīt parāṅmukham tatas kuruṣu bhagneṣu bībhatsuḥ aparājitaḥ bhīmasena abhyanujñātaḥ tatas prāyāt dhanaṃjayaḥ nādayan ratha ghoṣeṇa pṛthivīm divam ca bhārata tatas parivṛtaḥ bhīmaiḥ daśabhiḥ śatru puṃgavaiḥ ātateṣu asanāḥ krūrāḥ nṛtyantaḥ iva bhārata apasavyān tu tān cakre rathena madhusūdanaḥ niyuktān hi sa tān mene yamāya āśu kirīṭinā tatas te prādravan śūrāḥ parāṅmukha rathe arjune teṣām āpatatām ketūn rathān cāpāni sāyakān atha anyaiḥ daśabhiḥ bhallaiḥ śirāṃsi eṣām nyapātayat roṣa saṃrakta netrāṇi saṃdaṣṭa oṣṭhāni bhū tale tāni vaktrāṇi vibabhuḥ vyomni tārā gaṇāḥ iva rukma aṅgadān rukma puṅkhaiḥ viddhvā prāyāt amitra hā uvāca yuddhāya abhyadravan vīrāḥ kurūṇām navatiḥ rathāḥ kṛtvā saṃśaptakāḥ ghorān śapathān brāhma laukikān kṛṣṇaḥ śvetān mahā vegān aśvān kanaka bhūṣaṇān muktā jāla praticchannān praiṣīt karṇa ratham prati tatas karṇa ratham yāntam arīn ghnantam dhanaṃjayam bāṇa varṣaiḥ abhighnantaḥ saṃśaptaka rathāḥ yayuḥ tvaramāṇān tu tān sarvān sa sūta iṣvasana dhvajān jaghāna navatim vīrān arjunaḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ te apatanta hatāḥ bāṇaiḥ nānā rūpaiḥ kirīṭinā sa vimānāḥ yathā siddhāḥ svargāt puṇya kṣaye tathā tatas sa ratha nāga aśvāḥ kuravaḥ kuru sattama kṣipram eva abhisaṃkruddhāḥ samare ari jighāṃsayā tat āyastam amukta astram udīrṇa vara vāraṇam putrāṇām te mahat sainyam samarautsīt dhanaṃjayaḥ śakti ṛṣṭi tomara prāsaiḥ gadā nistriṃśa sāyakaiḥ prācchādayan mahā iṣvāsāḥ kuravaḥ kuru nandanam tām kurūṇām pravitatām śastra vṛṣṭim samudyatām vyadhamat pāṇḍavaḥ bāṇaiḥ tamaḥ sūryaḥ iva aṃśubhiḥ pārśvatas abhyahanan pārtham te putrasya śāsanāt karṇi nālīka nārācaiḥ tomaraiḥ prāsa śaktibhiḥ tām astra vṛṣṭim prahitām dvipa sthaiḥ yavanaiḥ smayan atha tān dviradān sarvān nānā liṅgaiḥ mahā śaraiḥ sa patākān saha ārohān girīn vajraiḥ iva abhinat te hema puṅkhaiḥ iṣubhiḥ ācitāḥ hema mālinaḥ hatāḥ petuḥ mahā nāgāḥ sa agni jvālāḥ iva adrayaḥ tatas gāṇḍīva nirghoṣaḥ mahān āsīt viśām pate stanatām kūjatām ca eva manuṣya gaja vājinām kuñjarāḥ ca hatāḥ rājñ prādravan te samantataḥ aśvāḥ ca paryadhāvanta hata ārohāḥ diśaḥ daśa rathāḥ hīnāḥ mahā rāja rathibhiḥ vājibhiḥ tathā gandharvanagara ākārāḥ dṛśyante sma sahasraśas aśva ārohāḥ mahā rāja dhāvamānāḥ tatas tatas nardantaḥ kūjamānāḥ ca manuṣya gaja vājinaḥ tatra tatra eva dṛśyante patitāḥ pārtha sāyakaiḥ tasmin kṣaṇe pāṇḍavasya bāhvoḥ balam adṛśyata yat sādinaḥ vāraṇān ca rathān ca ekaḥ ajayat yudhi asaṃyuktāḥ ca te rājan parivṛttāḥ raṇam prati dṛṣṭvā parivṛtam rājan bhīmasenaḥ kirīṭinam hata avaśeṣān utsṛjya tvadīyān kati cit rathān dṛṣṭvā yat arjunam bhīmaḥ jagāma bhrātaram prati hata avaśiṣṭān turagān arjunena mahā javān bhīmaḥ vyadhamat abhra antaḥ gadā pāṇiḥ mahā āhave gadā pāṇim tadā bhīmam dṛṣṭvā bhārata bhāratāḥ kālarātrim iva ati ugrām nara nāga aśva bhojanām prākāra aṭṭa pura dvāra dāraṇīm ati dāruṇām tatas gadām nṛ nāga aśveṣu āśu bhīmaḥ vyavāsṛjat gajān aśvān haya ārohān uddiśya uddiśya bhārata sā jaghāna bahūn aśvān aśva ārohān ca māriṣa kāṃsya āyasa tanutrān tān narān aśvān ca pāṇḍavaḥ pothayām āsa gadayā sa śabdam te apatan hatāḥ kṣaṇena bhīmaḥ saṃkruddhaḥ tān ninye vai yama kṣayam tatas sa samara ślāghī gaja anīkam apātayat gadayā vyadhamat saṃkhye daṇḍa pāṇiḥ iva antakaḥ gajān sa kaṅkaṭān mattān sa ārohān sa patākinaḥ nyahanat līlayā rājan śikṣayā ca balena ca te gajāḥ bahu aśobhanta hanyamānāḥ mahā raṇe vinadantaḥ yathā tūrṇam pakṣavantaḥ iva adrayaḥ nipetuḥ urvyām samare bhīmasenena pīḍitāḥ chinna pakṣāḥ yathā kāle vajra rugṇāḥ iva adrayaḥ dantaiḥ daśantaḥ vasudhām śerate kṣataja ukṣitāḥ bhagna mūrdha asthi caraṇāḥ kravyāda gaṇa bhojanāḥ asṛj māṃsa vasābhiḥ ca tṛptāḥ māṃsa vasā aśanāḥ asthīni api aśnatī tasthau kālarātriḥ iva durdṛśā sahasrāṇi daśa aśvānām hatvā pattīn ca bhūyasā bhīmaḥ abhyadhāvat saṃkruddhaḥ gadā pāṇiḥ itas tatas gadā pāṇim tatas bhīmam dṛṣṭvā bhārata tāvakāḥ menire samanuprāptam kālam daṇḍa udyatam yathā sa mattaḥ iva mātaṃgaḥ saṃkruddhaḥ pāṇḍu nandanaḥ praviveśa gaja anīkam makaraḥ sāgaram yathā vigāhya ca gaja anīkam pragṛhya mahatīm gadām kṣaṇena bhīmaḥ saṃkruddhaḥ tān ninye yama sādanam gajān sa kaṅkaṭān mattān sa rohān sa patākinaḥ patataḥ samapaśyāma sapakṣān parvatān iva hatvā tu tat gaja anīkam bhīmasenaḥ mahā balaḥ punar sva ratham āsthāya pṛṣṭhatas arjunam anvagāt hatam parāṅmukha prāyam nirutsāham param balam vyālambata mahā rāja prāyaśas śastra veṣṭitam dṛṣṭvā prācchādayat bāṇaiḥ arjunaḥ prāṇa tāpanaiḥ nara aśva ratha mātaṃgāḥ yudhi gāṇḍīvadhanvanā śara vrātaiḥ citāḥ rejuḥ kadambāḥ iva kesaraiḥ tatas kurūṇām abhavat ārta nādaḥ mahā mṛdhe śataśas vadhyamānānām niśitaiḥ arjuna iṣubhiḥ ratha aśva nāga asu haraiḥ vadhyatām arjuna iṣubhiḥ kurūṇām tu mahā rājaḥ āsīt ārta svaraḥ mahān nara aśva nāga asu harān dṛṣṭvā bāṇān kirīṭinaḥ hāhākṛtam bhṛśam tasthau līyamānam parasparam tatas śara dhvastam abhūt kurūṇām su mahat balam āsīt sva śoṇita klinnam phulla aśoka vanam yathā tat sainyam bharata śreṣṭha vadhyamānam śitaiḥ śaraiḥ tatra adbhutam apaśyāma kauravāṇām parākramam tat dṛṣṭvā kuravaḥ tatra vikrāntam savyasācinaḥ nirāśāḥ samapadyanta sarve karṇasya jīvite aviṣahyam tu pārthasya śara saṃpātam āhave matvā nyavartan kuravaḥ jitāḥ gāṇḍīvadhanvanā te hitvā samare pārtham vadhyamānāḥ ca sāyakaiḥ pradudruvuḥ diśaḥ bhītāḥ cukruśuḥ ca api sūtajam abhyadravata tān pārthaḥ kiran śara śatān bahūn harṣayan pāṇḍavān yodhān bhīmasena purogamān agādhe majjatām teṣām dvīpaḥ karṇaḥ abhavat tadā kuravaḥ hi mahā rāja nirviṣāḥ pannagāḥ iva karṇam eva upalīyanta bhayāt gāṇḍīvadhanvanaḥ yathā sarvāṇi bhūtāni mṛtyoḥ bhītāni bhārata tathā karṇam mahā iṣvāsam putrāḥ te narādhipa upālīyanta saṃtrāsāt pāṇḍavasya mahātmanaḥ tān śoṇita pariklinnān viṣama sthān śara āturān saṃbhagnam hi balam dṛṣṭvā balāt pārthena tāvakam viṣphārayitvā durdharṣaḥ cāpam ādhirathiḥ mahat tān vidrutān kurūn dṛṣṭvā karṇaḥ śastrabhṛtām varaḥ visphārya su mahat cāpam tatas ca ādhirathiḥ vṛṣaḥ pāñcālān punar ādhāvat paśyataḥ savyasācinaḥ tatas kṣaṇena kṣitipāḥ kṣataja pratima īkṣaṇāḥ karṇam vavarṣuḥ bāṇa oghaiḥ yathā meghāḥ mahīdharam śara oghaiḥ chādayām āsa mahā meghaḥ iva acalam tatas śara sahasrāṇi karṇa muktāni māriṣa vyayojayanta pāñcālān prāṇaiḥ prāṇabhṛtām vara pāñcālānām harat prāṇān tamāṃsi iva tamonudaḥ tatas raṇaḥ mahān asīt pāñcālānām viśām pate vadhyatām sūtaputreṇa mitra arthe amitra ghātinām uvāca tatas karṇaḥ kuruṣu pradruteṣu varūthinā śveta hayena rājan pāñcāla putrān vyadhamat sūtaputraḥ mahā iṣubhiḥ vātaḥ iva abhra saṃghān sūtam rathāt añjalikena pātya jaghāna ca aśvān janamejayasya śatānīkam sutasomam ca bhallaiḥ avākirat dhanuṣī ca api akṛntat dhṛṣṭadyumnam nirbibheda atha ṣaḍbhiḥ jaghāna ca aśvam dakṣiṇam tasya saṃkhye hatvā ca aśvān sātyakeḥ sūtaputraḥ kaikeya putram nyavadhīt viśokam śaraiḥ vibhinnam bhṛśam ugra vegaiḥ karṇa ātmajam saḥ abhyahanat suṣeṇam sa syandanāt gām apatat gatāsuḥ paraśvadhaiḥ śālaḥ iva avarugṇaḥ hata aśvam añjas gatibhiḥ suṣeṇaḥ śini pravīram niśitaiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ pracchādya nṛtyan iva sauti putraḥ śaineya bāṇa abhihataḥ papāta putre hate krodha parīta cetāḥ karṇaḥ śinīnām ṛṣabham jighāṃsuḥ śikhaṇḍinaḥ kārmukam sa dhvajam ca chittvā śarābhyām ahanat sujātam śikhaṇḍinam ṣaḍbhiḥ avidhyat ugraḥ dāntaḥ dhārṣṭadyumna śiraḥ cakarta atha abhinat sutasomam śareṇa sa saṃśitena ādhirathiḥ mahātmā pāñcālānām ratha saṃghāḥ sametāḥ pratiśrutā hi antarikṣe gata ābhā dhanuḥ pravīrāḥ tu ratha pravīrāḥ atha ākrande tumule vartamāne dhārṣṭadyumne nihate tatra kṛṣṇaḥ a pāñcālyam kriyate yāhi pārtha karṇam jahi iti abravīt rāja siṃha bhaye teṣām trāṇam icchan su bāhuḥ abhyāhatānām ratha yūthapena visphārya gāṇḍīvam atha ugra ghoṣam jyayā samāhatya tale bhṛśam ca bāṇa andhakāram sahasā eva kṛtvā jaghāna nāga aśva rathān narān ca prītāḥ śukāḥ prādravan antarikṣe guhā girīṇām apatan vayāṃsi yat maṇḍala jyena vijṛmbhamāṇaḥ tam bhīmasenaḥ anu yayau rathena pṛṣṭhe rakṣan pāṇḍavam eka vīram ratha aśva mātaṃga gaṇān jaghāna pracchādayām āsa diśaḥ śaraiḥ ca karṇam vineduḥ sahitāḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ saṃmardamānāḥ saha pārṣatena te pañca pāñcāla rathāḥ su rūpaiḥ vaikartanam karṇam abhidravantaḥ tasmāt rathāt cyāvayitum na śekuḥ dhairyāt kṛta ātmānam iva indriyāṇi teṣām dhanūṃṣi dhvaja vāji sūtān tūṇam patākāḥ ca nikṛtya bāṇaiḥ teṣām dhvajān vāji sūtān patākāḥ tūṇīḥ dhanūṃṣi pracakarta bāṇaiḥ tān pañcabhiḥ sa tu ahanat pṛṣatkaiḥ karṇaḥ tatas siṃhaḥ iva unnanāda sa adri drumā syāt pṛthivī viśīrṇā iti eva matvā janatā vyaṣīdat sa śakra cāpa pratimena dhanvanā bhṛśa ātatena ādhirathiḥ śarān sṛjan babhau raṇe dīpta marīci maṇḍalaḥ yathā aṃśumālī pariveṣavān tathā śikhaṇḍinam dvādaśabhiḥ parābhinat śitaiḥ śaraiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ atha uttamaujasam parājitāḥ pañca mahā rathāḥ tu te mahā āhave sūta sutena māriṣa tatas śinīnām ṛṣabhaḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ nikṛtya karṇa prahitān iṣūn bahūn vidārya karṇam niśitaiḥ ayasmayaiḥ tava ātmajam jyeṣṭham avidhyat aṣṭabhiḥ kṛpaḥ atha bhojaḥ ca te ātmajaḥ tathā svayam ca karṇaḥ niśitaiḥ atāḍayat samānatena iṣvasanena kūjatā bhṛśa ātatena amita bāṇa varṣiṇā punar samāsādya rathān su daṃśita śini pravīram jugupuḥ paraṃtapa sametya pāñcāla rathāḥ mahā raṇe marut gaṇāḥ śakram iva ari nigrahe tatas abhavat yuddham atīva dāruṇam tava ahitānām tava sainikaiḥ saha ratha aśva mātaṃga vināśanam tathā yathā surāṇām asuraiḥ purā bhavat ratha dvipāḥ vāji padātayaḥ api vā tathā gate bhīmam abhīḥ tava ātmajaḥ sasāra rāja avarajaḥ kiran śaraiḥ paraspareṇa abhiniviṣṭa roṣayoḥ udagrayoḥ śambara śakrayoḥ yathā śaraiḥ śarīra anta karaiḥ su tejanaiḥ nijaghnatuḥ tau itaretaram bhṛśam samam ca śūrau ca sa sārathī tadā bhīmaḥ abravīt yāhi duḥśāsanāya duḥśāsanaḥ yāhi vṛkodarāya bhīmaḥ divi iva pūrvam bala śakrayoḥ raṇe diṣṭyā asi duḥśāsana adya dṛṣṭa ṛṇam pratīccheḥ saha vṛddhi mūlam cira uditam tam yat mayā te sabhāyām kṛṣṇa abhimarśena gṛhāṇa mattaḥ duḥśāsanaḥ vākyam uvāca vīraḥ udīryamāṇam śṛṇu bhīmasena yat jātuṣe veśmani rātrī ahāni viśvāsa hīnāḥ mṛgayām carantaḥ tathā upabhogāt ca sukhāt ca hīnāḥ vaneṣu aṭantaḥ giri gahvarāṇi pāñcāla rājasya puram praviṣṭāḥ māyām yūyam kām api saṃpraviṣṭā yatas vṛtaḥ kṛṣṇayā phalgunaḥ vaḥ saṃbhūya pāpaiḥ tat anārya vṛttam kṛtam tadā mātṛ kṛta anurūpam ekaḥ vṛtaḥ pañcabhiḥ sā abhipannā saṃjayaḥ dāsīkṛtāḥ stha saha kṛṣṇayā tu pragṛhya cāpam bhṛkuṭīm lalāṭe kṛtvā tu roṣa ujjvala tāmra netraḥ lalāṭam api asya bibheda pattriṇā śiraḥ ca kāyāt prajahāra sāratheḥ sa rāja putraḥ anyat avāpya kārmukam vṛkodaram dvādaśabhiḥ parābhinat svayam niyacchan turagān ajihmagaiḥ śaraiḥ ca bhīmam punar abhyavīvṛṣat tatas śaram sūrya marīci saprabham mahā indra vajra aśani pāta duḥsaham mumoca bhīma aṅga vidāraṇa kṣamam prasārya bāhū ratha varyam āśritaḥ punar ca saṃjñām upalabhya ca anadat uvāca duḥśāsanena nikṛtaḥ nikṛtyā tatra akarot duṣkaram rāja putraḥ duḥśāsanaḥ tumule yudhyamānaḥ ciccheda bhīmasya dhanuḥ kṣureṇa ṣaḍbhiḥ śaraiḥ sārathim api avidhyat vivyādha bhīmam navabhiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ śaktim ca ugrām prāhiṇot te sutāya tām āpatantīm sahasā ati ghorām dṛṣṭvā sutaḥ te jvalitām iva ulkām ākarṇapūrṇaiḥ iṣubhiḥ mahātmā ciccheda putraḥ daśabhiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ dṛṣṭvā tu tat karma kṛtam su duṣkaram prāpūjayan sarva yodhāḥ prahṛṣṭāḥ atha āśu bhīmam ca śareṇa bhūyas gāḍham sa vivyādha sutaḥ tvadīyaḥ bhṛśam prajajvāla ruṣā abhivīkṣya viddhaḥ asmi vīra āśu bhṛśam tvayā adya jagrāha tām bhīma gadām vadhāya uvāca ca adya aham aham durātman pāsyāmi te śoṇitam āji madhye śaktim vegāt prāhiṇot mṛtyu rūpām āvidhya bhīmaḥ api gadām su ghorām vicikṣipe roṣa parīta mūrtiḥ putram tava ājau tāḍayām āsa mūrdhni sa kārmukam gṛhya tu bhāra sādhanam pañcāśatā bāṇa gaṇaiḥ stanāntare duḥśāsanaḥ bhīmasenam cakāra chittvā ratha īṣām punar eva ca akṣipat vṛkodaraḥ gadayā tasya vāhān yama kṣayam preṣayitvā mahātmā ratham samākarṣata rāja sūnoḥ tatas krodhāt bhīmasenaḥ kṛtāni sarvāṇi duḥkhāni anusaṃsmaran vai saṃsmṛtya saṃsmṛtya tathā pratijñām trayodaśa abdam puruṣa pravīraḥ pragṛhya vajra aśani tulya vegām gadām kareṇa atha vṛkodaraḥ ruṣā nipātayitvā pṛthivī tale bhṛśam saṃtāḍayām āsa balī vṛkodaraḥ atīva saṃtāḍita bhinna gātraḥ duḥśāsanaḥ vai nipapāta bhūmau ākramya kaṇṭhe yudhi rāja putram saṃrakta netraḥ hi abravīt dhārtarāṣṭram tat brūhi kim tvam parimārgamāṇaḥ hi asmān parābhūya iha āgatān punar tat idam adya bhṛśa saṃbhṛtam me madhu prapāsye tava koṣṭha bhājanāt duḥśāsanam kaṇṭha deśe pramṛdnan tatas krūram bhīmasenaḥ cakāra tam vyaṃsayitvā sahasā sasāra balāt asau dhārtarāṣṭraḥ tarasvī sapatna tām darśayan dhārtarāṣṭre mṛgam muhur siṃha śiśuḥ yathā vane tathā āśu abhidrutya mahā balam balī nigṛhya ca enam parameṇa karmaṇā bhūmau tadā niṣpipeṣa atha vīraḥ asim vikośam vimalam cakāra kaṇṭhe samākrāmya ca vepamānam kṛtvā tu rūpam paramam su ghoram kāla antakābhyām pratimam tadānīm duḥśāsanasya ripu śāsanasya tayā aharat daśa dhanvantarāṇi duḥśāsanam bhīmasenaḥ prasahya tayā hataḥ patitaḥ vepamānaḥ duḥśāsanaḥ gadayā vegavatyā hayāḥ sa sūtāḥ ca hatāḥ narendra cūrṇīkṛtaḥ ca asya rathaḥ patantyā vidhvasta varma ābharaṇa ambara sraj viceṣṭamānaḥ bhṛśa vedanā ārtaḥ duḥśāsanam pāṇḍavāḥ prekṣya sarve hṛṣṭāḥ pāñcālāḥ siṃhanādān amuñcan tam pātayitvā atha vṛkodaraḥ ayam jagarja harṣeṇa vinādayan diśaḥ mūrchā ākulāḥ patitāḥ tu ājamīḍha cakāra khedam manasā cintām ca paramām yayau vastreṇa avījayat ca enam tena saṃjñām avāpa ha dṛṣṭvā sa saṃjñam sa avajñam pādena ākramya vakṣasi prahṛṣṭa rūpaḥ bhīmaḥ tu sa āsīḥ provāca tam tadā bhīmaḥ api vegāt avatīrya yānāt duḥśāsanam vegavān abhyadhāvat pradhāna bhūyiṣṭhataraiḥ samantāt duḥśāsanam tatra samīkṣya rājan smṛtvā atha keśa grahaṇam ca devyā vastra apahāram ca rajasvalāyāḥ anāgasaḥ bhartṛ parāṅmukhāyāḥ jajvāla krodha amarṣeṇa bhīma ājya prasiktaḥ hi yathā hutāśaḥ kṛpam drauṇim kṛtavarmāṇam eva nihanmi duḥśāsanam adya pāpam saṃrakṣyatām adya samasta yodhāḥ nigṛhya duḥśāsanam eka vīraḥ katham draupadīm keśa pakṣe pradharṣīḥ hṛṣṭaḥ samam karṇa suyodhanābhyām durātman śrutvā tu tat bhīma vacaḥ su ghoram duḥśāsanaḥ bhīmam idam nirīkṣya uvāca bhīmam sa tadā smitena saṃpaśyatām kaurava somakānām eṣa tvayā rājya haraḥ samīkṣya dyūta chalāt vañcayitā sametām kliṣṭām āryām paśyataḥ te tu anena bhikṣā bhujaḥ yena kṛtāḥ samastā aṣṭādaśa dvā ca kuruṣva yatnam bhīmaḥ duḥśāsanaḥ diśyatām ca sa me pāpin kam tam utpāṭayāmi aham ayam kari kara ākāraḥ kāminī kuca mardanaḥ saṃjayaḥ go sahasra pradātā ca kṣatriya anta karaḥ karaḥ utpāṭayām āsa bhujam vāmetaram ariṃdama asim samuddhṛtya śitam su dhāram kaṇṭhe samākramya ca vepamānam ye rājasūya avabhṛthe pavitrā jātāḥ kacāḥ yājñasenyāḥ durātman te pāṇinā katareṇa avakṛṣṭāḥ prabrūhi tvām pṛcchate bhīmasenaḥ ayam kari kara ākāraḥ pīna stana vimardanaḥ go sahasra pradātā ca kṣatriya anta karaḥ karaḥ anena yājñasenyāḥ me bhīma keśāḥ vikarṣitāḥ paśyatām kuru mukhyānām tvaṣmākam ca sabhāsadām bruvantam ājau vinipīḍya vakṣaḥ bhīmaḥ balāt bāhum dorbhyām uvāca yasya asti balam kulam ca duḥśāsanam jīvitam utsṛjantam ākṣipya yodhāḥ tarasā mahā balam utpāṭya vīraḥ sahasā eva rājan duḥśāsanam tena tu vīra madhye utkṛtya vakṣaḥ patitasya bhūmau atha apibat śoṇitam asya koṣṇam tatas nipātya asya śiraḥ apahṛtya satyām cikīrṣuḥ matiman pratijñām āsvādya ca āsvādya ca vīkṣamāṇaḥ kruddhaḥ ativelam prajagāda vākyam anyāni pānāni ca yāni loke sudhā amṛta svādu rasāni tebhyaḥ duḥśāsanam krodha parīta cetāḥ kim vā kuryām mṛtyunā rakṣitaḥ asi evam bruvāṇam punar ādravantam āsvādya valgantam ati prahṛṣṭam ye bhīmasenam dadṛśuḥ tadānīm bhayena te api vyathitāḥ nipetuḥ ye ca api tatra āpatitāḥ manuṣyāḥ teṣām karebhyaḥ patitam ca śastram bhayāt ca saṃcukruśuḥ uccakais te nimīlita akṣāḥ dadṛśuḥ ca tat na ye tatra bhīmam dadṛśuḥ samantāt dauḥśāsanam tat rudhiram pibantam sarve palāyanta bhaya abhipannāḥ na ayam manuṣyaḥ iti bhāṣamāṇāḥ saṃjayaḥ sa pītvā rudhiram tasya caraṇau gṛhya bhārata dṛṣṭvā ca tat śoṇitam pīyamānam saṃprādravan citrasenena sārdham bhīmam rakṣaḥ bhāṣamāṇāḥ bhaya ārtāḥ mahā anīkam sma abhyayāt rāja putraḥ vivyādha ca enam niśitaiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ vyapeta bhīḥ saptabhiḥ āśu muktaiḥ mahā uragaḥ krodha viṣam sisṛkṣuḥ tribhiḥ śaraiḥ sārathim ca api avidhyat su saṃśita agreṇa śareṇa śūraḥ kruddhaḥ karṇaḥ pauruṣam darśayānaḥ dudrāva tat pāṇḍavānām anīkam bhīmaḥ api hatvā tatra eva duḥśāsanam amarṣaṇam śṛṇvatām loka vīrāṇām idam vacanam abravīt eṣa te rudhiram kaṇṭhāt pibāmi puruṣa adhama brūhi idānīm su saṃrabdhaḥ punar gauḥ iti gauḥ iti pramāṇakoṭau śayanam kālakūṭasya bhojanam daśanam ca ahibhiḥ kaṣṭam dāham ca jatu veśmani dyūtena rājya haraṇam araṇye vasatiḥ ca yā draupadyāḥ keśa pakṣasya grahaṇam ca su dāruṇam iṣu astrāṇi ca saṃgrāmeṣu asukhāni ca veśmani virāṭa bhavane yaḥ ca kleśaḥ naḥ pṛthagvidhaḥ anubhūtāni duḥkhāni teṣām hetuḥ tvam eva hi duḥkhāni etāni jānīmaḥ na sukhāni kadā cana dhṛtarāṣṭrasya daurātmyāt sa putrasya sadā vayam sukhāni etāni jānīmaḥ labdhavantaḥ na saṃśayaḥ iti uktvā vacanam rājñ jayam prāpya vṛkodaraḥ punar āha mahā rāja smayan tau keśava arjunau gadā pāṇiḥ kāle iva antakāle itas tatas dhāvati vāhinīm te tatas kṣaṇāt bhārata śūnyam āsīt āyodhanam ghorataram kurūṇām duḥśāsanasya rudhiram krodha dīptaḥ pūrṇa kāmaḥ mada udagraḥ siṃhaḥ rurum iva utkaṭam rudhira ārdraḥ mahā rāja hi aśobhata paraṃtapaḥ brūhi idānīm pāpa mate nṛśaṃsa patitaḥ hi asi brūhi idānīm pāpa mate nṛśaṃsa duḥśāsane yat raṇe saṃśrutam mama tat vai sarvam kṛtam adya iha vīrau adya eva dāsyāmi aparam dvitīyam duryodhanam yajña paśum viśasya śiraḥ mṛditvā ca padā durātmanaḥ śāntim lapsye kauravāṇām samakṣam yā ca apatiḥ sā sapatiḥ hi jātā yāḥ tāḥ sapatayaḥ apatayaḥ tu jātāḥ ye vai tilāḥ ṣaṇḍa tilāḥ babhūvuḥ kim citra rūpam bata jīva loke etāvat uktvā vacanam prahṛṣṭaḥ nanāda ca uccais rudhira ārdra gātraḥ dṛṣṭvā tu nṛtyantam udagra rūpam kālam yathā tu antakāle prajānām jaye nirāśāḥ ca sutāḥ tvadīyāḥ uvāca duḥśāsane tu nihate putrāḥ te mahā rathāḥ mahā krodha viṣāḥ vīrāḥ samareṣu apalāyinaḥ daśa rājan mahā vīryaḥ bhīmam prācchādayan śaraiḥ kavacī niṣaṅgī pāśī daṇḍadhāraḥ dhanurdharaḥ ete sametya sahitāḥ bhrātṛ vyasana karśitāḥ bhīmasenam mahā bāhum mārgaṇaiḥ samavārayan sa vāryamāṇaḥ viśikhaiḥ samantāt taiḥ mahā rathaiḥ bhīmaḥ krodha abhirakta akṣaḥ kruddhaḥ kālaḥ iva ābabhau tatas parivṛtaḥ rājan navabhiḥ śatru tāpanaiḥ duḥśāsanāt avarajaiḥ putraiḥ te vṛkodaraḥ tān tu bhallaiḥ mahā vegaiḥ daśabhiḥ daśabhiḥ śitaiḥ hateṣu teṣu vīreṣu pradudrāva balam tava paśyataḥ sūtaputrasya pāṇḍavasya bhaya arditam tatas karṇaḥ mahā rāja praviveśa mahā raṇam dṛṣṭvā bhīmasya vikrāntam antakasya prajāsu iva tasya tu ākāra bhāva jñaḥ śalyaḥ samiti śobhanaḥ uvāca vacanam karṇam prāpta kālam ariṃdama ete dravanti rājānaḥ bhīmasena bhaya arditāḥ duryodhanaḥ ca saṃmūḍhaḥ bhrātṛ vyasana duḥkhitaḥ duḥśāsanasya rudhire pīyamāne mahātmanā kṛpa prabhṛtayaḥ karṇa hata śeṣāḥ ca sodarāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ labdhalakṣāḥ ca dhanaṃjaya purogamāḥ tvām eva abhimukhāḥ śūrāḥ yuddhāya samupāsthitāḥ sa tvam puruṣa śārdūla pauruṣe mahati sthitaḥ bhāraḥ hi dhārtarāṣṭreṇa tvayi sarvaḥ samarpitaḥ tvayi moha samāpanne pāṇḍavān abhidhāvati hṛdi mānuṣyakam bhāvam cakre yuddhāya su sthiram tatas kruddhaḥ vṛṣasenaḥ abhyadhāvat ātasthivāṃsam sva ratham hata arim vṛkodaram kālam iva ātta daṇḍam gadā hastam tvadīyān bhīmam samāyāntam amitra sāham bāṇaiḥ kirantam pratiyātya ca ugram vyātta ānanam kālam iva āpatantam tam abhyadhāvat nakulaḥ pravīraḥ roṣāt amitram pratudan pṛṣatkaiḥ karṇasya putram samare prahṛṣṭam jiṣṇuḥ jighāṃsuḥ maghavā iva jambham karṇa ātmajasya iṣvasanam ca citram bhallena jāmbūnada paṭṭa naddham atha anyat ādāya dhanuḥ su śīghram karṇa ātmajaḥ pāṇḍavam abhyavidhyat divyaiḥ mahā astraiḥ nakulam mahā astraḥ duḥśāsanasya apacitim yiyāsuḥ śara abhighātāt ca ruṣā ca rājan svayam ca bhāsā astra samīraṇāt ca iddhaḥ yathā jyā āhutibhiḥ hutāśaḥ karṇasya putraḥ nakulasya rājan sarvān aśvān akṣiṇot uttama astraiḥ yuddham tadā karṇa ja pāṇḍavābhyām vanāyu jān su kumārasya śubhrān alaṃkṛtān jātarūpeṇa śīghrān jaghāna ca aśvān nakulasya vīro tatas hata aśvāt avaruhya yānāt ādāya carma ruciram ca aṣṭa candram ākāśa saṃkāśam asim gṛhītvā poplūyamānaḥ khaga vat cacāra tatas antarikṣe nṛ vara aśva nāgān ciccheda mārgān vicaran vicitrān dvi sāhasrān nakulaḥ kṣiprakārī te prāpatan asinā gām viśastāḥ yathā aśvamedhe paśavaḥ śamitrā dvi sāhasrāḥ viditāḥ yuddha śauṇḍāḥ nānādeśyāḥ su bhṛtāḥ satya saṃdhāḥ ekena śīghram nakulena kṛttāḥ sāra īpsunā iva uttama candanāḥ te raṇe jighāṃsum niśitaiḥ anekaiḥ bhūmau carantam nakulam ratha sthāḥ samantataḥ sāyakaiḥ pratyagṛhṇan mahā bhaye rakṣyamāṇaḥ mahātmā bhrātrā bhīmena akarot tatra bhīmam krīḍantam aṣṭādaśabhiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ vivyādha vīram sa cukopa viddhaḥ mahā āhave vṛṣasenena rājan tatas abhyadhāvat samare jighāṃsuḥ karṇa ātmajam pāṇḍu sutaḥ nṛ vīraḥ śyenam yathā eva āmiṣa lubdham ājau avākirat vṛṣasenaḥ tatas tam śitaiḥ śaraiḥ nakulam udāra vīryam sa tān moghān tasya kurvan śara oghān cacāra mārgān nakulaḥ citra rūpān tasya āyasam niśitam tīkṣṇa dhāram asim vikośam guru bhāra sāham kṣipram śaraiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ amitra sāhaḥ cakarta khaḍgam niśitaiḥ su dhāraiḥ punar ca pītaiḥ niśitaiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ stanāntare gāḍham atha abhyavidhyat kṛtvā tu tat duṣkaram ārya juṣṭam śara abhitaptaḥ nakulaḥ mahātmā sa bhīmasenasya ratham hata aśvaḥ mādrī sutaḥ karṇa suta abhitaptaḥ āpupluve siṃhaḥ iva acala agram saṃprekṣamāṇasya dhanaṃjayasya tatas kruddhaḥ vṛṣasenaḥ mahātmā vavarṣa tau iṣu jālena vīraḥ śaraiḥ prabhindan iva pāṇḍaveyau kṣipram ca khaḍge viśikhaiḥ nikṛtte bhīma arjunau vṛṣasenāya kruddhau vavarṣatuḥ śara varṣam su ghoram atha abravīt mārutiḥ phalgunam tu paśyasva enam nakulam pīḍayantam tasmāt bhavān pratyupayātu kārṇim sa tat niśamya eva vacaḥ kirīṭī kapidhvajam keśava saṃgṛhītam praiṣīt ugraḥ vṛṣasenāya vāham pavana dhuta patākāḥ hrādinaḥ valgita aśvāḥ vara puruṣa niyattāḥ te rathāḥ śīghram īyuḥ drupada suta variṣṭhāḥ pañca śaineya ṣaṣṭhāḥ drupada duhitṛ putrāḥ pañca ca amitra sāhāḥ dvirada ratha nara aśvān sūdayantaḥ tvadīyān bhujaga pati nikāśaiḥ mārgaṇaiḥ ātta śastrāḥ śakuni śuka vṛkāḥ ca krātha devāvṛdhau ca dvirada jalada ghoṣaiḥ syandanaiḥ kārmukaiḥ ca su kalpitā haimavatā mada utkaṭā raṇa abhikāmaiḥ kṛtibhiḥ samāsthitāḥ suvarṇa jāla avatatāḥ babhuḥ gajāḥ tathā yathā vai jaladāḥ sa vidyutaḥ kuṇinda putraḥ daśabhiḥ mahā āyasaiḥ kṛpam sa sūta aśvam apīḍayat bhṛśam tatas kuṇindeṣu hateṣu teṣu atha prahṛṣṭa rūpāḥ tava te mahā rathāḥ bhṛśam pradadhmuḥ lavaṇa ambu saṃbhavān parān ca bāṇāsana pāṇayaḥ abhyayus atha abhavat yuddham atīva dāruṇam punar kurūṇām saha pāṇḍu sṛñjayaiḥ śara asi śakti ṛṣṭi gadā paraśvadhaiḥ bhṛśa ākulam tatas śatānīka hatān mahā gajān tathā rathān patti gaṇān ca tāvakān jaghāna bhojaḥ ca hayān atha apatan viśastra kṛttāḥ kṛtavarmaṇā dvipāḥ atha apare drauṇi śara āhatāḥ dvipāḥ trayaḥ sa sarva āyudha yodha ketavaḥ nipetuḥ urvyām vyasavaḥ prapātitāḥ tathā yathā vajra hatāḥ mahā acalāḥ tava ātmajam tasya tava ātmajaḥ śaraiḥ śitaiḥ śarīram bibhide dvipam ca tam sa nāga rājaḥ saha rāja sūnunā papāta raktam bahu sarvatas kṣaran sa vāji sūta iṣvasanaḥ tathā apatat yathā mahā vāta hataḥ mahā drumaḥ vṛkaḥ dvipa stham girirāja vāsinam bhṛśam śaraiḥ dvādaśabhiḥ parābhinat tatas vṛkam sa aśva ratham mahā javam tvaran caturbhiḥ caraṇe vyapothayat parābhinat dvādaśabhiḥ śilīmukhaiḥ vṛkeṇa bāṇa abhihataḥ apatat kṣitau dvipena devāpṛthu daivāvṛdham abhyapīḍayat sa ca api devāvṛdha sūnuḥ arditaḥ papāta nunnaḥ sahadeva sūnunā viṣāṇa potra apara gātra ghātinā gajena hantum śakuneḥ kuṇinda jaḥ jagāma vegena bhṛśa ardayan ca tam tatas asya gāndhāra patiḥ śiraḥ aharat tatas śatānīka hatāḥ mahā gajāḥ hayāḥ rathāḥ patti gaṇāḥ ca tāvakāḥ suparṇa vāta prahatāḥ yathā nagāḥ tathā gatāḥ gām avaśāḥ vicūrṇitāḥ tatas asya kāyāt nicakarta nākuliḥ śiraḥ kṣureṇa ambuja saṃnibha ānanam tatas śatānīkam avidhyat āśugaiḥ tribhiḥ śitaiḥ karṇa sutaḥ arjunam tribhiḥ tribhiḥ ca bhīmam nakulam ca sapta janārdanam dvādaśabhiḥ ca sāyakaiḥ tat asya karma ati manuṣya karmaṇaḥ samīkṣya hṛṣṭāḥ kuravaḥ abhyapūjayan tatas kirīṭī para vīra ghātī hata aśvam ālokya nara pravīram samīkṣya kṛṣṇam bhṛśa vikṣatam ca tam āpatantam nara vīram ugram mahā āhave bāṇa sahasra dhāriṇam kuru uttamam bāṇa sahasra dhāram sasarjatuḥ śara saṃghān anekān saṃbhrānta rūpau su bhṛśam tadānīm nanāda nādam su mahā anubhāvaḥ viddhvā iva śakram namuciḥ purā vai tathā eva kṛṣṇam navabhiḥ samārdayat punar ca pārtham daśabhiḥ śita agraiḥ pūrvam tathā vṛṣasenena viddhaḥ mahā javaiḥ śvetahayaḥ śaraiḥ taiḥ tatas kirīṭī raṇa mūrdhani kopāt kṛtvā tri śākhām bhrukuṭim lalāṭe mumoca tūrṇam viśikhān mahātmā uvāca karṇam bhṛśam utsmayan tadā duryodhanam drauṇi mukhān ca sarvān aham raṇe vṛṣasenam tam ugram saṃpaśyataḥ karṇa tava adya saṃkhye nayāmi lokam niśitaiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ aham haniṣye bhavatām samakṣam saṃrakṣyatām ratha saṃsthāḥ sutaḥ ayam aham haniṣye vṛṣasenam enam paścāt vadhiṣye tvām api saṃpramūḍham yasya ānayāt eṣa mahān kṣayaḥ abhavat saḥ evam uktvā vinimṛjya cāpam lakṣyam hi kṛtvā vṛṣasenam ājau mumoca bāṇān viśikhān mahātmā vadhāya rājñ sūtaputrasya saṃkhye vivyādha ca enam daśabhiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ marmasu asaktam prasabham kirīṭī sa pārtha bāṇa abhihataḥ papāta rathāt vibāhuḥ viśirāḥ dharāyām su puṣpitaḥ parṇa dharaḥ atikāyaḥ vāta īritaḥ śālaḥ iva adri śṛṅgāt tam prekṣya bāṇa abhihatam patantam rathāt sutam sūtajaḥ kṣiprakārī ratham rathena āśu jagāma vegāt kirīṭinaḥ putra vadha abhitaptaḥ saṃjayaḥ garjantam su mahā kāyam durnivāram suraiḥ api arjunam prāha dāśārhaḥ prahasya puruṣa ṛṣabhaḥ ayam sa rathaḥ āyāti śveta aśvaḥ śalya sārathiḥ paśya ca enam samāyuktam ratham karṇasya pāṇḍava śveta vāji samāyuktam yuktam rādhāsutena ca nānā patākā kalilam kiṅkiṇī jāla mālinam uhyamānam iva ākāśe vimānam pāṇḍuraiḥ hayaiḥ dhvajam ca paśya karṇasya nāga kakṣam mahātmanaḥ paśya karṇam samāyāntam dhārtarāṣṭra priya eṣiṇam śara dhārāḥ vimuñcantam dhārā sāram iva ambudam eṣa madra īśvaraḥ rājā ratha agre paryavasthitaḥ śṛṇu dundubhi nirghoṣam śaṅkha śabdam ca dāruṇam siṃhanādān ca vividhān śṛṇu pāṇḍava sarvaśas antardhāya mahā śabdān karṇena amita tejasā dodhūyamānasya bhṛśam dhanuṣaḥ śṛṇu nisvanam ete dīryanti sa gaṇāḥ pāñcālānām mahā rathāḥ dṛṣṭvā kesariṇam kruddham mṛgāḥ iva mahā vane sa deva asura gandharvān trīn lokān sa carācarān bhīmam ugram mahādevam tryakṣam śarvam kapardinam na śaktāḥ draṣṭum īśānam kim punar yodhitum prabhum tvayā sākṣāt mahādevaḥ sarva bhūta śivaḥ śivaḥ yuddhena ārādhitaḥ sthāṇuḥ devāḥ ca vara dāḥ tava jahi karṇam mahā bāho namucim vṛtrahā yathā dhruvaḥ eva jayaḥ kṛṣṇa mama na asti atra saṃśayaḥ codaya aśvān hṛṣīkeśa ratham mama mahā ratha adya karṇam hatam paśya mad śaraiḥ śakalīkṛtam mām vā drakṣyasi govinda karṇena nihatam śaraiḥ evam bruvan tadā pārthaḥ kṛṣṇam akliṣṭa kāriṇam punar ca āha mahā tejāḥ pārthaḥ kṛṣṇam ariṃdamam codaya aśvān hṛṣīkeśa kālaḥ ayam ativartate evam uktaḥ tadā tena pāṇḍavena mahātmanā jayena saṃpūjya sa pāṇḍavam tadā saṃrambham āgamya param mahātmā kṛṣṇa arjunau sahasā eva abhyadhāvat eka iṣuṇā vṛṣasenasya saṃkhye kopa agninā caturaṅgam dadāha uvāca vṛṣasenam hatam dṛṣṭvā śoka amarṣa samanvitaḥ muktvā śoka udbhavam vāri netrābhyām sahasā vṛṣaḥ yuddhāya amarṣa tāmra akṣaḥ samāhūya dhanaṃjayam tau rathau sūrya saṃkāśau vaiyāghra parivāraṇau śveta aśvau puruṣa ādityau āsthitau ari mardanau śuśubhāte mahātmanau candra ādityau yathā divi tau dṛṣṭvā vismayam jagmuḥ sarva bhūtāni māriṣa hasti kakṣyām ca karṇasya vānaram ca kirīṭinaḥ tau rathau saṃprasaktau ca dṛṣṭvā bhārata pārthivāḥ siṃhanāda ravān cakruḥ sādhuvādān ca puṣkalān śrutvā tu dvairatham tābhyām tatra yodhāḥ samantataḥ ājagmuḥ kuravaḥ tatra vāditra anugatāḥ tadā karṇam praharṣayantaḥ ca śaṅkhān dadhmuḥ ca puṣkalān rādheyam abhitas dadhmuḥ śaṅkhān śata sahasraśas tathā eva pāṇḍavāḥ sarve harṣayantaḥ dhanaṃjayam tūrya śaṅkha ninādena diśaḥ sarvāḥ vyanādayan kṣveḍita āsphoṭita utkruṣṭaiḥ tumulam sarvatas abhavat bāhu ghoṣāḥ ca vīrāṇām karṇa arjuna samāgame tau dṛṣṭvā puruṣa vyāghrau ratha sthau rathinām varau pragṛhīta mahā cāpau śara śakti gadā āyudhau varmiṇau baddha nistriṃśau śveta aśvau śaṅkha śobhinau tūṇīra vara saṃpannau dvau api sma su darśanau siṃha skandha pratīkāśau vyūḍha uraskau mahā balau āśīviṣa sama prakhyau yama kāla antaka upamau yadṛcchayā sameyātām sūryācandramasau iva tau dṛṣṭvā puruṣa vyāghrau śārdūlau iva vegitau babhūva paramaḥ harṣaḥ tāvakānām viśām pate saṃśayaḥ sarva bhūtānām vijaye samapadyata ubhau astrabhṛtām śreṣṭhau ubhau siṃha parākramau ubhau ca sadṛśau yuddhe śambara amararājayoḥ sārathī pravarau ca eva tayoḥ āstām mahā balau tau tu dṛṣṭvā mahā rāja rājamānau mahā rathau siddha cāraṇa saṃghānām vismayaḥ samapadyata dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ tatas karṇam sa balāḥ bharata ṛṣabha tathā eva pāṇḍavāḥ hṛṣṭāḥ dhṛṣṭadyumna purogamāḥ yamau ca cekitānaḥ ca prahṛṣṭāḥ ca prabhadrakāḥ nānādeśyāḥ ca ye śūrāḥ śiṣṭāḥ yuddha abhinandinaḥ te sarve sahitāḥ hṛṣṭāḥ parivavruḥ dhanaṃjayam rirakṣiṣantaḥ śatru ghnāḥ pati aśva ratha kuñjaraiḥ tathā eva tāvakāḥ sarve yattāḥ senā prahāriṇaḥ tāvakānām raṇe karṇaḥ glahe asīt viśām pate tathā eva pāṇḍaveyānām glahaḥ pārthaḥ abhavat yudhi tatra eṣām glahamānānām dhruvau jaya parājayau tābhyām dyūtam samāyattam vijayāya itarasmai vā naḥ paṇḍavānām ca sthitānām raṇa mūrdhani tau ubhau prajihīrṣetām indra vṛtrau iva abhitas bhīma rūpa dharau āstām mahā dhūmau iva grahau tatas antarikṣe sa ākṣepāḥ vivādāḥ bharata ṛṣabha mithas bhedāḥ ca bhūtānām āsan karṇa arjuna antare vyāśrayanta diśaḥ bhinnāḥ sarva lokāḥ ca māriṣa deva dānava gandharvāḥ piśāca uraga rākṣasāḥ dyauḥ āsīt karṇatas vyagrā sa nakṣatrā viśām pate bhūmiḥ viśālā pārthasya mātā putrasya bhārata vṛkṣāḥ ca oṣadhayaḥ tatra vyāśrayanta kirīṭinam asurāḥ yātudhānāḥ ca guhyakāḥ ca paraṃtapa karṇataḥ samapadyanta khecarāṇi vayāṃsi ca hṛṣṭa rūpāḥ samantataḥ munayaḥ cāraṇāḥ siddhāḥ ratnāni nidhayaḥ sarve vedāḥ ca ākhyāna pañcamāḥ sa upaveda upaniṣadaḥ sa rahasyāḥ sa saṃgrahāḥ vāsukiḥ citrasenaḥ ca takṣakaḥ ca upatakṣakaḥ parvatāḥ ca tathā sarve kādraveyāḥ ca sa anvayāḥ viṣavantaḥ mahā roṣāḥ nāgāḥ ca arjunāt abhavan airāvatāḥ saurabheyāḥ vaiśāleyāḥ ca bhoginaḥ īhāmṛgāḥ vyāḍa mṛgāḥ maṅgalyāḥ ca mṛga dvijāḥ maṅgaḷyāḥ paśavaḥ ca eva siṃha vyāghrāḥ tathā eva ca pārthasya vijayam rājan sarve eva abhisaṃśritāḥ vasavaḥ marutaḥ sādhyāḥ rudrāḥ viśve aśvinaḥ tathā karṇāt samapadyanta śva sṛgāla vayāṃsi ca mṛgāḥ ca paśavaḥ ca eva siṃha vyāghrāḥ tathā eva ca viśaḥ śūdrāḥ ca sūtāḥ ca varṇa saṃkara jāḥ ca ye devāḥ tu pitṛbhiḥ sārdham sa gaṇa arjunāt abhavan yamaḥ vaiśravaṇaḥ ca eva varuṇaḥ ca yatas arjunaḥ brahma kṣatram ca yajñāḥ ca dakṣiṇāḥ ca arjunam śritāḥ asurāḥ yātudhānāḥ ca kravyādāḥ ca mṛga aṇḍajāḥ rākṣasāḥ saha yādobhiḥ śva sṛgālāḥ ca karṇāt deva brahma nṛpa ṛṣīṇām gaṇāḥ pāṇḍavataḥ abhavan devarṣi brahmarṣi gaṇāḥ sarve ca khacarāḥ ca ye prāveyāḥ saha mauneyaiḥ gandharva apsarasām gaṇāḥ saha apsarobhiḥ śubhrābhiḥ deva dūtāḥ ca guhyakāḥ kirīṭinam saṃśritāḥ sma puṇya gandhāḥ manoramāḥ amanojñāḥ ca ye gandhāḥ te sarve karṇam āśritāḥ viparītāni aniṣṭāni bhavanti vinaśiṣyatām praviśanti naram kṣipram mṛtyu kāle abhyupāgate te bhāvāḥ sahitāḥ karṇam praviṣṭāḥ sūta nandanam manaḥ tuṣṭiḥ jayaḥ ca api tathā ānandaḥ nṛpa uttama īdṛśāḥ ca nara vyāghra tasmin saṃgrāma sāgare nimittāni ca śubhrāṇi viviśuḥ jiṣṇum āhave ṛṣayaḥ brāhmaṇaiḥ sārdham abhajanta kirīṭinam tatas deva gaṇaiḥ sārdham siddhāḥ ca saha cāraṇaiḥ dvidhā bhūtāḥ mahā rāja vyāśrayanta nara uttamau vimānāni vicitrāṇi guṇavanti ca sarvatas didṛkṣavaḥ samājagmuḥ karṇa arjuna samāgamam antarikṣe mahā rāja deva gandharva rākṣasāḥ evam sarveṣu bhūteṣu dvidhā bhūteṣu bhārata āśaṃsamāneṣu jayam rādheyasya arjunasya ca vimāna ayuta saṃbādham ākāśam abhavat tadā īhāmṛga vyāḍa mṛgaiḥ dvipāḥ ca ratha pattibhiḥ uhyamānāḥ tathā meghaiḥ vāyunā ca manīṣiṇaḥ didṛkṣavaḥ samājagmuḥ karṇa arjuna samāgamam deva dānava gandharvāḥ nāgāḥ yakṣāḥ patatriṇaḥ tapaḥ vidyāḥ tathā oṣadhyaḥ nānā rūpa ambara tviṣaḥ bhavena avasthitaḥ yānam divyam tam deśam abhyayāt sametau tau mahātmanau dṛṣṭvā karṇa dhanaṃjayau jayatām arjunam karṇaḥ iti sūryaḥ abhyabhāṣata dvaipakṣam āsīt devānām asurāṇām tathā eva ca sametau tau mahātmanau dṛṣṭvā karṇa dhanaṃjayau akampanta trayaḥ lokāḥ saha deva ṛṣi cāraṇāḥ sarve deva gaṇāḥ ca eva sarva bhūtāni yāni ca yatas pārthaḥ tatas devāḥ yatas karṇaḥ tatas asurāḥ ratha yūthapayoḥ pakṣau kuru pāṇḍava vīrayoḥ tatas prajāpatiḥ tūrṇam ājagāma mahīpate dvairatham yudhi tam draṣṭum karṇa pāṇḍavayoḥ tadā vijitya karṇaḥ svid imām vasuṃdharām iti īśvarasya api babhūva saṃśayaḥ saṃjayaḥ prajāpatiḥ tu tam dṛṣṭvā deva bhāgam samāgatam ubhau atirathau śūrau ubhau dṛḍha parākramau dṛṣṭvā prajāpatim devāḥ svayambhum upāgaman karṇa arjuna vināśena mā naśyatu akhilam jagant vyajñāpayata deveśam idam matimatām varaḥ pūrvam bhagavatā proktam kṛṣṇayoḥ vijayaḥ dhruvaḥ iti abravīt mahā rāja mahān brahmā prajāpatiḥ brahma īśānau atho vākyam ūcatuḥ tridaśeśvaram khāṇḍave yena hutabhuj uṣitaḥ savyasācinā svargam ca samanuprāpya sāhāyyam śakra te kṛtam karṇaḥ ca dānavaḥ pakṣa atas kāryaḥ parājayaḥ evam kṛte bhavet kāryam devānām eva niścitam ātma kāryam ca sarveṣām garīyaḥ tridaśeśvara vijayaḥ tasya niyatam jāyate na atra saṃśayaḥ toṣitaḥ bhagavant yena mahātmā vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ yasya cakre svayam viṣṇuḥ sārathyam jagantaḥ prabhuḥ manasvī balavān śūraḥ kṛtāstraḥ ca tapodhanaḥ pārthaḥ sarva guṇa upetaḥ deva kāryam idam yatas kliśyante pāṇḍavāḥ nityam vana vāsa ādibhiḥ bhṛśam saṃpannaḥ tapasā ca eva paryāptaḥ puruṣa ṛṣabhaḥ na vidyate vyavasthānam kṛṣṇayoḥ kruddhayoḥ kva cit sraṣṭārau hi asataḥ ca ubhau sataḥ ca puruṣa ṛṣabhau nara nārāyaṇau etau purāṇau ṛṣi sattamau na etayoḥ tu samaḥ kaḥ cit divi vā mānuṣeṣu vā anugamya trayaḥ lokāḥ saha deva ṛṣi cāraṇaiḥ sarva deva gaṇāḥ ca api sarva bhūtāni yāni ca karṇaḥ lokān ayam mukhyān prāpnotu puruṣa ṛṣabhaḥ vīraḥ vaikartanaḥ śūraḥ vijayaḥ tu astu kṛṣṇayoḥ vasūnām ca sa loka tvam marutām vā samāpnuyāt sahitaḥ droṇa bhīṣmābhyām nāka loke mahīyatām kleśitaḥ hi vane pārthaḥ dīrgha kālam pitāmaha pūrvam bhagavatā proktaḥ kṛṣṇayoḥ vijayaḥ dhruvaḥ na uvāca tat jayam tulyam tayoḥ karṇa kirīṭinoḥ tasmāt āśām gataḥ śakraḥ tūṣṇīṃbhūte pitāmahe vijayam pāṇḍaveyasya vadham karṇasya ca āhave iti uktaḥ devadevābhyām sahasrākṣaḥ abravīt vacaḥ āmantrya sarva bhūtāni brahma īśāna anuśāsanāt tat tathā na anyathā tat hi tiṣṭhadhvam gata manyavaḥ iti śrutvā indra vacanam sarva bhūtāni māriṣa na ūcuḥ tadā jayam tulyam tayoḥ puruṣa siṃhayoḥ vyasṛjan ca sugandhīni nānā rūpāṇi khāt tathā puṣpa varṣāṇi vibudhāḥ deva tūryāṇi avādayan didṛkṣavaḥ ca apratimam dvairatham nara siṃhayoḥ yau tau karṇa arjunau rājan prahṛṣṭau abhyatiṣṭhatām samāgatāḥ loka vīrāḥ śaṅkhān dadhmuḥ pṛthak pṛthak vāsudeva arjunau vīrau karṇa śalyau ca bhārata rāhu ketū yathā ākāśe uditau jagantaḥ kṣaye karṇasya āśīviṣa nibhā ratna sāravatī dṛḍhā kapi śreṣṭhaḥ tu pārthasya vyādita āsyaḥ bhayaṃkaraḥ bhīṣayan eva daṃṣṭrābhiḥ durnirīkṣyaḥ raviḥ yathā yuddha abhilāṣukaḥ bhūtvā dhvajaḥ gāṇḍīvadhanvanaḥ nakhaiḥ ca daśanaiḥ ca eva garuḍaḥ pannagam yathā su kiṅkiṇīka ābharaṇā kāla pāśa upama āyasī avidhyat puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ śalyam nayana sāyakaiḥ sa ca api puṇḍarīkākṣam tathā eva abhisamaikṣata tatra ajayat vāsudevaḥ śalyam nayana sāyakaiḥ karṇam ca api ajayat dṛṣṭyā kuntī putraḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ atha abravīt sūtaputraḥ śalyam ābhāṣya sa smitam uvāca praṇayāt rājñ sāma pūrvam idam vacaḥ uvāca yadi karṇa raṇe hanyāt adya tvām śvetavāhanaḥ ubhau eka rathena aham hanyām mādhava pāṇḍavau uvāca tam prahasya abravīt kṛṣṇaḥ pārtham param idam vacaḥ patet divākaraḥ sthānāt śīryeta anekadhā kṣitiḥ hanyām karṇam tathā śalyam bāhubhyām eva saṃyuge iti kṛṣṇa vacaḥ śrutvā prahasan kapiketanaḥ arjunaḥ pratyuvāca idam kṛṣṇam akliṣṭa kāriṇam sa patākā dhvajam karṇam sa śalya ratha vājinam draṣṭāsi adya śaraiḥ karṇam raṇe kṛttam anekadhā adya enam sa ratham sa aśvam sa śakti kavaca āyudham saṃcūrṇitam iva āmarde pādapam paśya dantinā adya rādheya bhāryāṇām vaidhavyam samupasthitam dhruvam svapneṣu aniṣṭāni tābhiḥ dṛṣṭāni mādhava dhruvam adya eva draṣṭāsi vidhavāḥ karṇa yoṣitaḥ na hi me śāmyate vairam kṛṣṇām yat prāhasat purā kṛṣṇām sabhā gatām dṛṣṭvā mūḍhena a dīrghadarśiṇā asmān tathā avahasatā kṣipatā ca punar punar adya draṣṭāsi govinda karṇam unmathitam mayā adya tāḥ madhurāḥ vācaḥ śrotāsi madhusūdana diṣṭyā jayasi vārṣṇeyaḥ iti karṇe nipātite adya abhimanyu jananīm anṛṇaḥ sāntvayiṣyasi kuntīm pitṛṣvasāram ca saṃprahṛṣṭaḥ janārdana adya bāṣpa mukhīm kṛṣṇām sāntvayiṣyasi mādhava vāgbhiḥ ca amṛta kalpābhiḥ dharmarājam yudhiṣṭhiram uvāca brahmarṣi rājarṣi suparṇa juṣṭam babhau viyat vismayanīya rūpam nānadyamānam ninadaiḥ manojñaiḥ vāditra gīta stutibhiḥ ca nṛttaiḥ sarve antarikṣe dadṛśuḥ manuṣyāḥ kha sthān ca tān vismayanīya rūpān tatas prahṛṣṭāḥ kuru pāṇḍu yodhāḥ vāditra pattra āyudha siṃhanādaiḥ nānā aśva mātaṃga ratha ayuta ākulam vara asi śakti ṛṣṭini pāta duḥsaham abhīru juṣṭam hata deha saṃkulam raṇa ajiram lohita raktam ābabhau babhūva yuddham kuru pāṇḍavānām yathā surāṇām asuraiḥ saha abhavat tathā pravṛtte astrabhṛtām parābhave dhanaṃjayaḥ ca ādhirathiḥ ca sāyakaiḥ diśaḥ ca sainyam ca śitaiḥ ajihmagaiḥ parasparam prorṇuvatuḥ sma daṃśitau bhayāt tu tau eva rathau samāśrayan tamonudau khe prasṛtāḥ iva aṃśavaḥ mṛdaṅga bherī paṇava ānaka svanaiḥ ninādite bhārata śaṅkha nisvanaiḥ sa siṃhanādau babhatuḥ nara uttamau śaśāṅka sūryau iva megha samplave didhakṣamāṇau sa carācaram jagat yuga asta sūryau iva duḥsahau raṇe tatas mahā astrāṇi mahā dhanurdharau vimuñcamānau iṣubhiḥ bhayānakaiḥ tatas visasruḥ punar ardayantaḥ śaraiḥ nara uttamābhyām kuru pāṇḍava āśrayāḥ sa nāga patti aśva rathāḥ diśaḥ gatāḥ tathā yathā siṃha bhayāt vanaukasaḥ mahā rathāḥ pañca dhanaṃjaya acyutau śaraiḥ śarīra anta karaiḥ atāḍayan dhanūṃṣi teṣām iṣudhīn hayān dhvajān rathān ca sūtān ca dhanaṃjayaḥ śaraiḥ te pañca vīrāḥ satatam hata āyā rathāḥ nikṛtta deha arjuna bāṇa vegaiḥ atha abhyadhāvan tvaritāḥ śatam rathāḥ śatam ca nāga arjunam ātatāyinaḥ śakāḥ tukhārāḥ yavanāḥ ca sādinaḥ saha eva kāmboja varaiḥ jighāṃsavaḥ vara āyudhān pāṇi gatān karaiḥ saha kṣuraiḥ nyakṛntan tvaritāḥ śirāṃsi ca hayān ca nāgān ca rathān ca yudhyatām dhanaṃjayaḥ śatru gaṇam tam akṣiṇot tadā sa teṣām yudhi savyasācī nāgān hayān ratha sūtān ca tatra śirāṃsi teṣām iṣubhiḥ kirīṭī kṣaṇena sarvam kṣayam āviveśa tatas antarikṣe sura tūrya nisvanāḥ sa sādhuvādāḥ hṛṣitaiḥ samīritāḥ nipetuḥ api uttama puṣpa vṛṣṭayaḥ su rūpa gandhāḥ pavana īritāḥ śivāḥ tat adbhutam deva manuṣya sākṣikam samīkṣya bhūtāni visiṣmiyuḥ nṛpa samīkṣya devāḥ ca nṛrāja mukhyāḥ śaśaṃsu kṛṣṇa arjunayoḥ mahat yaśaḥ atha abravīt droṇa sutaḥ tava ātmajam karam kareṇa pratipīḍya sāntvayan aham tu avadhyaḥ mama ca api mātulaḥ praśādhi rājyam saha pāṇḍavaiḥ ciram vrajantu śeṣāḥ sva purāṇi pārthivāḥ nivṛtta vairāḥ ca bhavantu sainikāḥ na ced hatam śroṣyasi ca eva karṇam vihāya rājyam tu akhilam samastam idam ca dṛṣṭam jagatā saha tvayā kṛtam yat ekena kirīṭamālinā vṛddham pitaram ālokya gāndhārīm ca yaśasvinīm kṛpāluḥ dharmarājaḥ hi yācitaḥ śamam eṣyati bhīmasena arjunau ca ubhau mādrī putrau ca pāṇḍavau vāsudeva mate ca eva pāṇḍavasya ca dhīmataḥ jīvite yatnam ātiṣṭha jīvan bhadrāṇi paśyati rājyam śrīḥ ca eva bhadram te jīvamāne tu kalpyate loka vṛttam idam vṛttam pravṛttam paśya bhārata śāmya tvam pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdham rakṣa śeṣam kulasya ca mā bhūt sa kālaḥ kauravya yadā aham ahitam vacaḥ brūyām kāmam mahā bāho mā avamaṃsthāḥ vacaḥ mama dharmiṣṭham hitam atyantam rājñaḥ ca eva kulasya ca rocatām te nara śreṣṭha mama etat vacanam śubham atas anyathā hi rāja indra vināśaḥ su mahān bhavet tava anuyātrām ca tathā kariṣyati prasīda rājñ jagantaḥ śamāya vai na ca ati tīvram pitṛ vairam udyatam prakāśitam sādhuḥ iha adya pāṇḍavaiḥ mama api mānaḥ paramaḥ sadā tvayi bravīmi atas tvām paramāt ca sauhṛdāt nivārayiṣyāmi hi karṇam api aham yadā bhavān sa praṇayaḥ bhaviṣyati mayā hi pūrvam kathitam kṛpā ādibhiḥ viṣṇuḥ sakhiḥ yasya sakhā na vigrahaḥ karmāṇi yasya akhilāni adbhutāni sarvāṇi vaḥ saṃsmara tāni pūrvam karṇasya putra adhi mā vyanīnaśaḥ tathā hatam drakṣyasi pāṇḍavaiḥ balam atha arjunam kāla sama prabhāvam katham na draṣṭāsi raṇe carantam bhoktā hi rājyam bhuvi dharmasūnuḥ pārthasya pakṣāt yudhi jāta harṣāt vṛkodaram hanmi sa bāndhavam raṇe pratāpataḥ ca upanatam caturvidham tat asti sarvam tvayi pāṇḍaveṣu ca yathā bhavān āha sakhe tathā eva tat mama api ca jñāpayataḥ vacaḥ śṛṇu nihatya duḥśāsanam uktavān bahu prasahya śārdūla vat eṣa durmatiḥ na ca āśvasiṣyanti pṛthā ātmajāḥ mayi vasuṃdharāyāḥ parivartanam bhavet vrajet ca śoṣam makara ālayaḥ arṇavaḥ apām pṛthivyāḥ nabhasaḥ nabhasvataḥ tam evam uktvā abhyanunīya ca asakṛt tava ātmajaḥ svān anuśāsti sainikān samāghnata abhidravata ahitān imān sa bāṇa śabdān kim u joṣam āsyate uvāca āśīviṣau agnim iva utsṛjantau balāhakena iva yathā balāhakaḥ yadṛcchayā vā giriṇā giriḥ yathā śara astra śakti ṛṣṭi gadā asi sarpau pravṛddha śṛṅga druma vīrudh oṣadhī pravṛddha nānāvidha parvata okasau śaraiḥ vibhugna aṅga niyantṛ vāhanaḥ su duḥsahaḥ anyaiḥ paṭu śoṇita udakaḥ bhujāḥ sa vajra aṅgulayaḥ samucchritāḥ sa siṃhanādāḥ hṛṣitaiḥ didṛkṣubhiḥ tatas kurūṇām atha somakānām śabdaḥ mahān prādurabhūt samantāt yadā arjunam sūtaputraḥ aparāhṇe mahā raṇe śoṇita māṃsa kardame chinddhi asya mūrdhānam alam cireṇa śraddhām ca rājyāt dhṛtarāṣṭra sūnoḥ tathā mama bahavaḥ tatra yodhāḥ karṇam tadā yāhi yāhi iti avocan jahi arjunam karṇa tatas sa cīrāḥ punar vanam yāntu cirāya pārthāḥ karṇaḥ atha pūrvam daśabhiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ gāṇḍīvadhanvānam avidhyat āśu jaghāna tam ca api tatas kirīṭī śaraiḥ tathā aṣṭādaśabhiḥ su muktaiḥ tam ca api pārthaḥ daśabhiḥ śita agraiḥ kakṣyā antare tīkṣṇa mukhaiḥ avidhyat karṇaḥ tatas bhārata sāṃparāye jaghāna pārtham navabhiḥ śita agraiḥ dvābhyām kṣurābhyām harim āśukārī samājaghāna tvarayā mahātmā tam pāṇḍavaḥ pañcabhiḥ āyasa agraiḥ ākarṇapūrṇaiḥ nijaghāna karṇam te śoṇitam tasya papuḥ tadānīm kālasya dūtāḥ iva pārtha bāṇāḥ karṇaḥ api pārtham sahavāsudevam parasparam tau viśikhaiḥ su tīkṣṇaiḥ tatakṣatuḥ sūtaputraḥ arjunaḥ ca bhujau ubhau gāṇḍivam ca anumṛjya nārāca nālīka varāhakarṇān kṣurān tathā sa añjalika ardhacandrān pārtha iṣavaḥ karṇa ratham viśantaḥ avāk mukhāḥ pakṣi gaṇāḥ dina ante viśanti keta artham iva āśu vṛkṣam yān arjunaḥ sa bhrukuṭi kaṭākṣaḥ karṇāya rājan asṛjat jita ariḥ kṣiptān kṣiptān pāṇḍavasya iṣu saṃghān tatas karṇaḥ bhārgaveṇa abhisṛṣṭam prāduścakre brāhmam astram mahātmā jaghāna karṇaḥ nara nāga saṃghān mumoca karṇāya sureśvara ātmajaḥ jvālābhiḥ atyartha viniḥsṛtābhiḥ bhūmi antarikṣe ca diśaḥ arka mārgam prāvṛtya dehaḥ asya babhūva dīptaḥ yodhāḥ ca sarve jvalita antara ārtāḥ samīkṣya karṇaḥ jvalana astram udyatam sa vāruṇam tat praśama artham āhave samutsṛjan sūta sutaḥ pratāpavān sa tena vahnim babhūva balāhaka astreṇa diśaḥ tarasvī cakāra sarvān timireṇa saṃvṛtāḥ nītaḥ śamam vahniḥ ati pracaṇḍaḥ vyāptāni sarvāṇi yathā nabhaḥ ca meghaiḥ vṛtā na pradṛśyeta kim cit apāvahat megha gaṇān tatas tān samīraṇa astreṇa samīritena saḥ tatas saḥ astram dayitam devarājñaḥ gāṇḍīva jyām vimṛśan ca ati manyuḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ śatru saṃgha pramāthī tatas kṣura prāñjalikā ardhacandrā nārāca nāḷīka varāhakarṇāḥ gāṇḍīvataḥ prādurāsan su tīkṣṇāḥ sahasraśas vajra samāna vegāḥ pārtha iṣavaḥ karṇa ratham vihaṃgāḥ adhomukhāḥ pakṣi gaṇāḥ dina ante niśāniketa artham iva āśu vṛkṣam jagrāha tān sūtaputraḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ kṣiptān tathā pāṇḍava bāṇa saṃghān dhanaṃjayasya jyotiṣprabhām yadvat udāgataḥ san divākaraḥ nāśayate kṣaṇena pārthasya tān bāṇa gaṇān samagrān te karṇam āsādya mahā prabhāvāḥ su tejanāḥ gārdhra patrāḥ su vegāḥ gātreṣu sarveṣu hayeṣu ca api nirbhidya tūrṇam viviśuḥ su tīkṣṇāḥ tārkṣya trastāḥ bhūmim iva uragāḥ te śara ācita aṅgaḥ rudhira ārdra gātraḥ karṇaḥ tadā roṣa vivṛtta netraḥ ghoṣam prāduścakre bhārgava astram mahātmā mahā indra śastra abhimukhān vimuktān chittvā karṇaḥ pāṇḍavasya iṣu saṃghān jaghāna karṇaḥ nṛ gaja aśva saṃghān amṛṣyamāṇaḥ tu mahā vimarde mahā rathaḥ bhārgava astra prabhāvāt pāñcālānām pravarān ca api yodhān krodha āviṣṭaḥ sūtaputraḥ tarasvī bāṇaiḥ vivyādha āhave su pramuktaiḥ prahasya kṛṣṇau tu nara pravīraḥ tatas pāñcālāḥ somakāḥ ca api rājan karṇena ājau pīḍyamānāḥ śara oghaiḥ krodha āviṣṭāḥ vivyadhuḥ tam samantāt tīkṣṇaiḥ bāṇaiḥ sūtaputram sametāḥ tān astān taiḥ sa nikṛtya āśu bāṇān pāñcālānām ratha nāga aśva saṃghān pāñcālānām pravarān saṃnihatya tatas sa rājan virarāja karṇaḥ śarān vaman meghaḥ iva ambu dhārāḥ karṇasya matvā tu jayam tvadīyāḥ parām mudam siṃhanādān ca cakruḥ karṇena kṛṣṇau iti kaurava indra tat tādṛśam prekṣya mahā rathasya dṛṣṭvā tu karṇena dhanaṃjayasya amṛṣyamāṇaḥ ca mahā vimarde tatra akrudhyat bhīmasenaḥ mahātmā atha abravīt pāṇinā pāṇim āghnan saṃdaṣṭa oṣṭhaḥ nṛtyati vādayan iva vātātmajaḥ pāṇinā pāṇim ārchat amarṣitaḥ niḥśvasan jāta manyuḥ roṣāt pradīptaḥ su mahān vimarde pāṇim sa pāṇau vinipiṣya roṣāt pāñcālānām yodha mukhyān anekān nijaghnivāḥ tava jiṣṇo samakṣam pūrvam daityaiḥ ajitam kālakeyaiḥ sākṣāt sthāṇoḥ bāhu saṃsparśam etya katham nu tvām sūtaputraḥ kirīṭin mahā iṣubhiḥ daśabhiḥ avidhyat agre tvayā kṣiptān ca agrasat bāṇa saṃghān kṛṣṇa a parikleśam anusmara tvam yathā bravīt ṣaṇḍhatilān sma vācaḥ vācaḥ su tīkṣṇa asthi bhidaḥ amanojñāḥ sūta ātmajaḥ ayam gata bhīḥ durātmā saṃsmṛtya sarvam tat iha adya pāpam jahi āśu karṇam yudhi savyasācin kasmāt upekṣām kuruṣe kirīṭin upekṣitum na ayam iha adya kālaḥ yayā dhṛtyā sarva bhūtāni ajaiṣīḥ grāsam dadat vahnaye khāṇḍave tvam tayā dhṛtyā sūtaputram jahi tvam aham vā enam gadayā pothayiṣye sametya pārtham sa nṛśaṃsa vādī jīvan na ayam yāsyati kāla pakvaḥ atha abravīt vāsudevaḥ api pārtham dṛṣṭvā ratheṣūn pratihanyamānān amīmṛdat sarvathā te adya karṇaḥ hi astraiḥ astrāṇi kim idam kirīṭin sa vīra kim muhyasi na avadhīyase nadanti ete kuravaḥ saṃprahṛṣṭāḥ yayā dhṛtyā nihatam tāmasa astram yuge yuge rākṣasāḥ ca api ghorāḥ dambhodbhavāḥ ca asurāḥ ca āhaveṣu tayā dhṛtyā tvam jahi sūtaputram darpa utsiktam vīryam antam kirīṭin karṇam samāsādya ripu pramāthin mayā nisṛṣṭena sudarśanena kirāta rūpī bhagavān yayā ca tvayā mahatyā paritoṣitaḥ abhūt tām tvam dhṛtim vīra punar gṛhītvā saha anubandham jahi sūtaputram tatas mahīm sāgara mekhalām tvam sa pattanām grāmavatīm samṛddhām prayaccha rājñe nihata ari saṃghām yaśaḥ ca pārtha atulam āpnuhi tvam tava astram urvyām pratihatya vīrāḥ dravanti amī sṛñjaya somakāḥ ca dṛṣṭvā ca karṇam samare prahṛṣṭam tvām ca api dṛṣṭvā parihīyamānam saṃcoditaḥ bhīma janārdanābhyām smṛtvā tadā ātmānam avekṣya sattvam prāduṣkaromi eṣa mahā astram ugram śivāya lokasya vadhāya sauteḥ iti sma uktvā pāṇḍavaḥ savyasācī namaskṛtvā brahmaṇe saḥ amita ātmā muktvā śarān meghaḥ iva ambu dhārāḥ samīkṣya karṇena kirīṭinaḥ tu nanu tu āhuḥ veditāram mahā astram brāhmam vidheyam paramam janāḥ tat tatas diśaḥ ca pradiśaḥ ca sarvāḥ samāvṛṇot sāyakaiḥ bhūri tejāḥ divākara aṃśu pratimaiḥ jvaladbhiḥ sasarja bāṇān bharata ṛṣabhaḥ api śataṃśatān eka vat āśu vegān prācchādayan karṇa ratham kṣaṇena yugānta vahni arka kara prakāśāḥ tatas ca śūlāni para svadhāni cakrāṇi nārāca śatāni ca eva bhayena saḥ api āśu papāta bhūmau anyaḥ pranaṣṭaḥ patitam vilokya kṣura prakṛttaḥ patitaḥ dharaṇyām vidhvaṃsayām āsa kirīṭamālī śaraiḥ śarīra anta karaiḥ su ghoraiḥ vaikartanena api tathā āji madhye sahasraśas bāṇa gaṇāḥ visṛṣṭāḥ te ghoṣiṇaḥ pāṇḍavam abhyupeyuḥ parjanya muktāḥ iva vāri dhārāḥ sa bhīmasenam ca janārdanam ca kirīṭinam ca api amanuṣya karmā sa karṇa bāṇa abhihataḥ kirīṭī bhīmam tathā prekṣya janārdanam ca amṛṣyamāṇaḥ punar eva pārthaḥ śarān daśa aṣṭau ca tatas ratha agrāt apatat prabhagnaḥ paraśvadhaiḥ śālaḥ iva abhikṛttaḥ punar ca karṇam tribhiḥ aṣṭabhiḥ ca dvābhyām caturbhiḥ daśabhiḥ ca viddhvā catuḥśatān dviradān sa āyudhīyān hatvā rathān aṣṭaśatam jaghāna sahasram aśvān ca punar ca sādīn aṣṭau sahasrāṇi ca pattivīrān karṇam sa sūtam sa ratha aśva ketum muñca abhividdhya arjunam āśu karṇa bāṇaiḥ purā hanti kurūn samagrān mumoca bāṇān su bahūn abhīkṣṇam te pāṇḍu pāñcāla gaṇān nijaghnuḥ marma chidaḥ śoṇita māṃsa digdhāḥ tau uttamau sarva dhanurdharāṇām mantra auṣadhābhyām virujaḥ viśalyaḥ kṛtaḥ suhṛdbhiḥ bhiṣajām variṣṭhaiḥ dṛṣṭvā mudā sarva bhūtāni anandan aṣṭāṅga vidyā āśramam udvahadbhiḥ ābaddha paṭṭaḥ vraṇa lāghavena yathā sureśaḥ ditijaiḥ kṣata aṅgaḥ dṛṣṭvā āji mukhyau atha yudhyamānau didṛkṣavaḥ śūra varau ari ghnau karṇam ca pārtham ca niyamya vāhān kha sthāḥ mahī sthāḥ ca jana avatasthuḥ sa kārmuka jyā tala saṃnipātaḥ tatas dhanuḥ jyā sahasā atikṛṣṭā su ghoṣam ācchidyata pāṇḍavasya tasmin kṣaṇe sūtaputraḥ tu pārtham samācinot kṣudrakāṇām śatena ṣaṣṭyā nārācaiḥ vāsudevam bibheda tad antaram somakāḥ prādravanta marut sutam ca ayutaśas śara agraiḥ kṛṣṇam ca pārtham ca tathā dhvajam ca pārtha anujān somakān pātayan ca prācchādayan te niśitaiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ jīmūta saṃghāḥ nabhasi iva sūryam vyaṣṭambhayat sūtaputraḥ kṛtāstraḥ jaghāna teṣām ratha vāji nāgān tathā tu sainya pravarān ca rājan abhyardayat mārgaṇaiḥ sūtaputraḥ kruddhena siṃhena yathā aśva yūthyā punar ca pāñcāla varāḥ tathā anye tad antaram karṇa dhanaṃjayābhyām karṇena bāṇaiḥ nihatāḥ prasahya jayam tu matvā vipulam tvadīyāḥ talān nijaghnuḥ siṃhanādān ca neduḥ karṇena kṛṣṇau iti te vineduḥ tatas nava jyām su dṛḍhām kirīṭī sva bāhu vikṣepaṇa jām pragṛhya samādade gāṇḍive kṣiprakārī nimeṣa mātreṇa mahā dhanuṣmān jyā chedanam jyā vidhānam ca tasya pārthasya saṃkhye dviṣatām nihantuḥ pārthaḥ api tām jyām avadhāya tūrṇam su saṃrabdhaḥ karṇa śara kṣata aṅgaḥ raṇe pārthaḥ somakān pratyagṛhṇāt jyām ca anumṛjya abhyahanat talatre bāṇa andhakāram tu akarot kṣaṇena śalyam ca karṇam ca kurūn ca sarvān bāṇaiḥ avidhyat yugapad kirīṭī na pakṣiṇaḥ saṃpatanti antarikṣe kṣepīyasā astreṇa kṛte andhakāre vyuvāha bāṇān avalokayadbhiḥ śalyam ca pārthaḥ daśabhiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ bhṛśam tanutre prahasan avidhyat sa pārtha bāṇāsana vega nunnaiḥ dṛḍha āhataḥ pattribhiḥ ugra vegaiḥ vibhinna gātraḥ kṣataja ukṣita aṅgaḥ karṇaḥ babhau rudraḥ iva ātata iṣuḥ prakrīḍamānaḥ atha śmaśāna madhye śarān tu pañca jvalitān iva uragān pravīrayām āsa jighāṃsuḥ acyute vegena gām āviviśuḥ su vegāḥ snātvā ca karṇa abhimukhāḥ pratīyuḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ te nyapatan pṛthivyām mahā ahayaḥ takṣaka putra pakṣāḥ tatas prajajvāla kirīṭamālī krodhena kakṣam pradahan iva agniḥ tathā vinunna aṅgam avekṣya kṛṣṇam sarpa iṣubhiḥ karṇa bhuja prasṛṣṭaiḥ sa karṇam ākarṇa vikṛṣṭa sṛṣṭaiḥ śaraiḥ śarīra anta karaiḥ jvaladbhiḥ prāduścakāra atha śarān mahātmā śarāḥ tu te kāñcana citra puṅkhāḥ saṃpetuḥ urvyām śataśas mahantaḥ tatas śara oghaiḥ pradiśaḥ diśaḥ ca ravi prabhā karṇa rathaḥ ca rājan adṛśyaḥ āsīt kupite dhanaṃjaye tuṣāra nīhāra vṛtam yathā nabhaḥ sa cakrarakṣān atha pādarakṣān puraḥsarān pṛṣṭhagopān ca sarvān mahā iṣubhiḥ pārtha kara praṇunnaiḥ mahā anubhāvaḥ samare nihantā dvi sāhasrān samare savyasācī kuru pravīrān ṛṣabhaḥ kurūṇām kṣaṇena sarvān sa ratha aśva sūtān nināya rājan kṣayam eka vīraḥ atha apalāyanta vihāya karṇam tava ātmajāḥ kuravaḥ ca avaśiṣṭāḥ hatān avākīrya śara kṣatān ca lālapyamānān tanayān pitṝn ca sarve praṇeśuḥ kuravaḥ vihīnāḥ pārtha iṣubhiḥ saṃparitapyamānāḥ suyodhanena atha punar variṣṭhāḥ pracoditāḥ karṇa ratha anuyāne bhoḥ kṣatriyāḥ śūratamāḥ ca sarve kṣātre ca dharme niratāḥ stha yūyam na yukta rūpam bhavatām samīpāt tava ātmajena api tathā ucyamānāḥ pārtha iṣubhiḥ saṃparitapyamānāḥ na eva avatiṣṭhanta bhayāt vivarṇāḥ kṣaṇena naṣṭāḥ pradiśaḥ diśaḥ ca sa sarvatas prekṣya diśaḥ viśūnyāḥ bhaya avadīrṇaiḥ kurubhiḥ vihīnaḥ uvāca tatas apayātāḥ śara pāta mātram avasthitāḥ kuravaḥ bhinna senāḥ vidyut prakāśam dadṛśuḥ samantāt dhanaṃjaya astram samudīryamāṇam kruddhena pārthena tadā āśu sṛṣṭam vadhāya karṇasya mahā vimarde karṇaḥ su ghora iṣvasanam dṛḍha jyam visphārayitvā visṛjan śara oghān udīryamāṇam sma kurūn dahantam suvarṇa puṅkhaiḥ iṣubhiḥ mahātmā rāmāt upāttena mahā mahimnā ātharvaṇena ari vināśanena anyonyam āsādayatoḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ viṣāṇa ghātaiḥ dvipayoḥ iva ugraiḥ tatas astra saṃghāta samāvṛtam tadā babhūva rājñ tumulam raṇa ajiram tat karṇa pārthau śara vṛṣṭi saṃghaiḥ tat bāṇa jāla eka mayam mahā astram sarve adrākṣuḥ kuravaḥ somakāḥ ca na anyam ca bhūtam dadṛśuḥ tadā te dṛṣṭvā tu tau saṃprati saṃprayuktau parasparam chidra niviṣṭa dṛṣṭī deva ṛṣi gandharva gaṇāḥ sa yakṣāḥ saṃtuṣṭuvuḥ tau pitaraḥ ca hṛṣṭāḥ tau saṃdadhānau aniśam sma rājan dhanurdharāṇām pravarau kṛtāstrau sūta ātmajaḥ abhūt adhikaḥ kadā cid pārthaḥ kadā cit tu adhikaḥ kirīṭī dṛṣṭvā tatas tam yudhi saṃprahāram ghoram tadā durviṣaham raṇe anyaiḥ hṛṣṭāḥ procuḥ saṃghaśas prītimantaḥ padāti saṃghāḥ vasudhām vyakampayan tatas tu pātāla tale rājan tadā khāṇḍava dāha muktaḥ kṛtvā su vegam vasudhā tala sthaḥ saṃdṛśya karṇa arjunayoḥ vimardam saṃcintya tūṇam praviveśa ca eva karṇasya rājan śara rūpa dhārī tatas astra saṃghāta samākulam tadā babhūva jālam vitata aṃśu jālam tat karṇa pārthau śara saṃgha vṛṣṭibhiḥ tad bāṇa jāla eka mayam mahāntam na anyat kim cit dadṛśuḥ saṃpatat vai bāṇa andhakāre tumule atimātram samutkṣepaiḥ vīkṣamāṇau siktau candana vāriṇā śakra sūrya kara abjābhyām pramārjita mukhau ubhau karṇaḥ tu pārtham na viśeṣayat yadā dṛḍham ca pārthena śaraiḥ nipīḍitaḥ tatas sa karṇaḥ śara vikṣata aṅgaḥ sadā arcitam candana cūrṇa śāyinam suvarṇa nālī śayanam mahā viṣam ākarṇapūrṇam pravikṛṣya karṇaḥ pradīptam airāvata vaṃśa saṃbhavam śiraḥ jihīrṣuḥ yudhi phalgunasya mumoca śīghram sa ripu pramāthī ulkāḥ ca ghorāḥ sahasā nipetuḥ hāhākṛtāḥ sarva lokāḥ sa śakrāḥ bāṇe praviṣṭam yoga balena nāgam daśa śata nayanaḥ ahim dṛśya bāṇe praviṣṭam jalaja kusuma yoniḥ śreṣṭha bhāvaḥ ajita ātmā tridaśa patim avocat mā vyadhiṣṭhāḥ jaye śrīḥ sa sūtaputraḥ tam apāṅga deśe avāṅmukham saṃdhayati sma roṣāt na tam sma jānāti mahā anubhāvam apāṅga deśa abhiniviṣṭam ājau na karṇa grīvām iṣuḥ eṣa prāpsyate saṃlakṣya saṃdhatsva śaram śiraḥ ghnam atha abravīt krodha saṃrakta netraḥ karṇaḥ śalyam saṃdhita iṣuḥ prasahya na saṃdhatte dvis śaram śalya karṇaḥ na mādṛśāḥ śāṭhya yuktāḥ bhavanti prāptasya pārthaḥ praṇatāḥ sva svāhāḥ saṃsthāpya kṛṣṇena punar tadīyam saṃdhīyamānam bhujagam dṛṣṭvā karṇena mādhavaḥ ākramya syandanam padbhyām balena balinām varaḥ avagāḍhe rathe bhūmau jānubhyām agaman hayāḥ tatas śaraḥ saḥ abhyahanat kirīṭam tasya dhīmataḥ sa sāyakaḥ karṇa bhuja abhisṛṣṭaḥ hutāśana arka pratimaḥ su ghoraḥ kurvan sīmantam nabhasaḥ bhīma rūpaḥ tam prekṣya dīptam yudhi mādhavaḥ tu tvarā anvitaḥ kaṃsa ripuḥ sa līlam padā viniṣpiṣya ratha uttamam tam prāveśayat jagatīm kiṣku mātram kṣitim gatāḥ jānubhiḥ te tu vāhāḥ tatas śaraḥ saḥ abhyahanat kirīṭam tam āpatantam jvalitam nirīkṣya viyat gatam vṛṣṇi kula pravīraḥ pañcāṅgulam majjayati sma vīraḥ saṃpūjana artham madhusūdanasya divyāḥ ca vācaḥ sahasā babhūvuḥ divyāni puṣpāṇi atha siṃhanādāḥ tasmin tathā vai dharaṇīm nimagne tatas śaraḥ saḥ abhyahanat kirīṭam tasya indra dattam su dṛḍham ca dhīmataḥ atha arjunasya uttama gātra bhūṣaṇam viśrutam divākara indu jvalana graha tviṣam suvarṇa muktā maṇi jāla bhūṣitam puraṃdara artham tapasā prayatnataḥ svayam kṛtam yat bhuvanasya sūnunā mahārha rūpam dviṣatām bhayaṃkaram vibhāti ca atyartha sukham sugandhi tat nijaghnivase deva ripūn sureśvaraḥ svayam dadau yat sumanāḥ kirīṭine hara ambupa ākhaṇḍala vittagoptṛbhiḥ pināka pāśa aśani sāyaka uttamaiḥ kṣatam nayat rudra gaṇaiḥ pinākinā sahāyavān pāvaka saṃnibhaiḥ śaraiḥ ciram dhṛtena aditinā iha rājan sa duṣṭa bhāvaḥ vitatha pratijñaḥ viśuddha jāmbūnada ratna bhūṣitam pārtha uttamāṅgāt aharat tarasvī tat hema jāla avatatam su ghoṣam jājvalyamānam nipapāta bhūmau tatas kirīṭam bahu ratna maṇḍitam jahāra nāgaḥ arjuna mūrdhataḥ balāt mahī viyat dyauḥ salilāni vāyunā yathā vibhinnāni vibhānti bhārata vinā kirīṭam śuśubhe sa pārthaḥ śyāmaḥ yuvā śailaḥ iva asta śṛṅgaḥ vibhāti saṃpūrṇa marīci bhāsvatā śiraḥ gatena udaya parvataḥ yathā suvarṇa puṅkhaiḥ su dṛḍhaiḥ ayasmayaiḥ yama agni daṇḍa pratimaiḥ stanāntare tatas śarāvāpam apāsya sūtajaḥ dṛḍha āhataḥ san ca punar tatas tatas uvāca kim pāṇḍava he pramādyasi na eva āhitānām satatam vipaścitaḥ kṣaṇam pratīkṣanti api durbalīyasām viśeṣataḥ arīn vyasaneṣu tam eka vīram tava ca āhitam sadā tathā yathā śambaram ambarādhipaḥ go karṇā su mukhī kṛtena iṣuṇā go putra saṃpreṣitā dṛṣṭvā go gatakam jahāra mukuṭam go śabda gopūri vai kirīṭam ākṛṣya tathā arjunasya mahā uragaḥ kṛta vairaḥ sa tūrṇam yathā sṛjat pārtha vadhāya karṇaḥ vyāvṛtya tasmāt ca tatas kirīṭāt tam utpatantam sa kirīṭam īkṣya pārthaḥ abravīt vāsudevam mahātmā tam ca api dagdhvā tapanīya citram kirīṭam ākṛṣya tat arjunasya punar sa matvā praviveśa tūṇam pṛṣṭaḥ ca karṇena tatas abravīt idam muktaḥ tvayā aham na samīkṣya karṇa samīkṣya mām muñca raṇe tvam āśu hantāsmi śatrum te ca ātmanaḥ ca tatas sa nāgaḥ prahasan iva āhitam tam abravīt viddhi kṛta āgasam me kṛṣṇa adya mātuḥ vadha jāta vairam nāgaḥ mātā purā hi utpatitā nabhastaḥ tathā api yātā pitṛrāja veśmani karṇaḥ balam samāsthāya jayam bubhūṣet yadi arjunānām śatam eva hanyāt tam āha karṇaḥ punar eva nāgam svayam prāyāt pārtha vadhāya rājan kṛtvā iṣu rūpam vijighāṃsuḥ arjunam tatas abravīt vāsudevam sa pārthaḥ dāśārha kaḥ hi eṣa mahān hi nāgaḥ tvam mā avamaṃsthāḥ kuru me vacaḥ adya nihanmi śatrum te muñca mām tvam tvayā na saṃdhānavatā aham muktaḥ tena api kṛṣṇena ca vañcitaḥ asi vadāmi kṛṣṇasya samakṣam eva eṣaḥ adya hatvā yudhi pāṇḍavānām etat vratam jānamānaḥ prayātu nāgaḥ kim vai kṛtā pāṇḍave te pratijñā karṇaḥ yatnaḥ śarīre yat apāti vīra hantā yadi tvam raṇa mūrdhni pārtham nāgaḥ aham eva haniṣyāmi pārtham ca eva na saṃśayaḥ tatas kṛṣṇaḥ pārtham uvāca saṃkhye mahā uragam kṛta vairam jahi tvam nāga astram aṅge su dṛḍham vimuktam tam utpatantam dvipadām variṣṭhaḥ dṛṣṭvā vacaḥ pārtham uvāca kṛṣṇaḥ mahā uragam pāṇḍava paśya paśya saḥ evam uktaḥ madhusūdanena gāṇḍīvadhanvā ripuṣu ugra dhanvā uvāca kaḥ nu eṣa mama adya nāgaḥ svayam yaḥ āgāt garuḍasya vaktram tatas abravīt vāsudevam mahātmā dāśārha kaḥ nu eṣa mama adya nāgaḥ dhanuḥ cyutaḥ śaraḥ iva śīghra vegaḥ uvāca yaḥ asau tvayā khāṇḍave citrabhānum saṃtarpayānena dhanurdhareṇa tvām adya ca āyāti vadhāya pārtha nabhaḥ cyutām prajvalitām mahā ulkām tatas tu jiṣṇuḥ parihṛtya śeṣān ciccheda ṣaḍbhiḥ niśitaiḥ su dhāraiḥ svayam vibhuḥ pārthiva bhū talāt atha samujjahāra āśu mahā bhujaḥ sa tam ratham bhujābhyām puruṣottamaḥ punar tasmin muhūrte daśabhiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ śilā śitaiḥ barhiṇa vājitaiḥ ca vivyādha karṇaḥ puruṣa pravīram dhanaṃjayam tiryak avekṣamāṇam nārācam āśīviṣa tulya vegam ākarṇapūrṇa āyatam utsasarja karṇasya pītvā rudhiram viveśa vasuṃdharām śoṇita vāja digdhaḥ tatas vṛṣaḥ bāṇa nipāta kopitaḥ mahā uragaḥ daṇḍa vighaṭṭitaḥ yathā tathā āśukārī vyasṛjat śara uttamān mahā viṣaḥ sarpaḥ iva uttamam viṣam saṃchādya bāṇaiḥ sa tu gārdhra pattraiḥ śareṇa ghoreṇa punar ca pāṇḍavam vibhidya karṇaḥ abhyanadat jahāsa ca tam asya harṣam mamṛṣe na pāṇḍavaḥ bibheda marmāṇi tatas asya marma vid tatas śarāṇām navatīḥ nava arjunaḥ sasarja karṇe antaka daṇḍa saṃnibhāḥ purā ruṣā gotra samūha bhidyatā maṇi praveka uttama vajra hāṭakaiḥ alaṃkṛtam ca asya varāṅga bhūṣaṇam su dīrgha kālena tat asya pāṇḍavaḥ kṣaṇena bāṇaiḥ bahudhā vyaśātayat tasya iṣubhiḥ khaṇḍita kuṇḍala antar parikṣataḥ ca abhyadhikam tadānīm sa lohita aṅga śravaṇaḥ cakāśe sa lohitāṅga śravaṇaḥ yathā divi sa tam vivarmāṇam atha uttama iṣubhiḥ śaraiḥ caturbhiḥ kupitaḥ parābhinat dṛḍha āhataḥ pattribhiḥ ugra vegaiḥ pārthena karṇaḥ vividhaiḥ śita agraiḥ sa aśvam tu karṇam sa ratham kirīṭī samācinot bhārata vatsadantaiḥ pracchādayām āsa diśaḥ ca bāṇaiḥ sarva prayatnāt tapanīya puṅkhaiḥ sa vatsadantaiḥ pṛthu pīna vakṣāḥ samācitaḥ sma ādhirathiḥ vibhāti su puṣpita aśoka palāśa śālmaliḥ yathā acalaḥ spandana candana āyutaḥ śaraiḥ śarīre bahudhā samarpitaiḥ vibhāti karṇaḥ samare viśām pate mahīruhaiḥ ācita sānu kandaraḥ yathā mahā indraḥ śubha karṇikāravān sa bāṇa saṃghān dhanuṣā vyavāsṛjan vibhāti karṇaḥ śara jāla raśmivān bāhu antarāt ādhiratheḥ vimuktān bāṇān mahā ahīn iva dīpyamānān vyadhvaṃsayan arjuna bāhu muktāḥ śarāḥ samāsādya diśaḥ śita agrāḥ tatas sa karṇaḥ samavāpya dhairyam bāṇān vimuñcan kupita ahi kalpān vivyādha pārtham daśabhiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ kṛṣṇam ca ṣaḍbhiḥ kupita ahi kalpaiḥ mahā śaram sarpa viṣa anala upamam mahā āhave kṣeptu manāḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ kālaḥ hi adṛśyaḥ nṛpa vipra śāpān nidarśayan karṇa vadham bruvāṇaḥ brāhmam mahā astram manasi pranaṣṭam śāpāt tadā brāhmaṇa sattamasya na ca asya ghoram pratibhāti ca astram yathā asya kālaḥ mṛtyupatiḥ vyatiṣṭhat śāpāt tadā brāhmaṇa sattamasya prāptam vadham śaṃsati ca api atha astram praṇaśyamānam dvijamukhya śāpāt ghūrṇe rathe brāhmaṇasya abhiśāpāt rāmāt upātte ca astre pārthena tasmin viṣasāda karṇaḥ a mṛṣyamāṇaḥ vyasanāni tāni hastau vidhunvan sa vigarhamāṇaḥ cartum yathāśakti yathāśrutam ca evam bruvan praskhalita aśva sūtaḥ vicālyamānaḥ arjuna śastra pātaiḥ stanāntare kṛṣṇa dhanaṃjayau saḥ indra aśani samān ghorān asṛjat pāvaka upamān kampita ātmā tathā karṇaḥ śaktyā ceṣṭām adarśayat gāṇḍīvam jyām ca bāṇān ca anumantrya dhanaṃjayaḥ asṛjat śara varṣāṇi varṣāṇi iva puraṃdaraḥ tatas tejaḥ mayāḥ bāṇāḥ rathāt pārthasya niḥsṛtāḥ prādurāsan mahā vīryāḥ karṇasya ratham antikāt tān karṇaḥ tu agratas abhyastān moghān cakre mahā rathaḥ tatas abravīt vṛṣṇi vīraḥ tasmin astre vināśite visṛja astram param pārtha rādheyaḥ grasate śarān chādayitvā tatas bāṇaiḥ karṇam prabhrāmya ca arjunaḥ tasya karṇaḥ śaraiḥ kruddhaḥ ciccheda jyām su tejanaiḥ dvitīyām ca tṛtīyām ca caturthīm pañcamīm tathā ṣaṣṭhīm atha asya ciccheda saptamīm ca tathā aṣṭamīm navamīm daśamīm ca asya tathā ca ekādaśīm vṛṣaḥ jyā śatam śata saṃdhānaḥ sa karṇaḥ na avabudhyate tatas jyām avadhāya anyām anumṛjya ca pāṇḍavaḥ śaraiḥ avākirat karṇam dīpyamānaiḥ sahasraśas tasya jyā chedanam karṇaḥ jyā avadhānam ca saṃyuge tatas kṛṣṇaḥ arjunam dṛṣṭvā karṇa astreṇa abhipīḍitam tatas anyam agni sadṛśam śaram sarpa viṣa upamam raudram astram samādāya kṣeptu kāmaḥ kirīṭavān tatas avatīrya rādheyaḥ rathāt āśu samudyataḥ cakram bhujābhyām ālambya samutkṣeptum iyeṣa saḥ saptadvīpā vasumatī sa śaila vana kānanā gīrṇa cakrā samutkṣiptā karṇena catur aṅgulam bho bho pārtha mahā iṣvāsa muhūrtam paripālaya saḥ abravīt arjunam ca api muhūrtam kṣama pāṇḍavaiḥ madhye cakram avagrastam dṛṣṭvā daivāt idam mama pārtha kāpuruṣa ācīrṇam abhisaṃdhim vivarjaya na tvam kāpuruṣa ācīrṇam mārgam āsthātum arhasi viśiṣṭataram eva tvam kartum arhasi pāṇḍava prakīrṇa keśe vimukhe brāhmaṇe ca kṛtāñjalau a bāṇe bhraṣṭa kavace bhraṣṭa bhagna āyudhe tathā na śūrāḥ praharanti ājau na rājñe pārthivāḥ tathā na vimuñcanti śastrāṇi śūrāḥ sādhu vrate sthitāḥ tvam ca śūratamaḥ loke sādhu vṛttaḥ ca pāṇḍava abhijñaḥ yuddha dharmāṇām tasmāt kṣama mama kṣaṇam na vāsudevāt tvattaḥ vā pāṇḍaveya bibhemi aham smṛtvā tu dharmam śūrāṇām muhūrtam pratipālaya tvam hi kṣatriya dāyādaḥ mahā kula vivardhanaḥ smṛtvā dharma upadeśam tvam muhūrtam kṣama pāṇḍava yāvat karomi sajjam matimatām vara uvāca dharme hi gṛddhāḥ satatam hi pārthāḥ prāyeṇa nīcāḥ vyasaneṣu magnāḥ nindanti daivam kukṛtam na tat tat yat draupadīm eka vastrām sabhāyām ānāyya tvam ca eva suyodhanaḥ ca duḥśāsanaḥ śakuniḥ saubalaḥ ca na te karṇa pratyabhāt tatra dharmaḥ yadā sabhāyām kaunteyam an akṣa jñam yudhiṣṭhiram akṣa jñaḥ śakuniḥ jetā tadā dharmaḥ kva te gataḥ yat vāraṇāvate pārthān suptān jatu gṛhe tadā yadā rajasvalām kṛṣṇām duḥśāsana vaśe sthitām sabhāyām prāhasaḥ karṇa kva te dharmaḥ tadā gataḥ yat anāryaiḥ purā kṛṣṇām kliśyamānām anāgasam vinaṣṭāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ kṛṣṇe śāśvatam narakam gatāḥ patim anyam vṛṇīṣva iti vadan tvam gaja gāminīm rājya lubdhaḥ punar karṇa samāhvayasi pāṇḍavam gāndhāra rājam āśritya kva te dharmaḥ tadā gataḥ parivārya raṇe bālam kva te dharmaḥ tadā gataḥ kim sarvathā tālu viśoṣaṇena punar yathā rājyam avāpa vīryāt prāptāḥ tathā pāṇḍavāḥ bāhu vīryāt sarve samastāḥ parivṛtta lobhāḥ tathā gatāḥ dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ vināśam dharma abhiguptaiḥ satatam nṛ siṃhaiḥ uvāca yodhayām āsa vai pārtham mahā vega parākramaḥ manyuḥ abhyāviśat tīvraḥ smṛtvā tat tat dhanaṃjayam tam samīkṣya tatas karṇaḥ brahmāstreṇa dhanaṃjayam brahmāstreṇa eva tam pārthaḥ vavarṣa śara vṛṣṭibhiḥ tat astram astreṇa āvārya prajahāra asya pāṇḍavaḥ vāruṇena tatas karṇaḥ śamayām āsa pāvakam jīmūtaiḥ ca diśaḥ sarvāḥ cakre timira durdināḥ pāṇḍaveyaḥ tu asambhrāntaḥ vāyavya astreṇa vīryavān apovāha tadā abhrāṇi rādheyasya prapaśyataḥ tatra adbhutam bhārata sūtaputraḥ vivyādha ca enam daśabhiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ babhūva kopena bhṛśam pradīptaḥ ghṛta avasiktaḥ sadasi iva vahniḥ tatas śaram mahā ghoram jvalantam iva pāvakam ādade pāṇḍu putrasya sūtaputraḥ jighāṃsayā cacāla pṛthivī rājan sa śaila vana kānanā vavau sa śarkaraḥ vāyuḥ diśaḥ ca rajasā vṛtāḥ hāhākāraḥ ca saṃjajñe surāṇām divi bhārata tam iṣum saṃdhitam dṛṣṭvā sūtaputreṇa māriṣa viṣādam paramam jagmuḥ pāṇḍavāḥ dīna cetasaḥ śakra aśani prakhya ruciḥ śita agraḥ sa gāḍha viddhaḥ samare mahātmā vighūrṇamānaḥ ślatha hasta gāṇḍivaḥ tad antaram prāpya vṛṣaḥ mahā rathaḥ rathāṅgam urvī gatam ujjihīrṣuḥ śaśāka daivāt na mahā balaḥ api tatas kirīṭī pratilabhya saṃjñām jagrāha bāṇam yama daṇḍa kalpam dīptaḥ arjunaḥ prāñjalikam mahātmā chinddhi asya mūrdhānam areḥ śareṇa na yāvat ārohati vai ratham vṛṣaḥ tatas kṣuram prajvalitam pragṛhya jaghāna kakṣām amala arka varṇām tam hasti kakṣyā pravaram ca bāṇaiḥ suvarṇa muktā maṇi vajra mṛṣṭam tatas kṣureṇa ādhiratheḥ kirīṭī suvarṇa puṅkhena śitena yattaḥ yaśaḥ ca dharmaḥ ca jayaḥ ca māriṣa priyāṇi sarvāṇi ca tena ketunā tadā kurūṇām hṛdayāni ca apatan babhūva hāhā iti ca nisvanaḥ mahān dṛṣṭvā dhvajam tam patitam pṛthivyām kuru pravīreṇa nikṛttam āśu jayam janāḥ bhārata ye tvadīyāḥ ādatta pārthaḥ añjalikam niṣaṅgāt sahasraraśmeḥ iva raśmim uttamam marma chidam śoṇita māṃsa digdham vaiśvānara arka pratimam mahārham nara aśva nāga asu haram tri aratnim ṣaṣ vājam añjas gatim ugra vegam pināka nārāyaṇa cakra saṃnibham bhayaṃkaram prāṇabhṛtām vināśanam jagrāha pārthaḥ tam ati prahṛṣṭaḥ saṃpūjitaḥ yaḥ satatam mahātmā deva asurān yaḥ vijayet mahā iṣuḥ yam vai prakṛṣṭam prasamīkṣya yuddhe svasti jagat syāt ṛṣayaḥ pracukruśuḥ gāṇḍīvadhanvā dhanuṣi nyayojayat yuktvā mahā astreṇa pareṇa mantra vid vikṛṣya gāṇḍīvam uvāca sa svanam ayam mahā astraḥ apratimaḥ dhṛtaḥ śaraḥ śarīra bhid ca asu haraḥ ca durhṛdaḥ tapaḥ asti taptam guravaḥ ca toṣitāḥ mayā yat iṣṭam suhṛdām tathā śrutam anena satyena nihantu ayam śaraḥ su daṃśitaḥ karṇam arim mama ajitaḥ dharma ātmā satya saṃdhaḥ ca dharmarājaḥ dayā paraḥ iti ūcivān tam sa mumoca bāṇam dhanaṃjayaḥ karṇa vadhāya ghoram kṛtyām atharva āṅgirasīm iva ugrām dīptām asahyām yudhi mṛtyunā api bruvan kirīṭī tam ati prahṛṣṭaḥ ayam śaraḥ me vijaya āvahaḥ astu jighāṃsuḥ arka indu sama prabhāvaḥ karṇam samāptim nayatām yamāya prajvālayām āsa diśaḥ nabhaḥ ca tena iṣu varyeṇa kirīṭamālī prahṛṣṭa rūpaḥ vijaya āvahena gāṇḍīva muktaiḥ vijayena bhallaiḥ chinnam papāta añjalikena tūrṇam kāyaḥ asya paścāt dharaṇīm jagāma śara uttamena añjalikena rājan atha asya kāyaḥ nipapāta paścāt śareṇa karṇasya śiraḥ jahāra varāṅgam urvyām apatat camū pateḥ divākaraḥ astāt iva rakta maṇḍalaḥ pareṇa kṛcchreṇa śarīram atyajat gṛham mahā ṛddhi iva sa saṅgam īśvaraḥ dehāt tu karṇasya nipātitasya tejaḥ dīptam kham vigāhya acireṇa tatas śaṅkhān pāṇḍavāḥ dadhmuḥ uccais dṛṣṭvā karṇam pātitam phālgunena tathā eva kṛṣṇaḥ ca dhanaṃjayaḥ ca hṛṣṭau tadā dadhmatuḥ āśu śaṅkhau atha antarikṣe api vigāhya sūryam hṛta uttamāṅgam ca śarīram ājau papāta karṇasya śara avakīrṇam tam somakāḥ prekṣya hatam śayānam prītāḥ nādam saha sainyaiḥ akurvan tūryāṇi ca ājaghnuḥ atīva hṛṣṭāḥ vāsāṃsi ca eva ādudhuvuḥ bhujān ca pārtham samājagmuḥ atīva hṛṣṭāḥ bala anvitāḥ ca api apare hi anṛtyan anyonyam āśliṣya nadantaḥ ūcuḥ dṛṣṭvā tu karṇam bhuvi niṣṭanantam hatam rathāt sāyakena avabhinnam mahā anilena agnim iva apaviddham yajña avasāne śayane niśā ante rarāja karṇasya śara avakīrṇaḥ sva raśmi jātau atataḥ yathā arkaḥ pratāpya senām khalu pāṇḍavām raṇe śara aṃśubhiḥ pāvaka tulya dīptibhiḥ kirīṭi kālena tu vyanīyata astam divasa avasāne tat ānanam sūtapurasya rājan śaraiḥ ācita sarva aṅgaḥ śoṇita ogha pariplutaḥ vibhāti dehaḥ karṇasya sva raśmibhiḥ iva aṃśumant pratāpya senām āmitrām dīptaiḥ śara gabhastibhiḥ balinā arjuna kālena nītaḥ astam karṇa bhāskaraḥ evam jīvitam ādāya karṇasya iṣuḥ jagāma ha aparāhṇe parāhṇasya sūtaputrasya māriṣa upari upari sainyānām tasya śatroḥ tat añjasā tat śiraḥ bharata śreṣṭha śobhayām āsa medinīm yadṛcchayā mahā rāja ādityaḥ iva gām gataḥ tam dṛṣṭvā samara vimarda labdha nidram daṣṭa uṣṭham rudhira parīta kātara akṣam rādheyam
