ratha vara pṛṣṭha saṃniṣaṇṇam hīna aṃśuḥ divasakaraḥ muhūrtam āsīt niḥśabda tūryam hata yaudha mukhyam praśānta darpam dhṛtarāṣṭra sainyam na śobhate sūryasutena hīnam vṛndam grahāṇām iva candra hīnam uvāca karṇam tu śūram patitam pṛthivyām śara ācitam śoṇita digdha gātram dṛṣṭvā śayānam bhuvi madra rājaḥ chinna dhvajena apayayau rathena karṇe hate kuravaḥ prādravanta bhaya arditāḥ gāḍha viddhāḥ ca saṃkhye avekṣamāṇāḥ muhur arjunasya dhvajam mahāntam vapuṣā jvalantam gāḍha viddhāḥ ca saṃkhye te bāṇaiḥ gāṇḍīvadhanvanā avekṣamāṇāḥ pārthasya dhvajam bhīṣaṇa vānaram pratīpa sainya hantāram prādravan te diśaḥ daśa vaikartane dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ sa śalyāḥ avekṣamāṇāḥ muhur arjunasya ketum mahāntam yaśasā jvalantam vyūḍha uraskam kamala nayanam tapta hema avabhāsam karṇam dṛṣṭvā bhuvi nipatitam pārtha bāṇa abhitaptam pāṃsu grastam malinam asakṛt putram anvīkṣamāṇaḥ uvāca śalyaḥ tu karṇa arjunayoḥ vimarde balāni dṛṣṭvā mṛditāni bāṇaiḥ duryodhanam yāntam avekṣamāṇaḥ saṃdarśayat bhārata yuddha bhūmim ye somaka pāṇḍavaiḥ ca helīkṛtaḥ sṛñjaya somakaiḥ ca śalyaḥ tu karṇe nihate kirīṭinā trastam balam prasamīkṣya ārta rūpam nipātita syandana vāji nāgam dṛṣṭvā balam tat hata sūtaputram uvāca babhūva rūpam kuru sṛñjayānām karṇam tu śūram patitam pṛthivyām śara ācitam śoṇita digdha gātram yadṛcchayā sūryam iva avani stham didṛkṣavaḥ saṃparivārya tasthuḥ prahṛṣṭa vitrasta viṣaṇṇa vismṛtāḥ tathā apare śoka gatāḥ iva abhavan pare tvadīyāḥ ca paraspareṇa yathā yathā eṣām prakṛtiḥ tathā abhavan niśamya karṇam kuravaḥ pradudruvuḥ hata ṛṣabhāḥ gāvaḥ iva a kula ākulāḥ nādam kṛtvā rodasī kampayānaḥ hate karṇe trāsayan dhārtarāṣṭrān tathā eva rājan somakāḥ sṛñjayāḥ ca śaṅkhān dadhmuḥ sasvajuḥ ca api sarve parasparam kṣatriyāḥ hṛṣṭa rūpāḥ sūta ātmaje nihate vai tadānīm kṛtvā vimardam bhṛśam arjunena karṇam hatam kesariṇā iva nāgam tīrṇā pratijñā puruṣa ṛṣabheṇa vairasya antam gatavan ca api pārthaḥ dṛṣṭvā śayānam bhuvi madra rājaḥ bhītaḥ apasarpat sa rathaḥ su śīghram madra adhipaḥ ca api vimūḍha cetāḥ tūrṇam rathena apahṛta dhvajena duryodhanasya antikam etya śīghram saṃbhāṣya duḥkha ārtam uvāca vākyam viśīrṇa nāga aśva ratha pravīram balam yama rāṣṭra kalpam anyonyam āsādya hatam mahadbhiḥ nara aśva nāgaiḥ giri kūṭa kalpaiḥ na etādṛśam bhārata yuddham āsīt yathā adya karṇa arjunayoḥ babhūva daivam tu yat tat sva vaśam pravṛttam tat pāṇḍavān pāti hinasti ca asmān kubera vaivasvata vāsavānām tulya prabhāva ambu pateḥ ca vīrāḥ avadhya kalpāḥ nihatāḥ narendrāḥ tava artha kāmāḥ yudhi pāṇḍaveyaiḥ etat vacaḥ madra pateḥ niśamya svam ca apanītam manasā nirīkṣya duryodhanaḥ dīna manāḥ visaṃjñaḥ punar punar nyaśvasat ārta rūpaḥ uvāca dṛṣṭvā tu sainyam vinivartyamānam saṃtrasta rūpaḥ parimūḍha cetāḥ duryodhanam vākyam idam babhāṣe uvāca babhūva rūpam kuru sṛñjayānām uvāca śṛṇu rājan avahitaḥ yathā vṛttaḥ mahā kṣayaḥ ghoraḥ manuṣya dehānām ājau nara vara kṣayaḥ na saṃdhātum anīkāni na ca eva atha parākrame vaṇijaḥ naau bhinnāyām agādhe hi aplavāḥ yathā apāre pāram icchantaḥ hate dvīpe kirīṭinā sūtaputre hate rājan vitrastāḥ śara vikṣatāḥ anāthāḥ nātham icchantaḥ mṛgāḥ siṃhaiḥ iva arditāḥ bhagna śṛṅgāḥ iva vṛṣāḥ bhagna daṣṭrāḥ iva uragāḥ pratyapāyāma sāyāhne nirjitāḥ savyasācinā hata pravīrāḥ vidhvastāḥ nikṛttāḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ viśastra kavacāḥ sarve kāṃdiśīkāḥ vicetasaḥ anyonyam avamṛdnantaḥ vīkṣyamāṇāḥ bhaya arditāḥ mām eva tūrṇam bībhatsuḥ mām eva ca vṛkodaraḥ abhiyāti iti manvānāḥ petuḥ mamluḥ ca saṃbhramāt hayān anye rathān anye gajān anye mahā rathāḥ āhatya java saṃpannāḥ pādātāḥ prādravan bhayāt kuñjaraiḥ syandanāḥ kṣuṇṇāḥ sādinaḥ ca mahā rathaiḥ padāti saṃghāḥ ca aśva oghaiḥ palāyadbhiḥ bhaya arditāḥ vyāla taskara saṃkīrṇe sārtha hīnāḥ yathā vane hata ārohāḥ tathā nāgāḥ chinna hastāḥ tathā narāḥ sarvam pārtha mayam lokam saṃpaśyantaḥ bhaya āturāḥ tān prekṣya dravataḥ sarvān bhīmasena bhaya arditān na atikramiṣyate pārthaḥ dhanuṣpāṇiḥ vyavasthitaḥ jaghanye eva sainyānām śanais aśvān acodayat jaghanye yudhyamānam hi kaunteyaḥ mām na saṃśayaḥ adya arjunam sa govindam māninam ca vṛkodaram nihatya śiṣṭān śatrūn ca karṇasya ānṛṇyam āpnuyām tat śrutvā kururājasya śūra artha sadṛśam vacaḥ sūtaḥ hema paricchannān śanais aśvān acodayat ratha aśva gaja hīnāḥ tu pādātāḥ te māriṣa pañcaviṃśati sāhasrāḥ yuddhāya eva vyavasthitāḥ tān bhīmasenaḥ saṃkruddhaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ ca pārṣataḥ pārtha pārṣatayoḥ ca anye jagṛhuḥ tatra nāmanī saḥ avatīrya rathāt tūrṇam gadā pāṇiḥ ayudhyata na tān ratha sthaḥ bhūmiṣṭhān dharma apekṣī vṛkodaraḥ yodhayām āsa kaunteyaḥ bhuja vīryam upāśritaḥ jātarūpa paricchannām pragṛhya mahatīm gadām avadhīt tāvakān sarvān daṇḍa pāṇiḥ iva antakaḥ padātinaḥ api saṃrabdhāḥ tyaktvā jīvitam ātmanaḥ āsādya bhīmasenam tu saṃrabdhāḥ yuddha durmadāḥ vineśuḥ sahasā dṛṣṭvā bhūta grāmāḥ iva antakam pañcaviṃśati sāhasrān tāvakānām apothayat hatvā tat puruṣa anīkam bhīmaḥ satya parākramaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnam puraskṛtya punar tasthau mahā balaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ api ca mahān amitra gaṇa mardanaḥ vipralīnān ratha aśvena padātīyān samantataḥ pañcaviṃśati sāhasrān avadhīt niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ śaraiḥ nikṛttāḥ samare dhṛṣṭadyumnena tāvakāḥ pañcaviṃśati sāhasrāḥ kālam ārchan padātayaḥ hatvā tat puruṣa anīkam dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ mahā balaḥ tam pārāvata varṇa aśvam kruddham kruddha antaka upamam dhṛṣṭadyumnam raṇe dṛṣṭvā tvadīyāḥ prādravan bhayāt mādrī putrau tu śakunim sātyakiḥ ca mahā rathaḥ javena abhyapatan hṛṣṭāḥ nighnantaḥ saubalam balam tasya aśvavārān su bahūn vinihatya śitaiḥ śaraiḥ viśrutam triṣu lokeṣu vyākṣipat gāṇḍivam dhanuḥ kṛṣṇasārathim āyāntam dṛṣṭvā śveta hayam ratham arjunam ca api yoddhāram tvadīyāḥ prādravan bhayāt viprahīnāḥ ratha aśvena gajaiḥ ca parivarjitāḥ pañcaviṃśati sāhasrāḥ kālam ārchan padātayaḥ hatvā tat puruṣa anīkam pāñcālānām mahā rathaḥ putraḥ pāñcāla rājasya dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ mahā rathaḥ mahā dhanurdharaḥ śrīmān amitra gaṇa sūdanaḥ pārāvata savarṇa aśvam kovidāra mahā dhvajam dhṛṣṭadyumna ratham dṛṣṭvā prādravanta bhayāt bhṛśam gāndhāra rājam śīghra astram anusṛtya yaśasvinau na cirāt pratyadṛśyetām mādrī putrau sa sātyakī cekitānaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca draupadeyāḥ ca māriṣa hatvā tvadīyam su mahat sainyam śaṅkhān atha adhaman te sarve tāvakān prekṣya dravamāṇān parāṅmukhān abhyadravan jighāṃsantaḥ vṛṣān jitvā yathā vṛṣāḥ senā avaśeṣam tam dṛṣṭvā tava sainyam parāṅmukham viśrutam triṣu lokeṣu vyākṣipat gāṇḍivam dhanuḥ tatas etān śaraiḥ rājan sahasrān samavārayan anya kārīkṛte loke śara bhūte mahī tale diśaḥ sarvāḥ mahā rāja tāvakāḥ prādravan bhayāt bhajyamāneṣu sainyeṣu kururājaḥ viśām pate tatas duryodhanaḥ sarvān ājuhāva atha pāṇḍavān yuddhāya bharata śreṣṭha devān iva purā baliḥ duryodhanaḥ api asambhrāntaḥ tān arīn niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ yat enam pāṇḍavāḥ sarve na śekuḥ ativartitum na ati dūra apayātam tu kṛta buddhim palāyane na tam deśam prapaśyāmi pṛthivyām parvateṣu ca yatra yātān na vaḥ hanyuḥ pāṇḍavāḥ kim sṛtena vaḥ alpam ca balam eteṣām kṛṣṇau ca bhṛśa vikṣatau viprayātān ca naḥ bhinnān pāṇḍavāḥ kṛta kilbiṣāḥ sukham sāṃgrāmikaḥ mṛtyuḥ kṣatra dharmeṇa yudhyatām mṛtaḥ duḥkham na jānīte pretya ca ānantyam aśnute śṛṇudhvam kṣatriyāḥ sarve yāvantaḥ stha samāgatāḥ yadā śūram ca bhīrum ca mārayati antakaḥ yamaḥ kaḥ nu mūḍhaḥ na yudhyeta mādṛśaḥ kṣatriya vrataḥ acireṇa hatāḥ lokam sarve yodhāḥ samāpnuta evam bruvati te putre sainikāḥ bhṛśa vikṣatāḥ tam dhyāna mūkam kṛpaṇam bhṛśa ārtam ārtāyaniḥ dīnam uvāca vākyam śara avabhinnaiḥ patitaiḥ ca vājibhiḥ śvasadbhiḥ anyaiḥ kṣatajam vamadbhiḥ dīnaiḥ stanadbhiḥ parivṛtta netraiḥ mahīm daśadbhiḥ kṛpaṇam nadadbhiḥ nara aśva nāgaiḥ ca rathaiḥ ca marditaiḥ mahī mahā vaitaraṇī iva durdṛśā viśīrṇa dantaiḥ kṣatajam vamadbhiḥ sphuradbhiḥ ārtaiḥ karuṇam raṇa ajire prakīrṇa tūṇīra patāka ketubhiḥ suvarṇa jāla avatataiḥ bhṛśa āhataiḥ saṃyantṛ yodha ācaraṇaiḥ mahā gajaiḥ viśīrṇa varma ābharaṇa ambara āyudhaiḥ vṛtā niśāntaiḥ iva pāvakaiḥ mahī śara prahāra abhihataiḥ mahā balaiḥ avekṣyamāṇaiḥ patitaiḥ sahasraśas pranaṣṭa saṃjñaiḥ punar ucchvasadbhiḥ mahī babhūva anugataiḥ iva agnibhiḥ karṇa arjunābhyām śara bhinna gātraiḥ hataiḥ pravīraḥ kuru sṛñjayānām śarāḥ tu karṇa arjuna bāhu muktāḥ vidārya nāga aśva manuṣya dehān prāṇān nirasya āśu mahīm atīyuḥ mahā uragāḥ vāsam iva abhitas astraiḥ rathaiḥ vara iṣūn mathitaiḥ ca yodhaiḥ saṃsyūta sūta aśva vara āyudha dhvajaiḥ viśīrṇa śastraiḥ vinikṛtta bandhuraiḥ nikṛtta cakra akṣa yuga triveṇubhiḥ prabhagna nīḍaiḥ maṇi hema maṇḍitaiḥ stṛtā mahī dyauḥ iva śāradaiḥ ghanaiḥ manuṣya mātaṃga ratha aśva rāśibhiḥ drutam vrajantaḥ bahudhā vicūrṇitāḥ sa hema paṭṭāḥ parighāḥ paraśvadhāḥ kaḍaṅgara ayaḥ musalāni paṭṭiśāḥ petuḥ ca khaḍgāḥ vimalāḥ vikośāḥ gadāḥ ca jāmbūnada paṭṭa baddhāḥ cāpāni rukma aṅgada bhūṣaṇāni śarāḥ ca kārtasvara citra puṅkhāḥ ṛṣṭyaḥ ca pītāḥ vimalāḥ vikośāḥ prāsāḥ sa khaḍgāḥ kanaka avabhāsāḥ chatrāṇi vāla vyajanāni śaṅkhāḥ srajaḥ ca puṣpa uttama hema citrāḥ kuthāḥ patākā ambara veṣṭitāḥ ca kirīṭa mālāḥ mukuṭāḥ ca śubhrāḥ prakīrṇakāḥ viprakīrṇāḥ kuthāḥ ca pradhāna muktā taralāḥ ca hārāḥ āpīḍa keyūra vara aṅgadāni graiveya niṣkāḥ sa suvarṇa sūtrāḥ maṇi uttamā vajra suvarṇa muktā gātrāṇi ca atyanta sukha ucitāni śirāṃsi ca indu pratima ānanāni dehān ca bhogān ca paricchadān ca tyaktvā manojñāni sukhāni ca api svadharma niṣṭhām mahatīm avāpya vyāptān ca lokān yaśasā samīyuḥ gatāḥ itas svarga lokāya rājan vrajasva rājan śibirāya mānada iti evam uktvā virarāma śalyaḥ duryodhanaḥ śoka parīta cetāḥ hā karṇa hā karṇa iti bruvāṇa ārtaḥ visaṃjñaḥ bhṛśam aśru netraḥ yuddhāya rājan viniviṣṭa buddhim hā karṇa hā karṇa iti bruvāṇam tam droṇaputra pramukhāḥ narendrāḥ sarve samāśvāsya saha prayānti nirīkṣamāṇāḥ muhur arjunasya dhvajam mahantam yaśasā jvalantam nara aśva mātaṅga śarīra jena raktena siktā rudhireṇa bhūmiḥ rakta ambara sraj tapanīya yogāt nārī prakāśā iva sarva gamyā pracchanna rūpāḥ rudhireṇa rājan raudre muhūrte ativirājamānāḥ na eva avatasthuḥ kuravaḥ samīkṣya pravrājitāḥ deva lokāḥ ca sarve vadhena karṇasya su duḥkhitāḥ te hā karṇa hā karṇa iti bruvāṇāḥ drutam prayātāḥ śibirāṇi rājan divākaram raktam avekṣamāṇāḥ gāṇḍīva muktaiḥ tu suvarṇa puṅkhaiḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ śoṇita digdha vājaiḥ śaraiḥ cita aṅgaḥ bhuvi bhāti karṇaḥ hataḥ api san sūryaḥ iva aṃśumālī spṛṣṭvā karaiḥ lohita rakta rūpaḥ siṣṇāsuḥ abhyeti param samudram iti iva saṃcintya sura ṛṣi saṃghāḥ saṃprasthitāḥ yānti yathā niketam tat adbhutam prāṇabhṛtām bhayaṃkaram niśamya yuddham kuru vīra mukhyayoḥ dhanaṃjayasya ādhiratheḥ ca vismitāḥ praśaṃsamānāḥ prayayuḥ tadā janāḥ śaraiḥ saṃkṛtta varmāṇam vīram viśasane hatam niṣṭapta hema vapuṣam jvalana arka sama tviṣam jīvantam iva tam śūram sarva bhūtāni menire vitresuḥ sarva bhūtāni siṃhasya iva itare mṛgāḥ na abhavat vikṛtam kim cit mṛtasya api mahātmanaḥ cāru veṣa dharam rājan cāru mauli śirodharam nānā ābharaṇavān rājan mṛṣṭa jāmbūnada aṅgadaḥ varṣitvā śara varṣāṇi pratāpya ripu vāhinīm śrīmān iva sahasrāṃśuḥ jvalan sarvān pratāpya ca arthinām pakṣi saṃghasya kalpavṛkṣaḥ nipātitaḥ kanaka uttama saṃkāśaḥ pradīptaḥ iva pāvakaḥ sa śāntaḥ puruṣa vyāghraḥ pārtha sāyaka vāriṇā yathā hi jvalanaḥ dīptaḥ jalam āsādya śāmyati karṇa agniḥ samare tadvat pārtha meghena śāmitaḥ visṛjya śara varṣāṇi pratāpya ca diśaḥ daśa sa putraḥ puruṣa vyāghraḥ saṃśāntaḥ pārtha tejasā pratāpya pāṇḍavān rājñ pāñcālān ca astra tejasā sadbhiḥ sadā sat puruṣaḥ sa hataḥ dvairathe vṛṣaḥ yasya brāhmaṇasāt sarvam ātma artham na mahātmanaḥ na a deyam brāhmaṇeṣu āsīt yasya svam api jīvitam sadā nṝṇām priyaḥ dātā priya dānaḥ divam gataḥ ādāya te putrāṇām jaya āśām śarma varma ca nabhaḥ paphāla atha nanāda ca urvī diśaḥ sa dhūmāḥ ca bhṛśam prajajvaluḥ mahā arṇavāḥ cukṣubhire ca sa svanāḥ sa kānanāḥ sa adri cayāḥ cakampuḥ pravivyathuḥ bhūta gaṇāḥ ca māriṣa bṛhaspatiḥ rohiṇīm saṃprapīḍya babhūva candra arka samāna varṇaḥ papāta ca ulkā jvalana prakāśā niśācarāḥ ca api abhavan prahṛṣṭāḥ śaśi prakāśa ānanam arjunaḥ yadā kṣureṇa karṇasya śiraḥ nyapātayat patākinā bhīma nināda ketunā hima indu śaṅkha sphaṭika avabhāsinā suvarṇa muktā maṇi vajra vidrumaiḥ alaṃkṛtena apratimāna raṃhasā raṇa ajire vīta bhayau virejatuḥ samāna yānau iva viṣṇu vāsavau ubhau tadā yādava pāṇḍu nandanau prasahya śaṅkhau dhamatuḥ su ghoṣau manāṃsi arīṇām avasādayantau suvarṇa jāla avatatau mahā svanau hima avadātau parigṛhya pāṇibhiḥ cucumbatuḥ śaṅkha varau nṛṇām varau vara ānanābhyām yugapad ca dadhmatuḥ pṛthivīm antarikṣam ca dyām apaḥ ca api apūrayat śaṅkha śabdena śūrasya mādhavasya arjunasya ca tau śaṅkha śabdena ninādayantau vanāni śailān saritaḥ diśaḥ ca tatas prayātāḥ kuravaḥ javena śrutvā eva śaṅkha svanam īryamāṇam vihāya madra adhipatim patim ca mahā āhave tam bahu śobhamānam dhanaṃjayam bhūta gaṇāḥ sametāḥ samācitau karṇa śaraiḥ paraṃtapau ubhau vyabhātām samare acyuta arjunau tamaḥ nihatya abhyuditau yathā amalau śaśāṅka sūryau iva raśmi mālinaḥ vihāya tān bāṇa gaṇān atha āgatau suhṛd vṛtau apratimāna vikramau sukham praviṣṭau śibiram svam īśvarau sadasya hūtau iva vāsava acyutau jaya abhivṛddhyā parayā abhipūjitau nihatya karṇam parama āhave tadā uvāca vīkṣamāṇāḥ diśaḥ sarvāḥ palāyante sma sarvatas vīram tu nihatam śrutvā śatrubhiḥ parama āhave sarve diśaḥ anvakīryanta tāvakāḥ bhaya mohitāḥ vāryamāṇāḥ bhaya udvignāḥ tava putreṇa bhārata teṣām tu matam ājñāya putraḥ te bharata ṛṣabha avahāram tatas cakre śalyasya anumate nṛpa yodhaiḥ mahā rathaiḥ sārdham vṛtaḥ bhārata tāvakaiḥ hata avaśeṣaiḥ tvaritaḥ śibirāya eva dudruve gāndhārāṇām sahasreṇa śakuniḥ parivāritaḥ hatam ādhirathim dṛṣṭvā śibirāya eva dudruve kṛpaḥ śāradvataḥ rājan nāga anīkena saṃvṛtaḥ aśvatthāmā tatas śūraḥ viniḥśvasya muhur muhur pāṇḍavānām jayam dṛṣṭvā śibirāya eva dudruve saṃśaptaka avaśeṣeṇa balena mahatā vṛtaḥ suśarmā api yayau rājan vīkṣamāṇaḥ bhaya āturān yayau śoka samāviṣṭaḥ cintayan vimanāḥ bahu prayayau śibirāya eva vīkṣamāṇaḥ diśaḥ daśa tatas apare su bahavaḥ bhāratānām mahā rathāḥ prādravanta raṇam hitvā bhaya āviṣṭāḥ vicetasaḥ aśru kaṇṭhāḥ bhaya udvignāḥ vepamānāḥ su vihvalāḥ kuravaḥ pradrutāḥ sarve dṛṣṭvā karṇam nipātitam praśaṃsantaḥ arjunam ke cid ke cid karṇam mahā rathāḥ teṣām yodha sahasrāṇām tāvakānām mahā mṛdhe hate karṇe mahā rāja nirāśāḥ kuravaḥ abhavan jīviteṣu atha rājyeṣu dāreṣu ca dhaneṣu ca tasya ājñām śirasā te api pratigṛhya viśām pate vivarṇa vadanāḥ dīnāḥ nyaviśanta mahā rathāḥ yathānurūpam pratipūjya tān atha praśasyamānau atulaiḥ ca karmabhiḥ uvāca āśliṣya pārtham dāśārhaḥ harṣāt vacanam abravīt vadham vai karṇa vṛtrābhyām kathayiṣyanti mānavāḥ vajriṇā nihataḥ vṛtraḥ saṃyuge bhūri tejasā tvayā tu nihataḥ karṇaḥ dhanuṣā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ vadham karṇasya saṃgrāme dīrgha kāla cikīrṣitam draṣṭum āyodhanam pūrvam āgataḥ dharmanandanaḥ su bhṛśam gāḍha viddha tvāt na aśakat sthātum āhave tatas sva śibiram yātaḥ sa rājā puruṣa ṛṣabha evam uktvā arjunam kṛṣṇaḥ sainikān idam abravīt dhṛṣṭadyumnam yudhāmanyum mādrī putrau vṛkodaram parān abhimukhāḥ yattāḥ tiṣṭhadhvam bhadram astu vaḥ yāvat āvedyate rājñe hataḥ karṇaḥ arjunena vai sa taiḥ śūraiḥ anujñātaḥ yayau rāja niveśanam śayānam rāja śārdūlam kāñcane śayana uttame agṛhṇītām ca caraṇau muditau pārthivasya tau tayoḥ praharṣam ālakṣya prahārān ca ati mānuṣān rādheyam nihatam matvā samuttasthau yudhiṣṭhiraḥ utthāya sa mahā bāhuḥ punar punar ariṃdamaḥ vāsudeva arjunau premṇā punar ca pariṣasvaje vāsudevam ca vārṣṇeyam papraccha kuru nandanaḥ tatas asmai tat yathāvṛttam vāsudevaḥ priyaṃvadaḥ īṣat utsmayamānaḥ tu kṛṣṇaḥ rājānam abravīt yudhiṣṭhiram hata amitram kṛtāñjaliḥ atha acyutaḥ diṣṭyā gāṇḍīvadhanvā ca pāṇḍavaḥ ca vṛkodaraḥ tvam ca api kuśalī rājan mādrī putrau ca pāṇḍavau muktāḥ vīra kṣayāt asmāt saṃgrāmāt loma harṣaṇāt kṣipram uttara kālāni kuru kāryāṇi pārthiva hataḥ vaikartanaḥ krūraḥ sūtaputraḥ mahā balaḥ diṣṭyā jayasi rāja indra diṣṭyā vardhasi pāṇḍava yaḥ sa dyūta jitām kṛṣṇām prāhasat puruṣa adhamaḥ tasya adya sūtaputrasya bhūmiḥ pibati śoṇitam śete asau śara dīrṇa aṅgaḥ śatruḥ te kuru puṃgava tam paśya puruṣa vyāghra vibhinnam bahudhā śaraiḥ hata amitrām imām urvīm anuśādhi mahā bhuja yattaḥ bhūtvā saha asmābhiḥ bhuṅkṣva bhogān ca puṣkalān uvāca yudhiṣṭhiraḥ tu dāśārham prahṛṣṭaḥ pratyapūjayat diṣṭyā diṣṭyā iti rāja indra prītyā ca idam uvāca ha na tat citram mahā bāho yuṣmat bāhu prasāda jam pragṛhya ca kuru śreṣṭhaḥ sa aṅgadam dakṣiṇam bhujam asakṛt ca api medhāvī kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ mama kathām etām mahā bāho divyām akathayat prabhuḥ tava kṛṣṇa prabhāveṇa gāṇḍīvena dhanaṃjayaḥ jayati abhimukhān śatrūn na ca āsīt vimukhaḥ kva cit jayaḥ ca eva dhruvaḥ mama na tu mama parājayaḥ bhīṣmaḥ droṇaḥ ca karṇaḥ ca mahātmā gautamaḥ kṛpaḥ anye ca bahavaḥ śūrāḥ ye ca teṣām padānugāḥ evam uktvā mahā rāja tam ratham hema bhūṣitam āsthāya puruṣa vyāghraḥ sva balena abhisaṃvṛtaḥ kṛṣṇa arjunābhyām vīrābhyām anumanya tatas priyam āgataḥ bahu vṛttāntam draṣṭum āyodhanam tadā ābhāṣamāṇaḥ tau vīrau ubhau mādhava phalgunau sa dadarśa raṇe karṇam śayānam puruṣa ṛṣabham citam śara śataiḥ karṇam dharmarājaḥ dadarśa ha gandha taila avasiktābhiḥ kāñcanībhiḥ sahasraśas dīpikābhiḥ kṛta uddyotam paśyate vai vṛṣam tadā saṃchinna bhinna kavacam bāṇaiḥ ca vidalīkṛtam gāṇḍīva muktaiḥ viśikhaiḥ sarvatas śakalīkṛtam sa putram nihatam dṛṣṭvā karṇam rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ saṃjāta pratyayaḥ atīva vīkṣ ca evam punar punar praśaśaṃsa nara vyāghrau ubhau mādhava pāṇḍavau adya rājā asmi govinda pṛthivyām bhrātṛbhiḥ saha tvayā nāthena vīreṇa viduṣā paripālitaḥ hatam dṛṣṭvā nara vyāghram rādheyam abhimāninam nirāśaḥ adya durātmā asau dhārtarāṣṭraḥ bhaviṣyati jīvitāt ca api rājyāt ca hate karṇe mahā rathe tvad prasādāt vayam ca eva kṛtārthāḥ puruṣa ṛṣabha tvam ca gāṇḍīvadhanvā ca vijayī yadunandana diṣṭyā jayasi govinda diṣṭyā karṇaḥ nipātitaḥ trayodaśa samāstīrṇāḥ jāgareṇa su duḥkhitāḥ evam sa bahuśas hṛṣṭaḥ praśaśaṃsa janārdanam arjunam ca api rāja indra dharmarājaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca dṛṣṭvā ca karṇam nihatam sa putram pārtha sāyakaiḥ praśaśaṃsuḥ tatas sarve rājānaḥ bhūri tejasaḥ tatas bhīma prabhṛtibhiḥ sarvaiḥ ca bhrātṛbhiḥ vṛtam vardhayanti sma rājānam harṣa yuktāḥ mahā rathāḥ nakulaḥ sahadevaḥ ca pāṇḍavaḥ ca vṛkodaraḥ sātyakiḥ ca mahā rāja vṛṣṇīnām pravaraḥ rathaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca pāṇḍu pāñcāla sṛñjayāḥ te vardhayitvā nṛpatim pāṇḍu putram yudhiṣṭhiram jita kāśinaḥ labdhalakṣāḥ yuddha śauṇḍāḥ prahāriṇaḥ stuvantaḥ stava yuktābhiḥ vāgbhiḥ kṛṣṇau paraṃtapau jagmuḥ sva śibirāya eva mudā yuktāḥ mahā rathāḥ evam eṣa kṣayaḥ vṛttaḥ su mahān loma harṣaṇaḥ uvāca śrutvā tat apriyam rājñ dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ mahīpatiḥ papāta bhūmau niśceṣṭaḥ kauravyaḥ parama ārtivān tathā satyavratā devī gāndhārī dharma darśinī śuśoca bahula ālāpaiḥ karṇasya nidhanam yudhi tam pratyagṛhṇāt viduraḥ nṛpatim saṃjayaḥ tathā paryāśvāsayataḥ ca evam tau ubhau eva bhūmipam tathā eva utthāpayām āsuḥ gāndhārīm rāja yoṣitaḥ parām pīḍām samāśritya naṣṭa cittaḥ mahā tapāḥ cintā śoka parīta ātmā na jajñe moha pīḍitaḥ tābhyām āśvāsitaḥ rājā tūṣṇīm āsīt vicetanaḥ tat āpnuyāt saṃśravaṇāt ca bhārata atas anasūyuḥ śṛṇute paṭhet ca yaḥ tat phalam labhate martyaḥ karṇa ākhyānam śṛṇoti hi hiraṇya vastra dhānyāni gām sa vatsām upānahau tena brahmā ca viṣṇuḥ ca rudrāḥ ca vasavaḥ tathā pūjitāḥ munayaḥ sarve pitaraḥ ca tathā aśvinaḥ yaḥ śṛṇoti sadā bhaktyā karṇa ākhyānam anuttamam dharma artha kāma mokṣāṇām caturvidha phalam labhet tām sarvadā bhaktim upāgatāḥ narāḥ paṭhanti puṇyām vara saṃhitām imām dhanena dhānyena yaśasā ca mānuṣā atas anasūyuḥ śṛṇuyāt sadā tu vai naraḥ sa sarvāṇi sukhāni ca āpnuyāt viṣṇuḥ svayambhuḥ bhagavān bhavaḥ ca veda avāptiḥ brāhmaṇasya iha dṛṣṭā raṇe balam kṣatriyāṇām jayaḥ yudhi dhana jyeṣṭhāḥ ca api bhavanti vaiśyāḥ śūdra ārogyam prāpnuvanti iha sarve tathā eva viṣṇuḥ bhagavant sanātanaḥ tatas sa kāmān labhate sukhī kapilānām sa vatsānām varṣam ekam nirantaram yaḥ dadyāt su kṛtam tat hi śravaṇāt karṇaparvaṇaḥ pāṇḍavānām mahā iṣvāsāḥ nyaviśanta paraṃtapāḥ prahṛṣṭa manasaḥ sarve jitvā śatrūn mahā rathān tatas yudhiṣṭhiram tatra niviṣṭam vai mudā anvitam arjunaḥ tu rathāt tūrṇam avaruhya mahā yaśāḥ dharmarājasya caraṇau pīḍayām āsa hṛṣṭa vat nakulaḥ sahadevaḥ ca pāṇḍavaḥ ca vṛkodaraḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca pāṇḍavānām ca ye rathāḥ tatas kṛṣṇaḥ mahā rāja sātyakiḥ ca api sātvataḥ avardhayetām rājānam nihate sūtanandane vāsudevaḥ ca kaunteyam praṇayāt idam abravīt adya rājan hatāḥ sarve dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ sa rājakāḥ yadi lokāḥ trayaḥ sarve yodhayeyuḥ sa vāsavāḥ tathā api durjayaḥ sūtaḥ te kopāt tu sūditaḥ te prasādāt govinda hataḥ karṇaḥ mahā yaśāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ ca jayam prāptāḥ nāśitāḥ ca api śatravaḥ tvam asya jagataḥ goptā pāṇḍavānām ca sarvadā tvām samāsādya śakraḥ api modate divi nityaśas tvam pātā pāṇḍu putrāṇām yathā eva jagataḥ tathā anāścaryaḥ jayaḥ teṣām bhaktiḥ yeṣām tvayi prabho yathā indreṇa purā devāḥ tvayā ca api janārdana svapsyāmi adya sukham kṛṣṇa nidrām lapsye vasan kṣapām vigatam hi bhayam mama adya tvad prasādāt na saṃśayaḥ evam uktaḥ tu pārthena keśavaḥ prāha pāṇḍavam yasya te bhrātaraḥ śūrāḥ bhīmasena ādayaḥ nṛpa saṃbandhinaḥ ca indra vīryāḥ pārṣata pramukhāḥ tathā āsthāya puruṣa vyāghraḥ sva balena abhisaṃvṛtaḥ prayayau bahu vṛttāntam draṣṭum āyodhanam prati saṃbhāṣamāṇau tau vīrau ubhau pāṇḍava mādhavau sa dadarśa raṇe karṇam śayānam puruṣa ṛṣabha gāṇḍīva muktaiḥ viśikhaiḥ sarvatas su nipīḍitam sa putram nihatam dṛṣṭvā karṇam rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ praśaśaṃsa nara vyāghrau ubhau pāṇḍava mādhavau adya rājā asmi sarvasyām pṛthivyām madhusūdana diṣṭyā jayasi govinda diṣṭyā śatruḥ nipātitaḥ evam su bahuśas rājan praśaśaṃsa janārdanam arjunam ca kuru śreṣṭhaḥ dharmarājaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ dṛṣṭvā ca nihatam karṇam sa putram pārtha sāyakaiḥ sametya ca kuru śreṣṭham kuntī putram yudhiṣṭhiram vardhayanti sma rājānam harṣa yuktāḥ mahā rathāḥ uvāca evam eṣa kṣayaḥ vṛttaḥ su mahān romaharṣaṇaḥ uvāca śrutvā etat vipriyam rājā dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ mahīpatiḥ papāta bhūmau niśceṣṭaḥ kauravyaḥ parama āsanāt tathā satyavratā devī gāndhārī divya darśinī tatas tūrṇam tu viduraḥ tam nṛpam saṃjayaḥ tathā paryāśvāsayatām ca etau ubhau eva tu bhūmipam tathā eva āśvāsayām āsa gāndhārī rāja sattamam tābhyām āśvāsitaḥ rājā tūṣṇīm āste viśām pate evam ākhyāya rājñe ca saṃjayaḥ rāja sattama jagāma śibiram bhūyas hate karṇe mahātmani sa dṛṣṭvā nihatam śalyam rājānam ca suyodhanam yodhān ca su bahūn rājan sainikān ca sahasraśas tathā eva pāṇḍavām senām nihatām prekṣya saṃjayaḥ sa hi dṛṣṭvā hatān sarvān samantāt yudhi saṃjayaḥ yodhaiḥ ca eva mahā rāja nānā deśa samudbhavaiḥ kurukṣetram tu tat sarvam śūnyam āsīt jagatpate nihataiḥ pāṇḍaveyaiḥ ca dhārtarāṣṭraiḥ ca saṃyuge yathā viṣaya jam vṛttam dhārtarāṣṭrasya saṃjayaḥ śaśaṃsuḥ nihitam karṇam phalgunena mahātmanā yayatuḥ tatra tau tūrṇam yatra āsīt vīra saṃkṣayaḥ pradīpa hastāḥ śataśas samantāt pratyayuḥ narāḥ punar ca śibiram prāptaḥ bhrātṛbhiḥ bharata ṛṣabhaḥ yat kṛtvā tu ca kartavyam sukha āsīnam yudhiṣṭhiram
